# Kwibohora 27 : Abanyarwanda batuye mu Busuwisi beretse amahanga ibyo u Rwanda rumaze kugeraho
Abanyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda batuye mu Busuwisi , Autriche , na Liechtenstein bizihije ku nshuro ya 27 Umunsi wo Kwibohora , baratira amahanga ibyo igihugu kimaze kugeraho kibikesha imiyoborere myiza ya FPR Inkotanyi .
Ni ibirori byabaye ku wa 06 Nyakanga 2021 hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu kwirinda COVID - 19 , byitabirwa na abahagarariye ibihugu byabo , abakozi ba Umuryango wa Abibumbye , ndetse na abakozi ba imiryango mpuzamahanga bakorera i Genève mu Busuwisi .
Insanganyamatsiko yagiraga iti " " " " Dufatanyije tugera ku iterambere . " " " "
Mu ijambo yagejeje ku bitabiriye , Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda mu Busuwisi , Umuryango wa Abibumbye na Imiryango Mpuzamahanga ikorera i Genève ; Rwakazina Marie Chantal yakeje ingabo za RPA zabohoye igihugu , azishimira ubutwari , ubwitange ndetse no kutizigama byaziranze .
Yashimiye cyane Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame waziyoboye zigahagarika Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , amahanga arebera .
Ambasaderi Rwakazina yagize ati " " " " Itariki ya 4 Nyakanga ntizibagirana mu mateka ya Isi haba ku Banyarwanda na abanyamahanga kuko ni ikimenyetso cya ihagarikwa rya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Jenoside yagombaga kuba yaraburijwemo , ariko igakorwa na Leta nkoramaraso yari yaramunzwe na amacakubiri , igategura ndetse igashyira mu bikorwa umugambi wayo amahanga arebera . " " " "
Yibukije ko nyuma yo guhagarika Jenoside intego za FPR Inkotanyi kwari ugutuza buri Munyarwanda mu gihugu akubaka ejo heza mu mahoro na ituze .
Yaboneyeho kugaragaza isura nshya u Rwanda rufite , anamurikira abitabiriye ibirori bimwe mu byo rwagezweho mu myaka 27 ishize mu bukungu na imibereho myiza ya abaturage , rukesha imiyoborere myiza ya Perezida Kagame .
Ambasaderi Rwakazina yakanguriye Abanyarwanda bya umwihariko urubyiruko rutuye imahanga gushishikarira guteza imbere igihugu cyabo kuko aribo maboko yacyo , abasaba kugira uruhare rugaragara mu gusigasira ibyagezweho no gutanga umusanzu mu iterambere ryacyo .
Ibirori byaranzwe n " " " " imbyino na indirimbo Nyarwanda bya Itorero rya Igihugu , Urukerereza ; ibiganiro , imivugo , ubuhamya bwa Abanyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda byose bishimira bikanarata ingabo zahoze ari iza RPA zarubohoye zikanahagarika Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi Abatutsi .
Abanyarwanda baba USA bibukijwe ko badakwiye gusinzira ngo bibagirwe ababohoye Igihugu
Abanyarwanda batuye muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika bya umwihariko mu gice cya Uburengerazuba bwo hagati , bizihije Isabukuru ya imyaka 27 yo kwibohora ka u Rwanda , bazirikana ubutwari na ubwitange bwa FPR Inkotanyi banibutswa ko badakwiye gusinzira ngo bibagirwe abaguye muri uru rugamba .
Uyu muhango wabaye ku wa 4 Nyakanga 2021 , muri Leta ya Indiana mu Majyepfo ya Umujyi wa Bend , aho Abanyarwanda benshi baturutse mu bice birimo Michigan , Illinois , Ohio na Tennessee bahuriye hamwe mu kwishimira ukwibohora ka u Rwanda .
Umuyobozi wa Diaspora Nyarwanda muri Midwest , Nxumalo Ruhaya , yashimiye Ambasade ya u Rwanda yohereje Lt Col . Raoul Bazatoha uyishinzwemo ibikorwa bya gisirikare ngo aze kwifatanya na Abanyarwanda .
Ruhaya yibukije abitabiriye uyu muhango ko batagomba gusinzira ngo bibagirwe abagabo na abagore , abasore na inkumi ba ingabo za RPA , bemeye guhara ubuzima bwabo kugira ngo Abanyarwanda bose bagire igihugu cyiza bishimira kandi bita iwabo .
Lt Col . Raoul Bazatoha , yibukije abitabiriye uyu muhango amateka yaranze urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda no guhagarika Jenoside yakorerwaga Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Yavuze ko FPR Inkotanyi ijya gutegura urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda hari impamvu zifatika yari ifite zirimo ubutegetsi bubi bwahereye mu myaka ya 1959 butanya Abanyarwanda , buvutsa benshi amahirwe yo kuba mu gihugu cyabo , ingengabitekerezo iganisha kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi na ibindi bitandukanye .
Lt Col Bazatoha yashimiye Perezida Kagame wayoboye urwo rugamba ndetse akaba akomeje kuyobora urundi rukomeye rwo kubaka u Rwanda no guhesha agaciro Abanyarwanda .
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ukwibohora kwacu kwagezweho kandi dukeneye kwibohora mu buryo burambye .
Ukwibohora kuzuye ni ukuba witeguye kurinda icyubahiro cya igihugu cyacu .
Urugamba rwo kwibohora rurakomeje , mu kubaka ubuhanga na ubushobozi ndetse no kwigira kwa igihugu cyacu . " " " "
Lt Col Bazatoha avuga ko ibyo byose bizagerwaho ari uko bigizwemo uruhare na abaturage bose bya umwihariko abagiye mu mahanga kubera impamvu zitandukanye zirimo guhaha ubumenyi na ubushobozi .
Ibirori bya isabukuru ya 27 yo Kwibohora , muri Amerika , igice cya Midwest byaranzwe na imbwirwaruhame za abayobozi batandukanye , ubuhamya bwa abarokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bwagarutse ku kuntu ingabo za FPR Inkotanyi zabarokoye , indirimbo zigaruka ku butwari bwa Inkotanyi na ibindi .
Uyu muhango wahurije hamwe bamwe mu Banyarwanda batuye mu burengerazuba bwo hagati bwa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika
Ushinzwe ibikorwa bya gisirikare muri Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri USA , Lt Col . Raoul Bazatoha , yibukije abitabiriye uyu muhango amateka yaranze urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda
Emmanuel Hategeka yatanze impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Bahrain
Ambasaderi Emmanuel Hategeka uhagarariye u Rwanda mu bihugu birimo Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu , yashyikirije Umwami wa Bahrain , Hamad bin Isa Al Khalifa , impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu .
Uyu muhango wabereye mu ngoro ya Umwami mu murwa mukuru Manama ku wa kabiri tariki ya 6 Nyakanga 2021 .
Nyuma yo gutanga izo mpapuro , Ambasaderi Hategeka yashimye umubano mwiza usanzwe hagati ya ibihugu byombi , avuga ko yiteguye guteza imbere ubufatanye hagati ya ibihugu byombi mu nzego zinyuranye .
Yagizi ati " " " " Ntewe ishema cyane no kuba nashyikirije Umwami Hamad bin Isa Al Khalifa impapuro zinyemerera guhagararira u Rwanda mu Bwami bwa Bahrain .
Niteguye guteza imbere umubano wa ibihugu byombi . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Nashyikirije Umwami indamutso ya Nyakubahwa Perezida Paul Kagame ndetse na ubushake bwe bwo guteza imbere umubano hagati ya ibihugu byombi na abaturage babyo . " " " "
Ambasaderi Hategeka yaboneyeho umwanya wo kwifuriza Umwami Hamad bin Isa Al Khalifa ubuzima bwiza ndetse yifuriza igihugu amahoro , iterambere na uburumbuke .
Igihugu cya Bahrain , ubusanzwe cyitwa Ubwami bwa Bahrain , giherereye mu kigobe cya Perse .
Ni Ikirwa kigizwe na uturwa duto karemano turenga 50 ndetse na utundi abantu bahimbye tugeze kuri 33 .
U Rwanda rufite umubano mwiza na Bahrain umaze imyaka irenga 25 , aho ibihugu byombi byasinye amasezerano ya Ubufatanye mu bya diplomasi muri Werurwe 1998 .
Ibihugu byombi bikorana mu nzego zirimo kwaguriramo ubufatanye mu bucuruzi na ishoramari , ubukerarugendo , serivisi za imari , ingufu , ikoranabuhanga , guhanga imirimo na udushya .
Nka Ambasaderi ufite icyicaro Abu Dhabi , Emmanuel Hategeka asanzwe ahagarariye u Rwanda muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu ( UAE ) , Ubwami bwa Saudi Arabia na Ikigo mpuzamahanga gishinzwe ingufu zisubir a ( IRENA ) .
Ambasaderi Hategeka yakiriwe na Umwami Hamad wa Bahrain .
# Kwibohora27 : Abanya - Singapore bashimye uko u Rwanda rwiyubatse mu gihe gito .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya itangazamakuru ya Singapore , Tan How Kiat , yavuze ko aho u Rwanda rugeze ari imwe mu nkuru za Afurika zibumbatiye intsinzi ikomeye , zihamya imbaraga na ukwiyubaka vuba kwa Abanyarwanda .
Ibyo Kiat yabitangarije mu muhango wo kwizihiza Umunsi wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 ku Banyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda baba muri Singapore , Australie , Nouvelle Zélande na Indonésie byabaye ku wa 5 Nyakanga 2021 hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Kuva ingabo za FPR Inkotanyi zahagarika Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , igihugu cyabayemo impinduka zikomeye bitoroshye kuzisobanurira utazibonera .
Kongera kwiyubaka mu gihe gito u Rwanda rukaba rubaye icyitegererezo mu ruhando mpuzamahanga , ni byo Minisitiri Kiat yavuze ko ari imwe mu nkuru za ubutsinzi bukomeye .
Yasobanuye ko nubwo ubukungu bwa Isi bwahungabanye kubera COVID - 19 , u Rwanda " " " " rwo rwabyitwayemo neza kubera ubuyobozi bwiza bururangaje imbere . " " " "
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Singapore , Uwihanganye Jean de Dieu , yashimiye umubano mwiza uri hagati ya ibihugu byombi ; aboneraho kugaragaza ko kuva byatangira imikoranire mu bya dipolomasi mu 2005 , habayeho ubufatanye mu kubaka ubushobozi , kungurana ubumenyi no guhanahana amakuru , ubumenyi na koranabuhanga , ishoramari , ubucuruzi
na ubukerarugendo .
Ubwo bufatanye bwateye imbere kandi buratanga icyizere .
Ambasaderi Uwihamganye yakomeje avuga ko ibihugu byombi biherutse gusinyana amasezerano ya imikoranire mu ikoranabuhanga ryo mu ishoramari , ubucamanza ndetse no mu burezi aho abanyeshuri bo mu gihugu kimwe bazajya boroherezwa kwiga mu kindi nta nkomyi .
Yagaragaje ko sosiyete za Abanya - Singapore zagiriye u Rwanda icyizere zikahashora imari mu nzego zitandukanye zirimo inganda , ubuhinzi na ubwikorezi ; hakaba hari na abandi bashoramari baho bashya bacyiza bafite gahunda za ishoramari zishimishije .
Umwe muri abo Banya - Singapore bageze mu Rwanda akaba na Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Magerwa , Kong Kok Chee , yatanze ubuhamya bwe ku ishoramari ryo mu Rwanda ndetse aboneraho kurushimira iterambere rumaze kugeraho .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Singapore , Uwihanganye Jean de Dieu , yashimiye umubano mwiza uri hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya itangazamakuru ya Singapore , Tan How Kiat , yavuze ko aho u Rwanda rugeze ari imwe mu nkuru za Afurika zibumbatiye intsinzi iikomeye .
Umwe Banya - Singapore bageze mu Rwanda akaba na Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Magerwa , Kong Kok Chee , yatanze ubuhamya bwe ku ishoramari ryo mu Rwanda .
Umunsi wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 ku Banyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda baba muri Singapore , Australie , Nouvelle Zélande na Indonésie wizihijwe ku wa 5 Nyakanga 2021 hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Amb . Mukantabana yakebuye Abanyarwanda bari mu mahanga barebera abasebya urwababyaye .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Mukantabana Mathilde , yongeye kwibutsa Abanyarwanda baba mu mahanga kutarebera abasebya igihugu cyabo ahubwo bakaba ba " " " " Perezida " " " " aho bari .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na One Nation Radio ku wa 29 Kamena 2021 , Ambasaderi Mukantabana yavuze ko buri Munyarwanda agomba kumva ko aho ari ahagarariye igihugu cye akakirwanira ishyaka , baba bagize amahirwe bakahahurira ari benshi bagafatanya .
Ati " " " " Aho uri hose uri Perezida waho ntabwo uri wenyine .
Uzi ko uri kumwe na abandi , [ guhangana na abasebya u Rwanda ] na iyo utanashaka kubikora wenyine wabikorana na abandi muri leta zose barahari .
Kuki umuntu yaza agatoba amateka yica igihugu [ . . . ] kandi muzi neza ko atari byo ? " " " "
Yagaragaje ko isura nziza u Rwanda rwubatse mu ruhando mpuzamahanga ari yo ituma bagera hanze bakubahwa , bityo ko bagomba kuyirinda kugira ngo icyubahiro bahabwa kigumeho .
Ati " " " " Igihugu cyanyu cyaragiye kibashyira mu mwanya abantu bose babubaha aho muri hose kubera ibyo gikora .
Icyo washobora kugikorera ni uko batazajya baza ngo bagitere amabuye kuko iyo bamaze kwica iryo zina cyubatse nawe ntusigara uhagaze neza . " " " "
Yakomoje ku bihugu na abanyamahanga bakunda kwifashisha itangazamakuru baharabika u Rwanda .
Ati " " " " Uzajya aza abeshya , muzi ko abeshya ; amakuru arahari , ibihamya birahari , ni ukugenda mugahangana nabyo mukabivuga kandi ntabwo bizaba ari bibi ni ugukiza igihugu kizaba icya abana banyu . " " " "
Abanditsi , abanyamakuru na abanyepolitiki bo mu Burengerazuba bwa Isi bakunze kumvikana baharabika u Rwanda , akenshi bakabivuga mu rwego rwa ubutabera .
Ambasaderi Mukantabana yabwiye Abanyarwanda ko " " " " ntawe ubarusha kwandika " " " " bityo ko niba abo banditse nabo bagomba kwandika babanyomoza kuko abenshi baba banabivuga batabisobanukiwe .
Amb . Karabaranga yagaragaje uko politiki yari yarimakaje ivangura yashyizweho iherezo .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Jean Pierre Karabaranga yasabye Abanyarwanda aho bari hose kuzirikana Umunsi wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 ariko bibuka aho igihugu cyavuye na aho kigeze mu rwego rwo kurushaho gutera indi ntambwe cyifuza mu iterambere , babigizemo uruhare .
Hari mu muhango wo kwizihiza umunsi wo kwibuhora ku nshuro ya 27 , Abanyarwanda baba muri Sénégal bateguye bifashishije ikoranabuhanga ndetse ukanitabirwa na inshuti za u Rwanda na abahagarariye abanyarwanda baba mu bihugu bimwe na bimwe byo muri Afurika ya Iburengerazuba harimo Sénégal , Mali , Gambie , Guinée - Bissau na Cap - Vert .
Ambasaderi Karabaranga yavuze ko Kwibohora byaje ari umusaruro uvuye mu bwitange bwa Inkotanyi ziyemeje guhagarika Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ndetse no kubohora Abanyarwanda ubutegetsi bubi bwari bwarasaritswe na ivanguramoko ndetse no gukandamiza rubanda .
Yagize ati " " " " Uyu munsi nka uko mubizi , tariki ya 4 Nyakanga mu mwaka 1994 ni bwo FPR yahagaritse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , aho abasaga miliyoni imwe bishwe .
Iyo ntsinzi kandi ihurirana no guhagarika ubutegetsi bubi bwa igitugu .
Umunsi wo kwibohora rero ku Rwanda na Abanyarwanda ni ingenzi cyane kandi ni umunsi wongera kuzamura imbamutima zacu . " " " "
" " " " Uyu munsi kandi ugaragaza iherezo rya imyaka 32 ya Politiki mbi yimakaje ivangura uhereye ku munsi u Rwanda rwaboneho ubwigenge , iyo politiki yatsinzwe mu 1994 .
Ukwibohora kwacu ni umusaruro wa intwari zitanze , abagabo na abagore basanzwe ariko abenshi muri bo bari urubyiruko , bahaye intsinzi igihugu bagashyiraho iherezo kuri ibyo byose . " " " "
Yavuze ko bashingiye ku butwari bwaranze Inkotanyi mu rugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda bakwiye gushyiraho umusanzu wabo mu iterambere rya igihugu cyane ko aho kigeze ari heza .
" " " " Ku bwa ibyo turibanda cyane kuri zo ntwari zacu , ibyo bakoze cyane ko na ubwigenge dufite uyu munsi ari bo .
Kuri uyu munsi twibuka aho twavuye , tukareba na aho tugeze .
Imyaka 27 irashize , abakuze murabizi ko u Rwanda rwari igihugu cyarimbutse , rwasenywe ku buryo bukomeye , ariko uyu munsi rwarahindutse kuko rwateye imbere mu ngeri zose . " " " "
" " " " Twageze kuri byinshi tutari gutekereza nyuma ya ihagarikwa rya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ibyo rwagezeho bisobanuye igihugu gifite ubuyobozi bwiza , buha buri muturage amahirwe .
Abanyarwanda turi hanze ya igihugu dukwiye kugira uruhare rugaragara mu iterambere rya igihugu cyacu , dushingiye ku buyobozi bwiza bwa Perezida Kagame . " " " "
Major Joseph Niyongabo Kabanda , wari intumwa ya RDF muri iki gikorwa , yavuze ko igitera umusirikare wese imbaraga zo kurwanira igihugu cye ari urukundo aba agifitiye no kukirwanira ishyaka .
Yavuze ko ahanini byatewe na akababaro banyuzemo no kubona agahinda Abanyarwanda bakomeje guhura na ko biyemeza kugaruka mu gihugu cyababyaye .
Nubwo inzira za ibiganiro ubutegetsi bwari buriho butigeza buzemera biyemeje kwitanga kandi ngo byatanze umusaruro .
Mu butumwa Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga muri Sénégal yageneye Abanyarwanda bwatanzwe na Ambasaderi Stephan Slyvain Sambou , yavuze ko ari ibya agaciro kuri bo kwifatanya na u Rwanda , anavuga ko iyo tariki idakwiye kwibagirana mu matwi ya Abanyarwanda na Abanyafurika cyane ko muri iki gihugu basobanukiwe amateka ya Jenoside
yakorewe abatutsi .
Mu bandi batanze ubutumwa harimo Minisitiri wa UbubanyI na Amahanga wa Mali , Abdoulaye Diop , kimwe na uwari uhagarariye Guinée - Bissau bavuze ko nubwo Abanyarwanda banyuze mu bihe bikomeye ariko baranzwe na ubutwari , kandi ko bazakomeza kwagura imikoranire na u Rwanda , bitewe na uko ubu ari urugero rwiza rwa igihugu gifite politiki
ihamye .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Jean Pierre Karabaranga yasabye Abanyarwanda baba mu mahanga kugira uruhare mu bikorwa biteza igihugu imbere .
Urubyiruko na rwo rwakurikiye ibiganiro byatanzwe kugira ngo rubashe kumenya amateka ya uko urwanda rwabohowe .
Major Joseph Niyongabo Kabanda , wari intumwa ya RDF muri iki gikorwa , yavuze ko igitera umusirikare wese imbaraga zo kurwanira igihugu cye ari urukundo aba agifitiye no kukirwanira ishyaka .
Dr Abdallah Utumatwishima yitabiriye iki gikorwa .
Kubera ko guhurira hamwe abantu ari benshi bitoroshye ikoranabuhanga ryifashishijwe muri iki gikorwa .
Benshi bakurikiye iki gikorwa hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga kubera ibihe isi irimo bya icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Habinshuti Antoinette Tony wayoboye ibiganiro .
Rwiyemezamirimo ukiri muto , Mammy Ingabire Muziga .
Abanyarwanda mu Burengerazuba bwa Afurika bibutse urubyiruko rwazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Abanyarwanda na inshuti zabo mu bihugu bya Uburengerazuba bwa Afurika birimo Sénégal , Mali , Gambie , Cap - Vert na Guinée Bissau , bibutse ku nshuro ya 27 urubyiruko rwishwe muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ; basaba abakiri bato kwigira ku ngabo za FPR Inkotanyi zayihagaritse .
Ni umuhango wabaye ku wa 26 Kamena 2021 , ukorwa hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo kubahiriza amabwiriza yo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Covid - 19 .
Abatanze ubutumwa barimo Jean Pierre Karabaranga , Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Mali , Gambia , Cap - Vert na Guinea Bissau ; Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Ikigo cya Ubushakashatsi na Ububikoshakiro muri Komisiyo ya Igihugu yo kurwanya Jenoside ( CNLG ) , Dr Jean Damasc ė ne Gasanabo ; Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Rwanda Airports Company , Charles Habonimana na abandi
Uyu muhango kandi witabiriwe na umuhanzi wa icyamamare muri Sénégal , Ismaël Lô ; Umunya - Sénégal wanditse inyandiko zitandukanye zamagana abahakana na abapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , Amadou Tidiane Fall na abandi benshi barimo Abanyarwanda na abanyamahanga .
Abitabiriye basobanuriwe amateka mabi yaranze u Rwanda kuva mu 1959 kugeza kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ; amateka yaranzwe no kwigisha ivangura na amacakubiri mu Banyarwanda bikozwe na ubutegetsi bubi bwagiye busimburana .
Hagaragajwe uko Jenoside yateguwe na ingengabitekerezo yayo igacengezwa mu Banyarwanda igihe kirekire , ndetse ikanageragezwa mu bihe bitandukanye kugeza ishyizwe mu bikorwa mu 1994 , aho Abatutsi basaga miliyoni bishwe mu gihe cya iminsi ijana gusa .
Abatanze ibiganiro kandi basobanuye ko urubyiruko rwagize uruhare rukomeye mu ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya Jenoside kubera inyigisho mbi rwahawe ; kandi no mu gihe nyirizina cya Jenoside hari umubare munini wa urubyiruko rwishwe bituma igihugu kibura ubwenge na imbaraga byagombye kugiteza imbere .
Abitabiriye gahunda yo kwibuka urubyiruko rwishwe muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bashimiye urubyiruko rwari mu ngabo zari iza FPR Inkotanyi zari ziyobowe na Perezida Kagame , rwitanze rutizigama , rugahagarika Jenoside yakorerwaga Abatutsi rukabohora igihugu .
Urubyiruko rukaba rwasabwe gufatira urugero kuri ubwo butwari bwaranze izo ngabo .
Urubyiruko rwitabiriye ibiganiro rwihaye umukoro wo guhangana na abagifite ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside , abayihakana na abayipfobya , rusaba ko abakomeje kwijandika muri ibyo bikorwa bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga bakurikiranwa bakabihanirwa bya intangarugero .
Rwasabye kandi ko hakorwa ubuvugizi kugira ngo icyaha cyo gupfobya no guhakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi no gukwirakwiza ingengabitekerezo yayo gishyirwe mu mategeko ya ibindi bihugu .
Ikindi rwasabye ni uko amahanga akurikirana abakidegembya hirya no hino mu bihugu bitandukanye kandi barasize bahekuye u Rwanda mu 1994 .
Abanyarwanda bo mu Burengerazuba bwa Afurika bifatanyije na inshuti zabo mu kwibuka urubyiruko rwazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Me Gisagara Richard uba mu Bufaransa na we yitabiriye iki gikorwa cyo kwibuka urubyiruko rwazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Umubyeyi Beata Mairesse atanga ibitekerezo muri iki gikorwa .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Jean Pierre Karabaranga , yashimye abagize uruhare mu migendekere myiza yo kwibuka abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Jessica Mwiza na we yitabiriye umuhango wibukiwemo urubyiruko rwazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Ikigo cya Ubushakashatsi na Ububikoshakiro muri Komisiyo ya Igihugu yo kurwanya Jenoside ( CNLG ) , Dr Jean Damasc ė ne Gasanabo , yatanze ishusho ya uburyo Jenoside yateguwe ikanashyirwa mu bikorwa .
Umunyamakuru wa IGIHE i Burayi , Karirima A . Ngarambe yatanze ibitekerezo muri iki gikorwa yayoboye .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Guinea Bissau bibutse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ( Amafoto ) .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Guinea Bissau bifatanyije na inshuti zabo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , yahitanye ubuzima bwa inzirakarengane zisaga miliyoni imwe mu gihe cya amezi atatu gusa .
Uyu muhango wabaye muri iki cyumweru , ku wa 24 Kamena 2021 .
Witabiriwe na abantu batandukanye barimo Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Urubyiruko na Siporo muri Guinea Bissau , Namil Pinto Morgado na abahagarariye Ambasade za ibihugu bya Nigeria , Mali , Gambia , Afurika ya Epfo , Guinea Conakry , abahagarariye Umuryango wa Ubumwe bwa Afurika na Umuryango wa Ubumwe bwa u Burayi .
Abawitabiriye bafashe umunota wo kuzirikana abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , hanacanwa urumuri rwa icyizere cya ahazaza .
Banaganirijwe ku buryo umugambi wa Jenoside wateguwe , ukanashyirwa mu bikorwa .
Perezida wa Umuryango wa Abanyarwanda baba muri Guinea Bissau , Moise Sande , yagarutse ku mateka ya u Rwanda mbere ya Jenoside yaranzwe na politiki mbi yo gucamo ibice abaturage bigishwa amacakubiri na ivangura , guheza Abatutsi mu mashuri no mu mirimo , ubwicanyi mu bihe bitandukanye kugera kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yagaragaje ko nyuma ya Jenoside hashyizwe ingufu mu kubungabunga umutekano wa Abanyarwanda na ibyabo , uburenganzira bwa muntu , ubumwe na ubwiyunge bya Abanyarwanda na ibikorwa bya iterambere bigamije imibereho ya Abanyarwanda na iterambere rirambye .
Ijambo rya Umuyobozi wari uhagarariye Guverinoma ya Guinea Bissau ryibanze ku gushima ubuyobozi bwiza bwa igihugu burangajwe imbere na Perezida Kagame .
Yavuze ko kuri ubu u Rwanda ari intangarugero ku Mugabane wa Afurika na ubwo rwaciye mu mateka mabi ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Abitabiriye uyu muhango kandi banasangijwe ubutumwa bwa urubyiruko bwibanze ku gukangurira abantu bose kwamagana abagifite ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside , abayihakana na abayipfobya .
Ibihe byo kwibuka abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 byahuriranye na icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyatumye uburyo byakorwagamo buhinduka .
Mu bihugu byinshi byakozwe hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu gihe abantu bake aribo babashaga kugera aho ibikorwa byabereye .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Guinea Bissau bibutse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Guinea Bissau bifatanyije na inshuti zabo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Abayobozi na abakozi ba EAC bahuriye mu bikorwa byo kwibuka Jenoside ku nshuro ya 27 .
Abayobozi ba Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba ( EAC ) na abo mu zindi nzego ziwushamikiyeho , bahuriye mu gikorwa cyo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 , Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ku wa Gatanu , ku kicaro cya uyu muryango i Arusha muri Tanzania .
Ku rwego rwa EAC , ibikorwa byo kwibuka byari byabaye ku ya 7 Mata , umunsi icyunamo gitangiriraho ariko Ubunyamabanga bwa uyu muryango bwemeza ko mu gihe cya iminsi ijana ( 100 ) yo kwibuka hakomeza gutegurwa ibikorwa byo kwibuka ari na ko hategurwa ibiganiro bihuje inzego zitandukanye , bakanaganira ku cyakorwa mu kurwanya
abapfobya Jenoside .
Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa EAC , Dr Peter Muthuki , yavuze ko m minsi 100 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yamaze , Abatutsi barenga miliyoni bavukijwe ubuzima bwabo isi yose irebera ntacyo ikora ngo iyihagarike , ariko ko igihe kigeze ngo buri wese ashimangire ko itazongera kubaho ukundi mu Rwanda na ahandi mu karere no kwa isi .
Dr . Peter Muthuki yasabye abitabiriye kwibuka ko buri wese afite uruhare rwo gushikama mu ngamba zo kurwanya ipfobya rya Jenoside ashishikariza abagize uwo muryango gusubiza amaso inyuma , bakarebera hamwe ibihungabanya amahoro na umutekano mu Karere maze hakabaho ubufatanye mu guteza imbere kubana mu mahoro .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Tanzania , Gen . Maj Charles Karamba yashimiye Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba kuba warateguye igikorwa cyo kwibuka , agaragaza ko ari ngomba kwibuka ku rwego rwa uyu muryango nkuko byemejwe na inama ya abakuru ba ibihugu biwugize mu mwaka wa 2014 .
Amb . Karamba yavuze ko hari abakoze Jenoside bakomeje kwidegembya mu bihugu bitandukanye birimo na ibyo ku mugabane wa Afurika ndetse no mu Karere u Rwanda ruherereyemo ariko ko bakwiye gufatwa bagashyikirizwa ubutabera .
Perezida wa Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba , Martin Ngoga , yavuze ko ubu ibikorwa bya ipfobya rya Jenoside bigeze ku rwego rwo gutanga ibisobanuro bya impamvu ngo yayiteye nyamara ari umugambi utegurwa igihe kirekire ukanashyirwa mu bikorwa , akaba ari na ko byagenze mu Rwanda .
Igikorwa cyakomeje hatangwa ibiteketerezo no gusubiza ibibazo byabajijwe na abitabiriye bashimangiye ko igikorwa cyo kwibuka kigomba kujya gitegurwa buri mwaka kandi bigakorwa hakiri kare , ndetse hakanatangwa ibikaniro bitandukanye mu rwego rwo kwibuka no gusubiza agaciro Abatutsi bishwe muri Jenoside .
Martin Ngoga yunamira abazize Jenoside ku kimenyetso cya urwibutso i Arusha .
Amb . Major Gen Charles Karamba Uhagarariye U Rwanda muri Tanzania .
Perezida wa Inteko ya Umuryango wa Afurika ya Iburasirazuba , Martin Ngoga .
Amb . Dan K . Kazungu Uhagarariye Kenya muri Tanzania .

Abanyarwanda batuye muri Queensland - Australia basabwe kutajenjekera ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside .
Kuri uyu wa Gatandatu tariki ya 12 Kanama 2021 , Abanyarwanda batuye muri Leta ya Queensland muri Australia bibutse ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , umuhango witabiriwe na abagera ku 150 .
Uyu muhango wabereye mu nzu ndangamuco iri mu Majyepfo ya Umujyi wa Brisbane muri Logan , wabimburiwe na urugendo rwo Kwibuka rwabereye muri Brisbane , aho hanacanywe na urumuri rwa icyizere hagafatwa na umunota wo kwibuka inzirakarengane zazize Jeonoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Mu butumwa yagejeje ku bitabiriye uyu muhango , Aimable Harusha , Umunyamabanga wa Ihuriro rya Abanyarwanda baba muri Queensland yibukije abari aho ko bagomba kwibuka kandi birinda icyabasubiza mu mahano yagwiririye u Rwanda .
Ati " " " " Tugomba kuzirikana inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , bikadufasha no kwibuka kandi twubaka ejo hazaza .
Twirinde icyadusubiza muri ayo mahano yabaye .
Twibuke ko kurwanya twivuye inyuma abagerageza gupfobya no guhakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ari inshingano zacu . " " " "
Muri uyu muhango kandi urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda batuye muri Queensland bakinnye umukino wahimbwe na Joyce Uwizeyimana utuye muri ako gace .
Umukino wigishaga ukanasobanurira abakiri bato bafite byinshi basanzwe bibaza kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Mu nshuti za u Rwanda zari muri uyu muhango ni Anne Hillsong wo mu Itorero rya Hillsong wavuze ko Abanyarwanda banyuze mu bihe bikomeye kandi bigoye ariko ko hari ibyiringiro ko ejo ari heza .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Singapore ari na we uhagarariye u Rwanda muri Australia , Uwihanganye Jean De Dieu , mu butumwa bwe yibukije Abanyarwanda kugira ibanze umukoro wo kwigisha no gusobanura amateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yagize ati " " " " Ni inshingano za buri wese gusobanura no kwigisha amateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi kugira ngo twime urwaho abarajwe ishinga no kuyihakana no kuyipfobya .
Guverinoma ya u Rwanda ishyize imbere Ndi Umunyarwanda kandi ibijeje ubufatanye nka uko yiyemeje kurwanya uwo ariwe wese ushaka gusubiza Abanyarwanda mu icuraburindi . " " " "
Ambasaderi Uwihanganye yavuze ko kwibuka bizahoraho mu rwego rwo gufasha abakiri bato kumenya ububi bwa Jenoside na ingaruka ziri mu kujenjekera uwo ari we wese ushaka gutuma yongera kubaho .
Umuhango wo kwibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 muri Queensland Australia watangijwe na urugendo rwo Kwibuka .
uyu muhango witabiriwe na Abanyarwanda na inshuti zabo bagera ku 150 .
Abana na urubyiruko batuye Queensland bakinnye umukino usobanura amateka ya Jenoside .
Abanyarwanda batuye Queensland muri Australia basabwe kugendera kure ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside .
Aimable Harusha yibukije Abanyarwanda ko bagomba kwibuka kandi birinda icyabasubiza mu mahano yagwiririye u Rwanda .
Beretswe na filime igaruka ku mateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yatanze impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Estonia ( Amafoto ) .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe Olivier yashyikirije Perezida wa Estonia , Kersti Kaljulaid impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira inyungu za u Rwanda muri iki gihugu .
Uyu muhango wabaye kuri uyu wa Kane , tariki 3 Kamena 2021 .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yakiriwe na Perezida Kersti ahagana Saa 12 : 15 za amanywa , ari zo 11 : 15 za igitondo mu Rwanda .
Amb . Nduhungirehe yahaye Perezida wa Estonia , Kersti Kaljulaid ubutumwa bwa indamukanyo ya mugenzi we Perezida Paul Kagame wa u Rwanda .
Ibiganiro bagiranye byibanze ku mubano wa ibihugu byombi , bishimira ibyagezweho kugeza ubu .
Barebeye hamwe uko umubano na ibikorwa byakomeza kurushaho kwiyongera mu ngeri zitandukanye zirimo gukomeza gukorana mu bijyanye na ikorana buhanga , ubucuruzi , ishoramari na ibindi .
Perezida Kersti Kaljulaid yongeye kwishimira uko umubano wa ibihugu byombi uhagaze , anashimangira ko igihugu cye cyitguye gukomeza kuwubungabunga ku buryo nta kizawuhungabanya .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yatanze impapuro zo guhagararira Estonia mu gihe asanzwe ahagarariye u Rwanda mu Buholandi .
Estonia na u Rwanda bihuriye kuri byinshi kandi bifite amahirwe akomeye mu gukorana mu bya iterambere ryo gushaka ibisubizo hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga na imikoreshereze yaryo muri gahunda za Leta kimwe no mu zindi gahunda .
Umubano wa ibihugu byombi umaze gushinga imizi ndetse bigaragarira mu guhura kwa Perezida Kagame na mugenzi we Kersti Kaljulaid .
Aba bakuru ba igihugu baheruka guhura ku wa 18 Gashyantare 2018 ubwo bari i Munich mu Budage mu Nama yiga ku Mutekano ku Isi " " " " Munich Security Conference . " " " "
Ibi biganiro byabaye nyuma ya uko tariki ya 16 Ugushyingo 2017 , Perezida Kersti yasuye u Rwanda aturutse muri Ethiopia .
Rwari uruzinduko rwe rwa mbere muri Afurika kuva yatorerwa kuyobora iki gihugu giherereye mu Majyaruguru ya u Burayi ku wa 10 Ukwakira 2016 .
Icyo gihe byatangajwe ko igihugu cye kiri gushaka uko cyakwagura imikorere hamwe na ibindi harebwa cyane ku hari amahirwe .
Estonia iherereye mu Majyaruguru ya u Burayi , ifite ubuso bwa kilometero kare 45 , 336 , ikaba ituwe na abaturage 1 , 294 , 455 nka uko ibarura ryo mu 2011 ribigaragaza .
Iza mu bya mbere mu bihugu byo mu Majyaruguru ya u Burayi mu mikoreshereze ya ikoranabuhanga muri gahunda zitandukanye .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yatanze impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Estonia .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Estonia , Nduhungirehe Olivier , yakiriwe mu cyubahiro gikwiye uhagarariye igihugu mu kindi .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe Olivier yashyikirije Perezida wa Estonia , Kersti Kaljulaid impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri iki gihugu .
Perezida wa Estonia , Kersti Kaljulaid na Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe Olivier bafashe ifoto ya urwibutso .
Nyuma yo gutanga impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Estonia , Nduhungirehe yagiranye ibiganiro byihariye na Perezida Kersti .
Minisitiri Mbabazi yasabye urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda mu Buholandi kurushaho kuba inkomezamihigo .
Minisitiri wa Urubyiruko na Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi , yasabye urubyiruko rwo mu Buholandi gukomeza kuba inkomezamihigo no gutanga umusanzu warwo mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika bifite icyerekezo .
Ibi yabivuze mu kiganiro yagiranye na urubyiruko rwa u Rwanda rubarizwa muri icyo gihugu kuri uyu wa Gatandatu tariki 29 Gicurasi 2021 .
Iki kiganiro cyabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga cyatanzwemo ibiganiro na abarimo Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda mu Buholandi , Olivier Nduhungirehe , Umuyobozi wa Umuryango ugamije kubohora Afurika ( Pan African Movement , PAM ) Ishami rya u Rwanda , Musoni Protais , ikiganiro cyayobowe na Solange Umwari akaba ari na Umuyobozi wungirije wa umuryango
wa Abanyarwanda mu Buholandi , hari kandi na Sado Mubyeyi watanze ikiganiro ku bumenyi afite nka urubyiruko rutuye mu Buholandi .
Insanganyamatsiko yacyo yagiraga iti " " " " Uruhare rwa urubyiruko rwa u Rwanda rutuye mu muhanga mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika twifuza .
Minisitiri Rosemary wari umushyitsi mukuru muri iki kiganiro , yibukije urubyiruko rwo mu Buholandi kuzirikana igihugu cyabo cyababyaye igihe bari mu muhanga , ababwira ko igiti cyidafite imizi cyuma bityo bakwiye guhora bazirikana u Rwanda .
Ati " " " " Murasabwa gukoresha ubwenge bwanyu , roho , impano na imbaraga mufite kugira ngo mwubake u Rwanda twifuza . " " " "
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yavuze ko imwe mu mpamvu Ambasade yateguye iki kiganiro ari ukugira ngo hizihizwe isabukuru ya imyaka 58 Umuryango wa Ubumwe bwa Afurika ubayeho ndetse hazirikanwe ubutwari abakurambere ba Afurika bagize mu kugerageza kuyiteza imbere .
Yongeyeho ati " " " " Muri iki kiganiro harimo ingingo eshatu , harimo ingingo ya urubyiruko , ingingo ijyanye no gukunda igihugu , hakabamo na ingingo ijyanye no guteza imbere Afurika . " " " "
" " " " Ibi bintu bitatu birajyanye kuko abaturage ba u Rwanda na abaturage ba Afurika abenshi ni urubyiruko .
Urwo rubyiruko rero ruba rugomba kugira uruhare mu kubaka ibihugu byabo . " " " "
Ambasaderi Nduhungirere yagarutse ku kiganiro cya Min .
Mbabazi wasabye urubyiruko rujya kwiga mu mahanga , guharanira ko ubwenge bagiye guhaha bwifashishwa mu kuzamura igihugu cyabo .
Min . Mbabazi yagize ati " " " " Ni ngombwa ko urubyiruko rujya mu mahanga kurahura ubwenge ariko rukibuka iwabo , Igiti kitakigira imizi kirazima . " " " "
Amb . Nduhungirehe yavuze ko banaganiriye ku mahirwe ahari ku Banyarwanda batuye mu mahanga na aho bashobora kubona ayo mahirwe .
Yavuze ko amahirwe ahari ari uko Guverinoma ya u Rwanda ishishikajwe na iterambere rigizwemo uruhare na bose , bitandukanye na Leta za mbere ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ati " " " " Hari Abanyarwanda bari mu mahanga batagifite uburyo bwa hafi bubahuza na igihugu nkuko byagagaragaye mubyo twavuyemo , twigobotoye byashize , ariko twebwe nka Guverinoma ya u Rwanda uyu munsi , twahisemo abanyarwanda bose babyifuza kuko ni uburenganzira bwabo kubaha agaciro kuko ari abanegihugu tugomba kubegera
ngo dufatanye kubaka igihugu . " " " "
" " " " Bitandukanye na uko byari bimeze kera mbere ya Jenoside aho umunyarwanda wo hanze ya igihugu atarebanaga na Leta , bumvaga ari umwanzi . " " " "
Biri no mu nshingano za Ambasade za u Rwanda kwegera abanyarwanda bose aho bari hose .
Umuyobozi wa Umuryango ugamije kubohora Afurika ( Pan African Movement , PAM ) Ishami rya u Rwanda , Musoni Protais , yagarutse ku ndangagaciro za u Rwanda zirimo ubumwe umurimo no gukunda igihugu , ahamagarira urubyiruko gukora rutizigamye , bagaharanira gukemura ibibazo bitakemuwe na abandi kandi bihora bituma Afurika idatera imbere nka indi migabane
, birimo intambara , inzara , ivangura na imiyoborere .
Ambasaderi Nduhungirehe yavuze ko ibiganiro nka ibi bifasha abana ba abanyarwanda bavukiye mu muhanga cyangwa na ababayeyo igihe kinini kwibona mu Rwanda ndetse bagahabwa agaciro nka abandi bakumva ko nabo bafite inshingano mu kubaka igihugu kavukire cyabo .
Bya umwihariko yatangaje ko iki ikiganiro na urubyiruko rwo mu Buholandi cyari kigamije kwerekana uruhare Abanyarwanda batuye mu Buholandi bashobora kugira mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika kandi ko biteze impinduka nyuma yacyo .
Ni ikiganiro cyari gifunguye kandi kiyobowe na urubyiruko ubwabo , cyatangiwemo ibitekerezo na urubyiruko rwari rwatumiwe rwaba abo mu Buholandi cyangwa abandi bo hirya no hino bifuje kugikurikira kuri Facebook , YouTube na Webex imbonankubone .
Urubyiruko rwahawe ibisubizo bya ibibazo bibazaga mu buryo burambuye .
Amb Nduhungirehe yavuze ko ikiganiro bagiranye na urubyiruko rwo mu Buholandi kigamije kwerekana uruhare rwabo mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika .
Minisitiri Rosemary Mbabazi yasabye urubyiruko rwo mu mahanga kuba inkomezabigwi bubakira ku byagezweho mu kubaka u Rwanda rwa ejo hazaza .
Musoni Protais yibukije abateraniye muri icyo kiganiro indangagaciro za u Rwanda , abasaba gukosora ibibazo bikigaragara muri Afurika bituma idatera imbere nka indi migabane .
Sado Mubyeyi ni umwe mu baganirije urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda baba mu Buholandi .
Umwari Solange niwe wayoboye ibiganiro .
Abatanze ikiganiro basabye urubyiruko kugira uruhare mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika .
Urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda mu Buholandi rugiye kumarwa amatsiko mu kubaka u Rwanda na Afurika rwifuza .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda mu Buholandi ku bufatanye na Umuryango wa Abanyarwanda muri icyo gihugu , bateguye ikiganiro cyo kwigisha urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda ruba muri icyo gihugu uko rwatanga umusanzu warwo mu kubaka Igihugu na Afurika rwifuza .
Ni ikiganiro kizaba ku wa 29 Gicurasi 2021 mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga , cyitabirwe na Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda mu Buholandi , Olivier Nduhungirehe , Minisitiri wa Urubyiruko na Umuco , Mbabazi Rosemary , Umuyobozi wa Pan African Movement Ishami rya u Rwanda , Musoni Protais , na umutumirwa Mubyeyi Sado .
Insanganyamatsiko yacyo iragira iti " " " " Uruhare rwacu nka Urubyiruko mu kubaka u Rwanda ndetse na Afurika twifuza . " " " "
Mu kiganiro IGIHE yagiranye na umuyobozi wungirije wa Diaspora Nyarwanda mu Buholandi ari nawe uzayobora icyo kiganiro , Umwari Solange yavuze ko kizibanda ku gusobanura uko urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda batuye muri icyo gihugu bashobora kwihutisha gahunda ya ubumwe , gukunda Igihugu na Afurika muri rusange .
Hazaganirirwamo uburyo bwo gutanga umusanzu ku iterambere rya imibereho myiza na ubukungu mu Gihugu cyabo no ku gushyira hamwe ku mugabane wabo , ndetse bakaba indorerwamo ya isura nziza ya u Rwanda mu Buholandi .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Abo batumirwa bazadusobanurira icyo guhirimbanira iterambere rya Afurika bivuze , uruhare rwa urubyiruko ni uruhe , ni iki twakwigezaho , ni iki twageza ku gihugu , ?
Ni iki dushobora gushishikariza abantu batazi Igihugu cyacu ? . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko urubyiruko ruzerekwa uko rushobora gusobanurira abanyamahanga u Rwanda , bakaba baza kuhasura bafite amakuru ahagije ya uko bakwakirwa , ibiciro bya amahoteli na ibindi .
Uretse kuratira abanyamahanga u Rwanda , hari na Abanyarwanda baba mu Buholandi batazi uko babasha kugera mu Rwanda na inzira byanyuramo babaye babyifuza , ahanini bitewe na uko ari ho bavukiye cyangwa akaba ari ho baba kuva bahungirayo ubwo habaga Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Muri icyo kiganiro bazasobanurirwa byose kuko abo bayobozi bazaba bacyitabiriye bazasubiza ibibazo byabo .
Icyo kiganiro kandi kizaba mu gihe hazaba hizihizwa imyaka 58 ishize hashinzwe Umuryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe .
Biteganyijwe ko ikiganiro kizatangira saa Cyenda kirangire saa Kumi na imwe za igicamunsi ku masaha ya i Kigali .
Kizakorwa hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga rya WebEx , gicishwe kuri You Tube na Facebook live .
