Kwibuka27 : IBUKA yasabye u Buholandi ubufasha mu kubaka urwibutso rwa Jenoside .
Umuryango uharanira inyungu za abarokotse Jenoside , Ibuka mu Buholandi , wasabye iki gihugu ubufasha mu kubaka urwibutso rwazajya rwifashishwa mu bikorwa byo kwibuka rukaba na ikimenyetso gitanga ubutumwa ku mateka ashaririye u Rwanda rwanyuzemo mu 1994 .
Ku wa 7 Mata ubwo u Rwanda na inshuti zarwo batangiraga iminsi ijana yo kuzirikana inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , Ambasade ya u Rwanda mu Buholandi nayo yateguye umuhango wo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 .
Uyu muhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Abawukurikiye bibukijwe kwibuka biyubaka kandi barwanya ingengabitekerezo na abapfobya Jenoside .
Nyuma yo gufata umunota wo kuzirikana abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , hatanzwe ibiganiro bitandukanye byagarukaga ku kwibuka no kurwanya Jenoside .
Umuyobozi wa Ibuka mu Buholandi , Safari Christine , yashimiye abacitse ku icumu uburyo babashije kurenga amateka bakongera kugira icyezere cya ubuzima kandi bakabaho .
Ati " " " " Usanga abarokotse bariyubatse ndetse babayeho , iki ni igikorwa cya indashyikirwa cyagezweho . " " " "
Safari yakomeje asaba Leta ya u Buholandi kubafasha kubaka urwibutso rwa Jenoside bakajya babasha kurukoresha mu gihe cyo kwibuka .
Ati " " " " Turasaba leta ya u Buholandi ko yazadufasha kubaka urwibutso twajya tujya kwibukiramo , ndetse turasaba buri wese kudufasha kurwanya abapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi . " " " "
Mu batanze ibiganiro harimo Perezida wa Urwego rwasigariyeho Inkiko Mpuzamahanga Mpanabyaha , IRMCT , Agius Carmel , wibukije Abanyarwanda bose ko badakwiye gucibwa intege na abapfobya Jenoside .
Ati " " " " Abantu bose ku Isi bari kwibuka inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , nubwo hari abapfobya ndetse bakanahakana jenoside ubona ko bikibangamiye ubumwe na ubwiyunge ariko ntibikuraho ukuri kwabaye kuri jenoside . " " " "
Ku ruhande rwa Umunyamabanga Mukuru muri Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga mu Buholandi , Paul Huijts , yagarutse ku kiganiro cyigisha abana amateka ya ibyabaye mu 1994 ndetse avuga ko igihugu cye kitazahishira abakoze jenoside .
Ati " " " " Mu myaka 25 ishize u Buholandi bwagerageje gufasha u Rwanda mu bijyanye na ubutabera , twagerageje guhugura urubyiruko kuri byo kuko ahazaza hari mu biganza byarwo .
Navuga ko u Buholandi butazigera buha umutekano abasize bakoze Jenoside . " " " "
Mu butumwa yageneye abari bitabiriye uyu muhango , Ambasaderi Olivier Nduhungurihe , yasabye Abanyarwanda na abatuye Isi muri rusange kwirinda amacakubiri na ikindi cyose cyaganisha kuri jenoside .
Ati " " " " Ndasaba buri wese kwibuka yiyubaka , turwanya ivanguraruhu , ivangurakarere , ivanguramoko , no kwirinda ibyaha byose bijyanye na ivangura bishobora kugeza abantu kuri jenoside . " " " "
Ibihe byo kwibuka abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 byahuriranye na icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyatumye uburyo byakorwagamo buhinduka .
Uwari uhagarariye Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga ya u Buholandi , Paul Huijts yavuze ko igihugu cye kitazigera gihishira abasize bakoze Jenoside mu Rwanda .
AU yifatanyije na u Rwanda kunamira abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Umuyobozi wa Komisiyo ya Umuryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe , Moussa Faki Mahamat hamwe na Intumwa ihoraho ya u Rwanda muri AU akaba na Ambasaderi warwo muri Ethiopia , Hope Tumukunde Gasatura , bifatanyije na Abanyarwanda kunamira inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ; bibutsa ko ayo mateka adakwiye gusubira ukundi kandi
hakwiye kwimakazwa umuco wo guhana abayagizemo uruhare .
Babitangaje kuri uyu wa 7 Mata 2021 , mu muhango wo gutangiza iminsi 100 yo kwibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ku nshuro ya 27 , wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Mu butumwa yatanze , Faki Mahamat yavuze ko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ari yo nkuru ya mbere ibabaje yabereye ku Mugabane wa Afurika , nyuma ya ubucuruzi bwa abacakara na ubukoloni .
Ati " " " " Abarenga miliyoni bishwe mu buryo bwa indengakamere , hakoreshejwe imihoro , amashoka na ubuhiri .
Mu minsi irenga 100 , abagabo , abagore , abana , abakuze yewe na impinja bakorewe ibiteye ubwoba no kubivuga , bazira kuba barisanze ari Abatutsi gusa . " " " "
Yavuze ko hazamara igihe kirekire hibazwa impamvu yatumye " " " " ibyo bikorwa bya ubugome bugoye kubwiyumvisha " " " " biba ku bantu bari bamaze ibinyejana basangiye ururimi , iyobokamana ndetse baturanye .
Ambasaderi Hope Tumukunde yibukije abitabiriye uwo muhango ko Jenoside itatewe na ihanurwa rya indege ya Habyarimana Juvénal nka uko abenshi mu bayihakana na abayipfobya bakunze kubikwirakwiza ahubwo " " " " yamaze igihe kirekire itegurwa na guverinoma . " " " "
Yagize ati " " " " Ntabwo yatangijwe na ihanurwa rya indege cyangwa urwo rupfu , ahubwo byatangiranye na ingengabitekerezo ya urwango , gucamo abantu ibice , ivangura , guheza bamwe muri gahunda runaka , kugabanya umubare wa abitabira ibikorwa ibi na ibi no kwitandukanya na bo . " " " "
" " " " [ Hari ] ingengabitekerezo ya ubwoko yo gusobanura Abatutsi no kubatandukanya na abatari bo , imvugo zihembera urwango , kubambura ubumuntu , kuvuga ko bagomba kwicwa na ibindi . " " " "
Tumukunde yavuze ko ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside yatangiye gukwirakwizwa mu Banyarwanda kuva mu 1957 humvikanishwa ko Abatutsi nta burenganzira bafite bwo kubaho .
Nyuma ya iyo myaka Guverinoma zagiye zijyaho zakomeje gushyigikira urwo rwango rwa Abatutsi , bimwa uburenganzira bwo kwiga , bagenda bicwa abandi barahunga bata Urwababyaye kugeza mu 1994 ubwo " " " " bishwe hagamijwe kubamaraho . " " " "
Ni cyo gihe ngo Afurika Yunze Ubumwe ihangane na ibikorwa byaganisha kuri Jenoside
Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 yabaye amahanga arebera , ibihugu byitwa ko ari ibihangange na imiryango mpuzamahanga ntibyagira icyo bikora ngo biyihagarike ; kugeza ubwo FPR Inkotanyi yabohoje igihugu ku wa 4 Nyakanga uwo mwaka ikarokora abari basigaye .
Ambasaderi Tumukunde yavuze ko igihe kigeze ngo Afurika Yunze Ubumwe ikumire ibyaha bya urwango na Jenoside byaba cyangwa bigasubira ahari ho hose kuri uyu mugabane mbere ya uko biba .
Yakomeje ati " " " " AU ikwiye kugira uruhare mu kurwanya ivangura , gushyirwa mu moko , gutandukanya abantu no kubasumbanya hashingiwe ku moko , kuko ari byo bifumbirira ibyaha bya urwango na ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside bigakomeza gukura . " " " "
Yavuze ko kwibuka kwa AU muri uyu mwaka ari amahirwe yo kurushaho kongera imbaraga mu guhangana na ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside haba mu nzego za igihugu , akarere no ku mugabane ; hakanabaho guhuriza hamwe imbaraga mu kurwanya abayihakana himakazwa ubutabera no kurwanya umuco wo kudahana .
Ibyo bikubiyemo no kugeza imbere ya ubutabera abagize uruhare muri Jenoside , abayipfobya na abayihakana bihishahisha hirya no hino mu bihugu bya Afurika , cyane ko abenshi banashyiriweho impapuro zo gutabwa muri yombi .
Faki Mahamat yatangaje ko ibyabaye ku Rwanda mu myaka 27 ishize byagatumye Afurika irushaho kwirinda ko byazasubira ukundi , hirindwa ibya amoko .
Ku rundi ruhande , u Rwanda rushimirwa intambwe rwateye rwiyubaka nyuma ya amahano yarubayemo , ubu rukaba ari intangarugero mu nzego zitandukanye nk " " " " umutekano , guteza imbere abagore , kuzamura ubukungu na ibindi .
Ni ibintu byabagariwe no kwimakaza gahunda ya ubumwe na ubwiyunge yomoye ibikomere bya abarokotse ndetse bakababarira ababiciye , bagahuriza ku mugambi wo guteza imbere igihugu cyabo .
Umuryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe wifatanya na u Rwanda kunamira inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi kuva mu 2010 .
# Kwibuka27 : Abanyarwanda baba muri Sénégal bamaganye abagiha rugari abasize bakoze Jenoside .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri Sénégal inakurikirana inyungu za u Rwanda mu bihugu bya Mali , Gambia , Cap Vert na Guinea - Bissau ifatanyije na Abanyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda batuye muri iki gihugu bibutse ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda mu 1994 .
Iyo gahunda yabereye kuri " " " " Place du Souvenir Africain " " " " ahari ikimenyetso cyo kwibuka inzirakarengane za Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Umuhango watumiwemo abahagarariye abandi mu rwego rwo kubahiriza ingamba zo kwirinda icyorezo cya Coronavirus , waranzwe no gucana urumuri rwa icyizere , gushyira indabo ahari ikimenyetso cyo kwibuka inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ubuhamya na ubutumwa bwa bamwe mu bayobozi bitabiriye iyo gahunda .
Perezida wa Umuryango wa Abanyarwanda baba muri Sénégal , Patrick Karamaga , watanze na ubuhamya nka uwacitse ku icumu rya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , yagarutse ku mateka mabi yo gukwirakwiza urwango mu Banyarwanda yahereye mu mashuri ya abana bato .
Yashimye bya umwihariko ingabo zari iza FPR Inkotanyi zahagaritse Jenoside yakorerwaga Abatutsi , zikabohora igihugu , anasaba ko Abanyarwanda bakomeza gutahiriza umugozi umwe mu guteza imbere igihugu , kandi bagakomera ku bumwe bwabo . .
Ambasaderi wa Gabon muri Sénégal , Michel Regis Onanga Ndiaye , wavuze mu izina rya Abahagarariye Ibihugu na Imiryango Mpuzamahanga muri Sénégal , yagarutse ku mwanzuro wa Inteko Rusange ya Umuryango wa Abibumbye mu 2018 yemeje ko itariki ya 7 Mata ya buri mwaka ari Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wo kuzirikana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda mu 1994 .
Yamaganye abagize uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bakihishahisha hirya no hino bakurikiranwa na ibihugu bihishemo kimwe na abahakana na abapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yagaragaje ko nyuma ya imyaka 27 Jenoside ihagaritswe , Abanyafurika bose batewe ishema na ibyiza u Rwanda rwagezeho muri icyo gihe , muri gahunda yo kubaka ubumwe bwa Abanyarwanda na gahunda za iterambere muri rusange .
Ndiaye yagarutse ku ijambo Perezida Paul Kagame yavuze mu gihe hibukwagwa ku nshuro ya 25 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi aho yagize ati " " " " Mu 1994 nta cyizere cyariho , hari umwijima gusa ariko uyu munsi hari urumuri , twapfutse ibikomere , ibyo byatumye turushaho kuba umwe kandi ku buryo buhoraho .
U Rwanda rwabaye umuryango umwe . " " " "
Mu bandi batanze ubuhamya harimo Abanya - Sénégal barimo Mabousso Thiam , washakanye na Umunyarwandakazi wagaragaje uko na we itotezwa rya Abatutsi na Jenoside yabakorewe byamugizeho ingaruka zikomeye kuko Jenoside yahitanye benshi mu bo mu muryango yashatsemo na inshuti nyinshi .
Yagaragaje ko ubu u Rwanda ari igihugu cyubashywe , cyihesheje agaciro kandi cyagaruriye Abanyarwanda icyizere cyo kubaho .
Undi watanze ubuhamya ni Eugénie Rokhaya Aw Na diaye , wabaye mu Rwanda akaba yagarutse ku kababaro na agahinda abagore batewe na Jenoside yabagize abapfakazi ndetse ikanahitana abana babo .
Yagarutse ku butwari bwabo ndetse na uruhare rwabo mu kubaka umuryango Nyarwanda nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Uwari uhagarariye Guverinoma ya Sénégal , Habib Leon Ndiaye , usanzwe ari Umunyamabanga Mukuru muri Minisiteri ya Umuco na Itangazamakuru yagaragaje ko Guverinoma ya Sénégal yifatanyije na Abanyarwanda muri iki gihe bibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yashimye uko Abanyarwanda bishatsemo ibisubizo nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi kandi agaragaza ko Sénégal izakomeza gushimangira umubano mwiza uri hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Jean Pierre Karabaranga , yashimye cyane umubano uri hagati ya ibihugu byombi , anashima ko icyo gihugu cyanahaye ahari ikimenyetso cyo kwibuka abishwe muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yasabye abantu bose gukomeza kwamagana abakirangwa na imvugo na ibikorwa byo guhakana no gupfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi kimwe na abakwirakwiza ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside barimo bamwe mu Banyarwanda basize bahekuye u Rwanda na bamwe mu banyamahanga babibafashamo .
# Kwibuka27 : Abanyarwanda bo mu Buyapani bibutse Jenoside , hashimwa iterambere rimaze kugerwaho .
Mu gihe u Rwanda rwinjiye mu minsi 100 yo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , Abanyarwarwa baba mu Buyapani binyuze muri Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu ku bufatanye na inshuti zabo batangije ibikorwa byo kwibuka .
Uyu muhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga , witabiriwe na abasaga 200 barimo abahagarariye ibihugu byabo mu Buyapani , abahagarariye Guverinoma ya u Buyapani , abarimu ba za Kaminuza na abashakashatsi , abanyamakuru , abikorera , abayobozi ba ibigo bya ubucuruzi , Abanyarwanda na inshuti zabo .
Guverinoma ya u Buyapani yari ihagarariwe na Minisitiri wungirije ushinzwe Ububanyi na Amahanga akaba na Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , Konosuke Kokuba , wagarutse ku bufatanye buri hagati ya u Rwanda na u Buyapani muri iki gihe Isi yibuka abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yongeye kugaragaza urukundo afitiye Abanyarwanda , abihanganisha mu Kinyarwanda aho yagize ati " " " " turi kumwe . " " " "
Konosuke yihanganishije Abanyarwanda ku nzikaregane zatakaje ubuzima muri Jenoside , anashima imbaraga za Perezida Paul Kagame na imiyoborere ihamye yagaragaje .
Uyu muyobozi yagarutse ku rugendo rwa iterambere u Rwanda rwagezeho mu myaka 27 ishize , aho yagaragaje ubushake bwa Perezida wa u Rwanda mu kuruteza imbere , no kurugeza ku mwanya wa kabiri mu bihugu bibungabunga ibidukikije Munsi ya Ubutayu bwa Sahara no mu iterambere mu ikoranabuhanga .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda mu Buyapani , Erneste Rwamucyo , yavuze ko kwibuka bigamije gufasha Abanyarwanda kwivana mu bibazo byasizwe na Jenoside , baharanira kwiteza imbere bubaka igihugu cyabo .
Yashimangiye umuco wo guhaguruka no kurwanya Jenoside na ingengabitekerezo yayo , ivangura rya amoko na andi macakubiri kugira ngo amahano nka ayagwiririye u Rwanda atazongera kuba ukundi .
Ambasaderi Rwamucyo yasobanuye intera ya iterambere u Rwanda rumaze kugeraho nyuma ya ihagarikwa rya Jenoside na uruhare ntangarugero u Rwanda rwagezeho rwiyubaka .
Abitabiriye uyu muhango beretswe amashusho ya ukuntu Jenoside yateguwe na uko yakozwe , ububabare na ubutwari bwa abarokotse na ukuntu u Rwanda rukomeje kwikura muri ayo magorwa no kwiteza imbere .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda yijeje ko hazakomeza ibindi bikorwa bigamije kwifatanya na Abanyarwanda mu minsi 100 yo kwibuka harimo kwigisha Abayapani amateka ya u Rwanda na uko Jenoside yakozwe , inabashishikariza kumenya uko u Rwanda rukomeje kwiyubaka no kwiteza imbere nyuma ya ayo marorerwa .
Minisitiri wungirije ushinzwe Ububanyi na Amahanga mu Buyapani , Kokuba Konosuke yashimye aho u Rwanda rugeze rwiyubaka .
Kwibuka27 : Abanyarwanda baba mu Bushinwa bahawe umukoro ngo Jenoside itazongera .
Abanyarwanda batuye mu Bushinwa na abadipolomate bahagarariye imiryango mpuzamahanga itandukanye , bibutse ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , kuri uyu wa Gatatu tariki 7 Mata 2021 .
Iki gikorwa cyabereye ku Cyicaro cya Ambasade ya u Rwanda i Beijing .
Cyaranzwe no gucana urumuri rwa icyizere nka ikimenyetso cya uko Abanyarwanda bavuye mu mwijima wa icuraburindi bakajya mu mucyo utanga icyizere .
Abacyitabiriye banafashe umunota wo kwibuka bazirikana inzirakarengane zahitanwe na Jenoside .
Abari bitabiriye uwo muhango barebye filime mbarankuru ivuga ku byo u Rwanda rwanyuzemo mu gihe cya Jenoside ndetse na filime mbarankuru kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abayahudi .
Umujyanama muri Ambasade ya u Rwanda mu Bushinwa , Virgile Rwanyagatare , yavuze ko kwibuka ari ugusubiza agaciro abakambuwe ndetse ko bifasha kubyutsa umutima wa igihugu watakaye ubwo Abanyarwanda bicaga bagenzi babo .
Ati " " " " Kwibuka Jenoside ni kimwe mu bikorwa bikomeye byo kugarura roho ya igihugu cyacu .
Ni kimwe mu byafashije u Rwanda guhangana na abashakaga kurusubiza inyuma , ahubwo rutangira urugendo rushya rwo kwiyubaka mu mahoro na umutekano , ubuyobozi bwiza ndetse no mu iterambere rya ubukungu . " " " "
Rwanyagatare yagarutse ku kuntu amahanga yatereranye u Rwanda mu gihe Abatutsi barimo bicwa , aho Umuryango wa Abibumbye wavanye mu Rwanda ingabo zawo zari zishinzwe kubungabunga amahoro , aho kuzisaba guhagarika ubwicanyi .
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Nubwo ariko byagenze gutyo , ubu amahanga arajwe inshinga no kurwanya Jenoside nubwo hakiri byinshi byo gukora birimo no kurwanya abahakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 [ . . . ] abayihakana ni abakoze Jenoside na ababashyigikiye , abashakashatsi na abanyamakuru bafite aho bahuriye bya hafi na abakoze
amahano mu Rwanda . " " " "
Habintwari Da Artagnan warokotse jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , yatanze ubuhamya bwa ibyo yabayemo , agaruka ku kuntu jenoside yamutwaye abo mu muryango we harimo na papa we ndetse na abana batanu bavukanaga .
Yatanze inama agira ati " " " " Ni ibya ingenzi nka ikiremwamuntu muri rusange kumenya ko Isi dutuyemo uyu munsi ari iyacu , ariko ejo izaba itakiri iyacu gusa tukibuka ko izaba ari iya abana bacu .
Ndatekereza ko iki ari igihe cyo gutekereza ku murage dushaka guha abana bacu . " " " "
Uhagarariye Umuryango wa Abibumbye mu Bushinwa , Siddharth Chatterjee , na we wari witabiriye uyu muhango yunamiye abishwe muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ati " " " " Mu izina rya Loni mu Bushinwa , nunamiye abagabo , abagore na abana bishwe muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda ndetse nifatanyije na abayirokotse babuze ababo . " " " "
Abandi bayobozi bitabiriye uwo muhango harimo uhagarariye Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga ndetse na uwari uhagarariye Umuryango wa Abibumbye .
Koreya ya Epfo : Abanyarwanda basabwe kongera imbaraga mu guhashya udutsiko twa abahakana Jenoside .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Koreya ya Epfo na inshuti za u Rwanda bifatanyije kuri uyu wa Gatatu , tariki 7 Mata 2021 , kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , basabwa imbaraga mu guhashya udutsiko twa abagishaka guhakana no gupfobya iyo Jenoside .
Iki gikorwa cyakozwe hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga kubera ibihe Isi irimo byo kwirinda icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Icyo gikorwa cyayobowe na Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu , Yasmin Amri Sued , cyahurije hamwe abantu basaga ijana na makumyabiri , barimo abayobozi batandukanye ndetse na Abanyarwanda batuye mu bihugu bya Koreya ya Epfo na Cambodia .
Abandi bitabiriye icyo gikorwa harimo Kim Gunn , Minisitiri wungirije ushinzwe ibya Politiki muri Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga ya Koreya ya Epfo , abahagarariye ibihugu byabo na imiryango mpuzamahanga muri icyo gihugu ndetse na Ambasaderi Colin Keating watanze ikiganiro nka inararibonye .
Ambasaderi Keating yahoze ahagarariye igihugu cye cya Nouvelle Zelande mu Muryango wa Abibumbye ndetse no mu Kanama gashinzwe Amahoro na Umutekano ku Isi , mu gihe Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yakorwaga mu Rwanda mu 1994 .
Igikorwa cyo kwibuka cyabimburiwe no gucana urumuri rwa icyizere , aho Ambasaderi Carlos Victor Boungou , uhagarariye Gabon muri Koreya ya Epfo , akaba ari na we Ambasaderi umaze igihe kinini muri icyo gihugu , yasabye abitabiriye uwo muhango bose gucana ururimo rwa icyizere bari bateguye buri umwe aho yaherereye hose .
Minisitiri Kim Gunn yavuze ko mu izina rya Guverinoma ya Koreya , igihugu cye cyifatanyije na Abanyarwanda muri ibi bihe byo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda .
Yongeraho ko igihe nka iki cyo kwibuka gihabwa uburemere bukomeye mu gihugu cye kigeze gusenyuka , kikanabura abacyo babarirwa muri za miliyoni , ubu kikaba cyarongeye kwiyubaka .
Kim Gunn yavuze ko igihe nka iki ari icyo gushimangira ingamba zo guharanira ko Jenoside atakongera kubaho aho ariho hose ku Isi .
Yatanze urugero ko bikorwa bya ivanguraruhu bikorerwa abirabura ndetse na Abanya - Aziya , aboneraho gusaba abitabiriye uwo muhango kwamagana bivuye inyuma ibyo bikorwa bya ivangura kugira ngo ibyabaye mu Rwanda mu gihe cya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bitazongera kubaho ukundi .
Ambasaderi Colin Keating yasobanuye uburyo Umuryango wa Abibumbye wateshutse ku nshingano zawo zo gutabara u Rwanda na Abatutsi bari barimo guhigwa no kwicwa mu gihugu .
Yavuze ko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 yateguwe igashyirwa mu bikorwa na leta yariho icyo gihe .
Yatanze umukoro ku bantu bose kwifatanya na Abanyarwanda mu rugamba rwo kurwanya abahakana Jenoside yo mu 1994 yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda ndetse no guhora baharanira ko ibyabaye mu Rwanda bitazongera kubaho .
Ambasaderi Colin Keating yavuze ko bishimishije kubona u Rwanda kuri ubu rufite umutekano usesuye , ubu rutera imbere , kandi rugira uruhare mu kugarura amahoro na ahandi ku Isi .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Koreya ya Epfo , Yasmin Amri Sued , yashimiye abitabiriye uyu muhango wo kwifatanya na Abanyarwanda kwibuka Jenoside .
Yavuze ku mateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda kuva mu itegura ryayo kugeza mu ishyirwa mu bikorwa , bigizwemo uruhare na ubuyobozi bubi bwari buriho .
Ambasaderi Amri Sued yavuze ko Jenoside yo mu 1994 yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda yaje guhagarikwa na Abanyarwanda batabaye igihugu , bagizwe na ingabo zahoze ari iza RPA zari ziyobowe na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Yavuze ko guhera ubwo u Rwanda ruharanira ubumwe mu gihugu himakazwa indangagaciro za ubunyarwanda , ubwiyunge , ubutabera , gukorera hamwe , kwishakamo ibisubizo no guharanira iterambere rirambye .
Ambasaderi Amri Sued yasabye abahagarariye ibihugu byabo na imiryango mpuzamahanga kurwanya bivuye inyuma udutsiko tugenda twaguka hirya no hino twa abapfobya na abahakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda .
Yavuze ko utwo dutsiko tugizwe na abaharanira guhindura amateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , baharanira kugira abere abayikoze no gusiga icyasha abayikorewe , abarokotse ndetse na abayihagaritse .
Yongeraho ko bamwe muri bo bashigikiwe na utundi dutsiko twa bamwe mu banyamahanga babatiza umurindi muri ibyo bikorwa bya ihakana na ipfobya bya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yasabye abitabiriye uwo muhango kurwanya bivuye inyuma iyo ngengabitekerezo mbi ya Jenoside na amacakubiri .
Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 yahitanye Abatutsi basaga miliyoni mu minsi ijana .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Singapore bibutse ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri Singapore , Australie , Nouvelle - Zélande , na Indonésie yateguye umuhango wo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , umuhango wabaye kuri uyu wa 7 Mata 2021 , mu gutangiza iminsi 100 yo kwibuka abarenga miliyoni bavukijwe ubuzima bazira uko bavutse .
Ni umuhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga hirindwa icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , witabirwa na abayobozi ba Ambasade , Abanyarwanda baba muri ibyo bihugu na inshuri za u Rwanda .
Hafashwe umunota wo guha icyubahiro inzirakarekane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , hacanwa urumuri rwa icyizere nka ikimenyetso cya ahazaza heza ; hanerekanwa filime mbarankuru ngufi igaragaza uko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yabaye yarateguwe .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Singapore Uwihanganye Jean de Dieu , yihanganishije abarokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , avuga ko imbaraga na umurava byabo na inzira ya ubwiyunge no kubabarirana " " " " byomoye ibikomere binagira uruhare mu rugendo rwo kongera kubaka u Rwanda . " " " "
Yibukije ko mu bihe byo kwibuka ari bwo abakwirakwiza amakuru ya ibinyoma , abapfobya na abahakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi biyongera , ahamagarira abitabiriye uwo muhango gushikama bagahangana nabo .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Ibihe byo kwibuka ni amahirwe yo kwibutsa Isi ko gushyira hamwe kwa ibihugu byose ari yo nzira yonyine izageza imbere ya ubutabera abakekwaho uruhare muri Jenoside [ yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ] ; bacyihishahisha hirya no hino mu bihugu bitandukanye .
[ Ibyo ] bizatuma abagizweho ingaruka nayo babona ubutabera , ndetse birinde kuba hari ahandi hazaba Jenoside mu Isi . " " " "
Ni ku nshuro ya Kabiri u Rwanda rwinjira mu minsi 100 yo kwibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 Isi igihanganye na icyorezo cya Coronavirus aho ibikorwa byinshi byo kwibuka bizakorwa hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Mu Rwanda , uwo muhango watangirijwe ku Rwibutso rwa Jenoside rwa Kigali ruri ku Gisozi , aho Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yacanye urumuri rwa icyizere .
Witabiriwe na abantu bake , abandi Banyarwanda bari mu Gihugu no hanze bawukurikiranira mu ngo zabo biciye ku itangazamakuru no ku ikoranabuhanga ritandukanye .
Amb . Mutsindashyaka yatanze kopi za impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda i Brazzaville .
Ambasaderi Mutsindashyaka Théoneste yashyikirije Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga wa Congo - Brazzaville , Jean - Claude Gakosso , kopi za impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu .
Uyu muhango wabaye ku wa Gatatu wa iki cyumweru , tariki ya 31 Werurwe 2021 .
Wabaye hubahirizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda Coronavirus arimo kwambara neza agapfukamunwa no guhana intera .
Nyuma yo gutanga impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Repubulika ya Congo , Ambasaderi Mutsindashyaka Théoneste yagiranye ibiganiro byihariye na Minisitiri Jean - Claude Gakosso .
Aba bombi baganiriye ku mubano mwiza umaze igihe kirekire hagati ya ibihugu byombi ndetse na izindi ngeri zitandukanye zihuriweho na ibihugu byombi .
Mutsindashyaka azwi cyane muri politiki ya u Rwanda kuko yabaye Umuyobozi wa Umujyi wa Kigali , Guverineri wa Intara ya Iburasirazuba na Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri ya Uburezi .
Kuva mu 2013 yari Umunyamabanga Nshingwabikorwa wa Umuryango ushinzwe kurwanya ikwirakwiza rya Intwaro nto na iziciriritse mu Karere ka Ibiyaga Bigari , mu Ihembe rya Afurika no mu bihugu bihana imbibi RECSA ( Regional Centre on Small Arms ) .
Mutsindashyaka yemerejwe nka Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Congo mu Nama ya Abaminisitiri yateranye ku wa 14 Kanama 2020 .
Yasimbuye Amb Dr Habyalimana Jean Baptiste .
U Rwanda na Congo bifitanye umubano wihariye mu bya dipolomasi ndetse kuva muri Kanama 2016 ruhafite ambasade .
Mu 2011 , u Rwanda na Congo byasinyanye amasezerano ya ubufatanye na imikoranire mu bwikorezi bwa indege , ubucuruzi , ubukerarugendo , imiturire , imicungire ya impunzi , ingufu , umutekano , ubutabera , kurengera ibidukikije , uburobyi , ikoranabuhanga , itumanaho na ibindi .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri Congo yanahawe ubushobozi bwo guhagararira inyungu za u Rwanda mu bihugu bitandatu bihuriye mu Muryango wa Ubukungu bwa Afurika yo Hagati CEEAC , aribyo Cameroun , Gabon , Guinée Equatoriale , Tchad , Repubulika ya Centrafrique na CEEAC ubwayo .
Kuva mu Ukwakira 2018 , Repubulika ya Congo yorohereje Abanyarwanda bajyayo , guhabwa viza bageze ku mipaka no ku bibuga bya indege .
U Rwanda na Congo bifitanye umubano mwiza , buri cyose gifite ugihagarariye mu kindi .
Ubuhahirane hagati yabyo kandi bunoroshywa na ingendo za RwandAir .
Ambasaderi Mutsindashyaka Théoneste na Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga wa Congo - Brazzaville , Jean - Claude Gakosso , banagiranye ibiganiro byihariye .
Ibuka France igiye gusuzuma raporo nshya ku ruhare rwa u Bufaransa muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Umuryango uharanira inyungu za abarokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , Ishami rikorerera mu Bufaransa , watangaje ko wakiriye ibyavuye mu bushakashatsi bushya ku ruhare rwa icyo gihugu mu mateka mabi ya u Rwanda ndetse ko uzagira icyo ubivugaho nyuma yo kubisuzuma .
Ku wa 26 Werurwe 2021 nibwo hasohowe iyo raporo yakozwe na abashakashatsi bayobowe na Prof Vincent Duclert bashyizweho na Perezida wa u Bufaransa , Emmanuel Macron .
Mu itangazo rigenewe abanyamakuru , Ibuka France yavuze ko ishimira ibyakozwe na abashakashatsi , abanyamateka na abanyamakuru batandukanye mu kugaragaza amakuru na ubumenyi bijyanye na Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi kuva mu 27 ishize .
Yavuze ko ubushakashatsi ku mateka ari ikintu kidapfa gushyirwaho akadomo na umwanzuro wa politiki , bityo ko " " " " yifatanyije na abazakomeza kwandika no gukuraho urujijo kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi . " " " "
Ibuka France yakomeje iti " " " " Iki ni ikintu gikomeye cyane kizadufasha kugera ku zindi ntego zacu zirimo ubutabera no gushyigikira abarokotse Jenoside . " " " "
Uwo muryango watangaje ko nyuma ya uko imyanzuro ya iyo raporo ishyizwe ahagaragara , ugiye kuyisuzuma ukazagire icyo uyivugaho .
U Bufaransa bwashinjwe kenshi kugira uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi no gukingira ikibaba abayigizemo uruhare ntibakurikiranywe na ubutabera , ahanini bishingiye ku mubano icyo gihugu cyari gifitanye na ubutegetsi bwa u Rwanda mu gihe yabaga .
Col Rutabana yatanze kopi za inyandiko zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Uganda .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Uganda Col Joseph Rutabana yatanze kopi za impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu .
Izo kopi zashyikirijwe Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na amahanga wa Uganda , Sam Kutesa kuri uyu wa Kane nkuko Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu yabitangaje ibinyujije kuri Twitter .
Muri Nzeri umwaka ushize nibwo Inama ya Abaminisitiri yagize Col Rutabana Joseph Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Uganda asimbuye Gen Maj ( Rtd ) Frank Mugambage wari umaze imyaka 11 ari ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri icyo gihugu .
Ambasaderi Rutabana yari asanzwe ari ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Israel .
Guhera mu 2017 umubano wa u Rwanda watangiye kuzamo agatotsi ubwo abanyarwanda batangiraga gutotezwa muri Uganda bikozwe na inzego zaho za umutekano , bamwe bagafungwa cyangwa bagatoteza binyuranyije na amategeko .
Kuva icyo gihe ni nabwo u Rwanda rwatangiye gushinja Uganda gukorana na abashaka kuruhungabanyiriza umutekano , bahabwa rugari muri icyo gihugu na ububasha bwo kugirira nabi abanyarwanda badashyigikiye ibyo bikorwa .
Umubano wa ibihugu byombi wakomeje kuzamba kugeza ubwo muri Kanama 2019 ku buhuza bwa Angola na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , ibihugu byombi byasinye amasezerano agamije kubyutsa umubano no guhosha ibibazo byari bimaze iminsi hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Muri Kamena na Nyakanga 2020 , Uganda yagiye yoherereza u Rwanda bamwe mu baturage barwo bari bamaze igihe bafungiwe muri icyo gihugu mu buryo bunyuranyije na amategeko , mu mugambi wo gukomeza guhosha ibibazo bihari .
Nubwo gutabwa muri yombi mu gihiriri ku banyarwanda bari muri icyo gihugu byagabanyutse , biracyakorwa ndetse hari abakijugunywa ku mupaka nyuma ya igihe bafunzwe mu buryo bunyuranyije na amategeko muri Uganda .
Mbere ya umwaka wa 2017 umubano wa u Rwanda na Uganda wagaragariraga cyane mu bucuruzi hagati ya ibihugu byombi bwiyongeraga umunsi ku munsi .
Imibare ya Banki Nkuru ya Igihugu yo mu mezi atandatu ya mbere ya 2016 , igaragaza ko ubucuruzi bwa ibihugu byombi bwari bwiyongereye ku kigero cya 26 . 9 % , ugereranyije na amezi atandatu ya mbere ya 2015 .
U Budage : Abanyarwanda bizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore hakomozwa ku ruhare rwabo mu iterambere .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda mu Budage iherereye i Berlin yizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore mu muhango witabiriwe na ingeri zitandukanye , harimo abadepite , abahanzi na Abanyarwanda batuye mu Rwanda no mu Budage .
Ubusanzwe uyu munsi wizihizwa ku tariki 8 werurwe , ariko Abanyarwanda baba mu Budage bawizihije tariki 20 Werurwe 2021 .
Ni umuhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga nka imwe muri gahunda zashyizweho mu rwego rwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Umujyanama wa mbere muri Ambasade ya u Rwanda i Berlin , wari uhagarariye Ambasaderi , Nshimiyimana Benedicto , yavuze ko agaciro ka umugore mu Rwanda no ku Isi muri rusange kamaze kugera ku ntambwe ishimishije ariko hakwiye kongerwamo ingufu abagore bakagaragara mu nzego za ubuyobozi ari benshi .
Ati " " " " Na ubwo intambwe yatewe ishimishije , dushingiye ku ngero za inkuru ebyiri zivugwa kuri ubu muri politiki , ari zo kuba Amerika yishimira kubona Visi Perezida wa umugore nyuma ya imyaka 245 ya ubwigenge na Tanzania bishimira kubona Perezida wa umugore nyuma ya imyaka 59 ya ubwigenge .
Dukwiye kwihutisha ingamba zatuma uburinganire na ubwuzuzanye bigerwaho mu gihe cya vuba . " " " "
Mukangango Marie uhagarariye itsinda rya abari na abategarugori muri Diaspora ya u Rwanda mu Budage we yagarutse ku ruhare Abanyarwandakazi bahatuye bagira mu iterambere rya u Rwanda .
Yagize ati " " " " Hari umushinga wakozwe na abari na abategarugori uherutse gutahwa mu Rwanda mu kwezi kwa gatatu uyu mwaka .
Icyo gihe hakusanyijwe Miliyoni icyenda za amafaranga ya u Rwanda yagenewe Koperative Igisubizo Gitara iri mu Karere ka Nyaruguru .
Uyu mushinga ukaba ugenewe gutera inkunga ubworozi bwa amatungo magufi ku miryango 90 iri mu Kagari ka Coko , Umurenge wa Cyahinda . " " " "
Ni umuhango witabiriwe kandi na Umudepite uhagarariye abagore mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda , Uwineza Beline , wavuze ku ntambwe igihugu cyateye mu kubahiriza ihame rya uburinganire na ubwuzuzanye .
Ati " " " " Umugore yahawe uburenganzira na uruhare ku mutungo , nka ubutaka na ibindi , hemejwe uburinganire bwa ibitsina byombi mu nzego zose , ndetse hemezwa ko kuri 30 % mu nzego zose za ubuyobozi bwa igihugu hakwiye kugaragaramo Abanyarwandakazi . " " " "
" " " " Ingamba igihugu cyafashe mu kurushaho guteza imbere uburinganire na ubwuzuzanye mu Rwanda tuzikesha ubuyobozi bwa igihugu bwiza no kubongerera ubushobozi mu kwitinyuka kuko bashoboye . " " " "
Uyu muhango witabiriwe na abahanzikazi ba Abanyarwanda barimo Audia Intore , uririmba indirimbo gakondo , Sonia Singh Mwumvaneza na Donatha Kankindi wavuze umuvugo utaka ubwiza , umutima mugari , inkingi ya umuryango utekanye na ubutwari bwa umutegarugori .
Ingabo za u Rwanda ziri muri Centrafrique zambitswe imidali ya ishimwe .
Ingabo za u Rwanda ziri mu butumwa bwa Umuryango wa Abibumbye bwo kugarura amahoro muri Centrafrique zambitswe imidali ya ishimwe kubera ubwitange na umurava uziranga mu kazi kazo .
Igikorwa cyo gutanga imidali ya ishimwe ku ngabo za u Rwanda cyabereye mu kigo cya Socatel Ma poko , ahari icyicaro cyazo mu Mujyi wa Bangui , ku wa Gatanu , tariki ya 19 Werurwe 2021 .
Umuyobozi wa Ingabo za MINUSCA , Brig Gen Driss Okaddour , yashimye umusanzu wa ingabo za u Rwanda mu kugarura amahoro na umutekano bya umwihariko ku wa 27 Ukuboza 2020 ubwo habaga amatora ya Umukuru wa Igihugu na abagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Yagize ati " " " " Akazi kanyu gahabwa agaciro na abanyamuryango ba MINUSCA na igihugu cyatwakiriye ari na bo bungukira bwa mbere muri izo nshingano zo kubungabunga amahoro .
Sinakwibagirwa ubwitange na umuhate wanyu ubwo inyeshyamba zateraga Umujyi wa Bangui .
Umuyobozi wanyu yambwiye ko ibintu biza kugenda neza kandi mwahise musubiza igitero inyuma . " " " " " " " "
U Rwanda ruri ku mwanya wa gatatu mu bihugu bifite ingabo nyinshi mu bikorwa bya Umuryango wa Abibumbye bigamije kubungabunga amahoro muri Repubulika ya Centrafrique ( MINUSCA ) , aho abasirikare na abapolisi barwo barenga 1389 .
Mu matora ya Umukuru wa Igihugu yabaye ku wa 27 Ukuboza 2020 , u Rwanda rwoherejeyo izindi ngabo 300 zo gufasha gucunga umutekano mu bihe bya amatora nyuma ya uko hari imitwe ya inyeshyamba yashakaga guhungabanya ayo matora .
Ingabo za u Rwanda ziri muri Batayo ya Karindwi ( Rwabatt7 ) zoherejwe i Bangui ku wa 6 Werurwe 2020 ; zakoze ibikorwa bitandukanye birimo kurinda Perezida wa Centrafrique no kubungabunga umutekano mu duce dutandukanye two mu Murwa Mukuru .
Izi ngabo zanatangije ibikorwa byo gukumira imirwano muri Bangui , gukora uburinzi bwo guhagarika ubwicanyi , kurinda abasivili gihugu ndetse ibi byose byiyongeraho ibikorwa bitandukanye birimo no guha abaturage amazi meza .
Umuyobozi wa Rwabatt7 , Lt Col JB SAFARI , yashimye umuhate wa ingabo mu gihe cya umwaka zimaze ziri mu nshingano .
Yagize ati " " " " Twishimiye gutanga umusanzu wacu mu rugendo rwo kugarura amahoro muri Centrafrique . " " " " " " " "
Centrafrique imaze igihe iri mu bibazo bya umutekano ariko byongeye gukara mu mpera za umwaka ushize ubwo hategurwaga amatora ya Perezida .
Imitwe ya inyeshyamba irimo UPC yari yiyemeje kuyadurumbanya ariko ingabo za Loni zirimo iza u Rwanda zirahagoboka .
Amatora yagenze neza ndetse Perezida Touadera yashimiye umusanzu wa ingabo za u Rwanda mu kugira ngo amatora agende neza .
Muri Centrafrique , u Rwanda rufite ingabo zirimo abakobwa na abagore 38 bakora mu mirimo itandukanye ariko bagahuriza ku ntego imwe yo kurinda abasivili .
USA : Ishimwe wa imyaka 17 yatawe muri yombi ashinjwa kwica mugenzi we .
Ishimwe Eric uba mu Mujyi wa Nashville muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika yatawe muri yombi na polisi ya icyo gihugu ashinjwa ubwicanyi bukoreshejwe intwaro .
WKRN yatangaje ko Ishimwe yafashwe na inzego za umutekano ku wa Gatatu wa iki Cyumweru , biturutse ku rupfu rwa Niyibizi Kevin wasanzwe mu rugo rwo kwa Ishimwe yishwe arashwe mu gituza .
Inzego za umutekano zavuze ko Ishimwe yabajijwe impamvu yarashe mugenzi we wa imyaka 16 , asobanura ko bari barimo gukinisha imbunda Niyibizi yari yazanye , maze birangira Ishimwe akoze mu mbarutso imbunda yerekeye nyakwigendera aba ahasize ubuzima .
Ishimwe wa imyaka 17 yahise ajyanwa mu kigo ngororamuco aho akurikiranyweho icyaha cyo kwica umuntu .
Bivugwa ko uyu musore Ishimwe afite inkomoko mu Rwanda .
Abanyarwanda baba muri Sénégal bizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri Sénégal ifatanyije na Abanyarwanda baba mu bihugu bya Mali , Gambia , Guinée - Bissau na Cap Vert na inshuti za u Rwanda bizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore .
Uyu munsi usanzwe wizihirwa tariki ya 8 Werurwe 2021 , ibirori byawo byabaye ku wa 13 Werurwe 2021 , mu muhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga rya WebEx unatambuka kuri Televiziyo Isango Star no ku zindi mbuga nkoranyambaga zirimo YouTube na Twitter .
Abatanze ibiganiro barimo Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Iyubahirizwa rya ihame rya Uburinganire na Ubwuzuzanye mu Rwanda ( GMO ) , Rwabuhihi Rose ; Umuyobozi uhagarariye UN Women mu Rwanda , Fatou Lo ; Umuyobozi wa Umuryango uharanira guteza imbere Uburinganire no kurwanya ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina ( RWAMREC ) , Rutayisire Fidèle ;
Ngeruka Fabiola ukorera muri UNFPA Mali , Agnès Ammeux ukorera Enabel muri Guinée - Bissau na Dr Mukeshimana Angelique wiga Ubuvuzi muri Kaminuza ya Havre mu Bufaransa .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Karabaranga Jean Pierre , yagarutse ku butumwa bugusha ku nsanganyamatsiko yo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore uyu mwaka igira iti " " " " Munyarwandakazi , ba ku ruhembe mu Isi yugarijwe na COVID - 19 . " " " "
Abatanze ibiganiro bikije bya umwihariko ku rwego umugore agezeho mu kwiteza imbere , uruhare afite mu iterambere rya igihugu ndetse na ibibazo bahura nabyo mu mibereho ya buri munsi na ibisubizo bikwiye kubifatirwa .
Ambasaderi Karabaranga yibukije ubutumwa bwa Perezida Kagame ubwo uwo munsi wizihizwaga .
Icyo gihe abinyujije ku rukuta rwa Twitter , yagize ati " " " " " " " " Uyu munsi ni ukwibuka ko uburinganire butareba abagore gusa .
Nta terambere ryabaho hatabaye ubwitabire na amahirwe angana kuri bose .
Buri wese muri twe afite uruhare mu kurwanya ubusumbane kandi ihezwa nta mwanya rifite mu gihe kiri imbere . " " " "
Abatanze ikiganiro bagarutse ku ntambwe ifatika u Rwanda rwateye mu byiciro birimo uburezi , ubuzima na ubuvuzi , ubukungu , imiyoborere na inzego za ubuyobozi , umutekano na ubutabera .
Bavuze ko ubwiyongere bwa abagore mu nzego zose , bikwiye kwishimirwa no guterwa imbaraga Kandi bigakomeza .
Mu nzego za ubuyobozi u Rwanda rwakoze amavugurura atandukanye atuma ruza ku myanya ya mbere ku Isi mu kugira umubare munini wa abagore mu nzego zifata ibyemezo , nka aho mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko bangana na 61 % , muri Guverinoma bagera kuri 50 % .
Itegeko Nshinga u Rwanda rugenderaho kuri ubu naryo riha abagore uburenganzira bwo kugira 30 % rya imyanya ifata ibyemezo .
Ambasaderi Karabaranga yibukije ko ibi byose byashobotse kubera ubuyobozi bwiza bwa Perezida Paul Kagame yubatse kuva igihugu kivuye mu icuraburindi rya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Kuva mu 1962 u Rwanda rubona ubwigenge kugeza mu 1994 , umugore na umwana wa umukobwa nta gaciro bahabwaga haba mu miryango yabo ndetse no muri politiki ya igihugu .
Nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi Guverninoma ya Ubumwe bwa igihugu yashyizweho na FPR ni yo yashyize mu bikorwa politiki yo guha agaciro abagore , kubateza imbere , kubashyigikira muri byose kuko na ubundi byari muri gahunda ya politiki ya FPR kuva yavuka . " " " " " " " "
U Rwanda kandi rwashyizeho gahunda nyinshi zakozwe zijanye no gufasha abagore mu kwiteza imbere muri rusange .
Abitabiriye ibi biganiro bagaragaje ko iki cyiciro gikeneye kwigwaho byihariye hagamijwe kumenya ibibazo abagore bahuye nabyo mu gihe cya Coronavirus mu buryo bwimbitse na uko byakemuka kandi abafatanyabikorwa ba Leta bakabyitabira ari benshi .
Hibukijwe kandi ko Umunyarwandakazi kuva kera yagaragaje ubushobozi , ubwitange no kwihangana mu bihe bikomeye nko mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu ku buryo bitanga icyizere ko na ubundi abagore bazashobora kuva mu bibazo batewe na Coronavirus cyane cyane ko Leta ibari inyuma kandi ibashyigikiye muri byose .
Umuyobozi wa Diaspora Nyarwanda muri Sénégal , Karamaga Patrick , yashimye ko umugore yahawe umwanya mu nzego zitandukanye .
Ati " " " " U Rwanda rwateye imbere ariko ntabwo turagera aho dushaka kugera .
Bitangirira mu rugo , ku mwana muto , ko umwana wa umukobwa agomba kwiga . " " " " " " " "
Abitabiriye ibiganiro batanze icyifuzo ko muri Diaspora ibiganiro bijyanye na uburinganire byashyirwamo ingufu cyane cyane mu miryango kugira ngo urubyiruko rwo Rwanda rwa ejo ruzashobore gusigasira ibyagezweho .
Ambasade ya u Rwanda muri Sénégal ifatanyije na Abanyarwanda baba mu bihugu bya Mali , Gambia , Guinée - Bissau na Cap Vert na inshuti za u Rwanda bizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Sénégal , Karabaranga Jean Pierre , yibukije ko umugore yahawe ijambo kubera ubuyobozi bwiza bwa Perezida Paul Kagame .
Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Iyubahirizwa rya ihame rya Uburinganire na Ubwuzuzanye mu Rwanda ( GMO ) , Rwabuhihi Rose , yagaragaje ko hari amategeko igihugu cyashyizeho aha ijambo umugore .
Urubyiruko rwa u Rwanda dufite amahirwe , kwinjira nta gukomanga - Uwineza Aline Nelly .
Rwiyemezamirimo Uwineza Aline Nelly yagaragaje ko urubyiruko rwo mu Rwanda rufite amahirwe adasanzwe yarushyiriweho , arufasha kwiteza imbere .
Yabigarutseho mu buhamya yatanze ubwo Abanyarwanda batuye mu bihugu bya Scandinavia bizihizaga Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore , wateguwe na Ambasade ya u Rwanda ifite Icyicaro muri Suéde ifatanyije na Umuryango wa Abanyarwanda batuye mu gace ka Ibihugu byo mu Majyaruguru ya u Burayi bya Suède , Danemark , Norvège na Finlande .
Uyu munsi ubusanzwe wizihizwa ku wa 8 Werurwe buri mwaka , Abanyarwanda batuye muri Scandinavia , bawizihije ku wa 13 Werurwe 2021 .
Witabiriwe na Minisitiri wa Uburinganire na Iterambere rya Umuryango ( MIGEPROF ) , Prof . Jeannette Bayisenge ; Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Suède , Nkulikiyinka Christine ; rwiyemezamirimo Uwineza Aline na Umuhanzi Masamba Intore .
Amb . Nkulikiyinka Christine yavuze ko ubushobozi bwa abagore bukwiye gushingirwaho mu kubaka ahazaza heza .
Ati " " " " Kuba abagore bashoboye ngira ngo ntibishidikanywaho , ni yo mpamvu bakwiye kugira uruhare mu iterambere ryo ku giti cyabo , imiryango na iryu Rwanda aho batuye hose . " " " " " " " "
Yabibukije ko bakwiye guhora bazirikana ko nubwo bari mu mahanga bakwiye kugira u Rwanda ku mutima , bakamenya ibiruberamo ndetse bakabigiramo uruhare .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Muri ibi bihugu byo mu Burayi bwa Amajyaruguru bamaze gutera intambwe ishimishije mu buringanire , nubwo nabo bagifite izindi ntambwe zo gutera .
Abanyarwandakazi baba ino , bafite amahirwe yo kwigira ku byiza babona ngo bashobore nabo kwiyubaka ariko badataye umuco wacu . " " " " " " " "
Minisitiri Bayisenge yashimiye abateguye uyu munsi kuko kubikora ugashyirwa mu bikorwa ubwabyo ari ibya agaciro gahambaye .
Yakomeje ati " " " " " " " " Ni ibintu byiza cyane byerekana ko mushaka guhura mukaganira ku cyabateza imbere nka abagore kandi nka Abanyarwanda muri rusange .
Icyo mbifurije kandi nabasaba ni uko mwagumana indangagaciro zizakomeza kubaranga nka Abanyarwanda , mugakomeza gukunda iwanyu , igihugu cyanyu , mukagira ubumwe bwo pfundo ryo gukorera hamwe no kumvikana , mukanakunda umurimo . " " " " " " " "
Mu buhamya bwe , Uwineza Aline yavuze ko urubyiruko rwashyiriweho amahirwe adasanzwe arufasha kwiteza imbere .
Uwineza Nelly Aline ari mu Banyarwandakazi batekereje bwangu ku musanzu we mu kwimakaza isuku ya ibiganza nka intwaro yo gutsinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus ubwo yabonekaga mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 .
Yakoze hand sanitizer ya umwimerere yise " " " " Tropical hand sanitizer " " " " ndetse ahita ayigeza ku isoko rya u Rwanda .
Uyu rwiyemezamirimo wa umukobwa yashinze Tropical Brewery and Winery ikora imivinyo na imiti yica udukoko abantu bakaraba mu ntoki nka abisiga amavuta ( hand sanitizer ) .
Tropical hand sanitizer ikoze mu birimo igihingwa cya igikakarubamba cya umwimerere kiva muri Amerika , alukoro ( Isopropyl , ethyl ) na amavuta ( essential oil ) aboneka mu Rwanda .
Uwineza yavuze ko hari abababereye icyitegererezo mu rugendo rwo kwihangira imirimo .
Yakomeje ati " " " " " " " " Dufite abo tureberaho beza kandi imiryango ya u Rwanda irafunguye nta gukomonga winjiye , ku rubyiruko dufite amahirwe rwose . " " " " " " " "
Umugiraneza Léontine wari ukuriye itsinda rya Abagore bateguye igikorwa cyo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore yasabye abakobwa kuzaba aba ingenzi mu buzima bwabo .
Yakomeje ati " " " " " " " " Muri make ndifuriza abakobwa bacu kuzaba nka Ndabaga , mugire ubutwari nka ubwe bwatumye atabarira igihugu ari umukobwa . " " " " " " " "
Yashimye ko igikorwa cyagenze neza kuko cyitabiriwe bishimishije na abantu benshi , anashimira Amb . Nkulikiyinka bya umwihariko ubaha inama akanababa hafi mu bikorwa bitandukanye .
Umuganwa Marie Christine uhagarariye Abagore muri Diaspora Nyarwanda Danmark - Jylland & Fyn , mu ijambo rye na we yashimiye uko umuhango wagenze .
Yakomeje ati " " " " " " " " Ibyavuye muri ibi biganiro bizatugirira akamaro kandi dukomeze tubyibakireho mu burere bwa abana bacu no gushyira hamwe nka abagore bafite u Rwanda nka igihugu bakunda . " " " " " " " "
Butera Josée yatanze ikiganiro ku ikoranabuhanga na urubyiruko , ibibi na ibyiza byaryo , atanga inama asaba ko hazabaho ikiganiro cyihariye kubera ibihe Isi irimo bijyanye na ikoranabuhanga rishobora kuba ryiza ku bana cyangwa kubabera ribi .
Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Abagore waranzwe na igitaramo cyayobowe na Masamba Intore na itsinda yari ayoboye , bataramiye abawitabiriye .
Uyu muhango wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga nka uburyo bwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Abanyarwanda batuye muri Scandinavia bizihije Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wa Abagore .
Amb . Hategeka yasabye urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga kwima amatwi abapfobya Jenoside .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu , Emmanuel Hategeka , yasabye urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga kwima amatwi no kwamagana abahakana bakanapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Yabigarutseho ku wa 21 Gicurasi 2021 ubwo Abanyarwanda na inshuti za u Rwanda baba muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu , Arabia Saoudite na Bahrain bibukaga ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Ni umuhango wabereye i Dubai muri UAE abandi bakurikira mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo kwibuka hanubahirizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda Covid - 19 .
Muri uyu muhango , Ambasaderi Hategeka yibukije ko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ari ugutsindwa kwa muntu ndetse na umuryango mpuzamahanga mu mateka ya vuba aha .
Yasabye urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga kwima amatwi no kwamagana abahakana na abapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yagize ati " " " " Hashize imyaka 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ihagaritswe .
Gusa ingengabitekerezo ya jenoside iracyahari ndetse abakekwaho kugira uruhare muri jenoside bakidegembya bakomeje gukwirakwiza ingengabitekerezo yayo .
Ndabasaba bya umwihariko urubyiruko , mwe Rwanda rwa ejo , kwima amatwi abahakana na abapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Mwime amatwi abashaka kubarangaza barajwe ishinga no gusubiza inyuma u Rwanda . " " " "
Ambasaderi Hategeka kandi yibukije abakuru ko bafite inshingano zo kuvuga amateka ya ukuri kugira ngo abato na abandi batayazi bayamenye .
Yibukije amahanga ko kuvuga ko jenoside itazongera kuba ukundi bidahagije ahubwo bisaba ibikorwa .
" " " " Twongeye guhamagarira amahanga kongera kwiyemeza ko jenoside itazasubira binyuze mu gushyikiriza ubutabera abakekwaho kugira uruhare muri jenoside bakidegembya .
Mu bo u Rwanda rwatanze impapuro zisaba ko batabwa muri yombi 1 , 100 baracyidegembya . " " " "
Umunyamabanga wa leta ushinzwe ubutwererane mpuzamahanga muri UAE , Reem Ebrahim Al Hashimy , yagaragaje ko igihugu cye cyifatanyije na u Rwanda ndetse na Abanyarwanda muri ibi bihe byo kwibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ati " " " " Ntewe ishema no guhagararira igihugu cyanjye muri iki gikorwa cyo kwibuka ku nshuro ya 27 Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu Rwanda .
Uyu ni umwanya wa ingenzi mu kwibuka inzirakarengane no gufata mu mugongo abarakotse .
Ni umwanya kandi wo kwiyemeza ko ibyabaye bitazasubira ukundi . " " " "
" " " " Abaturage na ubuyobozi bwa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Abarabu twifatanyije cyane na abavandimwe bari mu Rwanda na ubuyobozi bw " " " " u Rwanda burangajwe imbere na Nyakubahawa Perezida Paul Kagame twubaha cyane .
Dukomeje kugira imibanire myiza na u Rwanda . " " " "
Reem Al Hashimy yongeyeho ati " " " " Twifatanyije namwe , turasenga ngo ibyabaye ntibizongere kuba ukundi ndetse tugomba gukorera hamwe mu kurwanya icyitwa urwango cyose na ubuhezanguni . " " " "
Umunyemari Ashish J . Thakkar , washinze uruganda rwa Mara Phones ndetse akaba na umunyamigabane muri sosiyete Atlas Mara ni umwe mu batanze ibiganiro nka inshuti ya u Rwanda .
Yavuze ko mu myaka 27 ishize u Rwanda rwagize umugisha wo kugira ubuyobozi bureba kure kuko ngo iyo bitaba ibyo igihugu nticyari kuba kigeze ku ntambwe cyateye .
Mu bandi batanze ibiganiro harimo Dr Bideri Diogene wagaragaje amateka ya uburyo Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yateguwe igihe kirekire , agaragaza ko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi itabaye impanuka .
Uyu muhango kandi waranzwe no gucana urumuri rwa icyizere , ubuhamya ndetse na indirimbo zirimo ubutumwa bwo kwibuka no kwiyubaka .
Kwibuka 27 : Abanyarwanda batuye muri Perth - Australia bibutse abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Kuri uyu wa 16 Gicurasi , Abanyarwanda batuye mu mujyi wa Perth mu Burengerazuba bwa Australie bibutse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ku nshuro ya 27 , mu muhango witabiriwe na Abanyarwanda na inshuti zabo bagera ku 150 .
Mu bashyitsi bitabiriye uyu muhango wo kwibuka , harimo wa Meya wa Umujyi wa Stirling , Mark Irwin , wakunze kwitabira ibikorwa byo kwibuka kuva muri 2017 .
Harimo kandi abahagarariye imiryango ya abaturuka mu bindi bihugu batuye muri Australie .
Ambasaderi wa u Rwanda muri Singapore ari na we Uhagarariye u Rwanda muri Australie , Nouvelle - Zélande na Indonesie , akaba yitabiriye uyu muhango mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Ni umuhango waranzwe no gucana urumuri rwa icyizere ndetse no gufata umwanya wo guha icyubahiro abazize Jenocide yakorewe abatutsi , ndetse hanatangwa ubuhamya .
Muri uyu muhango kandi , urubyiruko rwavutse nyuma ya Jenocide yakorewe Abatutsi kandi rugakurira muri Australie , rukaba ruhuriye mu mushinga wa " " " " Amateka Series , " " " " rwamuritse bimwe mu bikoresho byakoreshejwe muri Jenocide yakorewe Abatutsi ndetse na imbwirwaruhame zavuzwe mu gutegura Jenoside , nka bimwe mu bizaba bigize umushinga
bateganya gutangiza muri iki cyumweru wo kumurika mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga amateka ya Jenoside yakorewe abatutsi , uko yateguwe , uko yashyizwe mu bikorwa na uko Abanyarwanda bagerageza gukira ibikomere no kwiyubaka .
Mu buhamya bwe , umwe mu barokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yagaragaje uko Jenocide yateguwe , yashyizwe mu bikorwa , imibereho ya abarokotse nyuma yo kurokoka , nzira ndende kandi ya umusaraba yanyuzemo kugeza arokotse na urugamba rwo kurwanya abahakana na abapfobya Jenoside .
Uwavuze ahagarariye Abanyarwanda batuye muri Perth ( RCA - Perth ) Ernest Kalisa , yashimiye abitabiriye igikorwa cyo kwibuka cyane cyane urubyiruko rwavutse nyuma ya Jenoside , avuga ko berekana umuhate wo kwiga amateka ya u Rwanda no guharanira ko Jenoside itazongera kubaho ukundi .
Kalisa yibukije ko kwibuka ari inshingano za buri wese mu rwego rwo kuzirikana ku ngaruka za amacakubiri na politiki ya ivangura ndetse ashimira ingabo za FPR - Inkotanyi zahagaritse Jenoside , anasaba buri wese kwibaza uko byari kugenda iyo FPR itagoboka u Rwanda ngo ihashye burundu abicanyi , ati " " " " Ubu Isi iba ivuga andi mateka kuko
nta na uwo kubara inkuru wari gusigara . " " " "
Ambassaderi Jean de Dieu Uwihanganye , yavuze ko ku barokotse , kwibuka ari ibya buri munsi , ariko ko igikorwa nka iki " " " " gituma dufatanyiriza hamwe guha icyubahiro abacu bazize Jenoside , gufata mu mugongo abarokotse , no kuzirikana imizi na intandaro bya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 . " " " "
Yongeyeho ati : " " " " Iyo twibuka , tuba kandi duha icyubahiro abitanze kugira ngo Jenoside ihagarare . " " " "
Ambasaderi Uwihanganye yavuze ko " " " " Guverinoma ya u Rwanda yahisemo gushyira imbere gahunda ya " " " " Ndi Umunyarwanda " " " " no kurenga amacakubiri ya ubwoko .
Kwiyunga no kurwanya amacakubiri si igikorwa cyoroshye cya igihe gito , ahubwo ni urugendo rusaba gushyira hamwe ku bari mu gihugu no hanze yacyo . " " " "
Uku gushyira hamwe gukwiye kwifashishwa mu kurwanya abapfobya bakanahakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatusi .
Ati " " " " Ikibabaje ariko kidatangaje , ni uko hari abakinangiye imitima bahakana kandi bagapfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ndetse na abakwirakwiza ko habaye jenoside ebyiri .
Icyiza gusa ni uko Leta ya u Rwanda yiyemeje kutazajenjekera uwo ari we wese uhakana cyangwa ngo apfobye Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi agamije kudusubiza mu bihe bya icuraburindi u Rwanda rwanyuzemo . " " " "
Meya wa Umujyi wa Stirling , Mark Irwin , yashimiye Abanyarwanda baba muri Perth , avuga ko Isi ikwiye kubigiraho kugira intero ya " " " " Ntibizongera " " " " mu rwego rwo kwirinda ko Jenoside yazongera kubaho ahandi hantu ku Isi .
Uyu muyobozi yavuze ko umuhango wo kwibuka utanga ubutumwa ndetse ukaba na isomo ku bandi , kuko ari bumwe mu buryo bwo gukumira ko Jenoside yazongera kubaho ukundi .
Nasubiye iwacu ndahayoberwa , ishingwa rya Ibuka - France mu ngorane : Ibikubiye mu gitabo cya Mutuyisa Brossard .
Espérance Mutuyisa Brossard yashyize hanze igitabo " " " " Mon histoire rwandaise , Ibuka ( souviens - toi ) : ma vie et mes combats ( Amateka yanjye nka umunyarwanda , amateka ya Ibuka na intambara narwanye , " " " " kigaruka ku mateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yaciyemo na uburyo umuryango we wishwe na abari inshuti .
Yavuze uburyo nyina yishwe na abana yigishaga , barumuna be bakicwa na abana biganye .
Espérance Mutuyisa Brossard mwene Kayihura na Munganyamariya Pétronille , yavukiye muri Nyaruhengeri ya Butare tariki ya 28 Ukuboza 1961 akaba imfura iwabo mu muryango wa abana bane .
Mu bana bavukana , harokotse babiri .
Mutuyisa , ni umubyeyi wa abana babiri , Umuriza - Brossard Jonathan wa imyaka 30 na Kayihura - Brossard Mickaël ufite imyaka 28 .
Uyu mubyeyi wagizwe Umuyobozi mukuru wa icyubahiro uhoraho na Ibuka France , yize ibijyanye na ibaruramari ( Comptable ) , ari nabyo akora mu gihe cya imyaka irenga 20 mu isomero ( Bibliothèques ) rihurirwemo na imijyi 47 , rifite ikicaro mu mujyi wa Niort .
Muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , Mutuyisa yiciwe abavandimwe barimo Uwambazisa Janviére , Ufituwe Marie - Thérèse na nyina Munganyamariya Pétronille .
Mu kiganiro kirambuye na IGIHE , Espérance Mutuyisa Brossard yavuze ko igitabo " " " " Mon histoire rwandaise , Ibuka ( souviens - toi ) : ma vie et mes combats " " " " yacyanditse agamije guha agaciro abe bishwe muri Jenoside .
Yavuze ko ikindi cyamuteye imbaraga zo kwandika , ari ukugaragaza uburyo Abatutsi batangiye gutotezwa kuva kera .
Ati " " " " Igice cya mbere kivuga uko Abanyarwanda babanaga mbere ya abakoloni , uko ubuzima bwabo bwahindutse nyuma ya aho Abakoloni bahageze , nerekana uko habayeho itotezwa rya Abatutsi ku bwa Parmuhutu kugeza hakozwe Jenoside . " " " "
" " " " Mbere ya ibyo byose navuze uko nanjye nabayeho aho nkomoka , uko nabayeho niruka mu bindi bihugu kimwe na abandi twari dusangiye ikibazo . " " " "
Impamvu nyamukuru yo kwandika , Mutuyisa avuga ko byatewe na ikiganiro yakurikiranye muri Gicurasi 2016 cyatambutse kuri France Inter aho umunyamakuru Natacha Polony yaganiraga na Raphaël Glucksmann wakoze film documentaire izwi ku mateka ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yise " " " " Tuez - les tous " " " "
Muri icyo kiganiro , Natacha Polony yabwiye Raphaël Glucksmann ko ngo muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi " " " " ari amasarigoma yarwanaga na andi . " " " "
Byababaje cyane Mutuyisa , ashaka icyo yakora ngo abahakanyi nka abo na abapfobya Jenoside babihagarike .
Ati " " " " Nibwo mbitekerejeho bimbuza gusinzira , bukeye niyemeza kwerekana ibyakozwe byose mu Bufaransa igihugu cyagize ubufatanye na Leta ya abicanyi , mbereka ibyagezweho mu kurwanya abahakana na abapfobya jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ntangira nerekana uko Ibuka - France yashinzwe na indi miryango ifasha abacitse ku
icumu rya jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , dufatanyije na Abafaransa bari mu bice no mu mirimo itandukanye bumva akababaro kacu , baharanira ko habaho ubutabera , ubucamanza bugata muri yombi ababigizemo uruhare bose bari ku butaka bwa u Bufaransa . " " " "
Ku bijyanye na ishingwa rya Ibuka - France , Mutuyisa yagize ati " " " " Kuva nagera mu Bufaransa ntabwo nicaye kubera amateka yanjye nashatse uburyo bwose bushoboka dushinga Ibuka - France , muri iki gitabo nanditse impamvu yo gusiga amateka , inzitizi twahuye nazo . " " " "
" " " " Ibuka - France tuyitangira rero nabanje kujya mu Rwanda mbona neza uko ibintu byagenze kuko Jenoside yabaye njye ndi hanze na umugabo wanjye aho twari mu kazi , nyuma ngaruka mu Bufaransa icyo gihe twafatanyaga na Adelaide Mukantabana , Dr Bizimana Jean Damascène , Esperance Patureau na abandi .
Hari uburyo twajyaga dutegura kwibuka hano dutuye ariko tukagira ibibazo kuko twabikoraga mu bushobozi bwa buri wese kuko hari hatarajyaho association tubikoreramo . " " " "
Mutuyisa yavuze ko inzitizi zindi bahuraga nazo ari uko Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi itari yakwemezwa na Loni , bigatuma nta wumva uburemere bwa igikorwa cyo kwibuka .
Ati " " " " Kandi n " " " " imibanire ya ibihugu byacu byombi ntiyagendaga neza nubwo ibyo njye numvaga bitatureba cyane . " " " "
Nyuma yo kwemererwa gushinga Ibuka France havutse ibindi bibazo kuko ibigo bimwe byangaga gukorana na uwo muryango mushya , bavuga ko baje guteza akaduruvayo bahiga abakoze Jenoside ku butaka bwa Abufaransa .
No mu biro bishinzwe iperereza mu Bufaransa ngo ntibabashiraga amakenga kuko bagiye bahamagazwa kenshi , bashinjwa kuba abakozi ba Kagame na FPR .
Ati " " " " Twigeze gutumira Perezida wa Ibuka - Rwanda ngo aze atuganirize uko mu gihugu bimeze , u Bufaransa bubima Visa , ubwo iyo twajyaga kwibuka ibiro bya iperereza byahitaga binsaba uko gahunda iteganyijwe , nkayibaha nkababwira ko ntacyo duhisha . " " " "
" " " " Bari baratubujije no kugira aho duhurira ngo twibuke , ahubwo bagaha urubuga abajenosideri , babaha uburenganzira bwo kujya gukora imyigaragambyo twe rwose bakatwangira , nibwo nifashishaga SOS racisme na UEJF ( Union des Étudiants Juifs de France ) bakadushakira aho duhurira , nyuma u Bufaransa bwaje kujya buduha ahantu
ariko hadashobotse . " " " "
Yavuze ko na za Kiliziya zari zarabimye aho gukorera imihango yo kwibuka , bavuga ko ngo batabaha urubuga rwo gukoreramo politiki .
Icyakora , Mutuyisa avuga ko nubwo bahuye na ingorane , bishimira kuba kuri ubu byarakemutse Ibuka France igakora neza .
Ati " " " " Uyu munsi rero ndishimye kuko ibyo byose byaje gukemuka .
Uzi kubona ukuntu twamaganwaga ntawe utwumva hano mu Bufaransa kuko tuvuze jenoside yakorerwe Abatutsi , nta muntu na umwe utwemera , ariko uyu munsi haremejwe itegeko rihana uyihakana .
Uyu munsi mu Bufaransa Perezida Macron akaba yaremeje ko tariki 7 Mata buri mwaka ari umunsi wo kwibuka mu gihugu cyose jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ni intambwe ishimishije . " " " "
Kandi jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ikigishwa no mu mashuri yose mu bufaransa .
Muri ki gitabo kandi Mutuyisa yagarutse ku bikorwa bitandukanye umuryango Ibuka - France wagezeho , nka imanza zitandukanye zarezwemo abapfobya na abahakana na abasize bakoze jenoside na ibindi .
Mutuyisa mu gitabo cye avugamo uburyo abo mu muryango we bishwe bazira ko ari Abatutsi , bigakorwa na abantu bari basanzwe baziranye , banagiriye neza .
Papa na Mama ba Mutuyisa bari abarimu muri Kibirizi , babanye neza na abantu bose kuri uwo musozi .
Ati " " " " Ni ahantu twabaye neza , tubana na abantu bose neza kandi bishimiye uko ababyeyi banjye bigishaga abana ba abaturanyi . " " " "
" " " " Kibirizi rero ukaba umusozi mwiza cyane nkuko mbivuga mu gitabo , ariko sinawugiriyemo amahirwe igihe cyose kuko na ubwo nari umuhanga ntabwo nigeze mpabwa ishuri rya Leta nka abandi , ndangije amashuri abanza , byabaye ngombwa ko njya kwiga i Burundi mu buryo bugoranye cyane . " " " "
Yavuze ko kuba hatashywe inyubako nshya za ambasade , ari umukoro ku Banyamerika wo gukomeza umutima wo gufasha no gushyigikira iterambere rya u Rwanda .
Ahagana saa cyenda , Bush na Laura bagiye muri Lycée de Kigali kuganira na abanyeshuri baho ibijyanye no kwirinda SIDA , ahava ahawe inkoni ya Kinyarwanda nka impano .
Ubwo yageraga ku kibuga cya indege atashye , yaganiriye gato na abasirikare bari baravuye mu butumwa bwa amahoro mu Ntara ya Darfur muri Sudani , dore ko igihugu cye cyari kimaze iminsi gitanga amahugurwa ku ngabo zigiye kujya mu butumwa bwa amahoro .
Lambda , ubwoko bushya bwa Covid - 19 budakangwa na inkingo .
Abashakashatsi bo muri Kaminuza ya Chile bahangayikishijwe na ubwoko bushya bwa Covid - 19 bwitwa Lambda bwagaragaye bwa mbere muri Peru , bufite ubushobozi bwo kwihagararaho imbere ya inkingo za Covid - 19 ziri gutangwa .
Ubu bwoko burimo gukwirakwira cyane aho bumaze kugera mu bihugu 30 ku Isi yose , ariko bukiganza mu bihugu byo muri Amerika ya Epfo , birimo nka Peru aho 80 % bya abarwayi ba Covid - 19 barwaye iya ubu bwoko .
Iri kandi mu bihugu nka Chile , Argentine , Equateur na ibindi .
Igiteye impungenge ni uko ibyo bihugu bigifite ubwiyongere bwa Covid - 19 nubwo biri kwitwara neza mu bikorwa bya ikingira , ibituma abantu bibaza niba inkingo zakorewe mu Bushinwa ziri gutangwa muri Amerika ya Epfo zifite ubushobozi bwo kwirinda icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
OMS ivuga ko hakenewe ubushakashatsi buzemeza niba ubu bwoko bwa Covid - 19 bufite ubudahangarwa ku cyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Ibyamenyekanye kuri " " " " Lambda " " " " na " " " " Epsilon " " " " ; ubundi bwoko bwa COVID - 19 yihinduranya .
Mu bwoko butandatu bumaze kugaragara , bune bubarwa nka ubuhangayikishije .
Ubwo ni Alpha yabonetse bwa mbere mu Bwongereza , Beta yaturutse muri Afurika ya Epfo , Delta yavumbuwe mu Buhinde na Gamma yagaragaye bwa mbere muri Brésil .
Bwose bwandura ku muvuduko uri hejuru ugereranyije na COVID - 19 [ iterwa na agakoko ka Coronavirus ] isanzwe nubwo nabwo burutanwa hagati yabwo , ndetse inyigo zitandukanye zagaragaje ko inkingo zifashishwa hirya no hino zitagira ubushobozi bwo guhangana nabwo ku rwego rumwe na ubwo zihangana na COVID - 19 yavumbuwe i Wuhan mu
Bushinwa .
Nka Delta kuva yaboneka mu mpera za 2020 , imaze kugera mu bihugu birenga 100 birimo na u Rwanda kandi ku wa 11 Kamena 2021 habarwaga ko 90 % bya abanduye mu Bwongereza ari yo bafite ; ubu 51 , 7 % bya abandura muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ni yo basanganwa , mu Bufaransa abandura 50 % ni yo bafite , naho mu Buhinde aho yahereye bivugwa ko 70 %
bya abanduye mu nkundura ya kabiri yahitanaga ibihumbi buri munsi mu ntangiriro za 2021 ari yo basanganywe .
Ni yo ihangayikishije kurusha izindi zose bitewe na uko ikwirakwira bwangu ugereranyije nazo , kandi abarwayi bayo bakaremba mu buryo bwihuse .
Alpha yo imaze kugera mu bihugu bisaga 170 , Beta mu birenga 120 , naho Gamma yagaragaye mu birenga 70 .
Ubwoko bwagaragaye mu duce tumwe na tumwe bukatuzahaza ariko ntibwitwe ko buhangayikishije , burimo Lambda yaturutse muri Peru muri Kanama 2020 .
Habarurwa ko kuva muri Mutarama uyu mwaka 71 % bya abandura Coronavirus muri icyo gihugu ari yo bafite .
Nubwo imaze kugera mu bihugu 29 ndetse ikaba yibasiye Afurika ya Epfo cyane , Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye ryita ku Buzima ( OMS ) riherutse kwemeza ko idahangayikishije .
Abashakashatsi bamwe bagaragaza ko ibaye ikwirakwira vuba bikiyongera ku kuba na inkingo nka CoronaVac rwa Abashinwa [ rwakozwe na Sosiyete yitwa Sinovac Biotech ] zicika intege imbere yayo byatuma mu minsi iri imbere izaba ihangayikishije .
Abandi bemeza ko itazahangayikisha kuko inkingo zakozwe mu buryo bwa mRNA nka Pfizer na Moderna zagaragaje ko zishobora guhangana nayo ndetse bikaba bitarasobanuka neza niba ikwirakwira vuba cyane kuko aho yasanzwe akenshi igaragara ku baba bakoze ingendo zambukiranya imipaka .
Nta bimenyetso byihariye Lambda igira , abayandura na ubundi baba bafite ibirimo guhinda umuriro , inkorora no kudakora neza kwa ibyiyumviro bya ururimi na amazuru .
Ubundi bwoko bufatwa nka ubudahangayikishije ni Epsilon bwagaragaye bwa mbere i California muri Leta zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu mpera za 2020 .
Muri Mutarama 2021 abaganga ba Ibitaro bya Cedars - Sinai biri i Los Angeles batangaje ko 50 % bya abasanganywe icyorezo muri uko kwezi bari baranduye Epsilon , naho muri Gashyantare 16 % bya ubwandu bushya muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika bwari ubwayo .
Byatumye Ikigo gishinzwe Kurwanya Indwara ( CDC ) muri icyo gihugu kiyishyira mu zihangayikishije , ariko bigeze muri Kamena iboneka kuri 1 % bya abayanduye gusa bituma noneho ifatwa nka idakanganye .
Ikigo gishinzwe Kurwanya Indwara mu Burayi nacyo cyemeje ko Epsilon idakwiye kongerwa ku zihangayikishije kuko itagiye iboneka ku migabane yose mu buryo busanzwe nka izindi , ahubwo aho igaragara hamwe na hamwe iba yahagejejwe na abahakoreye ingendo .
Inyigo ya Kaminuza ya Washington yerekanye ko Epsilon ifite uburyo butatu yihinduranyamo ( mutations ) , ku buryo ubudahangarwa umubiri uba warakuye ku rukingo rwa COVID - 19 cyangwa wararemye nyuma yo kuyikira , bugabanukaho inshuro ziri hagati ya ebyiri na eshatu na igice mu gihe ubwo bwoko bugeze mu mubiri .
Kubera ko ubukana yari ifite ikigaragara bwagabanutse ndetse ikaba itarakwirakwira mu bihugu byinshi ku Isi , abashakashatsi bavuga ko idakwiye guhangayikisha .
Abarenga miliyoni 186 , 4 ni bo bamaze kwandura Coronavirus mu Isi yose , aho muri bo abasaga miliyoni 170 , 5 bayikize , naho abarenga miliyoni enye ikaba imaze kubahitana .
Kugaruza inguzanyo zatanzwe muri VUP byabaye agatereranzamba .
Ibi byagaragajwe na Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Imari ya Leta muri raporo ye avuga ko hari gahunda yo kugaruza inguzanyo yatanzwe mu gihe cya imyaka 11 ishize ariko inzego za ibanze zikaba zitarigeze zikora raporo ku mafaranga yabasha kugaruzwa cyangwa uburyo azagaruzwa .
Gahunda ya VUP yatangijwe mu 2008 ifite intumbero yo guhangana na ubukene no kwivana mu bukene nka imwe mu nkingi za Umuryango wa Abibumbye zigamije iterambere rirambye yo kurandura ubukene bukabije mu 2030 ariko u Rwanda rwifuzaga kubigeraho mbere ya imyaka icumi na ubwo bitagezwe .
Kuba hatabaho uburyo buhamye bwo kugaruza ayo mafaranga bituma atagera ku bagenerwabikorwa benshi ngo bikure mu bukene .
Muri gahunda ya VUP amafaranga yatangwaga mu byiciro bitatu bitandukanye birimo abashoboye gukora bahabwaga imirimo , inguzanyo zo gutangiza imishinga mito mu rwego rwo kwiteza imbere na amafaranga yahabwaga abageze mu za bukuru ( inkunga ya ingoboka ) batagishoboye gukora agamije kubafasha kubaho mu buzima bwa buri munsi .
Ibi ariko ntituri bubitindeho , reka twigarukire ku cyiciro cyo gukoresha abaturage bari hagati ya imyaka 18 na 65 bari bagize 40 % bya abaturage bashoboraga gukora muri icyo gihe ndetse bamwe muri bo bagahabwa na inguzanyo ngo bitangirire imishinga .
Mu gutanga izi nguzanyo hibandwaga cyane ku bakorera mu makoperative kugira ngo bahuze imbaraga bazamurane , mu bihe bitandukanye hagiye hakorwa igenzura bagasanga amwe mu makoperative yari baringa , yarashinzwe agamije kurigisa amafaranga yagenewe kuzamura ubukungu bwa igihugu .
Muri raporo ya Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Imari ya Leta ya 2019 / 20 , yerekana neza ko amafaranga 5 794 922 324 Frw yatanzwe nka inguzanyo zo guteza imbere Abanyarwanda kugeza muri Kamena 2020 hari hamaze kugaruzwa 390 947 193 Frw bingana 8 % bya ayatanzwe gusa .
Nyamara muri icyo gihe cyose cya imyaka isaga 11 ishize nta raporo igaragaza ashobora kugaruzwa na atagaruzwa , bigatuma habaho kudindira .
Ikigo cya Igihugu gishinzwe guteza imbere ibikorwa bya iterambere mu nzego za ibanze , LODA , gifite mu nshingano zacyo gukurikirana ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya gahunda yo kwihutisha iterambere , gahunda mbaturabukungu EDPRS na VUP ntikigeze kigaragaza uburyo bwo kugaruza ayo mafaranga angana na 82 % bya ayatanzwe .
Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Imari ya Leta yasabye LODA gufatanya na inzego za uturere hagakorwa raporo igaragaza amafaranga yagarujwe na ataragaruzwa kandi bagashyira imbaraga mu kugaruza ayo babona ba nyiri kuyatwara bafitiye ubushobozi bwo kuzishyura .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Umuyobozi Mukuru wa LODA , Nyinawagaga Claudine Marie Solange , yavuze ko impamvu amafaranga atagarujwe ku gihe byatewe na amakosa aba mu itangwa rya izo nguzanyo na imbogamizi zo kuba amakuru ajyanye nazo yarabikwaga mu makayi .
Ati " " " " Kubera ko zimaze igihe kinini , inyinshi zatanzwe tudafite uburyo bwa ikoranabuhanga bwo gutanga amakuru bityo ugasanga hari nka umuntu wimutse dufite amazina naho atuye ariko tudafite indangamuntu kuko ni inguzanyo zatanzwe mu mwaka wa ingengo ya imari ya 2008 / 09 , ugasanga inguzanyo zirandikwa mu makayi ariko ugasanga nta ndangamuntu yewe
harimo na abari batarabona telefoni icyo gihe . " " " "
Yavuze ko kandi impamvu zo gutinda kwishyura aho baboneye uburyo bwa ikoranabuhanga , hari aho baburaga amakuru yuzuye kuri wa muntu watwaye inguzanyo .
Ati " " " " Ikibazo cya mbere byari ukumenya amakuru ku bimutse aho bari batuye , amakuru ku bitabye Imana ndetse na imishinga imwe na imwe yagiye ihomba cyane bitewe na amapfa na ibindi bibazo ugasanga umuturage yari asanzwe afite amikoro make , inguzanyo yayihawe ngo yiteze imbere ariko yagize ikibazo arahomba . " " " "
Yavuze ko hari gahunda yo gukusanya amakuru bagamije kumenya umuntu wese utarishyura inguzanyo ufite ubushobozi , kumenya uwaba yarapfuye atishyuye , hagamijwe gusobanura amafaranga ashobora kugaruzwa na atagaruzwa .
Ku bazasangwa bafite ubushobozi biteganyijwe ko bazagirana amasezerano mashya agenga imyishyurire ku buryo nyuma ya umwaka umwe gusa ni ukuvuga ko mu mwaka wa 2022 amafaranga ashobora kugaruzwa azaba yaragarujwe .
Uyu muyobozi yagaragaje ko muri ibi bihe , izi nguzanyo zisigaye zitangwa mu buryo bwizewe kuko zinyuzwa muri Koperative Umurenge SACCO ziri mu mirenge ndetse hanashyizweho abantu bashinzwe gukurikirana ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya imishinga yakirwa inguzanyo .
Gutinda kwishyurwa ku bakoze imirimo
Uretse ibibazo byo kudakurikirana amafaranga yatanzwe nka inguzanyo , muri VUP , hakunze kuvugwa no kutishyura abakozi ku gihe , ibintu byabakomaga mu nkokora mu kwiteza imbere kabone na ubwo bakoraga ariko hari abagorwaga no kwibeshaho .
Ubusanzwe muri iyi gahunda byari biteganyijwe ko abakozi bagomba guhembwa nibura nyuma ya iminsi cumi na itanu ariko si ko byagendaga kuko wasangaga abaturage babogoza kugira ngo bishyurwe .
Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Imari ya Leta yagaragaje ko mu turere turindwi habayeho gukererwa kwishyura abakozi amafaranga angana na miliyoni 142 , 3 Frw kandi ubwo bukererwe bwari butwaye iminsi 309 bingana na amezi 10 abantu bakoze batarahembwa kandi ariho bari bategeye .
Nko mu 2018 hagaragajwe ko abakoze muri gahunda za VUP hishyuwe miliyoni 975 , 5 Frw nyuma ya ubukererwe bwa iminsi 187 .
Nyinawagaga yabwiye IGIHE ko ibibazo byo gutinda kwishyura abakozi kuri ubu byamaze gushakirwa umuti ariko nabyo byaterwaga ahanini na uburyo amakuru ya abakozi yatangwagamo .
Ati " " " " Twaricaye tubanza kureba ngo byaraterwaga na iki , dusanga ari uko wasangaga abaturage barakoze ariko lisite zihemba zikozwe impitagihe , aho twashyizeho uburyo bwo kuzikora mu buryo bwihuse , icya kabiri wasangaga iyo amafaranga yageraga ku karere rimwe na rimwe nta guhana amakuru hagati ya Umunyamabanga
Nshingwabikorwa wa Akarere na Umuyobozi ushinzwe imibereho myiza , ikindi cyagararaye ni uko hari na aho uturere twoherezaga amafaranga kuri SACCO nazo zikaryama . " " " "
Umugenzuzi Mukuru wa Imari ya Leta yasabye ko mu kugera ku iterambere ryifuzwa , Minisiteri ya Ubutegetsi bwa Igihugu , MINALOC , LODA na inzego za Intara bakwiye gutekereza umushinga ari uko uturere twerekanye ko twateguye na uburyo butarambiranye bwo kwishyura abakoze imirimo kuko akenshi ariho baba bateze amaramuko .

" " " " Ndabona hano ari abantu bake bambaye udupfukamunwa kandi nabo batwambaye nabi kuko bapfutse umunwa gusa amazuru yabo bayasiga agaragara .
Ku bwa iyo mpamvu rero ndasaba buri wese uri hano gukurikiza amabwiriza yose yo kwirinda Coronavirus nka uko tubisabwa na inzobere mu buzima . " " " "
Perezida Suluhu avuze ibi mu gihe hari hashize igihe gito yeruye agatangaza ko noneho muri Tanzania hari abarwayi ba Covid - 19 mu gihe iki gihugu cyaherukaga kubitangaza muri Gicurasi 2020 .

Afurika ya Epfo : Urukiko rwateye utwatsi icyifuzo cya Zuma cyo gusubika igifungo .
Kugeza ubu Zuma afunzwe nyuma ya aho Urukiko rwa Ikirenga rumukatiye gufungwa amezi 15 azira kwanga kwitaba Komisiyo Ishinzwe Kugenzura Ibyaha bya Ruswa byaranze ingoma ye kuva mu 2009 kugeza mu 2018 , ubwo yamukoragaho iperereza .
Nubwo yishyikirije polisi mu ijoro ryo ku wa Gatatu , Zuma ntabwo yemera igihano yakatiwe .
Yatanze ubusabe bwo kurekurwa biteganyijwe ko buzasuzumwa na Urukiko Rushinzwe Itegeko Nshinga , ku wa Mbere wa icyumweru gitaha .
Hagati aho ariko Umucamanza mu Rukiko Rukuru rwa Pietermaritzburg ukurikirana urubanza rwa Zuma , yamaganye ubu busabe .
Bamwe mu bashyigikiye Zuma bigaragambije mu bice bitandukanye byo mu Ntara ya KwaZulu - Natal atuyemo batwika amapine mu mihanda , bamagana ifungwa rye .
Jacob Zuma ashinjwa kuba yaremereye bamwe mu bagize ikigo cya Gupta afitemo inyungu , kugira uruhare mu byemezo yafashe birimo ibirebana na amasezerano akomeye ya ubucuruzi ndetse na ibyo gushyira abaminisitiri mu myanya .

Uganda : Perezida Museveni yasabye inzego za umutekano guhigisha uruhindu abakwirakwiza ko yapfuye .
Ku wa 26 Kamena 2021 ni bwo ku mbuga nkoranyambaga hatangiye gucicikana amakuru ko Perezida Museveni yapfuye , ababisakaje bagasobanura ko ngo yazize indwara za ubuhumekero zifitanye isano na COVID - 19 .
Nyuma ya aho yagiye agaragara mu ruhame ariko aho ageze " " " " abaturage bakagwa mu kantu " " " " kuko abenshi babaga bazi ko yapfuye .
Ibyo bihuha ngo byakomeje gukwirakwizwa cyane na abantu bifashisha imbuga zitandukanye zirimo na Facebook ariko bagahisha imyirondoro yabo nyayo nka uko Dail Monitor yabitangaje .
Kuko imbuga nkoranyambaga muri icyo gihugu zifunzwe kuva mu minsi ya amatora yabaye mu ntangiriro za uyu mwaka , abaturage benshi basigaye bizera ibihuha kurusha amakuru ya nyayo bya umwihariko iyo babibonye ku mbuga nkoranyambaga .
Ubwo yari mu muhango wa irahira rya abaminisitiri kuri uyu wa Kane tariki 8 Nyakanga 2021 , Perezida Museveni yavuganye umujinya uko yageze i Bombo mu Karere ka Luweero abaturage bakikanga kuko bari bazi ko yapfuye .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Nka uko mubizi imbuga nkoranyambaga ziravuga ko Museveni yapfuye .
[ Abashinzwe umutekano ] bakwiye kugaragaza uwazanye iyo nkuru vuba na bwangu . " " " "
Yahize ko na we ubwe ari bufashe abashinzwe umutekano gushakisha isoko ya ibyo bihuha , ati " " " " Nkeneye gufatanya nabo tukakugeraho .
Waba uri mu Burayi , turakwihannye tukubwira ngo ujye mu kuzimu kuko urimo gutakaza igihe cya abantu . " " " "
Perezida Museveni ayoboye manda ye ya Gatandatu kuva mu 1986 .
Ni manda itaravuzweho rumwe kuko amatora yatsindiyemo Robert Kyagulanyi ( Bobi Wine ) bari bahanganye bikomeye yavuzwemo ubujura bwa amajwi no guhohotera bamwe mu baturage bigatuma badatora , mu gihe hari na site za itora zabuzeho ibikoresho ahandi udusanduku twa amajwi tukaburirwa irengero .
Yabonye intsinzi ku majwi 58 , 64 % , Bobi Wine agira 34 , 83 % .
