Uganda : Bapfumuwe ibirenge , imigongo ihindurwa ibisebe - Iyicarubozo ryakorewe abakekwaho kurasa Gen Katumba .
Abagabo bakekwaho kurasa imodoka ya Minisitiri wa Umurimo na Ubwikorezi muri Uganda , Gen Edward Katumba Wamala , bagahitana umukobwa we na umushoferi beretse itangazamakuru iyicarubozo bakorewe , ubwo bavaga mu rukiko rwa ibanze rwa Nakawa nyuma ya iminsi irindwi batawe muri yombi .
Aba bagabo bashinjwa kugaba igitero ku modoka ya Gen Katumba ku itariki ya 1 Kamena 2021 , gihitana umukobwa we Brenda Nantongo Katumba wari umaze igihe gito avuye kwiga muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Tariki ya 1 Nyakanga 2021 , Polisi ya Uganda yatangaje ko yafashe abagabo bakekwaho uruhare muri icyo gikorwa , ariko babiri muri bo baraswa bashaka gutoroka barapfa .
Mu batawe muri yombi benshi bitwaga amazina atari ayabo , aho harimo uwitwa Kamada Walusimbi wiyitaga Mudinka , Hussein Wahab Lubwama bakunze kwita Master , Siriman Kisambira uzwi ku izina rya Mukwasi , Mustafa Kawawa Ramadan witwaga Amin , Muhammad Kagugube witwaga Bafumoya .
Abishwe ni uwitwa Lubwama na Kawawa
Ubwo bari bajyanwe kuburanishwa ku rukiko rwa ibanze rwa Nakawa , beretse itangazamakuru iyicarubozo bakorewe ubwo umucamanza , Douglas Singiza yari afashe akaruhuko .
Bamwe muri bo barakubiswe mu mugongo igera ubwo ihinduka ibisebe , abandi bapfumurwa ibirenge ndetse na iyo ubireba ubona ko bitarakira , abandi amaguru yaratobowe bigaragara ko bakorewe iyicarubozo koko .
Mu gihe urubanza rwabo rukiri kuburanishwa , bamwe muri aba bagabo barakwekaho kuba barakoze ibindi byaha mu bihe bitandukanye , harimo kuba baragize uruhare mu iyicwa rya Maj Muhammed Kiggundu muri Gashyantare 2021 , kuba barakoze ubujura bwa ibikoresho bya ikoranabuhanga mu gace ka Nansana mu 2019 ndetse no kwica abapolisi batatu mu bihe bitandukanye
bakabiba imbunda .
Polisi yavuze ko bazakorerwa dosiye ya ibi byaha byose bakabiburana icya rimwe mu rukiko .
Aba bagabo babyeretse itangazamakuru ubwo umucamanza yari asohotse agiye gufata akaruhuko
Bamwe imigongo yabaye ibisebe kubera inkoni
Amaguru ya bamwe yarapfumaguwe
Uyu yitabye urukiko ikirenge cye bigaragara ko cyapfumuwe
Babiri mu bafashwe bararashwe baricwa , polisi ivuga ko bashakaga gutoroka / Ifoto : Kampala Dispatch
Brenda Katumba yifotozanya na Papa we mbere gato ya uko bagabwaho igitero cyamuhitanye
Haiti yasabye ububasha bwa amahanga , u Bufaransa bugiye kuvana ingabo muri Sahel , Biden yihanije Putin ; Avugwa mu mahanga
Ubu busabe buje nyuma ya uko Perezida Jovenel Moïse arashwe amasasu 12 asanzwe iwe mu rugo , Polisi ikaba ikomeje gushaka abantu umunani bari mu gitero cyahitanye Perezida , mu gihe abandi 17 bafashwe naho batatu bakicwa .
Amerika yatangaje ko itahita ifata icyemezo cyo kohereza ingabo zayo muri Haiti , ariko yamaze koherereza abakozi ba Urwego rwa Iperereza ( FBI ) kugira ngo bafashe mu iperereza .
Iperereza rya ibanze ryerekanye ko bamwe mu bafashwe bari bafite ibikoresho biriho amashusho yerekana uko mu rugo rwa Perezida hameze , abandi bafatanywe intwaro mu gihe abandi bafatanywe ibikoresho bya Perezida bari bibye .
Biden yongeye kwihanangiriza Putin ku bitero bya ikoranabuhanga bigabwa kuri Amerika
Mu kiganiro cyamaze isaha kuri telefoni , Perezida Joe Biden wa Amerika yavuze ko yongeye kubwira Vladimir Putin wa u Burusiya ku ngamba igihugu cye kizafatirwa nigikomeza kwemerera abajura mu bya ikoranabuhanga , kugaba ibitero kuri Amerika .
Ibitero bya ikorabuhanga bikomeje gukaza umurego muri Amerika kuko mu kwezi gushize ibigo birenga 1 . 500 byagabweho ibitero biturutse mu Burusiya .
Iki kibazo cyari mu byaganiriweho mu nama iherutse guhuza Biden na Putin mu Busuwisi mu kwezi gushize , aho Biden yahaye Putin urutonde rwa inzego 16 zitagomba kugabwaho ibitero biturutse mu Burusiya , kuko nibikorwa Amerika izihorera mu buryo bukomeye .
Hagati aho , impande zimbi zikomeje kwitana ba mwana kuko Amerika ivuga ko yegereye u Burusiya inshuro nyinshi ibasaba kurangiza iki kibazo ariko bukanga , mu gihe u Burusiya buvuga ko butigeze bwegerwa na Amerika kuri iyi ngingo .
Biden yahagurukiye ibigo bya ikoranabuhanga muri Amerika
Joe Biden yasinye itegeko rigizwe na ingingo 72 rizashyirwa mu bikorwa na ibigo bya Leta 10 , rigamije gukumira ko ibigo bikomeye mu bya ikoranabuhanga muri Amerika , bikoresha ubushobozi bwabyo mu gusenya no kugura ibigo bito , ndetse no gukoresha amakuru ya abantu mu buryo bunyuranyije na amategeko .
Iri tegeko rije nyuma ya uko Abanyamerika banenze ibigo bikomeye bya ikoranabuhanga birimo Facebook , Amazon na Google , byakunze kugura ibigo bito bitanga serivise zimwe nka iby izitangwa na ibyo bigo , mu rwego rwo kugabanya ihangana ku isoko bityo bigakomeza kubyikubira .
Ibi bigo kandi bikomeje gushinjwa gutwara amakuru menshi ya abakiliya babyo , ku buryo iri tegeko ryashyizweho na Amerika rizagena uburyo akoreshwamo , uretse ko zimwe mu ngingo zirigize zishobora kuzajyanwa mu nkiko .
U Bufaransa bugiye kugabanya ingabo bufite mu gace ka Sahel
Perezida Emmanuel Macron wa u Bufaransa yatangaje ko igihugu cye kigiye kugabanya ingabo cyari gifite mu gace ka Sahel , mu rwego rwo kuvugurura uruhare rwa izo ngabo mu kubaka umutekano urambye .
Mu mezi atandatu ari imbere , u Bufaransa buzagabanya ingabo 2 . 000 mu 5 . 100 zari mu mutwe wa Barkhane zimaze imyaka umunani zirinda umutekano mu bihugu birimo Mali , Tchad , Niger , Burkina Faso na Mauritania .
Perezida Macron yavuze ko kugabanya izo ngabo bitavuze ko u Bufaransa butereranye ibyo bihugu bihanganye na imitwe ya iterabwoba ishamikiye kuri ISIS na Al Qaeda .
Ingabo za u Bufaransa zigiye gushyira imbaraga mu bijyanye no kurwanya iyo mitwe mbere ya uko zihindura uburyo bwa imirwanire , zikazajya zibanda cyane ku kurinda umutekano ku mipaka ihuza ibyo bihugu .
Temitope Balogun Joshua uzwi nka TB Joshua , yashyinguwe nyuma ya ukwezi kurenga yitabye Imana , nyuma ya uburwayi bwa igihe gito yagize .
Nka uko byari byetezwe , ishyingurwa rya TB Joshua ryitabiriwe na abantu benshi barimo na abaturutse mu mpande zitandukanye za Isi , uyu mugabo wa imyaka 57 wafatwaga " " " " nka Intumwa ya Imana " " " " asoza urugendo rwe rwa ubuzima .
TB Joshua ni umwe mu bavugabutumwa bari bakomeye muri Afurika , aho yabarirwaga umutungo uri hagati ya miliyoni 10 $ na 15 $ , urusengero rwe rwahoraga rwuzuyemo abantu bifuza gukorerwa ibitangaza birimo ibyo gukira indwara zirimo SIDA na izindi zikomeye nka cancer .
Mu munsi ishize ariko yari amaze iminsi ari mu nkiko nyuma ya uko urusengero rwe rugwiriye abantu barenga 100 bakitaba Imana , ndetse YouTube ikaba yari iherutse gusiba shene ye yakurikirwaga na abarenga miliyoni , kubera amakuru bise ibinyoma yanyuzwaga kuri uwo murongo .
OMS yaburiye Afurika ku bwiyongere bukabije bwa Covid - 19
Umuyobozi wa Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye ryita ku Buzima muri Afurika , Dr Matshidiso Moeti , yavuze ko Afurika ifite ibyago byinshi bya ubwiyongere budasanzwe bwa icyorezo cya Covid - 19 nyuma ya uko ikomeje kubura inkingo zo gukingira icyo cyorezo .
Afurika imaze kubona inkingo zingana na 2 % bya izikenewe , nyamara ubwiyongere bwa Covid - 19 buri kwikuba kabiri buri minsi 18 , bwarahoze bwikuba kabiri mu minsi 21 .
OMS ivuga ko inkingo miliyoni 20 zatanzwe na Amerika zikazagabanywa ibihugu 49 ari intambwe nziza ndetse ziri mu nzira , ariko zidahagije ku buryo Afurika yakwizera ko ubwiyongere buzagabanuka mu buryo bworoshye , usaba ko ibihugu bifite inkingo bitaratanga byakwihutisha iyo gahunda .
Abarenga miliyoni 5 . 7 bamaze kwandura Covid - 19 muri Afurika , mu gihe abarenga 147 bamaze kwicwa na icyo cyorezo , , uretse ko imibare nyakuri ya uburyo iki cyorezo gihagaze ishobora kuba iri hejuru cyane ya itangazwa .
Tanzania igiye kwakira gari ya moshi ya mbere ikoresha amashanyarazi
Leta ya Tanzania yahaye amasezerano ikigo cya Hyundai Rotem afite agaciro ka miliyoni 296 $ , azatuma gishyira gari ya moshi zikoresha amashanyarazi mu mijyi itandukanye ya icyo gihugu .
Tanzania ifite gahunda yo kuvugurura imihanda yayo ya gari ya moshi , igasanwa ndetse ikanavugururwa ku buryo ikoresha amashanyarazi , ibizatuma gari ya moshi zihuta ku muvuduko wa kirometero 160 ku isaha ( 160km / h ) , zivuye kuwa kirometero 40 zigenderaho ku isaha ( 40km / h ) .
Byitezwe ko uyu mushinga uzatangira gushyirwa mu bikorwa mu mwaka wa 2024 , ndetse ukazaba ubaye uwa mbere wa gari ya moshi zikoresha amashanyarazi , ariko ibikorwa byo kuvugurura inzira zazo bizakomeza mu myaka iri imbere , aho byagenewe ingengo ya imari ya miliyari 6 . 9 $ .
U Rwanda rwashyizwe mu bihugu byagejeje umuriro wa amashanyarazi ku baturage benshi .
Iyi Raporo yakozwe na ibigo bitandukanye birimo Banki ya Isi , Ikigo Mpuzamahanga cyita ku Ngufu ( IEA ) , Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye rishinzwe ibarurishamibare , UNSD , iryita ku Buzima , OMS , ndetse na Ikigo Mpuzamahanga cyita ku Ngufu za imirasire , IRENA , hagamijwe kureba aho Isi igeze mu kugeza
abaturage ku ntego ya 7 ya iterambere rirambye , SDG7 , yo kugeza umuriro wa amashanyarazi ku batuye Isi bose bitarenze 2030 .
U Rwanda rwashyizwe mu bihugu byabashije kugeza umuriro ku baturage benshi ugereranyije na ubwiyongere bwabo buri mwaka , aho mu 2019 rwagejeje umuriro ku baturarwanda ku rugero rwa 38 % ruvuye kuri 35 % rwari rufite mu 2018 .
Yagize iti " " " " Hagati ya 2010 na 2019 , kimwe cya kabiri cya ibihugu 20 bifite umuriro wa amashanyarazi muke byabashije kuwongera buri mwaka ku rugero rurenze uruba ruteganyijwe ku Isi .
Naho kuva mu 2017 kugeza mu 2019 , ibihugu birimo u Rwanda , Uganda Tanzania , Liberia , Guinea - Bissau na Guinea byongereye umuriro ku rugero ruruta urwa ubwiyongere bwa abaturage . " " " "
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda abaturage bafite umuriro wa amashanyarazi bangana na 65 % , muri bo 17 , 8 % bakaba bakoresha umuriro ukomoka ku mirasire ya izuba .
U Rwanda rwihaye intego ko mu 2024 , buri muturarwanda azaba ashobora gukoresha amashanyarazi yaba afatiye ku muyoboro mugari cyangwa izindi ngufu ( amashanyarazi akomoka ku mirasire ya izuba , nyiramugengeri , gaz methane iri mu Kiyaga cya Kivu na ibindi )
Mu kubigeraho , hashyizwe ingufu nyinshi mu gushyira mu bikorwa ingamba zigamije kongera umuriro nubwo zagiye zikomwa mu nkokora na icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Harimo ishyirwa mu bikorwa rya imishinga yagutse izatuma igihugu kirushaho kwihaza mu mashyanyarazi .
Muri yo harimo uruganda rwa Hakan Peat to Power rugiye gutangira gutanga amashanyarazi akomoka kuri Nyiramugengeri ruherereye mu Murenge wa Mamba mu Karere ka Gisagara aho mu cyiciro cyarwo cya mbere ruzajya rutanga Megawati 40 ndetse biteganyijwe ko nirumara kuzura neza ruzajya rutanga Megawatt 70 .
Hari kandi na umushinga wa inganda zo ku rwego rwa Akarere zirimo urwa Rusumo ruhuriweho na u Rwanda , Burundi na Tanzania , uzatanga Megawatt 80 , u Rwanda rukabonaho Megawatt 27 .
Umushinga wa Rusizi III nawo uri mu izatanga umuriro wa amashanyarazi , akaba ari umushinga u Rwanda ruhuriweho na Repubulika iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo na u Burundi , ukazatanga Megawatt 200 , u Rwanda rukazabonaho Megawatt 67 .
Raporo ya Energy Progress Report yerekanye ko kandi u Rwanda rufite umushinga rwatangiye mu 2019 , wo guha abaturage umuriro wa amashanyarazi akomoka ku mirasire ya izuba uzatwara miliyoni 45 $ .
Mu 2000 abari bafite umuriro wa amashanyarazi bari 2 % , mu mwaka wa 2010 bageze ku 9 % , muri uyu mwaka abagerwaho n " " " " amashanyarazi ni 65 % .
Uyu mwaka wa 2021 uzarangira bangana na 71 % .
Biteganyijwe ko bazaba ari 100 % mu 2024 .
Ibyo kumenya ku kibazo cya iterabwoba muri Mozambique cyahagurukije u Rwanda .
Ni ikibazo cyashituye amahanga guhera muri Werurwe uyu mwaka , ubwo izo nyeshyamba ziyitiriye umutwe wa Al Shabab nubwo ntaho bihuriye , zagabaga ibitero mu Mujyi wa Palma zigahitana ubuzima bwa abasaga 12 bishwe bunyamaswa , mu gihe ibihumbi bya abaturage bavuye mu byabo .
Ingabo na Abapolisi ba u Rwanda bagiye muri Mozambique mbere ho icyumweru ngo hagere iza umuryango wa ibihugu byo mu Majyepfo ya Afurika ( SADC ) zo zitezweho kuhagera kuwa 15 Nyakanga 2021 .
Inshingano ni ugufasha iza Mozambique guhashya ibikorwa bya iterabwoba na ubugizi bwa nabi mu ntara ya Cabo Delgado .
Uyu mwanzuro ugezweho nyuma ya uruzinduko Perezida Filipe Nyusi yagiriye mu Rwanda muri Mata uyu mwaka , akaganira na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Hari amakuru ya uko Nyusi akiva mu Rwanda , hari itsinda rya abashinzwe umutekano ba u Rwanda bakoreye ingendo muri Cabo Delgado bashaka kumenya neza uko ikibazo giteye .
Igihugu gikungahaye ariko kimaze igihe mu bibazo
Mozambique ni igihugu giherereye mu Majyepfo ashyira Uburasirazuba bwa Afurika gifite ubuso bungana na kilometero kare 801 . 590 , gikubye u Rwanda inshuro 30 .
Gituwe na abasaga miliyoni 31 aho icyizere cyo kubaho kiri ku myaka 56 .
Umuturage wacyo umwe abarirwa amadolari 1200 ku mwaka , ni ukuvuga hafi miliyon 1 , 2 Frw .
Iki gihugu gihana imbibi na ibindi bitandatu birimo na Tanzania mu Majyaruguru .
Gikungahaye ku mutungo kamere urimo amabuye ya agaciro na gaz .
Kuba ari igihugu gikora ku nyanja , bigiha amahirwe ya ubucuruzi bukorerwa mu Nyanja ya Abahinde .
Nubwo ari igihugu gifite umutungo , cyakunze guhura na ibibazo bya umutekano na politiki guhera mu 1975 ubwo cyabonaga ubwigenge .
Umutwe wa Renamo utavuga rumwe na ishyaka Frelimo riri ku butegetsi wakunze gushoza intambara kenshi , gusa Leta ikihagararaho .
Kuri ubu impande zombi ziri mu gahenge nyuma yo gusinya amasezerano ya amahoro mu 2019 .
Nubwo umwanzi wa igihe kirekire Mozambique yamuciye intege , mu 2017 havutse undi ufite ingufu zidasanzwe .
Mu ntara ya Cabo Delgado hadutse umutwe wa iterabwoba wiyise al shabab , nubwo nta mikoranire ufitanye na Al Shabab ya nyayo .
Uwo mutwe watangiye ari inyeshyamba zisanzwe ariko uko iminsi yicuma wagiye ugirana umubano na imitwe ya iterabwoba mpuzamahanga nka IS yo muri Syria na Iraq .
Ibitero uwo mutwe wagiye ugaba mu Majyaruguru ya Mozambique , wagiye wica abaturage bunyamaswa , ubaciye imitwe nka uko IS ibigenza .
Kugeza muri Mata uyu mwaka , abaturage basaga 3000 bari bamaze kwicwa bunyamaswa mu gihe abasaga ibihumbi 800 bavuye mu byabo .
Umutwe wavutse mu burakari bwa abaturage
Uyu mutwe wakomotse ku burakari bwa abaturage bari bamaze igihe binubira guhezwa no kutitabwaho na Guverinoma , nubwo batuye mu gace kinjiriza Leta akayabo .
Intara ya Cabo Delgado iherereye mu bilometero 1600 uvuye mu Murwa Mukuru Maputo , ikagira ubuso bwa kilometero kare 82 . 625 , bivuze ko ikubye gatatu ubuso bwa u Rwanda .
Ni agace gatuwe na abasaga miliyoni ebyiri .
Iyo ntara ikora kuri Tanzania , ikagira imijyi itatu ikomeye irimo Pemba , Montepuez na Mocimboa da Praia .
Uyu wa nyuma ni nawo inyeshyamba zimaze umwaka zigaruriye ku buryo ingabo za Leta zananiwe kubatsimbura .
Kubera gaz nyinshi iboneka muri Cabo Delgado , sosiyete ya Abafaransa Total niyo yahawe ikiraka cyo kuyicukura mu mushinga uzwi nka Liquid Natural Gas ( LNG ) .
Ni wo mushinga nka uwo ufite agaciro kanini muri Afurika kuko ubarirwa miliyari 60 za amadolari .
Abaturage batangiye binubira ko amafaranga ava muri iyo mishinga ikomeye , atagarurwa mu bikorwa remezo na iterambere muri Cabo Delgado , bagafata Leta nka umukoloni ugamije kubanyunyuza gusa .
Abarambiwe bafata intwaro .
Izo nyeshyamba ziyise al Shabab , ijambo rya Icyarabu risobanura " " " " abasore . " " " "
Nubwo biyita izina rya umutwe wa iterabwoba usanzwe warayogoje amajyaruguru ya Afurika cyane cyane muri Somalia , ntaho bahuriye na mba .
Al Shabab yo muri Mozambique ifitanye umubano na umutwe wa iterabwoba wa IS ukorera muri Iraq na Syria .
Batangiye gukorana na IS mu 2019 , kuva ubwo ufatwa nka ishami ryayo ryo muri Afurika yo hagati , ryiswe Islamic State Central Africa Province ( ISCAP ) .
Ubukana bwawo bwatangiye gushitura amahanga muri Werurwe uyu mwaka ubwo abasaga 12 bicwaga mu gitero cyagabwe mu Mujyi wa Palma .
Mu bishwe harimo na abanyamahanga bituma byinshi mu bikorwa bya amahanga muri ako gace bifunga imiryango harimo na umushinga wa Total .
Kuki ingabo za Leta zitabaje amahanga ?
Inyeshyamba zayogoje Amajyaruguru ya Mozambique zikomeye cyane mu bijyanye na ibikoresho ariko inzobere mu bya gisirikare zivuga ko zifite imyitozo ihagije cyane cyane mu mirwano ibera mu duce twa imijyi dutuwe .
Ni urubyiruko kandi ruterwa akanyabugabo na inyigisho za amahame akaze ya idini ya Islam na ubuhezanguni bigishwa na indi mitwe ya iterabwoba ikomeye ku Isi .
Icyakora , igisirikare cya Mozambique nacyo kivugwaho intege nke haba mu bikoresho no mu bumenyi bwatuma babasha gusubiza inyuma inyeshyamba nka izo , nubwo hari andi makuru avuga ko muri Cabo Delgado Leta itakunze koherezayo abasirikare bafite imyitozo ihagije .
Brigadier Ben Barry wo mu kigo International Institute for Strategic Studies ( IISS ) , yigeze kubwira BBC ko ikindi kigora ingabo za Leta ari amayeri ya inyeshyamba za IS mu kurwanira ahantu hatuye abantu benshi nko mu mijyi , ari nabyo Al Shabab ya Mozambique yatangije mu duce nka Palma na Mocimboa da Praia .
Yagize ati " " " " Kugira ngo utsinde mu ntambara yo mu mujyi bisaba ko ingabo za Guverinoma zigira imyitozo na imiyoborere yo ku rwego rwo hejuru .
Ibyo nibyo bigaragaza intege nke za ingabo za Mozambique .
Bafite ikibazo cyo kutabona abajyanama ba inzobere mu bya gisirikare ndetse na ubushobozi bwo kurwanira mu kirere , intwaro zikomeye na imodoka za intambara . " " " "
Guverinoma ya Mozambique imaze kubona ko yugarijwe , mu mpera za umwaka ushize yahaye ikiraka abajyanama 200 mu bya gisirikare bo mu kigo kigenga cyo mu Burusiya , Wagner Group .
Iyo mikoranire yatangiye muri Nzeri 2020 nyuma yo guhabwa umugisha na Leta ya u Burusiya .
Benshi mu bahawe icyo kiraka , bahoze mu mutwe udasanzwe wa ingabo za u Burusiya .
Ubudahangarwa bari bazanye bwashize ubwo bagabwaho ibitero bitandukanye na inyeshyamba zigahitana bamwe muri bo , biba ngombwa ko babivamo .
Muri Werurwe , igisirikare cya Amerika cyohereje itsinda rya abasirikare bo mu ngabo zidasanzwe bajya gutoza abo muri Mozambique .
Portugal nayo yohereje abasirikare bake bo gutoza ingabo za Leta .
Mu ntangiriro , ntabwo Leta ya Mozambique yifuzaga ingabo za amahanga ku butaka bwayo ariko uko ikibazo cyarushagaho gukomera , byabaye ngombwa ko iva ku izima .
Mu byo yatinyaga mbere , harimo kuba ubusugire bwayo bwavogerwa na ishusho mbi bizayisigira mu mahanga .
Icyakora mu kwezi gushize ubwo igihugu cyizihizaga umunsi wa ubwigenge , Perezida Nyusi yavuze ko ingabo za SADC na iz ibihugu bya inshuti zizabafasha guhashya inyeshyamba , gusa yizeza ko nta kindi bazakora kirenze kubafasha kugarura umutekano muri Cabo Delgado .
Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa SADC , Stergomena Lawrence Tax , aherutse kuvuga ko ingabo zizajya muri Mozambique zizaba zifite inshingano zo kubungabunga amahiro na umutekano , kurinda abaturage .
Kuwa Gatatu tariki 7 Nyakanga , Tax yandikiye Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa Loni , Antonio Guterres amumenyesha ibya ingabo za SADC zigiye gufasha iza Mozambique guhangana na imitwe ya iterabwoba .
Tax yavuze ko izo ngabo zizatangira imirimo yazo tariki 15 Nyakanga zikahamara amezi atatu ashobora kongerwa bitewe na uko ibintu bizaba byifashe .
Ntabwo umubare wa ingabo zizoherezwa na ibihugu bya SADC bizabohereza biramenyekana , gusa muri Mata hari raporo ya impuguke za uwo muryango yagiye hanze , igaragaza ko hakenewe ingabo 3000 zo kohereza muri Cabo Delgado .
Izo ngabo zizaba zifite inshingano zo gufasha Mozambique kurwanya iterabwoba na ibikorwa bya ubuhezanguni muri iyo ntara .
Tariki 28 Kamena , Inama ya Abaminisitiri ya SADC yemeje ingengo ya imari ya miliyari 12 za amadolari azakoreshwa na Umutwe wa ingabo zidasanzwe za uwo muryango muri Mozambique .
Ayo mafaranga bavuze ko agomba kuboneka bitarenze tariki 9 Nyakanga 2021 .
Raporo ya impuguke za SADC zabanje kujya gukora isesengura muri Cabo Delgado , yagaragaje ko kugira ngo Mozambique ibashe gutsinda intambara zisubirane umujyi wa Macimboa da Praia , bakeneye ibikoresho , ubutasi bukomeye na ingabo zihagije .
Iyo raporo yavuze ko hakenewe ingabo zo mu mutwe udasanzwe zihangana na ibitero bya inyeshyamba zinjirira mu nyanja ya Abahinde , ubwato bugendera munsi ya amazi , ingabo zirwanira mu kirere , kajugujugu esheshatu za intambara , indege enye zitwara ibikoresho , ubwato bubiri bushinzwe gucunga na drones ebyiri za ubutasi .
Ntabwo Mozambique iratangaza uburyo izo ngabo za SADC zizakorana na izivuye mu bindi bihugu birimo u Rwanda rwamaze kohereza izarwo .
Inshingano zihariye za buri ngabo nazo ntabwo zirashyirwa hanze .
Intambara irenze iya amasasu
Kubera agace intara ya Cabo Delgado iherereyemo no kuba ikora ku nyanja , yakunze kuba icyambu cya ubucuruzi bwa magendu burimo ibiyobyabwenge , icuruzwa rya abantu na ibindi birimo na ingingo za abantu .
Urugero , abantu bishwe muri Palma muri Werurwe uyu mwaka , bagiye bagaragara ingingo zabo zimwe zirimo na imitwe nta yiriho , bigakekwa ko yagiye ijyanwa kugurishwa .
Kubera ko iyo ntara iri kure ya umurwa mukuru no kuba Leta itarakunze kuhitaho cyane , byagiye bituma ruswa iba nyinshi hagati ya abayobozi ba inzego za ibanze na abanyabyaha bakorera muri ako gace ari nabyo byorohereza inyeshyamba .
Icyakora hari abasesenguzi babona ikibazo cya Cabo Delgado nka ikitazakemurwa na intambara kurusha amayeri yo kwigarurira abaturage .
Tekiniki inyeshyamba zo muri Mozambique zikoresha zigaba ibitero , niyo ikoreshwa na IS yo kwica bunyamaswa abasivile .
Ibyo bitandukanye na amayeri nka Al Qaeda ikoresha yo kurobanura ikamenya abo yica na abo itica kuko gukomera kwayo gushingira ku mubano mwiza na abaturage ba agace yagezemo .
Ikigaragaza ko nta mpuhwe inyeshyamba za Mozambique zifitiye abaturage , ni ubugome bakoresha mu kubica kugeza nka aho mu gitero cyo muri Werurwe , bishe umwana wa imyaka 11 bakamwicira mu maso ya nyina .
BBC yatangaje ko byakorohera Leta kumvisha abaturage ububi bwa uwo mutwe ariko ikabijyanisha no kubaha ibyo basabaga ubwo batangiraga kwivumbura .
Ibyo abatuye Cabo Delgado basabaga ni uguhabwa ibikorwa ibikorwa bya iterambere nka amashuri , imihanda , imirimo na ibindi bituma babona ko bitaweho .
Ibyo ngo bizatuma bagarukira Leta .
Urugero rutangwa ni urwo mu 2007 ubwo umutwe wa Al Qaeda wakoraga amakosa utera ubwoba abaturage ba aba - Sunni mu ntara ya Anbar muri Iraq .
Icyo gihe abagabo bo muri ako gace batangiye gutotezwa na inyeshyamba , baba bakoze amakosa yoroheje nko kunywa itabi , bagacibwa intoki .
Byarakaje abaturage , byorohera ingabo za Leta zibifashijwemo na igisirikare cya Amerika kwigarurira imitima ya abaturage .
Byatumye abaturage bahindukirana al Qaeda barayamagana , aho umusirikare wayo anyuze bagatunga agatoki ku buryo uwo mutwe watsinsuwe mu buryo bworoshye .
Huye : Miliyoni 98 Frw zimaze gucibwa abarenze ku mabwiriza yo kwirinda Covid - 19 .
Umuyobozi wa Akarere ka Huye , Sebutege Ange , yavuze ko muri rusange abanye - Huye bubahiriza amabwiriza yashyizweho yo kwirinda Covid - 19 ariko hari abagiye bafatwa bayarenzeho , bahabwa ibihano .
Bose hamwe bamaze gucibwa amande agera kuri miliyoni 98 Frw .
Ati " " " " Kuva Covid - 19 yagera mu Rwanda abarenze ku mabwiriza bamaze gucibwa amande angana na amafaranga miliyoni 98 Frw .
Ayo ni amafaranga baba bakwiye gukoresha mu bibateza imbere ariko kubera kutubahiriza amabwiriza , ibihano bigomba kubaho . " " " "
Sebutege yavuze ko ikigamijwe atari uguhana ahubwo ari ugukangurira abantu kwirinda icyorezo no kubibutsa ko icya mbere ari ukugira ubuzima bwiza .
Yavuze ko kugeza kuri uyu wa Gatatu imibare igaragaza ko abafite ubwandu bwa Covid - 19 mu Karere ka Huye ari abantu 127 naho abo imaze guhitana ari 19 .
Abahanwe ni abafatiwe mu makosa arimo gufungura utubari , gucururiza inzoga muri restaurant bakazihindura utubari , gutinda gutaha ku masaha yagenwe , kwambara nabi agapfukamunwa , gukora ibirori bitemewe , guhindura ingo utubari na andi .
Sebutege yongeye gusaba abaturage gushyira mu bikorwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda icyo cyorezo kuko ari yo ntwaro yonyine ihari muri iki gihe yo kugitsinda .
Kuri ubu mu Karere ka Huye Abajyanama ba Ubuzima bari gusura ingo zose bareba niba hari ufite ibimenyetso bya Covid - 19 kugira ngo yisuzumishe amemye uko ahagaze .
Hafashwe umwanzuro ko urugo rubonetsemo uwanduye , abarubamo bose basabwa kwishyira mu kato kugeza igihe bisuzumishirije .
Abarwariye mu ngo basabwe gukomeza gukurikiza amabwiriza bahawe na muganga , ubuyobozi bubizeza ko abafite ubushobozi budahagije bwo kubaho buzajya bubunganira .
Abaturage bo mu Karere ka Huye babwiye IGIHE ko biyemeje gufatanya na ubuyoboz guhashya Covid - 19 kuko ari icyorezo cyica kandi io hafashwe ingamba zibagiraho ingaruka mbi .
Mukamana Chantal ati " " " " Twabigize ibyacu kuko iki cyorezo gikomeje kwica abantu benshi .
Ubu ntitugikora buri munsi kubera ingamba zafashwe kandi nkatwe ducuruuza tubihomberamo .
Icyo tugomba gukora ni ugukomeza kubabiriza amabwiriza kugira ngo dutsinde Covid - 19 noneho ubuzima bwongere gukomeza nka uko byari bisanzwe mbere . " " " "
Kugeza ubu Umurenge wa Tumba mu Karere ka Huye ni wo ufite abanduye Covid - 19 kuko mu bagera ku 127 abagera kuri 70 ari abawutuyemo .
Huye : Abakobwa babiri bacucuye umugabo bamusindishije .
Abafashwe ni umukobwa wa imyaka 24 , uwa 21 na umusore wa imyaka 27 bafashwe nyuma yo gucyekwaho kwiba amafaranga ya u Rwanda ibihumbi 300 . 000 kuri telefoni umugabo wa imyaka 40 .
Umuvugizi wa Polisi mu Ntara ya Amajyepfo , SP Theobald Kanamugire , yavuze ko abo bantu bacyekwaho icyaha cya ubujura Polisi yabafashe biturutse ku bufatanye na abaturage .
Ati " " " " Tariki ya 24 Kamena [ uwo mugabo ] yagiye mu kabari kakoraga mu buryo butemewe kuko utubari tutemewe muri iki gihe cya COVID - 19 .
Yasanzemo bariya bakobwa babiri basanzwe bagakoramo yaka inzoga zidasembuye ariko bo bamuha inzoga yitwa Bazooka Coffee bamubwira ko idasindisha akomeje kuyinywa aza gusinda . " " " "
SP Kanamugire akomeza avuga ko uwo mugabo amaze gusinda abakobwa bamusabye kwishyura ababwira ko amafaranga ari kuri telefoni mu gihe ari kubishyura umwe abona umubare wa ibanga batangira kumwiba amafaranga yari ariho .
Ati " " " " Yabanje kumwiba telefoni kuko yari yamaze kumenya umubare wa ibanga , yibyeho ibihumbi 50 Frw ahita aha wa mubare wa ibanga mugenzi we nawe akuraho ibihumbi 15 Frw . " " " "
Muri iryo joro haje umusore agiye kunywera muri ako kabari nawe ahabwa umubare wa ibanga .
Yahise amwiba kuri iyo telefoni ibihumbi 160 .
Abakekwa bavuga ko amafaranga bavanye kuri telefoni ari ibihumbi 264 . 500 Frw mu gihe nyirayo we avuga ko hariho ibihumbi 300 . " " " "
SP Kanamugire yavuze ko muri iryo joro yahise yimuka ajya kunywera mu kandi kabari .
Nyuma mu gitondo tariki ya 25 Kamena uwo mugabo akimara kubona ko yibwe amafaranga ye yahise ajya gutanga amakuru kuri Polisi , ba bantu bamaze kumenya ko yabivuze bahita batoroka ariko Polisi ikomeza kubashakisha ifatanyije na abaturage bafatwa ku mugoroba wo kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki ya 06 Nyakanga .
Umuvugizi wa Polisi mu Ntara ya Amajyepfo yaburiye abararikira ibya abandi bakabitwara bakoresheje uburyo ubwo aribwo bwose .
Ati " " " " Abantu bazi ko bashinzwe kwakira umuntu bakamuha serivisi nka uko bikwiye bo bagahitamo no kumwambura ibye bibwira ko ahari uwo babikoreye atabimenya bashatse babicikaho burundu kuko ntibizabahira .
Abantu bakwiye gukora bagashaka ibyabo mu mucyo batambuye cyangwa ngo bararikire ibya abandi . " " " "
Yanibukije kandi abantu ko amabwiriza yo kurwanya Covid - 19 agomba kubahirizwa na buri wese harimo no kumenya ko utabari dufunze .
Nzabarushimana akabari ke karafungwa acibwe na amande kuko yarenze ku mabwiriza yo kwirinda COVID - 19 . Ni mugihe aba batatu bafashwe bashyikirizwa Urwego rwa Igihugu rwa ubugenzacyaha ( RIB ) rukorera kuri Sitasiyo ya Polisi ya Huye .
Itegeko n º 68 / 2018 ryo ku wa 30 / 08 / 2018 riteganya ibyaha na ibihano muri rusange Ingingo ya 166 ivuga ko Umuntu wese uhamijwe na urukiko icyaha cyo kwiba , ahanishwa igifungo kitari munsi ya umwaka umwe ( 1 ) ariko kitarenze imyaka ibiri ( 2 ) , ihazabu ya amafaranga ya u Rwanda atari munsi ya miliyoni imwe ( 1 . 000 . 000
FRW ) ariko atarenze miliyoni ebyiri ( 2 . 000 . 000 FRW ) , imirimo ya inyungu rusange mu gihe cya amezi atandatu ( 6 ) cyangwa kimwe gusa muri ibyo bihano .
Polisi ya u Rwanda ikorera mu Karere ka Huye mu Murenge wa Huye ku bufatanye na abaturage bafashe abantu batatu bari bamaze ibyumweru bibiri bashakishwa bacyekwaho kwiba umuturage amafaranga nyuma yo kumusindisha .
Tariki 08 Nyakanga ni umunsi wa ijana na mirongo cyenda mu minsi igize umwaka , hasigaye iminsi ijana na mirongo irindwi na umunani .
Dore bimwe mu byaranze uyu munsi
1099 : Mu ntambara ya mbere ya amadini , izwi nka Crusade ingaboz " " " " Abakirisitu bagera ku bihumbi cumi na bitanu bakoze imyigaragambyo yo kwiyicisha inzara hafi ya Yeruzalemu , biturutse ku Bayisilamu bari babagose .
1497 : Umushakashatsi Vasco da Gama , ukomoka mu gihugu cya Portugal yatangiye urugendo rwo kwerekaza mu gihugu cya u Buhinde .
1775 : Hashyizwe umukono ku masezerano yiswe Olive Branch Petition hagati ya intumwa zari zihagarariye Leta cumi na eshatu zakoze bwa mbere Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
1776 : Mu rukurikirane rwa Leta ya Philadelphia na Pennsylvania , zatangaje ku mugaragaro ubwigenge bwazo , havuzwa inzogera yiswe iya ubwigenge ( Liberty Bell )
1889 : Hatangiye gusohoka ikinyamakuru cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika cyitwa Wall Street Journal .
1948 : Igisirikare cyirwanira mu kirere cya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ( United States Air Force ) , cyatangiye kwakira abasirikare ba igitsinagore , muri gahunda yiswe Women in the Air Force ( WAF ) .
1970 : Perezida Richard Nixon , yatangarije congres ya Amerika , ubutumwa budasanzwe bwageneraga uburenganzira budasanzwe abaturage kavukire ba Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
1982 : I Dujail , mu Majyaruguru ya umurwa mukuru Bagdad hakozwe igikorwa cyo gushaka kwivugana Perezida Saddam Hussein , wayoboraga igihugu cya Irak .
1997 : NATO ( North Atlantic Treaty Organization ) yasabye igihugu cya Czech Republic , Hungary , na Poland kwinjira muri uyu muryango mu masezerano yagombaga gukorwa mu mwaka w " " " " 1999 .
1999 : Bwa nyuma , muri Leta ya Florida hatanzwe igihano cya urupfu hifashishijwe intebe ya amashanyarazi ( electric chair ) .
Bamwe mu bavutse uyu munsi
1895 : Igor Tamm , umuhanga mu bugenge ukomoka mu gihugu cya Uburusiya , akaba yarabiherewe na igihembo cyitiriwe Nobel .
1908 : Nelson A . Rockefeller , Visi Perezida wa 41 wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Abakuriye inzego za ubutasi bwa gisirikare mu Karere ka Ibiyaga Bigari bemeranyije guhashya iterabwoba .
Iyi nama yabaye ku nshuro yayo ya Kane , yibanze ku nsanganyamatsiko yo " " " " Kurwanyiriza hamwe imitwe yitwaje intwaro " " " " ; yitabiriwe na u Rwanda , u Burundi , Tanzania , Uganda na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .

Uburasirazuba bwa RDC bufatwa nka indiri ya imitwe yitwaje intwaro ihungabanya umutekano mu Karere ka Ibiyaga Bigari , dore ko habarurwa irenga 120 mu mashyamba ya ako gace .
Iyo irimo irwanya Leta ya u Rwanda , iya RDC , iya u Burundi , iya Uganda na iya RDC .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe Iperereza mu Burundi , Habarurema Ildephonse , yatangaje ko iyo nama yize ku bufatanye bwa ibihugu mu guhashya iyo mitwe kandi abayitabiriye babyemeranyijeho .

nka urupapuro ngenderwaho rwa ibizakorwa mu kurwanya iyo mitwe ; na ibizakurikiraho kugira ngo bashobore kuyica muri aka Karere . " " " "
