Huye : Abaturage bazajya bavoma amazi bifashishije ikarita imeze nka Tap & Go .
Iryo koranabuhanga ryo kuvoma amazi rikoresha imashini zitwa " " " " AQtap Water Dispenser Machine , " " " " ryamaze kugeza mu Mudugudu wa Sekera mu Kagari ka Kabatwa mu Murenge wa Kigoma .
Abaturage bagera kuri 564 bo muri uwo mudugudu bose bafite ikarita yo kuvoma .
Iyo karita iba iriho amafaranga noneho nyirayo akayirambika ahabugenewe ku mashini , agakanda amazi akaza , icyo avomesha cyamara kuzura akongera gukanda kugira ngo amazi ahagarare .
Iyo karita buri muturage ayihabwa ku buntu agashyirirwaho amafaranga ashaka bijyanye na ubushobozi bwe .
Litiro imwe igura 0 , 4 Frw naho ijerekani ya litiro 20 igura 8 Frw .
Umuyobozi wa umudugudu wa Sekera , Butorano Wellars , yabwiye IGIHE ko ari we ufasha abaturage gushyira amafaranga ku makarita yabo bavomeraho .
Ati " " " " Umuturage aba afite agakarita ke akaza isaha ku isaha agashyira mu mashini ikaka , agakanda ahabugenewe amazi akaza akavoma .
Amazi ashaka iyo amaze kugeramo , arongera agakanda akarekera aho kuza .
Iyo amafaranga ashize ku ikarita , araza tukamwongereraho andi kuko dufite ikarita yindi iyabashyiriraho . " " " "
Bamwe mu baturage bo muri uwo mudugudu bishimira ko begerejwe amazi meza kandi bahabwa na ikoranabuhanga ryo kuyavoma igihe bashakiye badategereje ubavomera , nka uko bigenda ku yandi mavomo .
Mukamuvara ati " " " " Bataratwegereza amazi nari mfite ikibazo cyane kuko ntari ngifite intege zizamuka kuri Nyamugari ku iriba riri mu kabande .
Mbere nanduranyaga na abana mbabaza impamvu batagiye kuzana amazi ariko ubu igihe cyose dushakiye turaza tukavoma kuko ari hafi yacu . " " " "
Imashini itanga ayo mazi ikoresha amashanyarazi .
Kuri ubu bifashisha amashanyarazi akomoka ku zuba kuko akomoka ku muyoboro mugari atarahagezwa .
Abo baturage bishimira ko kuvoma bakoresheje ikarita bibafasha no guteganya hakiri kare amafaranga bazakoresha kugira ngo babone amazi .
Sibomana Aphrodis ati " " " " Mu bintu byari bitugoye ni ukubona amazi meza hafi yacu .
Ubu buri wese abasha guteganya amafaranga azakoresha mu kuvoma amazi meza hakiri kare , ni ibintu twishimira kandi na igiciro baduheraho ni cyiza kuko ijerekani imwe tuyishyura 8 Frw . " " " "
Bemeza kandi ko isuku mu ngo zabo yiyongereye kuko bafite amazi , bitandukanye na mbere ubwo bajyaga kuyavoma mu kabande bakoresheje igihe kigera ku isaha imwe .
Niyonsaba Francine ati " " " " Mu rugo tugira isuku kuko amazi tuyafite hafi .
No muri ibi bihe bya Covid - 19 , tugira isuku cyane cyane dukaraba intoki kugira ngo hatagira uwanduza abandi . " " " "
Umuyobozi wa Akarere ka Huye , Sebutege Ange , avuga ko ubwo buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga bwatangiriye mu Murenge wa Kigoma ariko bateganya no kubugeza ahandi .
Ati " " " " Iki ni icyiciro cya ibanze , turakomeza gukurikirana uko bifasha abaturage , nyuma bikazagenda bigezwa na ahandi . " " " "
Yashimiye abaturage uruhare bagize mu kugira ngo ayo mazi abagereho kuko batanze umuganda mu gucukura aho umuyoboro uzanyura , abasaba kuyafata neza .
Ati " " " " Abaturage turabashimira uruhare rwabo mu kubaka umuyoboro .
Turabasaba kuwufata neza , bakirinda icyatuma cyose iki gikorwa kitaramba , bakarangwa kandi na isuku kuko ni isoko ya ubuzima bwiza . " " " "
Iryo koranabuhanga mu kuvoma amazi ryashyizweho mu mushinga mugari wa umuyoboro wa amazi wa kilometero 19 , 7 watwaye arenga miliyoni 205 Frw .
Akarere ka Huye katanze arenga miliyoni 143 Frw naho World Vision isanzwe ari umufatanyabikorwa wako itanga miliyoni 61 Frw .
Uwo muyoboro ugeza amazi ku baturage 7 . 943 babarizwa mu midugudu 19 no ku bigo bitatu bya amashuri .
Uwo muyoboro wa amazi ni kimwe mu bikorwa abaturage bavuga ko bishimiye mu kwizihiza ku nshuro ya 27 isabukuru yo kwibohora ka u Rwanda .
Dore impamvu ukwiye kwita ku nshuti yawe magara .
Abantu ba inshuti magara kandi usanga bakunda kwitana utuzina twa utubyiniriro baziranyeho , cyangwa se ugasanga bakunda guhana impano zitandukanye .
Ikigo cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika gikora ibikorwa na ubushakashatsi ku buvuzi , " " " " Mayo Clinic , " " " " kivuga ko inshuti magara zifasha abazifite guca mu bibazo bya ihungabana nka gatanya , uburwayi bukomeye , gutakaza akazi cyangwa kubura uwo umuntu akunda .
Ubu bushakashatsi kandi buvuga ko " " " " Inshuti itera umuntu imbaraga zo guhindura cyangwa se kwigobotora ubuzima bushaririye na imico mibi aba ari gucamo , nko kumufasha kugabanya cyangwa kureka kunywa ibisindisha mu gihe byamaze kumuhindura imbata , ndetse inshuti nka iyo ntinanirwa kukubyutsa igihe cyose uguye . " " " "
Urubuga Well + Good rutangaza ko abahanga mu bumenyi bwa imitekerereze ya muntu bahamya ko kugira inshuti magara ari ikintu cya ingenzi mu buzima ndetse ko kubona cyangwa kugira umuntu inshuti yawe magara atari ikintu cyoroshye .
Dr . Marisa Franco ufite impamyabumenyi ya ikirenga mu bijyanye na imitekerereze ya muntu na ubuzima bwo mu mutwe , akanaba inzobere mu mibanire hagati ya inshuti , avuga ko kugira nibura inshuti imwe , yaba isanzwe cyangwa magara , bigufasha kurwanya ubwigunge no guhora wumva uri wenyine .
Yagize ati " " " " Kugira inshuti magara nziza bishobora kuba ingirakamaro ku buzima bwo mu mutwe ndetse no kugira inshuti zifite imitekerereze itandukanye na byo bishobora kugira inyungu . " " " "
Akomeza avuga ko akunze kubazwa umubare wa inshuti umuntu yagakwiye kuba afite , ariko ashimangira ko atari cyo cya ingenzi cyane ahubwo imyitwarire yazo ari cyo gihebuje ibindi kuba ingenzi , ku buryo na iyo yaba inshuti imwe ariko nzima byakugirira akamaro .
Mu gitabo " " " " Best Friend Forever " " " " cya Dr . Marisa Franco , avuga ko umuntu wa inshuti magara ari uwo mubasha kuganira mu buryo bworoshye bitagoranye , uwo mufitanye ubwumvane bwisumbuye ndetse munabasha kubwizanya ukuri .
Ese umukunzi wawe yakubera inshuti magara ?
Dr . Franco avuga ko inshuti magara ya nyayo ari imwe izaza isubiza icyo abantu bakunze kwibaza kigira kiti " " " " Ni inde uzaba uhari igihe cyose mukeneye ? " " " "
Avuga ko inshuti zo mu kazi , izo musohokana , izikugira inama zose ari ingenzi ariko bya umwihariko ya nshuti wiyambaza mu gihe bigukomeranye ari yo ya nyayo .
Ubushakashatsi bugaragaza ko iyo umukunzi wawe ari inshuti magara yawe bituma ibyishimo byawe mu rukundo byikuba kabiri kurusha uko byamera umukunzi wawe aramutse atari inshuti magara yawe , nka uko bishimangirwa na Dr . Franco , nubwo anavuga ko bidasobanuye ko umukunzi wawe ari yo nshuti yonyine ugomba kugira .
Kuri iyi ngingo kandi , Dr . Irene Levine na we ufite Impamyabumenyi ya Ikirenga mu bya ubuzima bwo mu mutwe na imitekerereze ya muntu , avuga ko kugira umukunzi wawe wenyine nka inshuti magara bidahagije kuko hari ibintu uba ushobora kuganiriza inshuti zawe zindi ariko bitakorohera kuganiriza umukunzi wawe .
Philippines : Duterte arifuza umwanya wa Visi Perezida avuye kuwa Perezida .
Duterte wa imyaka 76 yavuze ko hari ibyo atabashije gukora mu myaka itanu amaze ayoboye Philippines , bityo ko byaba byiza abaye Visi Perezida akabirangiza .
Itegeko Nshinga rya Philippines ntabwo ryemerera Perezida kuyobora manda zirenze imwe .
Mu nama yagiranye na abayobozi ba amashyaka ya Politiki kuri uyu wa Gatatu , Duterte yavuze ko yakozwe ku mutima na amarangamutima abaturage bamugaragarije , bamwereka ko bakimukunze .
Yagize ati " " " " Icyifuzo cyo kuba nakwiyamamariza umwanya wa Visi Perezida , nanjye ndagishyigikiye .
Ndi kubitekerezaho . " " " "
Bamwe mu batavuga rumwe na Duterte bagize impungenge kuri icyo cyifuzo cye kuko Visi Perezida ari we uhabwa inshingano za Perezida iyo Perezida watowe apfuye cyangwa atakibasha kuzuza inshingano ze .
Bavuga ko biramutse bibayeho , byaba bihabanye na Itegeko Nshinga igihugu kigenderaho .
Nubwo ubutegetsi bwe bwazanye inkundura yo guhiga bukware abakekwaho gucuruza ibiyobyabwenge harimo no kubarasa , ibyegeranyo bitandukanye bigaragaza ko Duterte agikunzwe na abaturage .
CNN yatangaje ko Duterte ashobora kwiyamamariza kuba Visi Perezida umwaka utaha kugira ngo yirinde kuba yakurikiranwa na inkiko kuko byagiye biba ku bamubanjirije .
Duterte yavuze ko mu gihe yagira ibyago ubaye Perezida ntabe ari inshuti ye , kuba Visi Perezida kwe ntacyo byaba bimumariye .
Rutsiro : Umugabo yishe mugenzi we amukubise agafuni .
bi byabaye ahagana saa Mbili za igitondo cyo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , tariki ya 9 Nyakanga 2021 .
Abaturage babibonye bavuze ko uwo mugabo wa imyaka 30 yakubise agafuni mu mutwe uwitwa Semajeri Théoneste wa imyaka 47 , ahita apfa .
Umunyamabanga Nshingwabikorwa wa Umurenge wa Kivumu , Nkusi Pontien , yavuze ko uwabikoze asa naho afite ikibazo cya uburwayi bwo mu mutwe .
Ati " " " " Ntituramenya icyo yamuhoye kubera ko umuturage witwa Nshimiyimana Javan avuga ko yamubonye yiruka inyuma ya nyakwigendera afite ifuni akayimukubita mu mutwe , akagwa hasi ndetse agakomeza kuyimukubita kugeza apfuye . " " " " " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko bageze aho yamwiciye bagasanga ukekwa ahagaze hejuru ya imodoka afite ifuni yakoresheje amwica .
Yavuze yaje kumanuka arafatwa nyuma yo kubona akikijwe na abaturage benshi ndetse na Polisi .
Nkusi yavuze ko uwakoze icyaha acyemera ndetse akavuga ko yamwishe amuhoye ubusa .
Ati " " " " Urebye uko ameze , asa na aho afite ikibazo cya uburwayi bwo mu mutwe cyangwa akaba akoresha ibiyobyabwenge .
Kuri yafashwe afungirwa kuri Sitasiyo ya RIB ya Kivumu . " " " " " " " "
Umurambo wa nyakwigendera wajyanywe ku Bitaro bya Murunda gukorerwa isuzuma mbere ya uko ushyingurwa .
Ntawe uzavutswa amahirwe kuko arwaye Covid - 19 !
Imyiteguro ya ibizamini bya leta byatwaye arenga miliyari 12 Frw .
Ni ibitangazwa mu gihe kuva ku wa Mbere , tariki 12 kugeza ku wa 14 Nyakanga 2021 , aribwo hazakorwa ibizamini bya leta ku basoza amashuri abanza .
Abo mu Cyiciro rusange na abasoza Ayisumbuye bazakora ibizamini ku wa 20 - 30 Nyakanga 2021 .
Mu kiganiro na abanyamakuru cyo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , tariki 9 Nyakanga 2021 , Umuyobozi Mukuru wa NESA , Dr Bahati Bernard , yavuze ko imyiteguro irimbanyije ku ruhande rwa abanyeshuri na ahazakorerwa ibizamini muri rusange .
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ibikoresho nkenerwa nabyo byarateguwe ku buryo ubu imodoka zijyana ibikoresho bikenerwa na ibizamini ubwabyo ziri mu nzira zibishyikiriza buri turere .
Guhera ejo ibizamini bizatangira kugezwa mu bigo aho abanyeshuri bakorera . " " " " " " " "
Dr Bahati avuga ko abanyeshuri bagiye gukora ibizamini bya umwihariko harimo abazabikora barwaye Covid - 19 , cyangwa bakaba bakora bataha iwabo mu gihe baba bari mu kato cyangwa baranduye iki cyorezo .
Ati " " " " Turateganya ko dushobora kugira abanyeshuri bashobora kuba barwaye mu gihe cyo gukora ibizamini , icyo twakwizeza Abanyarwanda ni uko nta muntu uzavutswa amahirwe yo gukora ikizamini kubera ko yarwaye Covid - 19 . " " " "
NESA itangaza ko umwaka ushize yo ibijyanye na imyiteguro na ibihe byo gukora ibizamini bya leta hakoreshejwe ingengo ya imari iri hagati ya miliyari 10 Frw na 11 Frw mu gihe kuri ubu ibarirwa hagati ya miliyari 12 Frw na miliyari 13 Frw .
Muri rusange abanyeshuri 452 . 053 ni bo bazakora ibizamini bisoza ibyiciro bitandukanye bya amashuri abanza na ayisumbuye guhera muri Kamena uyu mwaka .
NESA igaragaza ko ikijyanye na ahantu hazakorerwa ibizamini hiyongereye bya umwihariko nko mu mashuri abanza , ahazakorerwa [ sites ] ari 1021 mu gihe mu 2019 , hari ahantu hagera kuri 980 .
Ibi byatewe no kuba hari ibyumba bya amashuri bishya byubatswe ndetse binajyana no kuba hagomba kubahirizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Covid - 19 , abanyeshuri bahana intera .
Gare na Guest House bya Kirehe byashyizwe ku isoko bibura abaguzi .
Kuva muri Gicurasi 2019 Akarere ka Kirehe kashyize ku isoko ibikorwaremezo kubatse kugira ngo bizamure iterambere ryako mu rwego rwo guha umwanya abikorera no kubegurira ibikorwa bimwe na bimwe .
Mu byashyizwe ku isoko harimo gare yari igiye kwegurirwa abikorera na Guest House ya Akarere ka Kirehe isanzwe yifashishwa mu kwakira inama zikomeye zikaberamo , ikanagira amacumbi .
Umuyobozi wa Akarere ka Kirehe , Muzungu Gérard , avuga ko kuva bashyize ku isoko ibi bikorwa mu 2019 , Guest House yabonye abifuza kuyegukana mu gihe gare yo yabuze abayigura .
Ati " " " " Gare ntitwabonye abayipiganirwa ariko Guest House yo turi mu biganiro bya ubufatanye na abikorera bo mu Karere kacu kugira ngo bazagiremo imigabane myinshi Akarere gasigarane mike .
Turacyari muri iyi nzira , hari ibiganiro dukora na inzego zitandukanye zirimo Minicom , Minecofin , LODA na intara kugira ngo icyo gikorwa kizagende neza . " " " "
Muzungu yavuze ko kuri ubu ibiganiro bigeze kure kandi biri kugenda neza ahamya ko mu gihe cya vuba bazaba bamaze kwemeranya bagatangira imikoranire .
Abikorera bifuza kugura iyi Guest House bakayubaka mu buryo bugezweho igahinduka hotel nziza kuko muri aka Karere nta hotel ikomeye ihabarizwa .
Akarere ka Kirehe kafashe icyemezo cyo gushyira ku isoko ibi bikorwaremezo kugira ngo gahe umwanya abikorera , amafaranga azavamo azashyirwa mu bindi bikorwa bya iterambere rusange rya abaturage .
Abagabo barenga 7000 bakorewe ihohoterwa ririmo irishingiye ku gitsina mu myaka ine .
Ni icyemezo ahanini gifitanye isano na umuco wa igihugu aho umuntu yumva ko kuba umugabo yavuga ko yakubiswe na umugore we cyangwa agakorerwa ibindi bikorwa bibabaza umubiri we byabaga ari nka ikinegu muri rubanda ; ko yafatwa nka udashoboye cyangwa inganzwa .
Mu muco wa Kinyarwanda , umugabo afatwa nka umunyembaraga , utunga urugo , urubirira icyuya kandi akaba wa muntu wirwanaho , ufatwa nka inkingi mwikorezi mu muryango .
Ibi bituma rero abakorewe ihohoterwa baceceka nubwo hari bake batobora bakavuga ibya uwo musaraba bahuriye na wo mu rushako cyangwa ahandi babarizwa muri sosiyete bitewe na icyiciro barimo .
Nubwo imibare ishobora kuba mito ugereranyije na ukuri kwa ibibera iyo mu bikari , hari ibigaragaza ko abagabo na bo bakorerwa ihohoterwa ndetse bikagera no ku rishingiye ku gitsina .
Raporo ngarukamwaka ya Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ibarurishamibare , NISR , yo mu 2020 , yerekanye ko hagati ya 2016 na 2019 , abagabo 7210 bakorewe ihohoterwa mu gihugu cyose .
Iyi raporo yerekana ko muri iyo myaka ine , aba igitsina gore bakorewe ihohoterwa bangana na 48 . 809 .
Raporo yerekana ko ubukana bwa ibi byaha bugenda bugabanuka kuko nko mu 2018 , abagabo bahohotewe bari 2 . 015 mu gihe mu mwaka wakurikiyeho bageze kuri 998 .
Mu gukusanya amakuru akubiye muri iyi raporo yakozwe na Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ubuzima , RBC , hifashishijwe imibare yakusanyijwe mu bitaro bya uturere hibanzwe ku kureba abakorewe ihohoterwa bagasigirwa ibimenyetso bifatika bya ihohoterwa ribabaza umubiri ndetse na ibifitanye isano na ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina
Abagabo bashya bakorewe ihohoterwa bagasigirwa ibimenyetso byaryo ku mubiri [ aha ni nko gukomeretswa ] bangana na 6 . 113 mu gihe abakorewe ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina ari 1097 .
Mu buryo bwa impurirane abagizweho ingaruka na ibikorwa bya ihohoterwa mu muryango Nyarwanda [ ni ukuvuga ubariyemo abagabo na abagore ] ni 56 . 019 hagati ya 2016 na 2019 .
Abagabo barikandagira mu gutanga ubuhamya ku ihohoterwa
Benshi mu bagabo na abahungu bakorerwa ihohoterwa batinya kuvuga kubera gutinya uko bakirwa na sosiyete ndetse na abatoboye rimwe na rimwe baba bafite impungenge ko nta wuzabatega amatwi .
Abagabo bo mu Karere ka Nyagatare muri Werurwe 2021 bavuze ku ihohoterwa bakorewe , banasaba ubuyobozi kwakira ibirego bya ababugana badashingiye ku gitsina .
Nduwamungu Bosco wo mu Murenge wa Karangazi yavuze ku ihohoterwa yakorewe na umugore we wamuhozaga ku nkeke .
Ati " " " " Nagerageje kubana na umugore neza arananira , yarankubise inshuro nka eshatu , nagerageza kujya mu buyobozi bwa umudugudu bati " " " " wowe nta jambo ufite , " " " " nabwo mvuyeyo umugore arankubita . " " " "
Mugenzi we utuye mu Murenge wa Mukama na we yakubiswe na umugore , ageza ikibazo cye mu buyobozi bwa ibanze arenzwa ingohe kugeza yahukanye .
Ati " " " " Nagiye mu buyobozi ndatsindwa , amafuti bakayangerekaho mera nka isaha ivuye ku gihe , ndahukana mva mu rugo .
Umugore na iyo yagubita nyine ntaho wajya kurega , uremera ukaryumaho kuko uwo urega ni we uregera . " " " "
Ihohoterwa ni igikorwa cyose gikorewe umuntu atabishaka kikaba gishobora kumugiraho ingaruka ku mubiri , mu bitekerezo cyangwa ku buryo bushingiye ku gitsina .
Umuyobozi wa Umuryango uharanira guteza imbere Uburinganire no kurwanya Ihohoterwa rishingiye ku Gitsina ( RWAMREC ) , Rutayisire Fidèle , yabwiye IGIHE ko bemeranya na imibare yatangajwe ku bagabo na abahungu bahohoterwa ariko ari mike bitewe no kuba hari abatavuga .
Ati " " " " Turakangurira abagabo kudahishira ibyabayeho kuko abenshi banga kuvuga ibyababayeho kubera ko batabona ubufasha , barasekwa bagashyirwa mu kato kuko bazi ko umugabo ahohotera , adahohoterwa .
Nka uko dushyira imbaraga mu kurwanya ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagore na abakobwa , dukeneye imbaraga mu kurwanya irikorerwa abagabo na abahungu . " " " " " " " "
Yavuze ko sosiyete imenyereye ko ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagore ndetse umuco utuma abagabo batavuga akaga bahuye na ko .
Yagize ati " " " " Iyo umugabo yahohotewe akajya nko kuri Polisi , abapolisi baramubwira bati " " " " uri umugabo mbwa , ni gute wakubitwa na umugore ? " " " "
Iyo agiye mu " " " " Nshuti za umuryango " " " " cyangwa abashinzwe kurwanya ihohoterwa mu Mudugudu , baramubwira bati " " " " nta mugabo ugomba guhohoterwa na umugore . " " " "
Icyo gihe iyo atabonye ubufasha acika intege ku buryo na ubutaha atajyayo . " " " " " " " "
COVID - 19 yongereye ibinyoro mu bibembe ?
Umuryango uri mu byiciro byahungabanyijwe bikomeye na icyorezo cya Covid - 19 ahanini kubera ingamba zashyizweho mu kwirinda ikwirakwira ryacyo , aho igihugu cyafashe ibyemezo birimo Guma mu Rugo , kugabanya amasaha yo gutaha na izindi .
Izi ngamba zose zatumye ababana barushaho kumarana umwanya munini , yewe no kumenyana byimbitse ku buryo hari ababonye ibyo batamenye ku bo basangiye indaro , aba imitima yoroshye bigasembura amarangamutima yabyaye amacakubiri , ari na yo ntandaro ya ihohoterwa .
Kuva COVID - 19 yagera mu Rwanda , RWAMREC yakoze ubushakashatsi muri gahunda yayo yise " " " " Bandebereho " " " " aho yasanze hari aho ihohoterwa ryiyongereye na aho ryagabanutse .
Ati " " " " Abitabiriye gahunda ya " " " " Bandebereho " " " " bashoboye kubana neza na imiryango yabo kandi ihohoterwa ryaragabanutse muri iyo miryango ariko aho itarashoboye kwitabira ayo matsinda kubera COVID - 19 , ihohoterwa ryariyongereye kandi amakimbirane na yo ariyongera .
Bishingiye ku kuba abagabo bari batunze ingo zabo babuze imirimo yabatungaga hanyuma bibongerera guhangayika , ihohoterwa rirazamuka , cyane irishingiye ku mutima kubera kudashobora kubahiriza inshingano zimwe na zimwe . " " " " " " " "
Inyigo yakorewe mu Turere ka Kicukiro na Huye mu 2020 yagaragaje ko imyumvire ku ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagabo na abahungu ikiri hasi cyane .
Kayisire yagize ati " " " " Umugabo iyo afashwe ku ngufu cyangwa umuhungu agasambanywa na umugore usanga abantu babifashe nka ishyano ; ntibabyihanganire kurusha uko umukobwa afatwa ku ngufu . " " " " " " " "
RWAMREC yakira abagabo bayigana ikabaha ubufasha bwa ubujyanama na aho bakurikiranira ibibazo byabo .
Nibura mu kwezi kumwe , uyu muryango wakira abari hagati ya 7 - 10 mu Mujyi wa Kigali bavuga ku ihohoterwa bakorewe .
Ingamba zafashwe mu guhangana na ihohoterwa ryo mu muryango
Nubwo nta mibare yerekana ubukana bwa ikibazo cya ihohoterwa hagati ya abashakanye nibura kuva mu mezi arenga 15 ashize COVID - 19 igeze mu Rwanda , ubuhamya bwa benshi bugusha ku kuba hari aho umuriro watse .
Minisitiri wa Uburinganire na Iterambere rya Umuryango ( MIGEPROF ) , Prof Bayisenge Jeannette , yabwiye IGIHE ko hari ibibazo byari mu muryango Nyarwanda iki cyorezo cyatije umurindi .
Yagize ati " " " " Amakimbirane yakomeje kuvugwa haba mu Rwanda no ku Isi muri rusange , yagiye yiyongera hariho na ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina .
No mu Rwanda ibyo byabayeho .
Nubwo twebwe tutavuga ngo byanze bikunze imibare yarazamutse ariko twakomeje kubona iryo hungabana rya uburenganzira bwa muntu cyane cyane irishingiye ku gitsina . " " " " " " " "
Yavuze ko u Rwanda rutigeze ruhagarika " " " " ingamba zo guhangana na ibibazo byugarije umuryango " " " " . " " " "
Yakomeje ati " " " " Twashatse ubundi buryo budasanzwe bwo gukora kugira ngo bijyane na igihe twari turimo cya Covid - 19 .
Iyo turwanya ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina ntituvuga ngo ni umugabo , umugore , umwana cyangwa umuhungu wahohotewe , kuri twebwe buri wese agomba guhabwa ubutabera . " " " "
MIGEPROF itanga miliyoni 200 Frw buri mwaka , yoherezwa mu turere agamije gufasha abarimo abana na abandi bantu bakuru bahohoterwa .
Urwego rwa Igihugu rwa Ubugenzacyaha , RIB , rutangaza ko hagati ya 2015 na 2018 rwakiriye ibirego 1 . 098 bifitanye isano na amakimbirane yo mu muryango birimo ibyo gukubita no gukomeretsa , ubwicanyi no kwiyahura .
Imibare ya NISR igaragaza ko mu 2015 , hakiriwe dosiye 669 zijyanye no gukubita no gukomeretsa , 89 za ubwicanyi na 23 zijyanye no kwiyahura .
Mu 2016 , dosiye zakiriwe ni 641 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , iza ubwicanyi ni 97 mu gihe izo kwiyahura ari 17 .
Mu 2017 kqndi hakiriwe dosiye 784 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , 86 za ubwicanyi na zirindwi zo kwiyahura .
Mu 2018 yakiriye dosiye 979 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , 95 za ubwicanyi mu gihe izo kwiyahura ari 24 .
Ni icyemezo ahanini gifitanye isano na umuco wa igihugu aho umuntu yumva ko kuba umugabo yavuga ko yakubiswe na umugore we cyangwa agakorerwa ibindi bikorwa bibabaza umubiri we byabaga ari nka ikinegu muri rubanda ; ko yafatwa nka udashoboye cyangwa inganzwa .
Mu muco wa Kinyarwanda , umugabo afatwa nka umunyembaraga , utunga urugo , urubirira icyuya kandi akaba wa muntu wirwanaho , ufatwa nka inkingi mwikorezi mu muryango .
Ibi bituma rero abakorewe ihohoterwa baceceka nubwo hari bake batobora bakavuga ibya uwo musaraba bahuriye na wo mu rushako cyangwa ahandi babarizwa muri sosiyete bitewe na icyiciro barimo .
Nubwo imibare ishobora kuba mito ugereranyije na ukuri kwa ibibera iyo mu bikari , hari ibigaragaza ko abagabo na bo bakorerwa ihohoterwa ndetse bikagera no ku rishingiye ku gitsina .
Raporo ngarukamwaka ya Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ibarurishamibare , NISR , yo mu 2020 , yerekanye ko hagati ya 2016 na 2019 , abagabo 7210 bakorewe ihohoterwa mu gihugu cyose .
Iyi raporo yerekana ko muri iyo myaka ine , aba igitsina gore bakorewe ihohoterwa bangana na 48 . 809 .
Raporo yerekana ko ubukana bwa ibi byaha bugenda bugabanuka kuko nko mu 2018 , abagabo bahohotewe bari 2 . 015 mu gihe mu mwaka wakurikiyeho bageze kuri 998 .
Mu gukusanya amakuru akubiye muri iyi raporo yakozwe na Ikigo cya Igihugu cya Ubuzima , RBC , hifashishijwe imibare yakusanyijwe mu bitaro bya uturere hibanzwe ku kureba abakorewe ihohoterwa bagasigirwa ibimenyetso bifatika bya ihohoterwa ribabaza umubiri ndetse na ibifitanye isano na ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina
Abagabo bashya bakorewe ihohoterwa bagasigirwa ibimenyetso byaryo ku mubiri [ aha ni nko gukomeretswa ] bangana na 6 . 113 mu gihe abakorewe ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina ari 1097 .
Mu buryo bwa impurirane abagizweho ingaruka na ibikorwa bya ihohoterwa mu muryango Nyarwanda [ ni ukuvuga ubariyemo abagabo na abagore ] ni 56 . 019 hagati ya 2016 na 2019 .
Abagabo barikandagira mu gutanga ubuhamya ku ihohoterwa
Benshi mu bagabo na abahungu bakorerwa ihohoterwa batinya kuvuga kubera gutinya uko bakirwa na sosiyete ndetse na abatoboye rimwe na rimwe baba bafite impungenge ko nta wuzabatega amatwi .
Abagabo bo mu Karere ka Nyagatare muri Werurwe 2021 bavuze ku ihohoterwa bakorewe , banasaba ubuyobozi kwakira ibirego bya ababugana badashingiye ku gitsina .
Nduwamungu Bosco wo mu Murenge wa Karangazi yavuze ku ihohoterwa yakorewe na umugore we wamuhozaga ku nkeke .
Ati " " " " Nagerageje kubana na umugore neza arananira , yarankubise inshuro nka eshatu , nagerageza kujya mu buyobozi bwa umudugudu bati " " " " wowe nta jambo ufite , " " " " nabwo mvuyeyo umugore arankubita . " " " "
Mugenzi we utuye mu Murenge wa Mukama na we yakubiswe na umugore , ageza ikibazo cye mu buyobozi bwa ibanze arenzwa ingohe kugeza yahukanye .
Ati " " " " Nagiye mu buyobozi ndatsindwa , amafuti bakayangerekaho mera nka isaha ivuye ku gihe , ndahukana mva mu rugo .
Umugore na iyo yagubita nyine ntaho wajya kurega , uremera ukaryumaho kuko uwo urega ni we uregera . " " " "
Ihohoterwa ni igikorwa cyose gikorewe umuntu atabishaka kikaba gishobora kumugiraho ingaruka ku mubiri , mu bitekerezo cyangwa ku buryo bushingiye ku gitsina .
Umuyobozi wa Umuryango uharanira guteza imbere Uburinganire no kurwanya Ihohoterwa rishingiye ku Gitsina ( RWAMREC ) , Rutayisire Fidèle , yabwiye IGIHE ko bemeranya na imibare yatangajwe ku bagabo na abahungu bahohoterwa ariko ari mike bitewe no kuba hari abatavuga .
Ati " " " " Turakangurira abagabo kudahishira ibyabayeho kuko abenshi banga kuvuga ibyababayeho kubera ko batabona ubufasha , barasekwa bagashyirwa mu kato kuko bazi ko umugabo ahohotera , adahohoterwa .
Nka uko dushyira imbaraga mu kurwanya ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagore na abakobwa , dukeneye imbaraga mu kurwanya irikorerwa abagabo na abahungu . " " " " " " " "
Yavuze ko sosiyete imenyereye ko ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagore ndetse umuco utuma abagabo batavuga akaga bahuye na ko .
Yagize ati " " " " Iyo umugabo yahohotewe akajya nko kuri Polisi , abapolisi baramubwira bati " " " " uri umugabo mbwa , ni gute wakubitwa na umugore ? " " " "
Iyo agiye mu " " " " Nshuti za umuryango " " " " cyangwa abashinzwe kurwanya ihohoterwa mu Mudugudu , baramubwira bati " " " " nta mugabo ugomba guhohoterwa na umugore . " " " "
Icyo gihe iyo atabonye ubufasha acika intege ku buryo na ubutaha atajyayo . " " " " " " " "
COVID - 19 yongereye ibinyoro mu bibembe ?
Umuryango uri mu byiciro byahungabanyijwe bikomeye na icyorezo cya Covid - 19 ahanini kubera ingamba zashyizweho mu kwirinda ikwirakwira ryacyo , aho igihugu cyafashe ibyemezo birimo Guma mu Rugo , kugabanya amasaha yo gutaha na izindi .
Izi ngamba zose zatumye ababana barushaho kumarana umwanya munini , yewe no kumenyana byimbitse ku buryo hari ababonye ibyo batamenye ku bo basangiye indaro , aba imitima yoroshye bigasembura amarangamutima yabyaye amacakubiri , ari na yo ntandaro ya ihohoterwa .
Kuva COVID - 19 yagera mu Rwanda , RWAMREC yakoze ubushakashatsi muri gahunda yayo yise " " " " Bandebereho " " " " aho yasanze hari aho ihohoterwa ryiyongereye na aho ryagabanutse .
Ati " " " " Abitabiriye gahunda ya " " " " Bandebereho " " " " bashoboye kubana neza na imiryango yabo kandi ihohoterwa ryaragabanutse muri iyo miryango ariko aho itarashoboye kwitabira ayo matsinda kubera COVID - 19 , ihohoterwa ryariyongereye kandi amakimbirane na yo ariyongera .
Bishingiye ku kuba abagabo bari batunze ingo zabo babuze imirimo yabatungaga hanyuma bibongerera guhangayika , ihohoterwa rirazamuka , cyane irishingiye ku mutima kubera kudashobora kubahiriza inshingano zimwe na zimwe . " " " " " " " "
Inyigo yakorewe mu Turere ka Kicukiro na Huye mu 2020 yagaragaje ko imyumvire ku ihohoterwa rikorerwa abagabo na abahungu ikiri hasi cyane .
Kayisire yagize ati " " " " Umugabo iyo afashwe ku ngufu cyangwa umuhungu agasambanywa na umugore usanga abantu babifashe nka ishyano ; ntibabyihanganire kurusha uko umukobwa afatwa ku ngufu . " " " " " " " "
RWAMREC yakira abagabo bayigana ikabaha ubufasha bwa ubujyanama na aho bakurikiranira ibibazo byabo .
Nibura mu kwezi kumwe , uyu muryango wakira abari hagati ya 7 - 10 mu Mujyi wa Kigali bavuga ku ihohoterwa bakorewe .
Ingamba zafashwe mu guhangana na ihohoterwa ryo mu muryango
Nubwo nta mibare yerekana ubukana bwa ikibazo cya ihohoterwa hagati ya abashakanye nibura kuva mu mezi arenga 15 ashize COVID - 19 igeze mu Rwanda , ubuhamya bwa benshi bugusha ku kuba hari aho umuriro watse .
Minisitiri wa Uburinganire na Iterambere rya Umuryango ( MIGEPROF ) , Prof Bayisenge Jeannette , yabwiye IGIHE ko hari ibibazo byari mu muryango Nyarwanda iki cyorezo cyatije umurindi .
Yagize ati " " " " Amakimbirane yakomeje kuvugwa haba mu Rwanda no ku Isi muri rusange , yagiye yiyongera hariho na ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina .
No mu Rwanda ibyo byabayeho .
Nubwo twebwe tutavuga ngo byanze bikunze imibare yarazamutse ariko twakomeje kubona iryo hungabana rya uburenganzira bwa muntu cyane cyane irishingiye ku gitsina . " " " " " " " "
Yavuze ko u Rwanda rutigeze ruhagarika " " " " ingamba zo guhangana na ibibazo byugarije umuryango " " " " . " " " "
Yakomeje ati " " " " Twashatse ubundi buryo budasanzwe bwo gukora kugira ngo bijyane na igihe twari turimo cya Covid - 19 .
Iyo turwanya ihohoterwa rishingiye ku gitsina ntituvuga ngo ni umugabo , umugore , umwana cyangwa umuhungu wahohotewe , kuri twebwe buri wese agomba guhabwa ubutabera . " " " "
MIGEPROF itanga miliyoni 200 Frw buri mwaka , yoherezwa mu turere agamije gufasha abarimo abana na abandi bantu bakuru bahohoterwa .
Urwego rwa Igihugu rwa Ubugenzacyaha , RIB , rutangaza ko hagati ya 2015 na 2018 rwakiriye ibirego 1 . 098 bifitanye isano na amakimbirane yo mu muryango birimo ibyo gukubita no gukomeretsa , ubwicanyi no kwiyahura .
Imibare ya NISR igaragaza ko mu 2015 , hakiriwe dosiye 669 zijyanye no gukubita no gukomeretsa , 89 za ubwicanyi na 23 zijyanye no kwiyahura .
Mu 2016 , dosiye zakiriwe ni 641 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , iza ubwicanyi ni 97 mu gihe izo kwiyahura ari 17 .
Mu 2017 kqndi hakiriwe dosiye 784 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , 86 za ubwicanyi na zirindwi zo kwiyahura .
Mu 2018 yakiriye dosiye 979 zo gukubita no gukomeretsa , 95 za ubwicanyi mu gihe izo kwiyahura ari 24 .
Inzu yagurishijwe iherereye mu Karere ka Muhanga mu Ntara ya Amajyepfo yagombaga kugurwa miliyoni 22 za amafaranga ya u Rwanda nyamara ibya ngombwa berekanaga byari ibihimbano .
Umwe muri bo yiyitaga ko ari nyirayo naho abandi bakigira abakomisiyoneri .
Bafashwe basigaje guhabwa miliyoni zirindwi na igice .
Uko ari batanu bemeye ibyaha baregwa banabisabira imbabazi kuri uyu Gatanu tariki ya 9 Nyakanga 2021 .
Umwe yagize ati " " " " Ndi hano kubera ko nafatiwe mu cyaha cyo kugurisha inzu itari iyanjye , umushinga wateguwe na mugenzi wanjye ariko ndabisabira imbabazi . " " " "
Uyu mugabo yemereye polisi kuyigaragariza abandi batekamutwe bose kugira ngo ibashe guhashya abakora ibi byaha .
Uwineza Ange uvuka mu muryango wari watanze amafaranga ugura inzu , we yashimiye RIB anashimangira ko iyo itahaba batari kuzongera kubona abo batekamutwe .
Ati " " " " Umwe muri bo yari inshuti ya umuryango , ni na we waje aturangira iyo nzu mu rugo .
Bayisuye kabiri noneho njye nagiyeyo bwa nyuma ni bwo nasanze banyirayo bahari batwereka ko ari iyabo na ibyangombwa dusanga bitandukanye na ibyo aba bari batweretse . " " " "
Yongeyeho ko nyuma yo gusanga ibyangombwa berekwagwa ari ibihimbano bahise bitabaza RIB itangira kubashakisha .
Ati " " " " Twahise tubibwira RIB noneho ikajya ibahamagara telefone ntiboneke nyuma nibwo yabahamagaye baza baziko tugiye kubishyura andi ihita ibafata . " " " "
Umuvugizi wa Urwego rwa Ubugenzacyaha , RIB , Dr Murangira B . Thierry , yavuze ko aba bagabo bakurikiranyweho ibyaha bine .
Ati " " " " Bafashwe mu gikorwa cyo kugurisha inzu itari iyabo bakaba bakurikiranywe ibyaha bine birimo gushyiraho umutwe wa abagizi ba nabi no kuwujyamo , kwihesha ikintu cya undi hakoreshejwe uburiganya , icyo guhimba , guhindura inyandiko cyangwa gukoresha inyandiko mpimbano ndetse hakanazamo na icyaha cyo kwigana ,
guhindura amafaranga cyangwa ibyitiranwa na yo . " " " "
Yasabye abaturage kujya bagura ibintu babanje gushishoza no kwishyurira abantu kuri banki kuko bituma imyirondoro yabo imenyekana anashimangirako ko amafaranga bari bahawe yagarujwe ndetse na ibintu bari bayaguzemo byafatiriwe .
Ahahoze Kaminuza ya Kibungo hashobora gutangira irindi shuri rikuru vuba .
Ibi bije nyuma yaho iyi kaminuza ifungiwe igateza ibihombo ku baturage bakodeshaga inzu abanyeshuri bayigagamo na ubucuruzi busubira inyuma mu gace yari iherereyemo .
Umuhoza Oliver utuye mu Mudugudu wa Gatare mu Kagari ka Karenge munsi ya ahakoreraga iyi kaminuza yabwiye IGIHE ko kuva bayifunga bagize igihombo gikomeye cyane .
Yavuze ko ubundi hahoraga urujya na uruza rwa abanyeshuri baguraga ibintu byinshi , abanyonzi , abamotari , abacuruzi na abafite inzu zikodeshwa ubu ngo abenshi barahimutse kubera kubura abakiriya bituma muri uyu Mudugudu hakonja cyane .
Ati " " " " Nko kuri njye ndi umwe mu bacuruzi , igihombo cya mbere nagize ni uguhomba abaturanyi kuko baradususurutsaga , igihombo cya kabiri nahombye abakiriya bituma ubucuruzi bwanjye busubira inyuma , ikindi hari bagenzi banjye bari bafite inzu bakodesha ariko kugeza kuri iyi saha ntizigikodeshwa kuko abazibagamo ni abanyeshuri
ubu babuze abandi bakiriya . " " " "
Umuyobozi wa Akarere ka Ngoma wungirije ushinzwe Iterambere rya Ubukungu , Nyiridandi Mapambano Cyriaque yavuze ko hari ibiganiro bari kugirana na andi mashuri kugira ngo aze kuhakorera kandi ngo ibyo biganiro biri kugenda neza .
Ati " " " " Hari ibiganiro byatangiye tubifashijwemo na ubuyobozi bwa Intara hamwe na Minisiteri ya Uburezi kugira ngo hariya yakoreraga harebwe ikintu cyahakorerwa ariko kijyanye na uburezi , twakwizeza abaturage ko igisubizo kiri gushakwa kandi kizaboneka mu minsi ya vuba . " " " "
Mapambano yavuze ko hashobora kugaruka kaminuza nubwo yaba ititwa UNIK ariko ko rizaba ari ishuri kandi rizatanga ubumenyi kuri benshi ryongere no gushyushya aka Karere .
Kaminuza ya UNIK yatangijwe mu mwaka wa 2003 ni imwe mu zagiriye umumaro abigaga uburezi kuko yabafashije mu kubigisha mu biruhuko , mu mpera za icyumweru ndetse no mu mibyizi , nyuma ya igihe gito yaje gufungura ishami mu Karere ka Rulindo ryafashaga abaturuka mu Burengerazuba na Amajyaruguru .
Yabarizwagamo amashami atatu arimo irya uburezi , imari na icungamutungo ndetse na ishami rya ubuhinzi na iterambere rya icyaro , yafunzwe imaze gushyira ku isoko abarenga 9500 .
Amb . Mutsindashyaka yatanze impapuro zimwemerera guhagararira u Rwanda muri Repubulika ya Congo .
Mu kiganiro bagiranye , Perezida Denis Sassou Na Guesso yashimye umubano na ubushuti u Rwanda na Congo Brazzaville bifitanye na uruhare rwa Perezida Kagame mu guteza imbere u Rwanda , hamwe na umurava we mu guharanira icyateza imbere Afurika Yunze Ubumwe .
Yavuze kandi ko igihugu cye cyiteguye gufatanya na u Rwanda mu kuzamura imikoranire igamije kuzamura ubukungu bwa ibihugu byombi .
Ambasaderi Mutsindashyaka nyuma yo gutanga ubutumwa yahawe na Perezida Kagame , yatangaje ko yishimiye guhagararira u Rwanda muri Congo isanzwe ifitanye umubano mwiza na u Rwanda , anizeza Perezida Denis Sassou Na Guesso ko azakomeza gushimangira ubufatanye ndetse na umubano mwiza biri hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Yavuze kandi ko azaharanira kuzamura ubuhinzi , ubworozi ndetse na inganda zitunganya ibibikomokaho .
Ibi bizashyirwamo ingufu hifashishijwe amasezerano ya umubano na ubufatanye hagati ya inzego za ubuyobozi zibishinzwe , kugira ngo bigirire akamaro abaturage ba u Rwanda na Congo .
Ambasaderi Mutsindashyaka yongeyeho ko azafatanya na abandi bayobozi , agakora ibishoboka byose kugira ngo uyu mubano urusheho kungura ibihugu byombi mu bijyanye na ubuhahirane , ubukerarugendo no bindi bifitiye akamaro ibihugu byombi ndetse na umugabane wa Afurika muri rusange .
Ngoma : Umuyobozi akurikiranyweho kunyereza asaga miliyoni 1 Frw yo kwishyura mituweli
IGIHE yamenye ko uyu muyobozi wa imyaka 31 yatawe muri yombi ku wa 7 Nyakanga 2021 .
Umuvugizi wa Urwego rwa Igihugu rwa Ubugenzacyaha , RIB , Dr Murangira B . Thierry , yavuze ko uwo muyobozi yafashwe ndetse iperereza riri gukorwa .
Yakomeje ati " " " " Uwafashwe afungiye kuri Sitasiyo ya RIB ya Kibungo mu gihe iperereza rikomeje kugira ngo hakorwe dosiye ishyikirizwe Ubushinjacyaha . " " " " " " " "
Yavuze ko abakora ibyaha byo kunyereza umutungo ufitiye inyungu rubanda batazihanganirwa .
Yakomeje ati " " " " RIB iributsa abaturarwanda ko itazihanganira uwo ariwe wese uzafatirwa mu cyaha cyo kunyereza umutungo ashinzwe kugenzura awukoresha mu nyungu ze bwite .
Abantu bakwiye kumenya ko iki ari icyaha gihanwa na amategeko . " " " " " " " "
Ingingo ya 10 ya itegeko N ° 54 / 2018 ryo ku wa 13 / 08 / 2018 ryerekeye kurwanya ruswa iteganya ko uhamijwe icyaha cyo kunyereza umutungo ahanishwa igifungo kitari munsi ya imyaka irindwi ariko kitarenze 10 n " " " " amafaranga ya u Rwanda yikubye inshuro kuva ku nshuro eshatu kugeza kuri eshanu za agaciro ka umutungo yanyereje .
Ntimukwiye gutegereza guhamagarwa ngo murwanire igihugu cyanyu - Gen James Kabarebe .
Ibi Gen . James Kabarebe yabigarutseho kuri uyu wa 9 Nyakanga 2021 , ubwo yagiranaga ibiganiro na itsinda rya abahungu na abakobwa baba mu bihugu bitandukanye ariko bakaba bamaze iminsi mu Rwanda , aho bari gusobanurirwa amateka ya Igihugu cyabo .
Iri tsinda rya urubyiruko rigizwe na abarenga 60 rimaze iminsi mu Rwanda riri gusura ibikorwa bifite aho bihuriye na amateka ya Igihugu cyabo .
Ririmo abakuriye mu Bufaransa , u Bubiligi , Canada , Denmark na ibindi bihugu .
Kuri uyu wa Gatanu uru rubyiruko rwasuye Ingoro ya amateka yo guhagarika Jenoside iherereye ku Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya u Rwanda ari naho bagize amahirwe yo kuganirizwa na Gen James Kabarebe , Minisitiri wa Ububanyi na Amahanga , Dr Vincent Biruta na Minisitiri wa Urubyiruko na Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi .
Gen James Kabarebe yabwiye uru rubyiruko ko urugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu rugikomeje kandi bakwiye kurugiramo uruhare .
Ati " " " " Murangije ibyiciro byose bya urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu , mwatangiriye Kagitumba , munyuze ku Mulindi kugera hano ku Nteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Icya ingezi mukwiye kumenya ni uko urugendo rwo Kubohora Igihugu rutarangirira hano ku Nteko Ishinga Amategeko rurakomeza kubera ko urugamba rwo kwibohora ubwarwo ni urugendo rukomeza . " " " "
" " " " Umusanzu muzatanga ku ruhande rwanyu nka urubyiruko nawo uzaba mu bigize uru rugendo rwo Kwibohora .
Nawo uzajya mu mateka ya iki gihugu nka umusanzu wanyu .
Kubera ko kwibohora bivuze impinduka mu bukungu na imibereho bya u Rwanda kandi ni urugendo rugikomeje ruzahererekanywa mu bisekuru . " " " "
Abajijwe na Gasore usanzwe utuye mu Bubiligi icyo bo nka urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga bakora kugira ngo barwanye abavuga Igihugu cyabo nabi , Gen Kabarebe yamubwiye ko buri cyiciro cya urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu cyagiye kigira imbogamizi zacyo kandi ko badakwiye gutegereza ko bahamagarwa kugira ngo batangire kurwanira
igihugu cyabo .
Ati " " " " Buri cyiciro cya urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu gifite imbogamizi cyihariye .
Icyiciro cya mbere cyo kubohora igihugu cyaranzwe no guhangana mu buryo bwa imbaraga , kurwana na abantu bafite intwaro . " " " "
" " " " Iki cyiciro cyo kwibohora gifite imbogamizi nyinshi zirimo na uko abagize uruhare muri Jenoside bakomeje kuvuga nabi Guverinoma bakoresheje imbuga nkoranyambaga kugira ngo gusa bavuge nabi Guverinoma . " " " "
Gen Kabarebe yakomeje avuga ko aho urugamba rugeze ubu ariho urubyiruko rwa u Rwanda rwaba uruba mu mahanga no mu gihugu rukenewe cyane .
Ati " " " " Muri iki cyiciro niho mugira uruhare nka urubyiruko kandi niho mwitezweho gutangira umusanzu kubera ko ntimubuze ibyo kuvuga , ntimubuze amakuru ajyanye na Igihugu cyanyu kuko niba hari igihugu gitanga amakuru kuri cyo ku bijyanye na ibyo cyagezeho , ibyo kiri gukorera abaturage ni u Rwanda .
Ku bwa ibyo amakuru arahari ariko icyo tutarabona ni urubyiruko rwacu rwinjira muri uru rugamba ngo rurwanire igihugu cyarwo rukoresheje imbuga abagisenya nabo bakoresha . " " " "
" " " " Bakoresha internet namwe murayifite , imbuga nkoranyambaga muba muziriho buri gihe .
Nta kintu na kimwe mubura kandi ntimugomba gutegereza guhamagarwa kugira ngo mubwirwe kurwanira igihugu cyanyu . " " " "
" " " " Oya murahari mugomba kuba mubikora ijoro na amanywa .
Bashyiraho ibinyoma ku gihugu cyanyu , muzi ukuri ku gihugu cyanyu kandi mushobora no kubaza , ubundi mu kinjira muri uru rugamba kandi mukarurwana mushyizeho umutima mukabatsinda .
Nimuvuge ibyiza muzaba mutumye abantu bamenya ibyiza . " " " "
Gen Kabarebe yavuze ko ikibazo u Rwanda ruri guhura na cyo cya abaruharabika na abagoreka amateka yarwo cyari cyitezwe kuko ngo nyuma yo gukora Jenoside abayikoze bakurikizaho kuyihakana .
Eric Ngabo ukuriye itsinda ryateguye iyi gahunda yo kuba urubyiruko rwava mu mahanga rukaza gusura u Rwanda yavuze ko iki gitekerezo ubwacyo cyaturutse mu rubyiruko barufasha kukinoza .
Ati " " " " Niba bagize igitekerezo baravuga bati urubyiruko ruba rushaka kujya gusura igihugu cyarwo bari hamwe nka itsinda .
Baravuga bati " " " " byaba byiza ariko urwo rugendo rugomba kuba rufite amasomo agamije kutwigisha amateka ya Igihugu , kutwereka ubwiza bwa Igihugu , ibibazo igihugu cyari gifite na uburyo byagiye bikemurwa . " " " " " " " "
Ngabo yavuze ko kuba urubyiruko rwahabwa amahirwe nka aya yo gusura igihugu bibaha ubumenyi bubafasha guhangana na abagoreka amateka ya u Rwanda .
Ati " " " " Guha urubyiruko amahirwe yo kuza kwirebera rukava mu byo rubwirwa gusa , biruha ubumenyi na ubushobozi bwo kuzahangana na bariya bavuga nabi u Rwanda kandi babeshya .
Nibo ba mbere bazadufasha mu kubwira ukuri abandi Banyarwanda bayobye cyangwa bayobejwe no kubatumira kuko turashaka ko iki kiba igikorwa ngarukamwaka . " " " "
Yavuze ko urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda ruba mu mahanga rugorwa no kumenya ukuri ku mateka ya igihugu cyarwo kuko aho baba haba hari amakuru avuga ibintu byinshi bitandukanye .
U Rwanda rugiye kohereza abasirikare na abapolisi 1000 muri Mozambique .
Cabo Delgado ni intara iri mu Majyaruguru ya Mozambique , ituwe na abaturage barenga miliyoni ebyiri bari ku buso bwa kilometero kare 82 . 625 .
Iri ku mupaka wa Tanzania ndetse ituwe na abaturage bo mu bwoko bwa aba - Makonde , Makua na Mwani .
Ibikorwa bya Guverinoma ya u Rwanda byo koherezayo ingabo muri iki gihugu bije nyuma ya ubusabe bwa Perezida wa Mozambique , Filipe Nyusi , wagiriye uruzinduko mu Rwanda muri Mata .
Kuva icyo gihe bivugwa ko u Rwanda rwahise rutangira kugenzura neza uko ikibazo cya umutekano muke na iterabwoba gihagaze muri ako gace .
Hari amakuru avuga ko rwahise rwoherezayo itsinda rigamije kureba uko byifashe .
Itangazo ryashyizwe ahagaragara na Guverinoma ya u Rwanda rivuga ko izi ngabo zizoherezwayo zizakorana na iza Mozambique cyo kimwe na iz Umuryango wa Iterambere rya Ibihugu byo mu Majyepfo ya Afurika , SADC .
Riti " " " " Uku kohereza ingabo gushingiye ku mubano mwiza hagati ya Repubulika ya u Rwanda na iya Mozambique , nyuma ya isinywa rya amasezerano ya ubufatanye atandukanye hagati ya ibihugu byombi mu 2018 kandi rishingiye ku bushake bwa u Rwanda ku mahame yo kurinda ( R2P ) na amasezerano yo mu 2015 ya Kigali yo kurinda abasivile . " " " "
Izi ngabo zigiye muri Mozambique nyuma ya ibiganiro hagati ya ibihugu byombi .
Muri Mata uyu mwaka , Perezida wa Mozambique , Filipe Nyusi yasuye u Rwanda aganira na Perezida Paul Kagame ku ngingo zitandukanye zirimo ubufatanye mu guhashya iterabwoba .
Ntabwo hatangajwe byinshi ku biganiro abakuru ba ibihugu byombi baganiriye , icyakora Perezida Nyusi yaje mu Rwanda mu gihe Mozambique yari imaze iminsi yibasiwe na ibitero bya iterabwoba bigabwa na umutwe ushamikiye ku mutwe wa iterabwoba wa ISIS ugendera ku mahame akaze ya kisilamu .
Nubwo ingabo za Leta zikomeje gutsinsura uwo mutwe mu Mujyi wa Palma mu Ntara ya Cabo Delgado iherereye mu Majyaruguru ya Mozambique , hari amagana ya abaturage bahitanwe na ibitero mu gihe abandi bavuye mu byabo .
Aka gace uwo mutwe ugabamo ibitero gakungahaye kuri gaz ndetse sosiyete ya Abafaransa , Total yashoye miliyari 20 za amadolari mu kubaka uruganda rwo gucukura iyo gaz .
Gusa nyuma ya ibitero , iyo sosiyete yatangaje ko ibaye ihagaritse uwo mushinga .
Mu bishwe muri ako gace harimo abanyamahanga ndetse ibikorwaremezo nka amabanki , amahoteli na ibindi na byo byarangiritse , bikaba byaratumye benshi bahagrika ibikorwa bahakoreraga .
Umujyi wa Palma wagabweho ibitero utuyemo abanyamahanga basaga 1000 bari mu bikorwa bifite aho bihuriye na icukurwa rya gaz .
Guhera mu 2017 , agace ka Cabo Delgado kagiye kibasirwa na ibitero bya imitwe ya iterabwoba rimaze guhitana ubuzima bwa abasaga 3000 mu gihe ibihumbi bya abaturage byahunze .
Mu kwezi gushize abakuru ba ibihugu bigize umuryango uhuza ibihugu byo muri Afurika ya Amajyepfo ( SADC ) , bahuriye i Maputo muri Mozambique baganira ku kibazo cya umutekano muke kiri mu Majyaruguru ya icyo gihugu .
Bemeje koherezayo umutwe wa SADC wa ingabo zishinzwe kurwana aho rukomeye ngo zifashe mu guhashya imitwe ya iterabwoba ikorera muri Cabo Delgado ishobora no gukwirakwira mu bindi bihugu byo mu karere idahagaritswe .
Inzira igejeje Ingabo za u Rwanda muri Mozambique
Mu Ukwakira 2017 , abagizi ba nabi bafitanye isano na umutwe wa Islamic State wo muri Iraq na uwitwa Levant ( ISIL ) batangiye kugaba ibitero mu gace ka Cabo Delgado muri Mozambique .
Rimwe na rimwe , abo barwanyi biyita al - Shabaab , nubwo nta sano na rito bafitanye na al - Shabaab yo muri Somalia .
Ingabo za Mozambique zimaze igihe zihangana na abo barwanyi gusa byatumye abasivili benshi bahunga iyo mirwano .
Abo barwanyi bagabye ibitero muri Kanama 2020 bafata Umujyi wa Mocimboa da Praia .
Muri Mata 2020 , abantu barenga 50 bishwe baciwe imitwe ndetse abagera kuri uwo mubare nanone bishwe muri ubwo buryo mu Ugushyingo 2020 .
Muri Nzeri 2020 , abarwanyi ba ISIL bagabye igitero ku kirwa cya Vamizi kiri ku Nyanja ya Abahinde .
Ku wa 24 Werurwe 2021 , aba barwanyi bafashe Umujyi wa Palma , bica na abaturage mu gihe abarenga 35 . 000 bya abaturage 75 . 000 bawutuyemo bavuye mu byabo .
Minisitiri Biruta na Mbabazi bahanuye urubyiruko rwa Abanyarwanda ruba mu mahanga .
Abayobozi barimo Minisitiri wa Urubyiruko , Rosemary Mbabazi na Minisitiri wa Ubabanyi na Amahanga , Dr Vincent Biruta na Umujyanama wa Perezida Kagame mu bya umutekano , Gen James Kabarebe ; baganirije urubyiruko rwa abanyarwanda ruba mu mahanga .
Kuri uyu wa 9 Nyakanga 2021 nibwo itsinda rya urubyiruko rutuye mu mahanga rumaze iminsi mu ruzinduko mu Rwanda ryagiranye ibiganiro na abayobozi batandukanye .
Iri tsinda rigezwe na abagera kuri 60 baturutse mu bihugu byiganjemo ibyo ku Mugabane wa u Burayi nka u Bubiligi , u Bufaransa na u Budage .
Uretse abakomoka ku babyeyi bose ba Abanyarwanda , iri tsinda ririmo na abavanze .
Ni ukuvuga abafite umubyeyi umwe wa Umunyarwanda .
Mu minsi bamaze mu Rwanda basuye ibikorwa bitandukanye byiganjemo ibifite amateka yihariye mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu .
Nyuma yo gusura aha hantu hatandukanye , babonanye na abayobozi bakuru ba igihugu kugira ngo babaganirize ku cyerekezo cya u Rwanda .
Minisitiri Biruta yashimiye uru rubyiruko kubera umuhate rwagize wo gusura u Rwanda ngo rumenye amateka ya aho rukomoka .
Ati " " " " Ndashaka kubashimira ku bwa uyu muhate mwagize wo kuza hano mugasura u Rwanda na ahantu ha umwihariko hafitanye isano na urugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu .
Nka urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga , aho abenshi muri mwe mutazi u Rwanda ni byiza ko mugira aya mahirwe yo kuza mugasura Igihugu cyanyu ndetse mukamenya amateka yacyo . " " " "
Yabagaragarije ko nyuma ya ibibazo u Rwanda rwanyuzemo ubu ruri mu bihugu biri kwitwara neza mu bintu bitandukanye birimo korohereza ubucuruzi .
Ati " " " " Biturutse aha muzabasha kubona ibyo mukeneye byose ngo muganire na bagenzi banyu batabashije kuzana namwe kandi muzabasha kubabwira byinshi bitari gusa urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu ahubwo na intambwe iki gihugu cyateye kuva mu 1994 . " " " "
" " " " Niba mwarabashije gusura ibindi bihugu bya Afurika mwabonye ko u Rwanda ruri gukora neza kurusha ibyinshi muri ibyo bihugu bitanyuze mu bikomeye nka ibyo twanyuzemo .
Twanyuze muri Jenoside mu 1994 ariko twabashije kubaka igihugu no kugera kuri byinshi . " " " "
" " " " Murabizi ko u Rwanda ruza imbere mu nzego zitandukanye , mu bijyanye no korohereza ishoramari , mu buzima , hari inzego nyinshi aho u Rwanda ruza imbere kurusha bimwe mu bihugu bya Afurika bitagize Jenoside cyangwa andi makimbirane . " " " "
Yabasabye gukomeza kugaragaza indangagaciro za Abanyarwanda aho baba hose kandi bagahangana na abakomeje guharabika igihugu bavuga ibitari byo .
Ati " " " " Murabizi hari uburyo bwinshi bwo kureba u Rwanda uturutse mu mahanga , mubana na abantu bari ku mbuga nkoranyambaga birirwa bangiza isura ya u Rwanda kandi buri gihe bagerageza kubona ibintu bibi ku gihugu nubwo byaba bidahari . " " " "
" " " " Kandi bumva ko bifashishije uburenganzira bwo gutanga ibitekerezo nka uko bivugwa na ibyo bihugu mubamo .
Bari kubukoresha nabi bumva ko ari byiza kuvuga ibinyoma ku gihugu cyawe , abayobozi bacyo bakumva ko ibyo biri mu bigize uburenganzira bwo gutanga ibitekerezo . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ariko nka Abanyarwanda dukwiye kuguma ku ndangagaciro zacu .
Tugomba kuvuga ko u Rwanda ari igihugu cyacu kandi dufite indangagaciro zo gukunda igihugu , indangagaciro ya ubunyangamugayo kandi dukwiye gutanga umusanzu mu kubaka igihugu .
Tugomba kuvuguruza aba bantu bumva ko gusebya igihugu ari demokarasi . " " " "
Yabasabye ko iki gikorwa batangiye cyo kugaruka bagasura igihugu cyabo cyazakomeza kandi bakarushaho kongera umubare wa abacyitabira .
Minisitiri Rosemary Mbabazi we yagaragarije uru rubyiruko bimwe mu bigize umuco wa u Rwanda .
Yababwiye ko mu gihe kinini cyashize Abanyarwanda bibonaga mu moko ya Abahutu , Abatutsi na Abatwa yemeza ko ariko ubu bose bibona nka Abanyarwanda binyuze muri Ndi Umunyarwanda .
Ati " " " " Imwe mu ndangagaciro zacu ni Ndi Umunyarwanda , murabizi mu myaka 27 ishize twitwaga Abahutu , Abatutsi , Abatwa aho kuba Abanyarwanda , niba ushaka gukomezanya Ubuhutu , Ubututsi na Ubutwa nta gaciro bifite , icya ingenzi ni uko uri Umunyarwanda .
Iki ni cyo kituranga kandi kikaduhuza , ni yo sano muzi . " " " "
Louise usanzwe utuye mu Bubiligi akaba na umwe mu bagize iri tsinda rya urubyiruko yavuze ko aya ari amahirwe yagize yo kumenya byinshi kuri politike ya igihugu cye ngo kuko aho aba atabasha kuyibonaho amakuru cyane .
Umwihariko mu birori bya imideli ya " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " ( Amafoto ) .
Ibi birori bya imideli byari byiswe " " " " Made in Rwanda Fashion Night Out " " " " byateguwe na abahanzi ba imideli bitabiriye imurikagurisha rya ibyakorewe mu Rwanda .
Aba bahanzi bagamije guteza imbere imideli yahangiwe mu Rwanda ndetse no kuzamura ireme rya abakora uyu mwuga bakamenyekana ku rwego mpuzamahanga .
Imideli yerekanywe irimo amakanzu , amashati , amapantaro , inkweto , ibikapu byo mu moko yose , ingofero na imirimbo inyuranye byose bikorerwa mu Rwanda .
Iyi mideli yakorewe mu Rwanda muri Sonia Mugabo , Uzi Collections , Inzuki Designs , Inkanda , Moshions , Haute Baso , Made in Kigali , Rwanda Clothing ndetse na Rupari Designs .
Ibi birori byabereye ahasanzwe habera imurikagurisha i Gikondo gusa kuri iyi nshuro abamurikabikorwa baryitabiriye ni abacuruza ibyakorewe mu Rwanda gusa [ Made in Rwanda ] .
Byari umwihariko ugereranyije na ibindi birori byo kumurika imideli bisanzwe bimenyerewe mu Rwanda kuko abanyamideli bambaraga imideli mu mok anyuranye hanyuma bagahagarara mu matsinda hanyuma abaje kureba ibirori bakabazengurukamo bareba imideli baje kumurika ubishoboye agahita agura .
Aba bahanzi ba imideli kandi bari bazanye imyenda , imitako na ibindi basanzwe bakora ku buryo ibirori byabaye bibangikanye na igikorwa cyo gusobanurira abari baje kwihera ijisho umwihariko wa buri nzu ya imideli .
Sonia Mugabo umwe mu bahanzi ba imideli bitabiriye iki gikorwa yabwiye IGIHE ko " " " " byamusigiye isomo ryiza no kurushaho kugira umuhate mu byo akora . " " " "
Ati " " " " Ibikorwa nka ibi byerekana ko Abanyarwanda baturi inyuma kandi ko bashaka kwambara ibintu byakorewe mu Rwanda , natwe biradusunika cyane ngo turusheho gukora cyane kandi byiza . " " " "
Yongeraho ati " " " " Ibi byerekana ko nshyigikiye gahunda ya leta yo guteza imbere Made in Rwanda , kandi bishimangira ko turi muri gahunda nziza yo kwishakira imirimo .
Nkanjye natangiye ndi umwe ariko ubu tumaze kuba abantu icumi . " " " "
Yavuze ko nyuma ya iri murikagurisha agiye gufungura iduka rinini muri Marriot Hotel mu kurushaho kwagura ibikorwa bye .
Ati " " " " Nyuma ya hano ngiye guhita mfungura iduka rindi muri Marriot Hotel , ni ugushyiramo ingufu tugakora cyane . . . " " " "
Ibi birori bibaye nyuma ya igihe gito habaye ikindi gikorwa kinini cyahurije hamwe abahanzi ba imideli bibanda cyane ku yakorewe mu Rwanda bibumbiye muri ikompanyi Collective Rw ari nayo benshi muri aba bamuritse ibikorwa byabo babarizwamo .
Iri murikagurisha rya ibikorerwa mu Rwanda ribaye ku nshuro ya kabiri , ryitabiriwe na abanshoramari bari mu byiciro bitandukanye birimo , abakora ibijyanye na u bwubatsi , ubuhinzi na ubworozi , imyenda , ibikoresho bya isuku , ubukorikori , abatanga servise mu ikoranabuhanga na ibindi .
Imurikagurisha rya uyu mwaka ku bikorerwa mu Rwanda rifite insanganyamatsiko igira iti " " " " Duharanire kwigira duhaha ibya iwacu . " " " "
Ubwiza bwa imideli ya Nyambo , umusore ukomeje kurimbisha abantu muri Afurika ya Epfo .
Masa Mara ni izina yahimbye , aryita inzu ye ya imideli arikomeye ku ijambo amamara .
Ubuhanzi bwa imideli bwo bwamukuriyemo kuko sekuru yari umudozi mu gihe nyina yacuruzaga ibitenge .
Nyambo wa imyaka 30 amaze imyaka irenga itanu akora akazi ko guhanga imideli gusa gutangira byaramugoye kubera ubushobozi buke .
Ati " " " " Byakomotse kuba naratangiye guhanga imyambaro nta mafaranga mfite icyo nari mfite icyo nari mfite ni inkuru nashakaga gusangiza abantu ndetse na uburyo bwo kongera kuvuga inkuru nyazo za Afurika . " " " "
" " " " Natangiye guhanga imideli mu 2012 ubwo nari ndi kurangiza kaminuza muri University of South Africa . " " " "
Avuga ko yisanze mu ruhando rwo guhanga imideli mu buryo atabitekerezaga gusa ko bitamutunguye kuko yakuze akunda gusa neza no kwitandukanya na abandi cyane .
Ati " " " " Bityo igihe cyose nageragezaga gutandukana na abandi ku kigo nigagaho bituma abantu benshi bashaka kumenya ikibintera mu kubasubiza byabaye ngombwa ko ntangira kwibaza aho iyo mpano ituruka nza gusanga mbikomora kuri sogokuru wari umudozi bikubirataho kuba narakuriye mu bitenge kuko aribyo mama yacuruzaga bituma ndushaho
gushaka kumenya byinshi ku bijyanye na imideli aribwo natangiye kwiyigisha bimviramo no gutangiza Masa Mara . " " " "
Avuga guhanga imideli kwe yibanda ku muco nyafurika no kwerekana isura nyayo ya abanyafurika , mu buryo bwo gukundisha abanyafurika ibya iwabo na abo baribo .

Amaze imyaka itanu yitabira ibirori byo kumurika imideli bitandukanye muri Afurika ya Epfo , nka South Africa Mena s Wear Fashion Week , Africa Exchange Fashion ihuza abahanga imideli baturuka mu bihugu bitandukanye , Africa Fashion International na ibindi bitandukanye .
Paul Van Doren watangije sosiyete ya inkweto zizwi nka Vans yitabye Imana .
Inkuru ya urupfu rwa uyu mugabo watangije sosiyete ikigarurira Isi nyuma yo gucikiza amashuri yisumbuye , yatangajwe ku wa 7 Gicurasi 2021 .
Ubutumwa yanditse bugira buti " " " " Na agahinda kenshi , Vans iramenyesha ko umwe mu bayishinze yitabye Imana .
Paul ntiyari rwiyemezamirimo , yari umunyadushya . " " " "
Paul Van Doren wavukiye i Boston muri Leta ya Massachusetts mu 1930 , yatangije Vans mu myaka ya 1960 afatanyije na murumuna we Jimmy Van Doren na abandi babiri .
Iduka rya urwo ruganda rya mbere ryafunguriye imiryango mu Mujyi wa Anaheim muri Leta ya California mu 1966 , abagera kuri 12 bahita bagura izo nkweto ku munsi wa mbere .
Vans zaje kwambarwa na Sean Penn ubwo yakinaga muri filimi yakunzwe cyane yitwa " " " " Fast Times at Ridgemont High ; " " " " igaragaza ubuzima bwo kuryoshya bwa abanyeshuri bo mu Majyepfo ya California , burimo inkundo , umuziki na ibindi bya irari nka imibonano mpuzabitsina no gukoresha ibiyobyabwenge .
Nyuma ya iyo filimi zakunzwe kurushaho , ugasanga imihanda yose ni zo zambawe haba ku rubyiruko , abanyamuziki na abamurika imideli .
Paul Van Doren yakomeje kuyobora iyo sosiyete kugeza mu 1980 ubwo yajyaga mu kiruhuko cya izabukuru akayishyira mu maboko ya Jimmy Van Doren , ariko iza guhomba bituma afata umwanzuro wo kugaruka kuyiyoborera .
Mu 1988 Vans yaragurishijwe , magingo aya iri mu maboko ya Ikigo cya Abanyamerika cyibanda ku nkweto , VF Corporation , gisanzwe kinafite izindi sosiyete za amazina akomeye nka Supreme , Timberland , Dickies , The North Face na Jansport .
Bivugwa ko ubu Vans imaze kugira amaduka 300 hirya no hino ku Isi .
Mbere ya uko Paul Van Doren atabaruka yari aherutse kumurika igitabo kigaruka ku buzima bwe yise " " " " A Memoir by the Founder of Vans " " " " gikubiyemo amakuru ya ubuzima yaciyemo na uko urwo ruganda rwakuze .
Inkweto za Vans zikoze mu buryo zishobora kuba zizamuye ku buryo zigera hejuru ya utubombambari cyangwa zikagera munsi yatwo .
Ni zimwe mu zikundwa cyane na abanyamideli , abahanzi na abandi ba abasirimu bambara ibikeye .
Uburyo bugezweho bwo kwisiga " " " " makeup " " " " ku bakunda gusa neza ( Amafoto na Video ) .
Makeup ikundwa cyane na igitsina gore , ariko na abagabo barayikoresha kuko hari byinshi yongera ku isura bituma uyikoresheje arushaho gusa neza .
Hari benshi bifuza gusa neza ariko bakabura aho bamenera kuko badafite ubumenyi mu bijyanye na " " " " makeup . " " " "
Gusa kubyiga ntibisaba ibihambaye kuko wanifashisha amashusho ukabyiga ukabimenya .
Mu kiganiro na Kenneth umaze kwamamara mu gusiga ibirungo bya ubwiza nka Trendy Shadow , yagaragaje ukuntu buri wese ashobora kwisiga " " " " makeup " " " " arebeye ku mashusho akazabimenya .
Ati " " " " Ubundi niba ushaka kujya wisiga " " " " makeup , " " " " ugomba kubanza kugura ibikoresho bya ibanze , iyo ubifite ushobora kujya ku muntu akakwigisha cyangwa ukabyigira kuri YouTube .
Icyo gihe ibyo bakoze uko ubisubiramo niko ubimenya cyane . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko kwisiga " " " " makeup " " " " bifite ikintu kinini byongera ku gusa neza ka umuntu , ari yo mpamvu uwifuza gukomeza gusa neza aba akwiye kubiharira umwanya .
Ati " " " " Makeup ifite ikintu kinini cyane yongera kuko uruhu rurushaho gusa neza iyo warusize , hari ubwo usiga amaso usanzwe ugira mato akaba manini akaba na umweru bitewe na ibyo wasizeho .
Muri rusange makeup igira ikintu kinini yongera ku buryo umuntu asa . " " " "
" " " " Makeup " " " " ibamo amoko atandukanye bitewe na aho umuntu agiye na icyo agiye gukora .
Mu mashusho , Trendy Shadow yerekana uburyo wakwisiga " " " " makeup " " " " ukajya ku kazi , mu bukwe , gutembera na ahandi hantu hatandukanye usa na bicye .
Mu kwisiga " " " " makeup , " " " " icya ibanze ugomba kwitaho ni ibikoresho ndetse na isuku yabyo .
Mbere ya byose ubanza koga mu maso warangiza ugasigaho amavuta yabugenewe atuma ya " " " " makeup " " " " itinjira mu ruhu imbere .
Iyo umaze kuyasigaho ukurikizaho gukora ibitsike na amaso , usigaho " " " " tiro " " " " ituma mu maso harushaho kugaragara neza , hejuru ya amaso usigaho " " " " mascara " " " " zituma amaso asa na ayabaye manini ndetse akanarushaho kuba umweru .
Ikindi cya ibanze ni ukwisiga neza ku ruhu aho ukoresha " " " " fond de teint " " " " cyangwa " " " " face powder , " " " " ariko biba byiza kubivanga kuko bituma uruhu rworoha kandi rukumuka .
Ibi byose iyo ubisoje usiga iminwa " " " " lipstick " " " " kugira ngo itumagara .
Mu kiganiro na Trendy Shadow , uramenya byinshi kuri Kenneth ndetse unarebe birambuye uburyo " " " " makeup " " " " ikorwa bikaryohera amaso .
Inkweto za Nike Kanye West yambaye mu 2008 zaciye agahigo ko kugurishwa akayabo .
zi nkweto zakozwe na uruganda rwa Nike zaguzwe mu buryo bwihariye na sosiyete ya RARES .
Uyu ni umuyoboro ushora imari mu kugura no kugurisha imigabane .
Umuyobozi wa iki kigo , Gerome Sapp , yavuze ko babikoze bashaka kugura inkweto zihenze mu mateka .
Umuyobozi wa Sothbeya s , Brahm Wachter , yari yashyize ku isoko izi nkweto yavuze ko kuba zaguzwe aka kayabo bigaragaza ibigwi bya Kanye West mu bijyanye no kurimba ndetse no mu bahanga inkweto za Sneakers .
Izi nkweto zashyizwe hanze nyuma ya imyaka 13 zambawe bwa mbere , zashyizwe ku isoko mu cyamunara yitwa Sothebya s .
Izi nkweto zifite nimero 12 , zibaye iza mbere zo mu bwoko bwa Sneakers zigurishijwe amafaranga menshi , zihita zikura ku mwanya wa mbere iza Nike Air Jordan zambawe bwa mbere na Michael Jordan mu 1985 , zagurishijwe mu 2020 agera ku bihumbi 615 $ .
Nike Air Yeezy za Kanye West zifite ibara rya umukara zakozwe mu 2007 , ishusho yazo yakozwe na Kanye West ubwe afatanyije na Mark Smith wo muri Nike .
Brahm Wachter , umukozi muri Sothbeya s yavuze ko izi nkweto za Kanye West zakunzwe cyane ku buryo byatumye abasaba uburenganzira bwo kuzikora baba benshi , bituma zandika amateka . " " " "
Ni zo nkweto za mbere Nike yari ikoranye na umuhanzi , mu gihe ubusanzwe uru ruganda rwamenyekanye cyane mu gukora inkweto rukunda kugirana ubufatanye bwo gukora inkweto na abakinnyi cyane aba Basketball .
Kanye West yazambaye bwa mbere mu bihembo bya Grammy Awards mu 2008 .
Turahirwa abinyujije mu mideli yahaye icyubahiro Umwamikazi Gicanda .
Uyu mudeli ukozwe mu gishushanyo cya isura ya Umwamikazi Gicanda , cyikaba cyiganjemo amabara ya umukara , umweru , umuhondo na icyatsi kibisi .
Rosalie Gicanda niwe mwamikazi wa nyuma wa u Rwanda akaba yari umugore w " " " " Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa , ari mu nzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi 1994 .
Gicanda yishwe ku wa 20 Mata 1994 azira ko ari Umututsi .
Mu kumuha agaciro no kumwibuka we na abandi bagore ba inzirakarengane bazize Jenoside , Turahirwa yakoze umudeli ugaragaza isura ye .
Mu kiganiro Turahirwa Moses , yagiranye na IGIHE , yavuze ko gukora uyu mudeli byamufashe amasaha 48 agira ngo yerekane uruhare rwa abahanzi mu kwibuka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi 1994 .
Ati " " " " Mu gihe twibuka abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi 1994 , natekereje ku ruhare rwa abahanzi mu ngeri zose .
Mu kuzirikana abavukijwe ubuzima .
Nakoze uyu mudeli mu kwerekana uko twakunamira abishwe binyuze mu gihangano . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko uyu mudeli yawukoze mu buryo bwa ikoranabuhanga ariko buzimije bufite ubutumwa butanga .
Ati " " " " Byamfashe amasaha 48 kuko gushushanya Umwamikazi bisaba ubushishozi na ubwitonzi bukarishye .
Nakoresheje uburyo bugezweho kugira ngo ishusho isohoke ijimije ariko ifite ubusobanuro bwimbitse . " " " "
Uyu mudeli ukozwe mu gishushanyo kigaragaza isura ya Umwamikazi Gicanda , Turahirwa yavuze ko yamuhisemo kuko ari umugore wa icyitegererezo , buri wese yashima kugira nka umubyeyi we .
Ati " " " " Umwamikazi Gicanda yari azwi cyane kandi yarakunzwe na benshi .
Yafatwaga nka icyitegererezo mu bwiza , ubuntu na ikinyabupfura .
Usanga kandi ababuze ababyeyi babo muri Jenoside , bagaruka ku myitwarire nka iyi yaranze Umwamikazi . " " " "
" " " " Nahisemo rero kwifashisha isura buri munyarwandakazi yakwibonamo , ariko nanone ishingiye ku muco dusangiye .
Buri mwari na umutegarugori wazize Jenoside ni Umwamikazi mu buryo bumwe cyangwa ubundi . " " " "
Abicishiej ku mbuga nkoranyambaga ze yavuze ko uyu mudeli utazigera ucapwa cyangwa ngo ube wagurishwa , akaba yasobanuye ko iki ari igihangano yakoze kigamije kunamira abazize Jenoside nta nyungu za amafaranga ategerejemo .
Ati " " " " Kiriya gishushanyo ndetse na ijipo .
Nabikoze mu buryo bwo kunamira abazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi . " " " "
" " " " Nta nyungu ya amafaranga igamijwe .
Ahubwo nifuza ko byatera abandi imbaraga zo gukoresha impano zabo mu kuganira ku mahano yakozwe .
Ariko bya akarusho , bagakoresha ubumenyi mu kubika amateka , bakayarinda kuzima cyangwa kugorekwa . " " " "
