Imyambaro iheruka iyi nzu yashyize hanze ni iyo bise " " " " Ishuri Collection " " " " yasohotse muri 2020 .
Chimano wa Sauti Sol yagaragaye mu mashusho ya indirimbo yambaye umwambaro ya Tanga Designs .
Uyu mwambaro uri mu yo aherutse gushyira hanze yise " " " " Ikamba Collection " " " " ariko wo ukaba uri mu ya abahungu .
Chimano yagaragaye yambaye uyu mwambaro mu ndirimbo nshya iheruka kujya hanze yasubiranyemo na umuhanzikazi wo muri Zimbabwe witwa Gemma Griffiths yitwa " " " " Easy . " " " "
Niyitanga Olivier yabwiye IGIHE ko kugira ngo umwambaro we wifashishwe muri iyi ndirimbo ariko uyu muhanzi yawubonye ku mbuga nkoranyambaga akawukunda akamusaba ko yawumukorera .
Ati " " " " Yakunze ibihangano byanjye ku mbuga nkoranyambaga , noneho mvugana na uwabikora kugira ngo mbone ibipimo bye bya nyabyo .
Ndawushushanya nyuma nza kuwukora . " " " "
Niyitanga aherutse kubwira IGIHE ko " " " " Ikamba Collection " " " " yagize igitekerezo cyayo mu bihe bya Miss Rwanda 2020 .
Ngo yayise gutyo kuko buri wese wahatanaga yari afite amahirwe yo gutsinda akegukana ikamba .
Iyi myambaro mu buryo ikozwemo , ijyanishwa na ibyitwa " " " " Ibyanganga " " " " byambarwa mu mutwe , biba biriho amasaro .
Biba bisa na umwitero wo ku ikanzu iba imeze nka umushanana .
Igaragaza umuco wa u Rwanda .
Mu ikamba Collection harimo amakanzu ya abakobwa yiswe " " " " Umutanana . " " " "
Kuyita gutya byaturutse na ubundi ku izina rya Tanga yahuje na umushanana .
Umutanana ni ikanzu igizwe na imitako igiye itandukanye ku buryo umuntu ashobora kukubona akagira ngo wambaye umushanana ariko yakwitegereza agasanga ari ikanzu .
Ifite nayo ibyanganga byayo .
Muri iyi myambaro harimo imeze nka imikenyero ariko ifite amababa ya ibinyugunyugu , ndetse na andi mababa .
Avuga ko impamvu yahisemo kurimbisha iyi myambaro amababa yiganjemo aya ibinyugunyugu ari uko utu dusimba tugira umwihariko wo kutajya dupfa ahubwo tugenda twihinduramo ibindi binyabuzima tugakomeza kuba ku Isi .
Niyitanga amaze kwambika ibyamamare bitandukanye mu Rwanda no hanze yarwo .
Ubwo Mr Eazi yakoreraga igitaramo mu Rwanda mu 2017 yari yambaye imyambaro ye .
Ni nawe ukunze kwambika ba nyampinga mu bihe bitandukanye .
Yari aherutse gushyira hanze imyambaro yise " " " " Out Of This World TangaSS21 . " " " "
Reba indirimbo Chimano aba yambayemo umwambaro wa Tanga Designs .
Imvano yo guhanga imideli kwa Umutoniwase urajwe ishinga no guteza imbere " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " ( Amafoto ) .
Abahanga imideli bavuka umunsi ku wundi bigatuma imyambaro ikorerwa mu Rwanda igenda iba myinshi kandi ari ubwoko butandukanye ku buryo ntacyo umuntu yaburana abahanga imideli mu Rwanda .
Mu bashya bakwiriye guhangwa amaso harimo umukobwa witwa Umutoniwase Brenda washinze inzu ya BrenFashion , wa imyaka 24 na we umaze igihe kitari kinini cyane yinjiye ku isoko ryo guhanga imyambaro .
Uyu mukobwa avuga ko ari ibintu abona bimaze kugira agaciro gakomeye mu Rwanda kuko abanyarwanda basigaye baterwa ishema na ibikorerwa iwabo .
Ati " " " " Maze imyaka ibiri gusa ntangiye guhanga imyambaro mu buryo bwa umwuga .
Ni byiza kugeza ubu kuko abanyarwanda ntabwo bagifite imitekerereze yo kwambara imyambaro yo hanze ahubwo bwose baba batewe ishema na ibikorerwa iwabo . " " " "
Yavuze ko ubusanzwe ari umudozi akaba akorana na abandi bakozi batatu bamufasha kuko atari yamara kwagura ibikorwa bye uko abyifuza , ariko akemeza ko ariho bigana .
Ati " " " " Ubusanzwe ndi umudozi .
Nakuze mbikunda ndetse numva ko nimara gusoza amashuri nzahanga imyambaro .
Nkora imyambaro yose yaba iya abakobwa na abagabo .
Nahisemo gukora imyambaro kuko ari ibintu nakundaga kandi mbona nshoboye .
Mpitamo kubikora kugira ngo ndusheho kuzanira abanyarwanda ibintu byiza kandi bikorewe iwacu . " " " "
Iyo abajijwe umwihariko asubiza ko ari uko ahanga imideli mishya adakuye ahandi , akavuga ko afite intego ikomeye yo guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda .
Ati " " " " Intego yanjye ni uguteza imbere imyambaro myiza ikorerwa mu Rwanda tunajyana hanze ya u Rwanda . " " " "
BrenFashion ya Umutoniwase Brenda ije nyuma ya izindi nzu za imideli zimaze kubaka izina mu Rwanda za ab igitsinagore , zirimo " " " " Joyce Fashion Designs " " " " ya Uwamahoro Joyce , Rupari Designs ya Rupari Cynthia , Sonia Mugabo , Mugeni Diane washinze Mundi Designs , Joselyne Umutoniwase watangije Rwanda Clothing na abandi batandukanye .
Umwaka Umujyi wa Kigali wahangiweho wahawe umwihariko ku myambaro ya KGL ( Amafoto ) .
Ubu imyaka 114 irashize Kigali ibayeho , amateka yayo ni mareremare gusa uwayigezemo wese anyurwa na isuku na umutekano biwuranga bigatuma atifuza gutaha .
Buri Munyarwanda wese atewe ishema no kugira umurwa mukuru mwiza nka uyu , bigatuma iteka ahora ashishikajwe no kuwushakira icyawuteza imbere no kuwurinda ngo hatagira ikiwuhungabanya .
Mu barinzi ba Umujyi harimo na Kigali Guardian For Life ( KGL ) , ikirango cya urubyiruko rwibumbiye mu itsinda ryitwa Dawn Central Investment Bureau ( DCIB ) rikora imyambaro itandukanye .
Iki kigo gikora imyambaro ariko igaruka ku mateka na ubwiza bwa Umujyi wa Kigali , kuri ubu bahisemo gusohora iriho umwaka wa 1907 .
Abadasobanukiwe na amateka bagira ngo uyu mubare ni umurimbo washyizwe kuri iyi myambaro , ariko ufite byinshi usobanuye ku mateka ya Kigali n " " " " u Rwanda muri rusange .
Hasohotse ingofero ziri mu mabara atandukanye zanditseho imibare minini ya 1907 nka umwaka Kigali yahangiweho , inyuma hari inyuguti nto za KGL nka ikirango cya iyi myambaro ndetse ku mpande hariho DCIB igaragaza iki kigo .
Umwe mu bayobozi ba DCIB , Habimana Félix , yabwiye IGIHE ko gukomeza kwibanda ku myambaro igaragaza Kigali ari ubutumwa bashaka gutanga ndetse no kurushaho kuyimenyekanisha .
Ati " " " " Igituma dukomeza kwibanda ku myambaro igaragaza Kigali ni ubutumwa dushaka guha urubyiruko kugira ngo barusheho kurinda umujyi , kandi ni no guteza imbere ubukerarugendo no kumenyekanisha amateka yawo . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko izi ngofero ziriho umwaka Kigali yabereyeho zakiriwe neza ku isoko kuko hari abakunda ibidafite amagambo , ubu bakaba babonye iriho imibare kandi igaragaza Kigali .
Ati " " " " Abantu bazakiriye neza ku isoko kuko hari abadakunda ingofero ziriho amagambo , ubu babona iziriho imibare kandi zisobanuye byinshi kuri Kigali bakazikunda .
Urumva ko ubu abantu bafite amahitamo atandukanye . " " " "
KGL imaze imyaka ine ikora ikaba yaratangiriye ku ngofero ebyiri gusa none ubu bafite ubushobozi bwo kugira iduka ririmo imyambaro itandukanye irimo ingofero za ubwoko butandukanye , imipira ndetse na inkweto .
Nike yatsinze ikirego cyo guhagarika inkweto ziswe " " " " Satan " " " " zikozwe mu maraso ya abantu .
Izi nkweto zikozwe mu mabara ya umukara na umutuku zakozwe ku bufatanye bwa ikigo MSCH na umuhanzi Lil Nas X . Ziriho amagambo yo muri Bibiliya muri Luka 10 : 18 ahanditse ngo " " " " Nabonye Satani avuye mu ijuru , agwa asa na umurabyo . " " " "
Nike ikimara kubona izi nkweto zarakozwe higanywe izayo , yahise ishyikiriza urukiko rwa i New York ikirego , isaba ko izi nkweto zahagarikwa gucuruza kuko nta ruhare yagize mu ikorwa ryazo bikaba bishobora guteza urujijo ku isoko .
Kuri uyu wa Kane urukiko rwanzuye ko izi nkweto zitongera gucuruzwa , gusa uyu mwanzuro ukaba uteye urujijo kuko na ubundi hari hasohotse imiguru 666 yose ihita ishira .
Buri muguru wa izi nkweto waguzwe amadolari 1 . 018 , kandi zari ziriho ikirango cya Nike , umusaraba , akamenyetso ka Pentagone na imirongo itukura yakozwe mu bitonyanga bya amaraso byatanzwe na bamwe mu bagize iki kigo cyazikoze .
Ku ruhande rwa abanyamategeko ba MSCHF bo bavugaga ko izi nkweto 666 atari ubwoko bushya bashyize ku isoko ahubwo ko ari igihangano cya ubugeni bakoze kigenewe abantu bake .
Inkweto ziswe Satani zatangiye guteza impagarara ku wa Mbere ubwo hasohokaga indirimbo ya umuhanzi Lil Nas X yise Montero ( Call Me By Your Name ) , imugaragaza ari ku cyuma cyikaraga ava mu ijuru ajya ikuzimu bigaragaza ya magambo yo muri Luka 10 : 18 .
Zikimara gusohoka zahise ziteza impagarara ku mbuga nkoranyambaga abantu batandukanye bagaragaza ko uku ari ugusebya abakirisitu .
Muri bo harimo Guverineri wa Leta ya South Dakota , Kristi Noem , wavuze ko ibyakozwe kuri izi nkweto ari amarorerwa .
Inkweto ziswe Satani zikoze mu maraso ya umuntu zateje ururondogoro .
Izi nkweto zikozwe mu mabara ya umukara na umutuku zakozwe ku bufatanye bwa ikigo MSCH na umuhanzi Lil Nas X . Ziriho amagambo yo muri Bibiliya muri Luka 10 : 18 ahanditse ngo " " " " Nabonye Satani avuye mu ijuru , agwa asa na umurabyo . " " " "
Ziriho ikirango cya Nike , umusaraba , akamenyetso ka pentagone na imirongo itukura yakozwe mu bitonyanga bya amaraso byatanzwe na bamwe mu bagize iki kigo kiri kuzicuruza .
Izi nkweto zasohotse kuri uyu wa Mbere hasohorwa imiguru 666 buri umwe ugura amadolari 1 . 018 , ariko mu gihe gito zari zashize ku isoko .
Nike imaze kubona ko hari abiganye ikirango cyayo , yatanze ikirego mu rukiko rwa i New York , ko rwabuza MSCHF gukomeza gucuruza izi nkweto kuko zishobora guteza urujijo mu bakiliya bayo bacyeka ko aribo bazikoze .
Bagize bati " " " " Nta bufatanye buri hagati ya Nike na MSCHF mu gukora inkweto za satani , izi bakoze zishobora guteza urujijo ku isoko ryacu abantu batekereza ko hari uruhare twagize mu ikorwa ryazo . " " " "
Izi nkweto zagaragaye bwa mbere mu ndirimbo nshya ya Lil Nas X yitwa Montero ( Call Me By Your Name ) , yari yabanje gutangazwa ku wa Gatanu .
Muhire watangije " " " " Inkanda House " " " " ihanga imyambaro yavuze uko " " " " Gourmette " " " " zambarwaga mu muco nyarwanda .
Ni mu kiganiro Muhire yagiranye Urusaro Carine cyari gifite umutwe ugira uti " " " " Imyambarire yo hambere mu iterambere rya Made in Rwanda " " " " aho aba bombi baganiriye ku ruhare rwa inzu ndangamurage mu gufasha bamwe mu bahanzi ba imideli .
Muhire yavuze ko imyumvire ku myambaro ikorerwa mu Rwanda imaze kugenda ihinduka bitewe ahanini na uko na Leta yabigizemo uruhare igaca imyambaro ya Caguwa .
Ati " " " " Kuba imyumvire igenda ihinduka ku bijyanye na imyambaro ikorerwa mu Rwanda ni intambwe ikomeye tugenda dutera .
Tukiza mu mwuga wo kudoda imyambaro nta kibazo twari dufite cya icyo kubona ibyo twifashisha mu guhanga imyambaro ariko ubu kubera ko twabaye benshi hari igihe bibaho .
Gusa , hari ibyo dufite twifashisha byo mu bihingwa , hari amagweja akora ubudodo dufite ibyo twifashisha bikorerwa inaha , ndetse hari na umusore wo mu Rwanda ukora ibipesu mu mahembe hari na ibiva hanze . " " " "
Yabajijwe niba abona ingoro ndangamurage ari ahantu umuntu yavoma ibintu byiza byamufasha gukora ibintu byiza nka ibyo akora undi mu gusubiza avuga ko bishoboka cyane ndetse anitangaho urugero .
Ati " " " " Natangiye gusura inzu ndangamurage cyane i Butare ndi umwana muto ubu ndashaje .
Hari ibintu byinshi nagiye mbona bikamfasha .
Hari ibintu byinshi byo mu nzu ndangamurage byagiye bintera imbaraga zo guhanga imyambaro . " " " "
Aha niho yavuze ko hari imirimbo yo hambere yitwa " " " " ubutega " " " " yambarwaga na abagore bo hambere , yatumye atangira guhanga imirimbo yakwambarwa na igitsinagore .
Ati " " " " Hariho imirimbo bitaga ubutega abagore bo hambere bambaraga ku birenge ntekereza ko na abagabo babyambaraga , tugerageza gukora utuntu na umuntu yakwambara ku birenge hari abajya bavuga ko ari imico mibi na ubwomanzi cyangwa uburara kandi ariko no mu Rwanda rwo hambere byarahabaga . " " " "
Yavuze ko inzu ndangamurage azishimira ko hari umusanzu ziha abahanga imyambaro iyo bazisuye .
Ati " " " " Nibaza ko inzu ndangamurage twabashimira cyane , hari ababona ari bito bitewe na uko bareba ariko njye ndabashimira cyane .
Ndabashimira aho mugeze ubu .
Hari byinshi mutuma tubona kandi nimubyongera bizaba ari akarusho . " " " "
Dr Kandt witiriwe iyi ngoro iherereye mu Mujyi wa Kigali muri Nyarugenge ari nayo umuyobozi wayo yaganiraga na Patrick Muhire , yabaye igihe kirekire mu bikorwa bya ubushakashatsi i Shangi , nyuma aza gusubira mu Budage , agarutse mu Rwanda yakomeje ibikorwa bya ubushakashatsi ariko aza no kugirirwa icyizere , agirwa Rezida wa u Rwanda , ahita
yimukira ahazwi nka Ingoro yo kwa " " " " Richard Kandt . " " " "
Iyi nzu yitiriwe ifatwa nka imwe mu zigezweho zimaze igihe kirekire mu Rwanda , ni imwe mu zisurwa cyane na ba mukerarugendo ndetse yihariye amateka yaranze Abanyarwanda na Abadage .
Muhire wari watumiwe mu kiganiro na umuyobozi wa Ingoro yitiriwe Richard Kandt yatangiye guhanga imideli mu 2008 .
Inkanda House yashinze ni imwe mu nzu zihanga imideli zimaze igihe mu Rwanda kuko yatangiye mu buryo bweruye mu 2010 .
Ikora imyambaro itandukanye irimo imico ivanze ya Abanyamahanga na uwo mu Rwanda .
Izina " " " " Inkanda " " " " risobanuye umwambaro wa abagore bo mu Rwanda rwo hambere nka uko abakobwa na abagabo bambaraga ishabure bagatega amasunzu , abagore bambaraga Inkanda bagasokoza uruhanika .
Inkanda yabaga ikoze mu ruhu bakayambara bayikenyereye mu mabere .
Uyu musore yahisemo iri zina mu gukomeza gusigasira umuco .
Intego Muhire yari afite atangira yari ukumvisha abanyarwanda ko uruganda rwa imideli atari umwuga wa injiji nka uko benshi bamubwiraga agitangira .
Imyambaro ya Inkanda House yamamaye harimo " " " " Inka ya Data Collection " " " " yagiye hanze mu 2018 , yari imyamabro ihuza gakondo nyarwanda na ibigezweho .
Hari kandi " " " " The black days of Marie Antoinette " " " " yerekanye ku bufatanye na Ambasade ya Ababiligi mu Rwanda .
Iyi myambaro avuga ko yayihimbye ashaka kwibuka abantu bagize uruhare mu ruganda rwa imideli batabarutse .
Patrick Muhire Nshuti yize ibijyanye no gucunga imari .
Iyi nzu ye ikora imyambaro ya abagabo na abagore .
Ni umwe mu batangije " " " " Kigali Fashion Week " " " " yamenyekaniyemo abamurika imideli na abayihanga benshi bo mu Rwanda .
Joyce Fashion Designs yashyize hanze imyambaro yatuye ba Nyampinga ( Amafoto ) . Iyi myambaro ya Uwamahoro yayise " " " " Nyampinga dedicated Collection . " " " "
Igizwe na amakanzu cyane cyane ndetse na indi mike irimo amashati na amakabutura byose bya abakobwa .
Uwamahoro yabwiye IGIHE ko iyi myambaro mishya yashyize hanze yatekereje kuykora mu gihe hari amarushanwa atandukanye aherutse kuba mu Rwanda arimo Miss Rwanda ndetse na Miss Supranational kuko hari abakobwa bamwe bo muri ayo marushanwa yambitse .
Ati " " " " Ni imyambaro natuye ba nyampinga kuko nayambitse abakobwa batandukanye barimo abo muri Miss Rwanda ndetse nabo muri Miss Supranational , byose bya ubu mwaka .
Natekereje kuyikora mu gihe aya marushanwa yari arimbanyije . " " " "
Nko muri Miss Rwanda yambitse abakobwa bari basanganywe amakamba ubwo bajyaga kuyatanga ku munsi wa nyuma wa iri rushanwa , aba barimo Umutesi Denise wabaye Igisonga cya kabiri muri Miss Rwanda mu 2020 ndetse na Umwiza Phionah wabaye Igisonga cya Mbere muri Miss Rwanda mu 2020 , uzahagararira u Rwanda mu irushanwa rya ubwiza rya Miss University Africa ribera muri Nigeria .
Uretse aba kandi niwe wambitse Musana Teta Hense ku munsi wo gutangaza abakobwa 20 bagombaga kujya mu mwiherero wa Miss Rwanda .
Musana Teta Hense ni nawe uyu mwaka ufite umushinga urimo Agashya .
Joyce Fashion Designs ni nayo yambitse abakobwa bose barindwi bageze mu cyiciro cya nyuma cya Miss Supranational mu 2021 , ku munsi wo gutanga ikamba .
Uwamahoro ni umwe mu bahanga imideli bahagaze neza muri iki gihe .
Avuga ko na ubwo atari yagera ku nzozi yari afite atangira , ashima Imana mu buryo bukomeye .
Uyu mukobwa ubusanzwe ufite inzu ihanga imyambaro ya " " " " Joyce Fashion Designs " " " " avuga ko kugira ngo amenye kudoda byaturutse ku kuba yarakuze abona iwabo hari imashini zibikora , akagenda abyiga akiri muto kugeza ubwo yabaye mukuru akabikomeza .
Ati " " " " Kubera ko nakundaga kubona imashini iri aho nta kintu bari kuyikoresha , natangiye kujya nyifata nkiga kudoda gusa ntabwo nabikundaga cyane .
Mu 2015 natangiye kwiga imashini neza ariko numvaga ntazabikora nka umwuga , nkirangiza kwiga imashini nahise njya kwiga kaminuza . " " " "
Mu 2017 nibwo yaje kubitangira bya kinyamwuga ariko biza kugenda biguru ntege kuko atari afite ubushobozi buhagije kandi anabifatanya na amasomo ya Kaminuza .
Nyuma yaje gushinga inzu ihanga imyambaro yise " " " " Joyce Fashion Designs . " " " "
Afite intego yo gukomeza gukora neza no guhaza isoko rya imyambaro mu Rwanda akagera no ku isoko mpuzamahanga .
Wig , imisatsi mihangano iharawe i Kigali ishobora gusubiza ku isuka abatunganyaga imisatsi .
Mu myaka yashize umuntu washakaga kwisukisha cyangwa kugira imisatsi mireremire yoroshye bizwi nko kudefiriza , yagana abize ibya uwo mwuga bakamufasha kuba yashyira ku mutwe ibyo ashaka .
Kuri ubu ibintu bimaze guhindura isura ko hasigaye hari imisatsi na ibisuko bicuruzwa bikozwe mu buryo bumeze nka ingofero , ku buryo igihe ushakiye kuwukoresha uhita uwambara bitagusabye kujya kubabyize .
Na mbere ubu buryo bwariho ariko ntibyari biteye imbere ku buryo buri wese yabonaga ibikoze neza , mu bwoko bwa imisatsi buri wese yakwifuza .
Wasangaga benshi bavuga ko abazikoresha ari abantu badasobanukiwe na ibyubwiza .
Kuri ubu ibintu byarahindutse ko iyi misatsi ishyirwaho igihe cyose yateye imbere , aho iboneka mu bwoko butandukanye , haba imiremire , imigufi na ibindi .
Iyi misatsi ikozwe mu ngofero usibye kuba yorohereza abayikoresha kandi igezweho cyane kuburyo umugore cyangwa umukobwa utayitunze aba atakisanga mu basirimu .
Wig ikoreshwa mu buryo bworoshye ku buryo uhita uyambara nka ingofero wabanje gusuka ibituta cyangwa waryamishije umusatsi usanganwe , washaka gufatisha ugakoreshaho amavuta yabugemewe ikaguma ku mutwe .
Bamwe mu bayikoresha baganiriye na IGIHE , bavuze ko igituma bayikunda ari uko yabaganyirije umwanya bamaraga mu nzu zitunganya imisatsi , ndetse bakaba bahinduranya ibyo bafite ku mutwe uko babishaka .
Umulisa Kelly Sandra yavuze ko gukoresha ubu buryo bimufasha guhora asa neza .
Ati " " " " Gukoresha wig biramfasha cyane kuko mba mfite iza imisatsi miremire na izisutse .
Icyo nkeneye nicyo nshyiraho kandi kuko nzi kubyikorera byatumye ngabanya wa mwanya namaraga muri Salon , kandi uhora ukeye kuko uba wahinduye uko usa kenshi . " " " "
Mutoni Barber we avuga ko ubu bwoko bwa imisatsi bumafasha guhora akeye kandi ko byamuruhuye ingoyi yo kwisukisha akababara umutwe nkuko byajyaga bimugendekera .
Ati " " " " Usibye kuba mpora nkeye none nkaba mfite ibisuko , ejo ngashyira imisatsi ya kinyafurika cyangwa imiremire uko nshaka byanduhuye kubabara bari kunsuka .
Mbere nasukaga amarasita nkarwara ariko ubu mpita nyishyiramo nta kibazo ngize . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko bibafasha no kudasesagura kuko wig uyigura ukayimarana igihe kinini , nyamara ibisuko bisanzwe nyuma ya ukwezi biba byashaje .
Ati " " " " Erega biranagufasha mu buryo bwo kudasesagura ko niba nko mu kwezi wasukishaga ukabikuraho ukajugunya , ubu siko bimeze ko uyikuraho ukayoza ukabika . " " " "
Ku ruhande rwa abazicuruza nabo bavuga ko abantu bakwiye kureka gusesagura bisukisha ibintu bakuraho kandi hari uburyo bwo gutunga ibirambye , kandi ko bituma na isuku yo mu mutwe yiyongera .
Umucuruzi wa ibirungo bya ubwiza , Maty Beauty yagize ati " " " " Kugura wig ni ukwiteganyiriza kuko uyikoresha igihe , ntabwo ipfa gusaza kandi iriya uyishyiraho wasutse ibituta cyangwa hejuru ya umusatsi wawe muke .
Uyikuraho ukoga mu mutwe uko ushaka , biroroha kurusha kuzategereza koga mu mutwe nyuma ya amezi atatu wasukuye . " " " "
Nubwo hari abashima ibyiza bya wig ariko abize umwuga wo gusuka no gutunganya imisatsi ya abagore bo bahangayikishijwe na ikwirakwira ryayo , kuko bishobora kuzatuma ibyo bize bibapfira ubusa .
Umusutsi ubimazemo imyaka itanu , Mujawamariya Valentine yavuze ko iterambere ari ryiza , ariko ko ubwiyongere bwa wig nibukomeza gusakara hose ibyo bize bizabapfira ubusa .
Ati " " " " Kuba haza ibintu bishya ni byiza , ariko se ko ureba abantu basigaye bagura iriya misatsi bakayishyiriraho ubwo tuzaba abande ?
Ikizakurikiraho tuzabura abo dusuka kandi ibi nibyo byari bidutunze na abacu . " " " "
Uyu mubyeyi wari usanzwe ufite abakiliya ba abanyamujyi yavuze ko batangiye kugabanuka bitewe na ubu bwoko bushya bwa imisatsi .
Ati " " " " Nari mfite ukuntu nkorana na abakobwa ba abanyamujyi kuko hari abo nziranye nabo bitabiriye amarushanwa ya ubwiza bakanzanira na bagenzi babo , ubu ntibakiza nkuko byari bisanzwe , aza ari uko yabuze wenda ubwoko bwa wig bwa ibisuko ashaka .
Ibi bintera ubwoba ko mu minsi iri imbere bazagenda burundu . " " " "
Izi mpungenge azihuje na Abubakar Mupenzi utunganya imisatsi ya abagore uvuga ko ahangayikishijwe no kuba abakiliya bakoresha imisatsi bagabanyuka .
Ati " " " " Abantu bazaga kudefiriza no kwiyogoshesha ari benshi ariko ushatse imisatsi idefirije agura wig ndende , yashaka imigufi akaba ariyo agura , bidatinze turashaka ikindi dukora . " " " "
Iyi misatsi kuri ubu ikoreshwa na abifite kubera ko igiciro kiri hejuru .
Imyiza iboneka guhera ku bihumbi 50frw ariko igenda igabanuka uko iminsi ishira .
Uko Guma mu rugo yatumye Dusenge Steffa yinjira mu bucuruzi bwa ibikomo .
Uyu musore mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE yavuze ko yahisemo gutangira uyu mushinga nyuma ya uko yari amaze igihe kinini atekereza kuwukora ariko akabura umwanya kubera akandi kazi yakoraga .
Ubwo Coronavirus yugarizaga abantu mu Rwanda na ahandi henshi ku Isi bakajya muri Guma mu rugo , nibwo yahisemo guhita yinjira mu gukora ibikomo ndetse kuri ubu yemeza ko yatangiye kungukirwa na ubu bucuruzi .
Ibi bikomo bye yabyise HIIGHK Bracelets .
Ati " " " " Nari mfite igitekezo kuva cyera cyo kubikora ariko nkabura umwanya ariko muri Guma mu rugo ya umwaka ushize nibwo nabonye umwanya uhagije wo gushyira mu bikorwa igitekerezo cyanjye .
Nashyize hanze agakomo kanjye mbona abantu barabikunze bintera imbaraga yo kubikomeza . " " " "
" " " " Ibikomo ntabwo ari ibintu byo kwambara habaye ibintu bidasanzwe runaka kandi ntabwo bigenewe itsinda runaka rya abagabo cyangwa abagore .
Ntabwo umuntu abyambara ashaka kwiyerekana cyangwa kugaragara neza .
Ahubwo byakwifashishwa mu kubara inkuru cyangwa kwerekana uwo uri we . " " " "
Ibi bikomo bigaragaramo ikamba , Gusenga akavuga ko impamvu batekereje kurishyiramo , ari uko bashakaga kugaragaza ko umwami yakoraga byiza abyikorera kandi akabikorera abandi .
Impamvu babikoze ni uko umuntu wambitswe aka gakomo aba ari kubara inkuru ze nka uko umwami yabikoraga , yikorera ibyiza kandi anabikorera abaturaga ayoboye .
Ntabwo mu Rwanda hazwi abantu benshi bakora ibikomo kuko bifatwa nka ibintu biciriritse ariko Dusenge asigaye abyaza impano ye umusaruro , kandi byatangiye kumufasha .
Yavuze ko hari abantu amaze guha akazi na ubwo atari benshi cyane , yemeza ko uko ubucuruzi bwe buzagenda bwaguka ariko na we azagenda yagura ubucuruzi bwe .
Ati " " " " Maze guha akazi abantu batanu barimo ushinzwe kunshyirira ibintu ku mbuga nkoranyambaga , ugeza ibintu ku bantu baba babisabye ndetse na abandi babiri bamfasha gukora no gutunganya udukomo na amasaro . " " " "
Yavuze ko ibintu bimuvuna ari ukumenyekanisha ibyo akora kuko hari benshi batarabimenya uko abyifuza .
Yemeza ko ubu akazi yari asanzwe akora yamaze kukareka .
Ati " " " " Akazi nakoraga narakaretse kuko nashaka kubanza gushyira imbaraga mu kubaka izina rya ibi nkora kugira ngo abantu bose babimenye baba abari mu Rwanda no hanze yarwo . " " " "
Yavuze ko ku munsi bashobora gukora udukomo turi hagati 10 na 20 , gusa akavuga ko umubare wa utwo bagurisha ukiri hasi bitewe na ibi bihe bya COVID - 19 .
Teddy Riley uri mu Rwanda yasuye House of Tayo ( Amafoto ) .
Amafoto yashyizwe ku mbuga nkoranyambaga za iyi nzu ikora imyambaro , agaragaza Teddy Riley ari kumwe na Mathew Rugamba watangije iyi nzu ndetse hari na aho agaragara yigera imyambaro ikorerwa muri iyi nzu .
Iyi nzu yanditse ku mbuga nkoranyambaga zayo iti " " " " Byari ibyishimo bya ikirenga kwakira umunyabigwi wa umuririmbyi akaba na utunganya indirimbo na uzandika , Teddy Riley ; aho dukorera ejo . " " " "
Uyu mugabo wa imyaka 53 yageze mu Rwanda ku wa Gatandatu abanza gushyirwa mu kato no gupimwa Coronavirus nka uko biri mu mabwiriza yashyizweho na inzego za ubuzima mu kwirinda ikwirakwira rya iki cyorezo .
Kuri uyu wa Mbere , tariki 7 Ukuboza 2020 , Teddy Riley yasuye Urwibutso rwa Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi rwa Kigali ruri ku Gisozi , anunamira inzirakarengane ziharuhukiye .
Teddy Riley uyu munsi yasuye Ishuri rya Umuziki rya Muhanga aho agirana ikiganiro na abanyeshuri baryigamo ndetse na abariyobora .
Azamara icyumweru mu Rwanda .
Ubusanzwe uyu mugabo wa Umunyamerika yitwa Edward Theodore Riley .
Ni umuririmbyi , umwanditsi wa indirimbo , akaba anazitunganya .
Azwi cyane nka umwe mu batangije injyana ya New jack swing , yamamaye cyane muri Amerika no ku Isi yose mu myaka ya 1980 .
Mu 1987 yari ari umwe mu bagize itsinda rya Guy , yari ahuriyemo na Aaron Hall na Timmy Gatling .
Nyuma yo gukora album ya kabiri ya iri tsinda afatanyije na uwitwa The Future bakoze kuri album ya Michael Jackson ya munani yitwaga " " " " Dangerous " " " " yagiye hanze mu 1991 , ikaza no gukundwa bihambaye .
Teddy Riley yaje gutandukana na bagenzi be babanaga muri Guy , mu 1991 ahita ashinga irindi tsinda ryitwaga Blackstreet .
Iri tsinda ryakunzwe mu ndirimbo zitandukanye zirimo " " " " Dona t Leave Me " " " " yagiye hanze mu 1997 , " " " " No Diggity " " " " yagiye hanze mu 1996 , bakoranye na Dr . Dre na Queen Pen na izindi .
Iri tsinda ryasenyutse mu 2011 rikajya ryongera rikihuza .
Ishimishamubiri ?
Bikini mu marushanwa ya ubwiza , umwambaro ukunze kuvugirizwa induru ku Isi yose .
Ku bo muri iri dini , abenshi bakunze kwambara umwambaro uzwi nka burkini wahanzwe na Umunya - Australia , Aheda Zanetti , uhisha umubiri wose uretse isura , intoki na amano .
Nawo hari ibihugu bitemerera abakobwa babyo kuwambara na iyo yaba agiye koga ku mazi .
Bikini isanzwe yambarwa mu marushanwa ya ubwiza ikunze kwambarwa , iyo hagezeho icyiciro kizwi nka " " " " Swim Suit competition . " " " "
Icyo gihe abakobwa bambara utwenda duhisha amabere ndetse na imyanya ya ibanga ubundi si ukwivayo bakiyekerekana imbere ya Akanama Nkemurampaka nta nkomyi .
Ni umwambaro washyizwe mu marushanwa ya ubwiza ugamije kugaragaza ubwiza bwa umukobwa bujyanye na uko ikimero cye gikurura abantu .
Uyu mwambaro akenshi wambarwa , hari sosiyete zatanze agatubutse zigamije kwamamaza cyangwa se gushaka abamurika imideli bajya bifashishwa mu kwambara imyambaro yazo .
Ariko , hari na abawifashisha mu marushanwa ya ubwiza bagamije ishimishamubiri ( kugaburira amaso yabo imiterere ya umukobwa ujya gusa na uwambaye ubusa ) , ibintu bikundwa cyane na abiganjemo abagabo bageze mu zabukuru .
Bikini yabaye kimwe mu bigize amarushanwa atandukanye akomeye ya ubwiza ku Isi arimo Miss Earth na Miss World , ndetse abaterankunga nka Hawaiian Tropic bari bamwe mu bamamaza mu gihe cya iki cyiciro .
Uretse kwambara bikini mu marushanwa ya ubwiza hari ibihugu akorerwa mu tubari , utubyiniro , imikino ya boxing na ahandi ; aho abahize abandi bahabwa ibikombe , amafaranga cyangwa se amasezerano yo gukora ibijyanye no kumurika imideli .
Muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , amarushanwa ya ubwiza ku bari na abategarugori arimo imyambaro ya bikini yatangiye kumenyakana mu myaka yo mu 1880 .
Na ubwo ayo marushanwa yabaga ari menshi , ntabwo yahabwaga agaciro .
Yatangiye kubahwa ubwo hatangiraga " " " " Miss America " " " " mu 1921 , ariko andi marushanwa yasaga nka aciriritse yakomeje kubaho na ubundi .
Amarushanwa ya bikini , hari akorwa agamije kureba umukobwa ufite ikibuno kinini kandi cyiza kurusha abandi , urugero nka Miss Bum Bum ibera muri Brésil ndetse na Miss Reef ibera mu bihugu bitandukanye byo mu Majyepfo ya Amerika .
Twirengagije ukwamamara kwa amarushanwa ya ubwiza atandukanye kandi umukobwa akaba yitabira ku bushake bwe , iyo bigeze ku cyiciro cyo kwambara bikini bikunze kuvugisha benshi .
Abanenga iki cyiciro mu marushanwa ya ubwiza , bavuga ko ubwiza bwa umwari budakwiriye kureberwa ku miterere ya umubiri we .
Ndetse amarushanwa amwe akomeye ku Isi yagiye yotswa igitutu kugeza afashe umwanzuro wo gukuramo iki cyiciro .
Miss World yabaye bwa mbere mu 1951 yateguwe na Eric Morley [ wahoze ari umugabo wa Julia Morley uhagarariye Miss World Oraganization itegura iri rushanwa uyu munsi ] , yashyizwemo uyu mwambaro agamije kumenyekanisha umwambaro wo kogana mu iserukiramuco ryo mu Bwongereza ryitwaga " " " " Festival Bikini Contest . " " " "
Umunya - Suède , Kiki H å kansson , wegukanye ikamba icyo gihe yaryambitswe yambaye bikini , maze ibihugu bigendera ku migenzo na imico ya amadini ntibyabivugaho rumwe , ndetse bimwe byafashe umwanzuro wo kutazongera kwitabira .
Bikini yaje gukurwamo ahubwo zisimbuzwa amakanzu maremare azwi nka Evening Gowns .
Bikini zongeye kugaruka muri iri rushanwa ariko nabwo biteza impagarara .
Mu myaka yo hagati yo mu 1970 no mu 1980 , ryamaganwe na benshi biganjemo abaharanira uburenganzira bwa igitsinagore .
Nyuma abategura irushanwa bahisemo ko icyiciro cya bikini cyajya kibera mu muhezo , imbere ya akanama nkemurampaka ka abantu bake ntibishyirwe mu itangazamakuru .
Ryaje kuba rihagaze gato , ryongera kuba mu 1996 mu Mujyi wa Bangalore mu Buhinde , ariko nabwo Abahinde benshi bararyamagana , bavuga ko ritesha agaciro umwari kubera bikini .
Habaye imyigaragambyo ikomeye muri icyo gihugu , ku buryo icyiciro cyo kwiyerekana muri bikini cyabereye mu birwa bya Seychelles .
Mu 2013 iri rushanwa rya Miss World ryabereye muri Indonesia ahantu habarizwa umuryango munini wa abemera amahame ya Islam , nabwo riramaganwa .
Hari na umuryango wo muri icyo gihugu wasabye ko irushanwa ritagomba kuhabera kuko ryamamaza ibikobwa bya ubusambanyi na ubunebwe mu bakobwa , kandi nta mpamvu na imwe yo kwerekana ibice bya abagore byakabaye bihishwa .
Icyo gihe , abateguraga iri rushanwa barisimbuje indi myambaro itagaragaza ubwambure bwa abakobwa .
Igitutu cyatumye amarushanwa amwe akura Bikini ku bigenderwaho hatangwa amanota . . .
Nyuma ya induru na imijugujugu yagiye ikurikizwa irushanwa rya Miss World kubera bikini kuva ryatangira , mu Ukuboza 2014 , byatangajwe iki cyiciro kitazongera kugaragara muri iri rushanwa ryari rimaze imyaka irenga 60 rihanganye na benshi bangaga bikini .
Bikini ikurwamo , Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Miss World Organization Julia Evelyn Pritchard Morley yavuze ko bafashe iki cyemezo bashaka ko " " " " aho kureba imiterere ya umukobwa bazajye bareba ubwenge bwe na indi myitwarire . " " " "
Muri Kamena 2018 , irushanwa rya Miss America naryo ryatangaje rigiye gukuraho icyiciro cyasabaga abakobwa kwiyerekana mu mwambaro wo kogana ndetse hakurwaho gusuzuma ubwiza bwa abahatanira ikamba hagendewe ku miterere ya umubiri wabo .
Gusa umukobwa ushaka kuwambara muri iri rushanwa ari ubushake bwe , we ntabwo yakumiriwe .
Ibihugu bimwe byashyizeho ingamba zikarishye ku bakobwa , zibuza kwambara bikini . . .
Umunya - Afghanistan , Vida Samadzai , yahataniye ikamba rya Miss Earth mu 2003 , yaje kutishimirwa mu gihugu cye yaba mu baturage ndetse no mu buyobozi bamunenga kujya mu irushanwa bambaramo bikini .
Uyu mukobwa yavukiye muri Afghanistan ariko akurira muri Amerika , gusa ajya muri iri rushanwa icyo gihe yabaga mu Buhinde .
Byatumye Afghanistan ica burundu kwambara bikini mu marushanwa ya ubwiza abera muri icyo gihugu ndetse no ku bakobwa bashobora kuyihagararira mu marushanwa ya ubwiza .
Uyu mwanzuro waje uherekejwe na ibisobanuro bivuga ko kugaragara umuntu yambaye ubusa mu marushanwa ya ubwiza bihabanye amahame ya Islam ndetse bihabanye na umuco wo muri Afghanistan , bigatesha umuntu ikuzo .
Icyo gihe , Habiba Sarabi wari Minisitiri ushinzwe ibijyanye na abagore yavuze ko kugaragara umuntu asa nka uwambaye ubusa atari ubwisanzure bwa umugore cyangwa umukobwa .
Ati " " " " Ahubwo ku giti cyanjye mbona ari mu rwego rwo gushimisha abagabo . " " " "
Icyo gihe iki gihugu cyavuze ko Vida Samadzai yagiye atagihagarariye .
Vida Samadzai wari wabaye umukobwa wa kabiri wambitswe ikamba rya Miss Afghanistan nyuma ya uwitwa Zohra Daoud wambitswe iri kamba mu 1972 , yagiye akangishwa kwicwa ndetse yamaze amezi atatu acungirwa umutekano na FBI .
Bikini yaketsweho kwifashishwa nka igikoresho ku bashaka gukoresha abakobwa ubusambanyi
Irushanwa rya Miss Tanguita risobanurwa nka irushanwa rya ubwiza rya abana rya bikini [ Miss Child Bikini ] ryo muri Colombia , rifatwa nka kamwe mu duce tugize del Rio Suarez Festival , ryashinjwe gukururira abana bato mu busambanyi .
Gusa abategura iri rushanwa bo babyamaganiye kure bavuga ko atari ko bimeze , ko ahubwo rigamije kugaragaza akamaro ka imiterere myiza ya umwana .
Impirambanyi ku burenganzira bwa muntu zavuze ko iri rushanwa na ubwo ryemewe rihonyora uburenganzira bwa abana batarageza imyaka ya ubukure .
No mu Rwanda Bikini ikunze kurikoroza !
Kuva mu 2016 nibwo bikini yatangiye kutavugwaho rumwe cyane mu Banyarwanda .
Icyo gihe , Miss Akiwacu Colombe wari uri mu irushanwa rya ubwiza rya Miss Supranational mu 2016 yemeye kwiyerekana yambaye " " " " Bikini " " " " mu gihe abandi bakobwa bari baragiye baserukira u Rwanda bajyagayo bakabyangaga .
Mu 2013 Mutesi Aurore wari uhagarariye u Rwanda yanze kwambara " " " " Bikini " " " " nka abandi kugira ngo yerekane indangagaciro za Abanyarwandakazi .
Mu 2014 , Neema Umwali na we yunze mu rya mugenzi we yanga kwambara utu twenda ahubwo yiyerekana yambaye umwitero .
Icyo gihe hari abacunaguje Mutesi Aurore bamushinja gukoza isoni igihugu no kucyandagaza mu maso ya amahanga we akavuga ko ataciye inka amabere .
Abanyarwandakazi batangiye gutinyuka bikini mu 2015 , Sonia Gisa yabimburiye abandi ayambara ntacyo yikanga ndetse icyo gihe yatahanye ikamba rya Nyampinga uhagarariye Umugabane wa Afurika .
Ubwo yitabiraga iri rushanwa mu 2016 , Akiwacu Colombe niwe wambaye bikini biravugwa cyane ndetse bamwe bavuga ko nyampinga wa u Rwanda atari akwiriye kujya kwanika amatako ku gasozi , gusa hari na abandi bavugaga ko ibyo yakoze aribyo .
Abandi bose bakurikiyeho mu irushanwa rya Miss Supranational barimo Ingabire Habiba wagiyeyo mu 2017 , Uwase Clémentine [ Tina ] wagiyeyo mu 2018 na Umunyana Shanitah bose bambaye uyu mwambaro ntacyo bikanga , gusa amafoto yabo yasakazwa agakurikizwa amagambo yiganjemo avuga ko " " " " bahonyoye umuco . " " " "
Miss Uwase Hirwa Honorine " " " " Miss Igisabo " " " " ubwo yitabiraga Miss Earth 2017 nawe yanze kwambara bikini , icyo gihe abantu bamwe bamwutse inabi bavuga atari akwiriye kwitabira abizi ko atazayambara .
Ibi bikomeza kuba urujijo ku mukobwa witabira amarushanwa asaba kwambara bikini , kuko yayambara cyangwa ntabikore atabura abamwibasira .
Ubwiza ntibureberwa mu busa
Tariki 25 Ukwakira 2020 bwa mbere mu Rwanda abakobwa bakoze amarushanwa ya Miss Africa Carabal , biyerekana muri bikini ibintu bitari bisanzwe kuko na abayambaraga mu myaka yashize bayambariraga hanze .
Hari habaye gutoranya abakobwa batanu bagomba gukurwamo umwe uzaserukira u Rwanda muri Miss Africa Calabar izabera muri Nigeria mu mpera za uyu mwaka .
Uku gutoranya aba bakobwa kwakurikiwe na induru , benshi bavuga ko batishimiye uburyo abakobwa basabwe kwiyerekana mu mwambaro wa bikini ubusanzwe benshi bavuga ko uhabanye na umuco nyarwanda .
Bamwe bavugaga ko mu gihe aya marushanwa abera mu bindi bihugu , nta kabuza abakobwa bo mu Rwanda bazasabwa kwambara bikini nta mananiza .
Abandi bakavuga ko bidakwiye ku munyarwandakazi , maze rubura gica !
Umuyobozi wa Umuryango Urwanya ruswa na Akarengane , Transparency International Rwanda , Ingabire Marie Immaculée , yavuze ko uburyo abakobwa bari bambayemo ntaho bitandukaniye na ubusa buri buri .
Yagize ati " " " " Ubusa ni ubusa nyine kandi ubwiza ntibureberwa mu busa . " " " "
Iyahoze ari Inteko Nyarwanda ya ururimi na umuco ( RALC ) ntabwo yigeze yemeranya na gato na abakobwa Bambara bikini mu marushanwa ya ubwiza ariko na abavagayo bakaza mu Rwanda nta bihano bafatirwaga .
Hari abantu bamwe bagiye bavuga ko " " " " Bikini " " " " yambawe mu rwego rwa akazi yaba idahabanye na umuco nyarwanda .
Reba amashusho ya abakobwa ba mbere 10 muri Miss Universe 2019 mu cyiciro cyo kwiyerekana bambaye Bikini .
Inkanda House yashyize hanze imyambaro mishya ( Amafoto ) .
Muhire yabwiye IGIHE ko iyi myambaro ari imyambaro yatekereje mu bihe bya Coronavirus , ashaka kwerekana ko nyuma ya ubuzima bubi hashobora kubaho ubundi bwiza .
Ati " " " " Nashatse kwerekana ko na nyuma ya urupfu hari ubuzima .
Nyuma ya iminsi mibi twaciyemo ya Covid - 19 ubuzima buracyakomeza .
Ni aho nakuye igitekerezo cyo guhanga iyi myambaro . " " " "
Iyi myambaro ni iya 23 mu yo yagiye ashyira hanze , akayereka abanyarwanda baba mu Rwanda ndetse na abo hanze .
Uyu musore avuga ko nka umuhanzi wa imideli , uri mu ba mbere bafashe iya mbere mu gukangurira abanyarwanda cyane cyane urubyiruko ko imideli ari ikintu cyateza umuntu ku giti cye imbere ndetse na igihugu muri rusange yishimira urwego uru ruganga rugezeho .
Ati " " " " Nishimira urwego imideli igezeho uyu munsi wa none mu Rwanda , tugitangira nta watwumvaga ndetse hari na abadusekaga ariko ubu tumaze kuba benshi .
Ibihangano byacu birambarwa hirya no hino mu Rwanda ndetse no hanze yarwo .
Ni ikintu gishimishije . " " " "
Inkanda House ni imwe mu nzu zihanga imideli zimaze igihe mu Rwanda kuko yatangiye mu 2010 .
Ikora imyambaro itandukanye irimo imico ivanze ya Abanyamahanga na uwo mu Rwanda .
Izina " " " " Inkanda " " " " risobanuye umwambaro wa abagore bo mu Rwanda rwo hambere nka uko abakobwa na abagabo bambaraga ishabure bagatega amasunzu , abagore bambaraga Inkanda bagasokoza uruhanika .
Inkanda yabaga ikoze mu ruhu cyangwa mu mpuzu bakayambara bayicyenyereye mu mabere .
Uyu musore yahisemo iri zina mu gukomeza gusigasira umuco .
Muhire yavuze ko intego yari afite atangira ari ukumvisha abanyarwanda ko uruganda rwa imideli atari umwuga wa injiji .
Ati " " " " Dutangira nari mfite icyifuzo cyo kurema mu mitwe ya abanyarwanda ko imideli cyangwa ubudozi atari umwuga wa injiji , ahubwo ko ushobora kurangiza kaminuza ugakora ubudozi kandi bugateza imbere igihugu nawe ubwawe . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Nashakaga gutinyura abana ba abanyarwanda ko kwihangira umurimo atari ugufungura Cyber Café gusa cyangwa Restaurant kandi nabigezeho .
Nashakaga no kumvisha abanyarwanda muri rusange ko bashobora kwambara ibya iwabo bakaberwa batiriwe birukira muri caguwa na imyenda iva i Burayi kandi bigenda biza rwose . " " " "
Imyambaro ya Inkanda House yamamaye harimo " " " " Inka ya Data Collection " " " " yagiye hanze mu 2018 , yari imyamabro ihuza gakondo nyarwanda na ibigezweho .
Hari kandi " " " " The black days of Marie Antoinette " " " " yerekanye ku bufatanye na Ambassade ya Ababiligi mu Rwanda .
Iyi myambaro avuga ko yayihimbye ashaka kwibuka abantu bagize uruhare mu ruganda rwa imideli batabarutse .
Ati " " " " Nashakaga kwibuka no guha agaciro abantu batuvuyemo baba Abanyarwanda cyangwa Abanyamahanga bagize uruhare mu mateka ya ya uruganda rwa imideli .
Marie Antoinette nayitiriye yari Umwamikazi mu Bufaransa . " " " "
Imyambaro Inkanda yatangiriyeho mu 2010 yayise " " " " Bagilinkanda , " " " " bishatse kuvuga ngo " " " " Arahirwa ufite icyo akinga ku mubiri , ni umugisha kubona icyo wambara . " " " "
Patrick Muhire Nshuti yize ibijyanye no gucunga imari .
Iyi nzu ye ikora imyambaro ya abagabo na abagore .
Ni umwe mu batangije " " " " Kigali Fashion Week " " " " yamenyekaniye abamurika imideli na abayihanga benshi bo mu Rwanda .
Mazimpaka Christelle wabaye igisonga cya Miss Career Africa mu 2019 yatangiye gukora imirimbo ya ubwiza .
Uyu mukobwa agiye kujya akora imirimbo itandukanye irimo amaherena ndetse na imikufi yo mu ijosi .
Azajya abikora binyuze muri sosiyete ye yatangije yise " " " " Ijunja Crystals . " " " "
Yabwiye IGIHE ko yatekereje gukora uyu mushinga kuko yabonaga mu Rwanda nta zindi sosiyete nyinshi zikora ibintu nka ibi .
Ati " " " " Ni ibintu ubusanzwe njye ubwanjye numvaga nzakora kuva kera .
Ni ibintu nkunda ku buryo gutangira kubikora ari intambwe ikomeye kuri njye .
Nkunda kugaragaza neza kandi mu buryo butandukanye na abandi .
Abantu bose dukorana dukunda gushyira ibyo dutekereza na inyungu zacu mu byo twabasha kugira . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga imirimbo yabo igenewe abantu ba ingeri zose .
Yavuze ko yahisemo gukora iyi mirimbo atekereza ko byafasha Abanyafurika bose , ndetse bikagera mu bihugu byose byo kuri uyu mugabane bakagabanya kugura ibituruka i Burayi na ahandi .
Mazimpaka Christelle yitabiriye Miss Career Africa mu 2019 , yegukana umwanya wa kabiri .
Aha yari afite umushinga witwa witwa Rugori .
Mu 2018 nabwo yegukanye umwanya wa gatatu .
Muri iri rushanwa rigamije gushishikariza abakobwa kuyoboka amasomo na ibigo bigaruka cyane ku bumenyi na ikoranabuhanga , yagaragaje umushinga wo kwifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu guhuza abashoramari na imishinga mito .
Icyo gihe yahawe igihembo cya 1 000 000 Frw no kwitabira imwe mu nama mpuzamahanga abihawe na RURA .
Kenz ō wagize uruhare runini mu kumenyekanisha u Buyapani mu ruganda rwa imideli yitabye Imana .
Uyu mugabo yubatse izina rikomeye mu ruganda rwa imideli ku Isi yari afite inzu ya imideli yitwa " " " " Kenzo . " " " "
Yapfiriye mu bitaro biherereye mu Bufaransa mu Mujyi wa Paris .
Yibukirwa ku buhanga bwe buhambaye mu guhanga imideli ndetse no kuba ariwe muhanzi wa imideli ukomoka mu Buyapani wabashije kugaragara muri Paris Fashion Week ku nshuro ya mbere .
Abayapani benshi ku rubuga rwa Twitter bagaragaje uyu musaza nka umuntu wagize uruhare rukomeye mu kongera kuvuka ka uruganda rwa imideli mu Buyapani .
Abandi bavuze ko kugira ikintu cyakozwe na uyu mugabo ari ishema kuri bo , umwe yanditse ati " " " " Ikofi ya mbere natunze yari yarakozwe na Kenzo .
Na ubwo ari akantu gato , nzahora mbyibuka .
Ruhukira mu mahoro . " " " "
Undi yagize ati " " " " Mfite umwambaro ya Kenzo nahawe na Mama , na na ubu ndacyawambara . " " " "
Kenzo yavutse mu 1939 ahitwa Himeji .
Yagiye mu Mujyi wa Paris mu 1965 akoresheje ubwato , yirengagije ko atari azi kuvuga Igifaransa na gato , atangira guhanga imyambaro akayigurisha ku nzu za imideli zikomeye , nyuma aza gufata umwanzuro wo gushinga iduka yari yarise " " " " Jungle Jap . " " " "
Yakoraga imyambaro igendanye na ubundi na umuco wo mu Buyapani , yigeze kuvuga ko impamvu yabikoze ko ariko atashakaga gukora nka ibyo yasanze Abafaransa bakora .
Kenzo yamamaye cyane ubwo Elle Magazine yashyiraga kimwe mu bikorwa bye ku gifuniko cyacyo .
Kenzo yatangiye kwamamara cyane mu ruganda rwa imideli mu Bufaransa ndetse na iwabo mu Bufaransa guhera mu myaka yo mu 1970 kuzamura ndetse atangira no kwegukana ibihembo bitandukanye .
Rwanda Cultural Fashion Show igiye gutangiza ishuri rya ibijyanye na imideli .
Iri shuri rizatangira mu 2021 , ryigisha kumurika imideli ndetse no kuyihanga ; aho nibura riteganya ko ku ikubitiro rizakira abanyeshuri 110 baziga ibi byombi .
Ntawirema Célestin usanzwe utegura ibirori bya Rwanda Cultural Fashion Show , yabwiye IGIHE ko impamvu batekereje gutangiza iri shuri ari uko nta rindi risanzwe riri mu Rwanda bityo abona hari icyuho gikomeye cyane .
Ati " " " " Ikintu cya mbere cyabiteye ni urukundo rwa uruganda rwa imideli .
Ni ikintu twabonaga ko ari icyuho gikomeye mu Rwanda kuba nta shuri ryigisha ibijyanye na imideli rihari .

Uko agapfukamunwa kabaye umudeli ujyanishwa na imyenda ku bashaka kurimba ( Amafoto )
Umwaka wa 2020 ni umwaka wari witezweho kuba umwaka wa icyerekezo ndetse Isi yose ijya kuwinjiramo abantu bari bafite amashyushyu yo kureba uko umwaka wa icyerekezo uzaba umeze .
Ibyari byitezwe siko byagenze !
Kuko ugitangira icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyahise cyugariza Isi maze umwaka wari witezweho kuba uba uwa amata na ubuki usharirira benshi nka umuravumba .
Umuhanzi Danny Vumbi niwe waririmbye ati " " " " nta gihoraho nka impinduka ! . " " " "
Hari abatakaje akazi kubera iki cyorezo abandi babura ababo , mbese na umwaka waratunguranye uzana ikintu gikomeye kizajya cyibukwa mu binyejana byose .
Niwo mwaka bwa mbere mu mateka abantu bategetswe kuguma mu ngo wasohoka ugahura na ingorane ; abandi bagasabwa gukaraba buri kanya aho bageze hose nka aho bagiye gufata amafunguro ; mbese ni uwa akumiro .
Agapfukamunwa ntikari kazwi na benshi uretse abakora muri serivisi zibasaba kwipfuka amazuru kugira ngo birinde kuba bakwandura indwara za ubuhumekero abandi bakumvaga nka umugani .
Mu 2020 yaba abari basanzwe bambara agapfukamunwa ndetse na abatari basanzwe bakazi batunguwe no kumva ko noneho bibaye itegeko kukambara mu gihe umuntu agiye mu bantu benshi .
Abakunda kurimba mu gushaka uburyo bagomba kwambara aka gapfukamunwa kandi ntibibicire uburyo bashakaga kwambara ; batangiye kujya bakambara bajyanishije na imyambaro aho umuntu asigaye ajya kudodesha umwambaro wo guserukana mu birori cyangwa ahandi akibuka ko agomba gushyiraho na agapfukamunwa bijyanye .
Christelle Kabagire usanzwe ari umunyamideli ndetse wanagiye akora ibiganiro bitandukanye bijyanye nabyo , yabwiye IGIHE ko udupfukamunwa twaje mu buryo butunguranye bigatuma abantu batangira gushaka uburyo badusanisha na imyambaro bagiye kurimba .
Ati " " " " Agapfukamunwa kaje hari utundi dusanzwe dukoreshwa amasaha atandatu ( Surgery Mask ) .
Byatumye hatangira gukorwa udupfukamunwa dutandukanye dukozwe mu myenda no mu bindi .
Mbere na mbere muri iki gihe cya icyorezo aho dusabwa kwambara udupfukamunwa ubanza kureba uwo mwenda ugiye kwambara . " " " "
" " " " Uhita ureba niba kwambara agapfukamunwa nirinze nkanarimba .
Hari ukuntu nshobora kwambara udupfukamunwa dufite ibara rimwe cyangwa se nkambara nka akumukara kajyana na ibara iryo ariryo ryose .
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Agapfukamunwa gafite irindi bara ricanye bisaba kwambara ibintu bijya kujyana nako .
Niyo icyorezo cyarangira bizaterwa na abantu kuba bareka kwambara agapfukamunwa .
Ibitaramo biri kubera ku mbuga nkoranyambaga muri iki gihe bya imideli bisigaye bigaragaramo imyambaro ijyanishijwe na udupfukamunwa .
Mbona iyo umuntu yambaye agapfukamunwa kajyanye na ibyo yambaye aba yarimbye neza . " " " "
Yagiriye inama abantu yo kujya bareba imyambaro bagiye bakwambara mbere yo guhitamo agapfukamunwa kagiye kujyana nayo .
Ati " " " " Hari ukuntu ukwambara agapfukamunwa wirinda hakabaho no kukambara wibuka no kujyanisha na ibyo wambaye .
Kugira ngo ntibibe akavuyo .
Icyo nashishikariza abanyarwanda ni ukwambara agapfukamunwa ureba uti aka karaza kujyana na umwe mu myambaro nambaye ? " " " "
Niyitanga Olivier washinze inzu ihanga imideli ya Tanga Designs we yavuze ko na ubwo abanyarwanda bari kwitabira kwambara udupfukamunwa batujyanishije na ibyo bambaye ( bikaryohera amaso ) hari abagifite imyumvire yo kumva ko tugomba kuba duhendutse .
Ati " " " " Mu Rwanda bari kwitabira kwambara udupfukamunwa ariko ntabwo ibyo kujyanisha udupfukamunwa byari byatera imbere neza cyane .
Ntabwo abantu barabyumva cyane .
Nko hanze ho byafashe indi ntera hari ako mperutse kubaza kuri internet bambwira ko kagura $ 5 000 .
Kari gakoze mu bintu bihenze .
Hari bamwe inaha bacyumva ko kagomba kugura 500 Frw kandi bakajya bakambara mu birori na ahandi . " " " "
Yavuze ko ariko na ubwo hari abantu batarabyumva , hari impinduka byazanye mu myambarire ndetse no mu buryo bwa ubukungu hakagira abahanga imideli babibyaza amafaranga .
Ubu mu Rwanda bitewe na uko umuntu yifite ashobora kubona agapfukamunwa ka make nka 500 Frw , 1000 Frw , 1500 Frw , 2000 Frw ndetse hari na uduhenze tugura amafaranga abarirwa mu 10 000 ya amanyarwanda .
Reba amafoto mu bihe bitandukanye ya abantu bambaye udupfukamunwa bajyanishije .
Ambara uberwe !
Imyenda 10 abasore bakwambara muri iki gihe cya impeshyi .
Abahanga mu kurimba , basobanura neza ko kwambara neza , bijyana na ibihe kandi na aho umuntu agiye .
Niba umuntu agiye mu nama , ntabwo agomba kwambara nka ugiye mu musangiro na inshuti cyangwa se kuruhuka .
Ibi ni yo mpamvu habaho umwambaro wagenewe ikintu runaka , ku buryo utabona uwambaye ingozi ari muri siporo .
Mu mico itandukanye , impeshyi ifatwa nka igihe cya ibiruhuko , aho abantu bafata akanya , bakajya ku mazi na ahandi , bakumva akayaga bashyira ubwenge ku gihe .
No ku banyarwanda ni uko bimeze , aho usanga akenshi mu mpera za icyumweru , bifashisha uyu mwanya , bagatembera mu bice nyaburanga bitatse u Rwanda .
Iraguha Prosper ni umucuruzi wa imyenda mu Mujyi wa Kigali , asobanura ko muri ibi bihe , benshi mu banyamujyi , bamugana bashaka imyenda yo gutemberana mu mpera za icyumweru .
Mu myenda umuntu ashobora kwambara muri ibi bihe , iyo yajyana gutembera no kuruhura umubiri nko mu mpera za icyumweru cyangwa iyo yakwirirwana mu rugo .
Ingero za imyenda ya abagabo wakwambara muri ibi bihe .
Perezida Kagame na Madamu Jeannette Kagame mu myambaro ya Moshions : Ibyishimo kuri Turahirwa wayihanze ( Amafoto ) .
Ni imyenda yihariye , guhera ku yo yise Inkingi , Ingoma yanjye , Intsinzi , Utopia , Rafiki , Ruheru na indi .
Moses Turahirwa ni umusore wa imyaka 28 umaze kwandika izina rikomeye mu guhanga imideli mu Rwanda ku buryo benshi bamwirahira .
Imyenda ye irangwa na uko iba yifiteho ikirango cya imigongo , umutako nyarwanda wo hambere .
Mu 2015 yashinze inzu ya imideli ayita Moshions .
Ni igitekerezo yagize biturutse ku gushaka gukora imyambaro ifite umwihariko wa Kinyafurika bya umwihariko mu Rwanda .
Izina Moshions , ni impine ya izina rye rya irikirisitu " " " " Moses " " " " yongeyeho ijambo ryaturutse ku " " " " Fashion " " " " [ " " " " Mo " " " " ya Moses na " " " " shion " " " " ya Fashion ] .
Yatangiye kwikorera nyuma ya igihe yerekana imyenda ya abandi bakoreshaga ibitenge bakavuga ko ari imyambaro ya kinyafurika , we yiha intego yo kugaragaza umwihariko wa u Rwanda .
Ubwo IGIHE iheruka kumusura yatangaje ko " " " " Nagerageje gukoresha nka umwitero mu buryo bugezweho , nkoresha imigongo itakwa mu nzu na ayo masaro ubona bataka ku myenda , ku buryo tugira wa mwimerere wa u Rwanda ariko noneho mu myambarire . " " " "
Ubu aho wajya hose wambaye umwenda wakozwe na Moshions , byakorohera uwo ariwe wese kuwutandukanya na indi , akabona byoroshye umwihariko wawo .
Uyu musore yatumye benshi bagira ibihe byiza , magingo aya mu bukwe imyambaro ye niyo isigaye yiganje , benshi bakarimba ariko banajyanisha na umuco nyarwanda ; bya umwihariko bakishimira ko ibyo bambaye bibahesha icyubahiro ku bwo kuba byarakorewe mu Rwanda .
Turahirwa washinze " " " " Moshions " " " " yagizwe Ambasaderi wa PSG .
Uyu musore yinjiye mu mikorere na PSG biturutse ku masezerano u Rwanda ruherutse kugirana na iyi kipe yo kujya yambara imyambaro yanditseho amagambo " " " " Visit Rwanda " " " " mu rwego rwa kwamamaza ubukerarugendo bwa u Rwanda no kumenyekanisha ibindi byiza bitatse igihugu .
Yanditse kuri Instagram agaragaza ko yishimiye kuba ari umwe mu batoranyijwe , ashimira RDB na Visit Rwanda kuba ariwe bahisemo .
Ati " " " " Ntewe ishema na ibyaranze impera za icyumweru bidasanzwe hamwe na ALL - Accor Live Limitless na PSG ndetse nishimiye gutoranywa nka umwe mu bagiye kuba aba Ambasaderi babo .
Ndashimira cyane RDB na Visit Rwanda ku buranga bankoreye . " " " "
Turahirwa yaratoranyijwe biturutse ku Kigo cya Igihugu cya Iterambere , RDB , cyamuhaye PSG na ALL nka umwe mu banyarwanda bamaze kwiteza imbere kandi bafite izina rikomeye mu Rwanda mu ruhango rwa imideli .
Uyu musore mu mpera za icyumweru gishize yagiye mu Bufaransa mu ifatwa rya amashusho azajya hanze mu minsi iri imbere yo kwamamaza iyi kipe ndetse na Sosiyete ya ALL .
Ubufatanye bwa PSG na RDB buzafasha abakurikirana iyi kipe na Isi muri rusange kumenya ubwiza bwa u Rwanda , umuco na udushya twaruhangwamo kimwe na ibicuruzwa birukorerwamo .
Nka uko bikubiye mu masezerano ya impande zombi , ikirango cya Visit Rwanda kigaragazwa kuri Stade ya Parc des Princes aho PSG yakirira imikino yayo ndetse no ku mugongo ku myenda iyi kipe ikoresha mu myitozo no mu gihe cyo kwishyushya mbere ya imikino ya Shampiyona .
U Rwanda rwiteze ko binyuze muri ubu bufatanye , abakinnyi ba PSG na ibindi byamamare mpuzamahanga , bizabafasha gusura u Rwanda , bakabona ibyiza bitatse igihugu cya imisozi igihumbi uhereye ku bijyanye na ubugeni , umuco , siporo , muzika , ubukerarugendo , amafunguro na ubwiza bwa igihugu muri rusange .
Ikindi ni uko icyayi cya u Rwanda na ikawa aribyo byonyine bizajya bitangwa kuri Parc des Princes mu mwaka utaha wa imikino .
Hazajya habaho kandi icyumweru cya imishinga ya abanyempano ba Abanyarwanda na Abafaransa .
Icyo cyumweru cyiswe " " " " Semaine du Rwanda à Paris " " " " kizajya gitegurwa na PSG mu kumenyekanisha ibintu byose bikorerwa mu Rwanda .
Paris Saint Germain ni imwe mu makipe akomeye ku Isi , aho ikinamo Umunya - Brésil Neymar waciye agahigo ko kuba umukinnyi uhenze mu mateka ya ruhago ubwo yagurwaga avuye muri FC Barcelone mu 2017 .
Ivumburamatsiko kuri Fred Lyon wambika benshi mu byamamare nyarwanda .
Ubusanzwe yitwa Fred Ndicunguye , amaze imyaka ibiri na igice akora akazi ko gucuruza imyambaro itandukanye , inkweto na ibindi .
Akundwa na benshi kuko agira imyambaro igezweho .
Ubaze umubare wa ibyamamare ntiwawurangiza kuko uhereye kuri Bruce Melodie , Shaddy Boo , Queen Cha , Safi Madiba , Dj Toyxxk , Marnaud na abandi benshi .
IGIHE yamwegereye imuganiriza byinshi abantu bashobora kumwibazaho ndetse na uko yatangiye gukora ubucuruza bwa imyenda bwaje gutuma yiharira isoko mu gukorana na ibyamamare .
Avuga ko gucuruza yabitangiye kuva kera yiga muri kaminuza mu Bushinwa , akaza kubona ko ari impano ye .
Ati " " " " Ni ibintu byari bisanzwe bindimo .
Nkiri muri kaminuza nabwo nari umucuruzi , hari ukuntu ushobora kuba ukora aka kazi ariko nta biro ugira , rero niko nakoraga .
Nabikoze nkiri mu ishuri mbona byavamo umugati . " " " "
" " " " Aho nasoreje kaminuza naratangiye , abantu baramenya nanjye icyo bakeneye ndakimenya .
Nize mu Bushinwa , ibijyanye na ubushabitsi mpuzamahanga .
Aho nigaga nakundaga gutembera mu masoko atandukanye ugasanga ni njye uhorana ibintu bishya , bikaba ngombwa ko bagenzi banjye banyifashisha , nkagenda mbibonamo inyungu nke ndabikomeza kuko nabonaga ari impano yanjye . " " " "
Yemeza ko atatangiye gukora agamije kwambika abantu imyenda gusa ahubwo yari afite na gahunda yo gukora ikintu cyiza gituma umuntu yambara ibijyanye kandi akaberwa .
Ati " " " " Naje nje gukemura ikibazo cyo kwambika abantu ntabwo naje gukora ubushabitsi gusa ahubwo kwari ukugira ngo abantu mbambike .
Iyo ushaka kwambika umuntu ntabwo umwambika imyenda ngo agende yambaye ibirenge .
Umwambika inkweto , ipantalo , ishati , amadarubindi byaba ngombwa ukamwambika na isaha . " " " " " " " "
Avuga ko ashaka gutangira kujya agurisha na imyambaro ya Made in Rwanda .
Kuri we ngo abashaka kurimba buri wese aza afite igitekerezo cya uko ashaka kuberwa ariko na Fred bitewe na uko akubona akaba yakongeraraho ibindi bitekerezo byatuma wambara mu buryo bunogeye ijisho .
Muri iki gihe akorana bya hafi na Bruce Melodie , ndetse na imyambaro yari yambaye aririmba muri East Africaa s Got Talent yari yayambitswe na uyu musore .
Ati " " " " Urebye Bruce Melodie wa mbere ya uko mfungura iri duka na uw ubu baratandukanye .

Yambara imyambaro ya abanyamujyi .
Nizo mpinduka nazanye kugira ngo ibintu abahanzi mpuzamahanga babona ku Isi bibashe kugera no ku bahanzi bacu .
Imyambaro ntabwo iba ihenze .

Miss Akiwacu Colombe yitabiriye Paris Fashion Week ( Amafoto ) .
Paris Fashion Week iri mu bikorwa byo kumurika imideli bikomeye ku Isi , ku buryo buri munyamideli wese mu bihugu bitandukanye aba yifuza umunsi umwe kuzagaragara atambuka imbere ya abitabiriye iki gikorwa .
Uretse kuba ari igikorwa gikomeye ni kimwe mu bihemba neza kandi ukigiyemo akaba yabasha kumenyana na abandi bantu bakomeye muri uru ruganda bikaba byamufungurira andi marembo .
Iki gikorwa ngarukamwaka kuri iyi nshuro cyabaye guhera ku wa 23 Nzeri kugeza ku wa 1 Ukwakira 2019 .
Akiwacu Colombe yabaye umwe mu bamurika imideli basaga ijana babashije kwitabira .
Uyu mukobwa we ari mu banyamideli biyerekanye ku munsi wa nyuma .
Imyambaro yamuritswe muri iki gikorwa yari iya abadozi ba imyenda bibumbiye muri Global Fashion Collective .
Miss Akiwacu Colombe yabwiye IGIHE ko kumurika imideli muri iki gikorwa byari akarusho kuri we , bya umwihariko ku mwuga asanzwe akora wo kumurika imideli .
Ati " " " " Kugira ngo njyemo nitabiriye itoranya rya abanyamideli barankunda .
Byari byiza cyane ku mwuga wanjye wo kumurika imideli , ikindi ndishyurwa gusa ndanabikunda . " " " "
Paris Fashion Week ni kimwe mu birori bimurikirwamo imideli bikomeye ku Isi , iri mu cyiciro kimwe na London Fashion Week , Milan Fashion Week na New York Fashion Week .
Iki gikorwa cyatangiye guhera mu 1973 bigizwemo uruhare na French Fashion Federation .
Miss Akiwacu yaherukaga ibikorwa nka ibi muri Kamena 2019 , aho yitabiriye imurika rya imisatsi rigamije kwamagana ivangura rikorerwa abafite imisatsi ya injwiri mu Mujyi wa Paris mu gace ka Place de la Opéra .
Iki gikorwa cyari cyateguwe na Murielle Kabile usanzwe akora imisatsi ya ubwoko butandukanye .
Iki gikorwa cyo kumurika imisatsi cyiswe " " " " Dona t Touch My Hair , " " " " cyakozwe mu rwego rwo kwamagana abantu bakora mu misatsi ya abafite injwiri nka uburyo bwo kubendereza cyangwa kubirataho , ibintu bifatwa nka ivanguraruhu .
Akiwacu Colombe amaze imyaka ine mu Bufaransa , amaze kwimariramo ibyo kumurika imideli ndetse ni kimwe mu bimutunze na ubwo afite akandi kazi ka buri munsi akora .
Uyu mukobwa yari aherutse kuza mu Rwanda muri Nzeri 2019 , aho , nyuma ya ubukangurambaga yagiye akora mu buryo butandukanye .
Akiwacu yatowe nka Nyampinga wa u Rwanda mu 2014 ubwo iri rushanwa ryatangiraga gutegurwa na Rwanda Inspiration Backup ikibikora kugeza na ubu .
Umusore uzahagararira u Rwanda muri " " " " Mister Africa 2019 " " " " yamenyekanye .
Uyu musore wa imyaka 20 yashyizwe mu bazatoranywamo uhiga abandi mu buranga muri Afurika mu irushanwa risanzwe rizwi cyane nka Mister Africa International ritegurwa na House of Twitch yo muri Nigeria nka uko Promise Adebayo ukuriye iyi sosiyete itegura irushanwa yabitangarije IGIHE .
Umwaka ushize u Rwanda rwagombaga guserukirwa na Nshongore wabaye Mister Elegancy Rwanda 2018 , ariko ntiyabasha kwitabira .
Ibirori nya ir izina byo kwambika ikamba umusore uzahiga abandi muri Mister Africa 2019 , bizaba ku wa 1 Ukuboza 2019 .
U Rwanda rumaze kwitabira iri rushanwa kabiri , ubwa mbere byari mu 2015 ubwo Turahirwa Moses yabaga Igisonga cya mbere cya Rudasumbwa ndetse no mu 2017 ubwo Ntabanganyimana Jean de Dieu yahigikaga bagenzi be akegukana ikamba rya Mister Africa International 2017 .
Umwaka ushize ikamba rya Mister Africa International ryatwawe na Calisah Jiwa wo muri Tanzania .
Yakurikiwe na Ibrahim Alton Mansaray wo muri Sierra Leone , Chuckie Ihebuzor wo muri Nigeria , Jason Asare Akoto wo muri Ghana na Makala Nganda Courtez wo muri Cameroon .
Christophe Carlos , Mister Africa - France yatowe nka uwubatse umubiri neza naho Tevin Lennox wahagarariye u Bwongereza atorwa nka uwifotoje neza ku mucanga .
Abanyarwanda bacanye umucyo muri Tokyo Africa Collections ( Amafoto ) .
Ni igikorwa cyabaye ku nshuro ya mbere cyitabiriwe na Abanyarwanda nyuma ya ubufatanye na abategura Kigali International Fashion Week .
Mbere ya igikorwa aba Banyarwanda bitabiriye Tokyo Fashion Week basuye ibigo bikomeye nka AOKI iri mu bigo bikora amakositimu akomeye mu Buyapani , kompanyi itegura icyayi cya u Rwanda na ibindi .
Aba Banyarwanda bageze mu Buyapani ku wa 27 Kanama 2019 bazagaruka i Kigali ku wa 5 Nzeri 2019 .
Abahanga imideli bo mu Rwanda bitabiriye Tokyo Africa Collections barimo Murorunkwere Sandrine ufite inzu ihanga imideli ya Sahorn Fashion House na Karen Uwera ufite inzu ya imideli ya KARSSH Collection .
Mu berekana imideli bitabiriye baturutse mu Rwanda barimo Bella Christa Kanyange na Kaneza Lynka Amanda .
Kuva mu 2017 , ibirori ngarukamwaka bya Kigali Fashion Week byagejejwe ku yindi ntera na ababitegura bitangira kubera i Burayi nyuma ya imyaka irindwi bibera mu Rwanda gusa .
Icyo gihe ku ikubitiro byatangiriye i Berlin mu Budage , bikomereza i Amsterdam mu Buholandi , hanyuma bisorezwa i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
Ku wa Gatandatu tariki 6 Nyakanga 2019 habayeho igikorwa cya Kigali Fashion Week ku nshuro yacyo ya cumi kuva gitangijwe mu Rwanda , cyabereye muri Kigali Serena Hotel .
Cyahurije hamwe abamurika imideli batandukanye bo mu Rwanda no hanze yarwo ndetse na abayihanga , biyerekanye mu buryo bwanyuze abacyitabiriye .
Herekanwe imyambaro itandukanye irimo iya inzu zihanga imideli nka Ucoco na The 5 Mith yo mu Burundi , By The Way Clothes yo mu Bubiligi na Gissa Fashion Design yo muri Suède .
Abahanga imideli bo mu Rwanda biyerekanye barimo Aqua , Ihogoza Design , Dk Textiles , Ibya iwacu Summer Collection , Mundi Design na Karen Karsh wa Karsh Collections .
Sayaka Akimoto ushinzwe kumenyekanisha Tokyo Africa Collection 2019 na Leo Sugo utegura iki gikorwa bari mu bacyitabiriye .
Kigali Fashion Week yatangiye mu 2012 , itangirana na ibindi birori birimo icya Kampala , Bujumbura na Nairobi Fashion week .
Inategura ibitaramo muri Ghana na ibindi bihugu bikomeye ndetse yanatangiye ibirori birimo Kigali International Fashion Week ibera mu Buholandi , u Bubiligi , u Budage na u Bwongereza .
Uyu mwaka bazatangira ibindi birori birimo ibizabera i New York , Thailand na Singapore .
Kim Kardashian yahinduye izina rya imideli ye nyuma yo kotswa igitutu na Abayapani .
Tariki 2 Kamena 2019 nibwo Kim Karashian yamuritse imyambaro ya imbere igaragaza imiterere ya abagore ayita " " " " Kimono . " " " "
Bikimara kumenyekana ko yise iyi myambaro atyo , ntibyishimiwe na benshi biganjemo abo mu Buyapani bifashishije imbuga nkoranyambaga bakamwamaganira kure bavuga ko ari gusuzugura umuco wabo .
Ubusanzwe Kimono ni umwambaro wubashywe mu muco wa Abayapani wambarwa mu birori bikomeye nka ubukwe , gushyingura na indi minsi mikuru .
Nyuma ya iki gitutu , Kim Kardashian , yemeje ko agiye gushaka irindi zina risimbura Kimono yambuwe na abayapani .
Abinyujije kuri Twitter na Instagram , Kim Kardashian yatangaje ko yamaze guhindura izina rya iyi mideli ayita " " " " SKIMS . " " " "
Ati " " " " Abakunzi banjye na abankurikira mbakuraho ibitekerezo byinshi .
Numva ibitekerezo byabo kandi nishimiye ko bampaye ibitekerezo ku mideli yanjye mishya .
Nyuma yo kubiha agaciro nishimiye kubatangariza ku mugaragaro SKIMS . " " " "
