Paul B ö ger yabwiye IGIHE ko nyuma yo gusoza amashuri yisumbuye aribwo yaje mu Rwanda mu imenyereza rya umwaka umwe mu kigo cya ibidukikije mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Binyuze muri iryo menyereza yakoze mu 2015 , yashituwe na uruganda rwa imideli mu Rwanda avuga ko yari amaze imyaka myinshi mu bijyanye na uru ruganda ariko muri icyo gihe ku nshuro ye ya mbere yahisemo gutangira guhanga imyambaro ye ikozwe muri Made in Rwanda bivuye mu bitekerezo bye .
Ati " " " " Byaranshimishije cyane gukora imyambaro ivuye mu bitekerezo byacu ariko noneho ari iya " " " " Made in Rwanda . " " " " " " " "
Mu 2016 avuga ko byamushimishije gukora imyambaro yishimiwe na benshi ndetse agenda yakira inyunganizi nziza zimwereka ko yagize igitekerezo cyiza .
B ö ger yahisemo gukorana na abakora ibijyanye na imyambaro bo mu Rwanda ndetse inzu ihanga imideli ye ayita " " " " Izuba Clothing . " " " "
Mu 2016 yashyize hanze imyambaro yahanze ya " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " anayimurika mu imurikagurisha rya Shaban Masengesho ryabereye muri Mainz .
Nyuma yo gukora imyambaro ayijyana iwabo mu Budage akayibika mu bubiko ahafite , iyo amaze kuyigezayo atangira kuyicuruza ku rubuga rwa internet kuri
Uyu musore amaze kwitabira ibikorwa bitandukanye mu Budage na ibindi bihugu bihana imbibi amenyekanisha umudeli we wihariye wa " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " akavuga ko benshi mu bazungu bagenzi be babyishimira .
Avuga ko abantu benshi batita cyane ku ho imyenda yabo yakorewe ndetse na uwayikoze gusa ngo kuri we ni ingenzi cyane kubivuga no kugaragaza aho imyambaro yaturutse na uri kuyikora .
Yahisemo guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda kuko yabonye imyambaro myinshi yo mu Rwanda iva hanze .
Ati " " " " Amaduka na amasoko yo mu Rwanda aba yuzuyemo ibyaturutse hanze ya u Rwanda mu bihugu bya ibituranyi cyangwa byinshi byaturutse i Burayi , Aziya cyangwa Amerika .
Ariko imyambaro yo mu Rwanda ntabwo icuruzwa mu Burayi .
Ntewe imbaraga na ubukangurambaga nasanze mu Rwanda bwa " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " nasanze byaba inzira nziza yo kumenyekanisha iyi myambaro ku rwego rwa Isi . " " " "
" " " " Hari isoko rinini mu bijyanye no gukora no gucuruza imyambaro , nshaka ko imyambaro ya " " " " Made in Rwanda " " " " igaragara cyane mu Burayi cyane cyane muri Budage iwacu . " " " "
Avuga igitekerezo cyo kwita iduka rye " " " " Izuba " " " " cyaturutse ku kuba izuba rirasa buri munsi , akaba ashaka ko iduka rye rikomeza kuba nka izuba .
Mu myaka itanu iri imbere ashaka kuzaba amaze gufatisha isoko rya imyambaro ye mu Rwanda .
Intego ye ni ukugira ububiko bwa imyambaro ye mu Rwanda no mu Budage .
Imyambarire igezweho mu banyamujyi ba abanyabirori ( Amafoto ) .
Akenshi usanga ibijyanye na imyambarire ari ibihe byisubiramo , bisa nka aho nta kintu gishya kigihangwa ahubwo imyambaro yakanyujijeho mu bihe bya kera ariyo yongera kwadukanwa na ikindi gisekuru .
Ingero ni nyinshi zihari ariko dufatiye ku nkweto ya DH yamamaye mu bihe byo hambere , abakurikirana bazi neza ko iyi mu minsi ya vuba yagarutse mu yindi sura ya " " " " All Star Converse " " " " yongera guhararwa na benshi mu rubyiruko ndetse na na ubu yambarwa na abatari bake barimo na ibyamamare .
Nta gishya mu myambarire ahubwo biba ari nko kongera kwiyibutsa ibyo abakurambere bakunze kurimba bikagenda bihererekanywa uko imyaka yahise .
IGIHE yakusanyije imwe mu myambarire igezweho muri iki gihe cyane cyane mu banyamujyi ariko igenda ituruka ku mico ya ahandi bitewe na ibiba bigezweho mu myambarire ya ibyamamare .
Gutebeza ishati igice kimwe ( Half Tuck )
The Guardian itangaza ko iyi myambarire yamamaye cyane kuva mu 2013 ikaza gusa nka aho icogora kugeza aho muri uyu mwaka yongeye kwigarurira imitima ya benshi .
Ni imyambarire igezweho muri iki gihe mu banyamujyi , iyi usanga benshi mu rubyiruko bayikunda cyane .
Kuva mu muhanda usanga abenshi bambaye muri ubwo buryo , aho ishati itebezwa igice kimwe ikindi kigasigara kirereta .
Biragoye kugenda metero zirenze 300 utarahura na uwarimbye muri ubwo buryo cyane mu duce duhuriramo abantu benshi .
Biba akarusho rero iyo ugiye mu bitaramo kuko kuva ku bahanzi kugera mu bafana babo usanga baserutse muri uwo mwambaro .
Ibi bigaragaza ko iyi myambarire ikunzwe bidasubirwaho .
Kwambara agakapu ko mu rukenyerero ( Waist Bag )
Kwambara ukarenzaho agakapu nabyo biri mu bigezweho cyane muri iki gihe .
Wikipedia igaragaraza ko udukapu twambarwa mu rukenyerero Abanyamerika batwita Fanny Pack , Belt bag cyangwa Belly bag mu gihe Abongereza bo batwita Bum Bag .
Mu mateka , utu dukapu abantu batwambaraga bashaka kwirinda ibisambo .
Utu dukapu twafatanywaga na imikandara mu mico itandukanye guhera mu bihe byo hambere .
Mu myaka yo mu 1980 nibwo utu dukapu twongeye gukorerwa ivugurura ndetse dushyirwa mu kinyamakuru cya Vogue kizwiho kwandika ku byerekeye imideli .
Mu 2012 abahanga imideli batandukanye bongeye kutwadukana batwise " " " " Belted Satchels " " " " cyangwa se " " " " Hands - Free Bags " " " " bashaka kuzana imyambaro ihenze ya abakunda kurimba .
Mu Bufaransa utu dukapu batwita Banana Bags , muri Espagne bakatwita Kidney Bags naho mu Butaliyani ho batwita Marsupio .
Mu 2018 , The Boston Globe yatangaje ko udukapu tunitwa " " " " Fanny Packs " " " " twagarutse muri Vogue dufite indi myihariko tuzanywe na abahanga imideli bakomeye barimo Gucci , Prada na Louis Vuitton .
Twambawe na ibyamamare bitandukanye birimo Kim Kardashian , Rihanna , Jaden Smith na Russell Westbrook .
Uretse kutwambara mu rukenyerero utu dukapu hari na abatwambara batunyujije mu gatuza tukamanuka tukanyura mu kwaha no mu mugongo .
Ubwoko bwa udukapu dukunzwe kwambarwa turimo utwa Supreme , Adidas na Fila na utundi .
Kwambara Jean Jacket ( Denim Jacket / Trucker Jacket ) na Hoodie
Mu myambarire igezweho mu Rwanda muri iki gihe harimo no kwambarira Jean Jacket ( ikoti rimeze nka ikoboyi ) inyuma ya umupira wa imbeho , urubyiruko rwinshi cyane cyane i Kigali na abandi basirimu bari mu bakunda kurimba muri ubu buryo .
Kwambara gutya mu Rwanda byatangiye kwamamara cyane mu ntangiriro za 2019 nyuma ya uko mu mwaka ushize habanje kugerwaho kwambara Jean Jacket nabyo bigaca ibintu .
Hari na amakoti yitwa " " " " Hooded Denim Jacket " " " " yo afite ishusho ya umupira wa ingofero ufatanye na Denim cyangwa se Jean Jacket .
Jean Jacket yatangiye kwambarwa muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu kinyejana cya 19 , yakunzwe na ab ingeri zose ukajya wambarwa na abagabo na abagore .
Uyu mwambaro wahanzwe na uruganda rwa imyenda rwa Levi Strauss & Co . ruri mu zikomeye muri Amerika .
Imikandara ya Cinture Donna
Ni imikandara miremire yambarwa hagamijwe kurimba , uwambaye arawuzengurutsa yawugeza imbere akawureka ukarereta igice kinini ukenda kugera ku mavi .
Mu Karere ka Afurika ya Iburasirazuba iyi mikandara yamamaye cyane guhera mu 2018 biturutse ku ndirimbo yakoreshejwemo mu mashusho ya Sauti Sol na Nyashinski bise " " " " Short N Sweet " " " " yagiye hanze muri Gicurasi umwaka ushize .
Iyi ndirimbo imaze kurebwa na abasaga miliyoni 13 mu mwaka na amezi asaga abiri imaze hanze .
Uyu na wo ni umwe mu myambaro abanyamujyi benshi usanga baserukana mu minsi ya none .
Ubundi wasangaga mu minsi ishize umukobwa akenshi agenda yitwaje igikapu kinini mu ntoki ; iyo yabaga yasohokanye na abandi wasangaga bibangamye , ariko muri iki gihe siko bimeze ahubwo benshi bitwaza udukapu duto duhekwa .
Utu dukapu tuba turimo ibintu nkenerwa birimo ibyo bakwifashisha mu kwiyitaho ku isuku , telefoni , indahuzo ( chargeur ) na utundi dukoresho twa ngombwa umuntu ashobora gukenera mu rugendo .
Kuri benshi usanga utu dukapu baradusimbuje amasakoshi yari asanzwe amenyerewe cyane .
Ni udutambaro twambarwa mu mutwe duharawe na benshi muri iki gihe .
Durags zatangiye kwambarwa mu kinyejana cya 19 na abakozi ba Abanyamerika bakomoka muri Afurika ba abakene ndetse na abakoreshwaga uburetwa bashaka kurinda imisatsi yabo ngo itandura .
Mu 1930 Durags zatangiye kwambarwa nka uturinda musatsi , nyuma ya icyiswe Black Power Movement mu 1960 ihinduka kimwe mu mirimbo mu Banyamerika bakomoka muri Afurika .
Zanambarwaga na abaraperi na abakinnyi ba imikino itandukanye cyane aba igitsinagabo bo mu myaka itandukanye .
Mu 2000 , kwambara Durags mu ruhame byabaye nka ibitakigezweho mu bice bimwe ariko zigumana ubwamamare bwazo ahandi .
Umuraperi A $ AP Ferg yongeye guhesha agaciro Durags mu myaka yashize bikubitanye no kugaruka kwa inyogosho benshi bazi nka " " " " Waves , " " " " Durags zongera kugira agaciro gakomeye mu muryango wa Abanyamerika bafite inkomoko muri Afurika .
Kwambara Durags muri Amerika byagiye biteza impagarara cyane , hari nka ubwo mu 2001 abakinnyi ba Shampiyona ya Umupira wa Amaguru yo muri Amerika bigeze kubuzwa kuzambara zo na bandana .
No mu mashuri yisumbuye bigeze kubuzwa kuzambara ; nko mu Ishuri ryisumbuye rya John Muir riherereye i Pasadena muri California ryarabikoze mu ntangiriro za 2019 abanyeshuri barigaragambya mu mutuzo .
Iyi myigaragambyo yakozwe na Ihuriro rya abanyeshuri ba abirabura .
Aba banyeshuri bakoze imyigaragambyo bashinja ubuyobozi bwa ishuri kuvuga ko " " " " Kwambara Durags bizatuma abanyeshuri bacengerwa na imico ya amabandi " " " " gusa umuyobozi wa ishuri we yireguye avuga ko ataribyo ahubwo babikoze kubera " " " " Indangagaciro za ishuri za uko bagomba kwitwara ku ishuri . " " " "
Athleisure ni uburyo bwa imyambarire aho imyenda isanzwe ikoreshwa muri siporo , abantu bayambara bagiye mu kazi , ku ishuri cyangwa ibindi birori .
Niba ukurikirana umuziki , indirimbo Safi Madiba yahuriyemo na Meddy bise " " " " Got it It " " " " igaragaza neza uko uyu mugabo wahoze muri Urban Boyz aseruka yambaye amatiriningi atukura .
Iyi myambarire nayo igezweho cyane muri iki gihe bya umwihariko cyane ko ari mu gihe cya impeshyi , kwambara gutya ni uburyo bwo gusubira mu bihe byo hambere ukajyanisha na inkweto za siporo .
Abamaze gusobanukirwa na ibijyanye na imyambarire usanga aribo bambara muri ubu buryo cyane cyane .
Iyi nayo ni imyambaro igezweho muri iki gihe , ni amapantalo asa nka acikaguritse ariko akaba asohoka mu ruganda ariko akozwe .
Ashobora kuba acitse ku ivi , ku kibero cyangwa ahandi .
Urubuga rwa Apparelsearch rugaragaza ko uyu mwambaro watangiye gukoreshwa ukanamamara cyane kuva mu kinyejana cya 20 , mu myaka ya 1980 kugeza mu 2000 .
Mu ntangiriro za 2010 nibwo yongeye kwambarwa cyane ku migabane itandukanye .
Guhera mu 2017 uyu mwambaro benshi biganjemo urubyiruko batangiye kuwambara cyane bitandukanye na indi myaka kugeza na na uyu munsi na umwe mu ya abanyabirori .
Iyi myambaro ya abakobwa nayo iri mu igezweho mu banyamujyi .
Ni ipantalo za abakobwa ziba zizamutse ugasanga zambariwe zikagera mu mayunguyungu .
Ni umwe mu myambaro igezweho mu bakobwa muri Kigali ntiwatera metero 100 utarahura na umukobwa uyambaye .
Ipantaro nka izi za abahungu zirahari ariko mu Rwanda ho ntabwo zamamaye cyane nka iz abakobwa .
Iyi myenda yoroheye cyane ikorwa na " " " " Off White " " " " ya Virgil Abloh ufite ababyeyi bo muri Ghana ariko wavukiye muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika akaba ari naho akorera ibikorwa bye bitandukanye bijyanye no guhanga imyenda .
Iyi myenda nayo ni myiza ku muntu ukeneye kwambara bijyanye na igihe cya impeshyi kuko yoroheye kandi ikaba igufasha iyo hari izuba ryinshi .
Ni yo umuhanzikazi Queen Cha aheruka guserukana ku rubyiniro ubwo yari mu gitaramo cya cyabereye mu Karere ka Rubavu ku wa 29 Kamena .
Ni amadarubindi asa nka aho aribwo ari gukundwa na benshi cya mu Rwanda , nyamara yatangiye kwamamara cyane mu 2018 cyane muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika biturutse kuri Kanye West .
Ibyamamare byayambaye birimo Kendall na Kylie Jenner , Bella na Gigi Hadid , Kim Kardashian , Kanye West na abana ba ibyamamare barimo Zoe Kravitz , Kaia Gerber na Hailey Baldwin .
Aya madarubindi yamamaye ubwo Kim Kardashian yayambaraga mu gace ka ikiganiro cyo muri Mutarama 2018 cya " " " " Keeping Up With the Kardashians " " " " gikorwa na uyu mugore .
Icyo gihe yavuze ko umugabo yamwoherereje ubutumwa amubuza kwambara amadarubindi manini ahubwo amwoherereza amafoto yaya ya " " " " Tinny " " " " amubwira ko ariyo agomba kwambara .
Icyo gihe mu binyamakuru bitandukanye birimo E !
Channel , Independent na HuffPost mu nkuru nyamukuru zabo habanzaga izivuga kuri aya madarubindi , ahita yamamara atyo .
Kanye West ntabwo ariwe wahimbye aya madarubindi ahubwo icyo yakoze ni ukuyamenyekanisha kuko yakozwe na Adam Selman uhanga imideli wanahanze iyambawe na abarimo Rihanna , Beyoncé na Lady Gaga .
High Heels ni zimwe mu nkweto abanyamujyi benshi bakunze kwambara , zambarwa ku makanzu cyangwa se ku mapantalo .
Ni inkweto zihora imbere mu bijyanye na imyambarire ya abagore kuko akenshi nizo bambara iyo bagiye mu birori bikomeye .
Iza Batzuzhi zikorwa na inzu ya imideli ya Batzuzhi yo mu Butaliyani ni zo zigezweho muri iki gihe .
Ni inkweto ndende usanga zifite talon ndende ndetse uzirebeye kure ubona ko zifite ubugenge mu kuzigenderamo .
Izi nkweto zifite imiterere itandukanye ndetse ziza mu mabara anyuranye .
Uzambaye aba muremure bitewe na uko ziba zitereye mu kirere .
nkweto za Balenciaga ziri mu zikunzwe cyane mu bazi kurimba , abashaka gukora siporo cyangwa se kwambara inkweto zinepa ariko zifite talon nini .
Benshi mu bakora siporo mu nzu zikomeye muri Kigali , usanga bazambaye .
Ni inkweto zikorwa na uruganda rwa Balenciaga S . A . rwashinzwe na Umunya - Espagne , Crist ó bal Balenciaga .
Imideli ikoranywe ubuhanga na intambuko zinogeye ijisho mu byaranze Kigali Fashion Week 2019 ( Amafoto ) .
Kigali Fashion Week " " " " ni igitaramo kimaze kubaka izina mu Rwanda kandi gikundwa na benshi mu bakurikiranira hafi ibijyanye na imideli .
Covid - 19 : Pfizer - BioNTech ishaka uburenganzira bwo gutanga urukingo rwa Gatatu .
Pfizer - BioNTech yavuze ko igeragezwa ryakorewe muri Israël ryagaragaje ko urukingo rwa Gatatu rwa Coronavirus rutanzwe nyuma ya amezi atandatu cyangwa 12 umuntu ahawe inkingo zombi za Covid - 19 , rwongerera umubiri abasirikare inshuro eshanu kugeza ku 10 , bityo ukagira ubushobozi bwo kurwanya virus zihinduranyije cyane nka iyitwa Beta
yagaragaye bwa mbere muri Afurika ya Epfo .
Ibi bigo kandi byatangaje ko uru rukingo rwa Gatatu ruzabasha guhangana na virus ya Delta yagaragaye bwa mbere mu Buhinde iri kwibasira abatuye Isi , ifite ubukana kurusha izindi virus zose ziriho kugeza ubu .
Pfizer - BioNTech yavuze ko ariko iteganya no gukora urukingo rwihariye rugenewe kurwanya virus ya Delta kuko imaze kuzahaza abatuye Isi cyane muri Afurika no muri Aziya ndetse yatangiye no kugera i Burayi no muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Ibi bigo byombi Pfizer na BioNTech bifite gahunda yo gusaba uburenganzira ibigo bishinzwe ubuvuzi , birimo Ikigo gishinzwe Ibiribwa na Imiti cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , FDA na Ikigo gishinzwe Ubuvuzi cya i Burayi , EMA , bwo gutanga urukingo rwa Gatatu ku baturage nyuma yo kurugerageza bagasanga rufite ubushobozi bwo
kurinda Covid - 19 yihinduranyije .
FDA ndetse na ibigo bishinzwe kugenzura indwara no kuzirinda byo muri Amerika byo byahise byerekana uruhande bihagazeho , bivuga ko ababishinzwe bazabanza kugenzura ngo barebe niba koko abantu bakeneye urukingo rwa Gatatu .
Bongeyeho bati " " " " Abanyamerika biteje inkingo ebyiri za Covid - 19 , ubu ntabwo bakeneye urukingo rwa Gatatu rwo kubongerera ubudahangarwa .
Tuzategura gutanga urukingo rwa Gatatu igihe siyansi izaba yerekana ko rukenewe koko . " " " "
Kugeza ubu inkingo za Coronavirus zimaze gukorwa zikanemezwa na Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye ryita ku buzima , OMS , ni Pfizer - BioNTech ndetse na AstraZeneca , ariko izi nkingo zagaragaje ko zidafite ubushobozi buhagije bwo kurinda Coronavirus zihinduranyije ziri kwibasira Isi mu nkubiri ya Gatatu .
Abantu 14 bishwe na COVID - 19 mu Rwanda , abayikize ni 984 .
Minisante yatangaje ko abitabye Imana bazize COVID - 19 kuri uyu wa Kane barimo abagabo batandatu na abagore umunani .
Yakomeje iti " " " " Twihanganishije imiryango ya abagore umunani ba imyaka 89 ( Rulindo ) , 82 ( Musanze ) , 74 ( Rubavu ) , 74 ( Rutsiro ) , 63 ( Musanze ) , 58 ( Nyamasheke ) , 43 ( Karongi ) , 37 ( Kigali ) na abagabo batandatu ba imyaka 95 , 65 ( Nyagatare ) , 58 ( Musanze ) , 55 , 49 ( Kigali ) 27 ( Rubavu )
bitabye Imana . " " " " " " " "
Abarwayi bashya babonetse uyu munsi ni 911 basanzwe mu bipimo 8 . 350 .
Kuva muri Werurwe 2020 hamaze gufatwa ibipimo 1 . 700 . 200 , byasanzwemo abarwayi 45 . 950 .
Itangazo rya Minisante ryerekanye ko abarwayi bashya biganje mu Mujyi wa Kigali wabonetsemo 326 , Rubavu [ 70 ] , Nyamagabe [ 63 ] mu gihe Uturere twa Gisagara , Ruhango , Bugesera , Gatsibo na Nyabihu nta murwayi wahabonetse .
Abarwayi bakize mu masaha 24 bo biyongereyeho 984 bituma abamaze gukira baba 30 . 191 .
Abakiri kwitabwaho ni 15 . 238 barimo 71 barembye .
Abagera ku 392 . 077 ni bo bahawe urukingo .
Abantu 252 . 580 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa COVID - 19 rwa AstraZeneca barimo 572 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Nubwo umubare wa abarwayi bakira uri kuzamuka , abaturage basabwe gukomeza kwirinda ikwirakwira ryacyo cyane ko mu Rwanda habonetse ubwoko bushya bwa iki cyorezo .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima , Dr Ngamije Daniel , yatangarije RBA ko hari ibimenyetso bifatika bya uko ubwoko bushya bwa Coronavirus buzwi nka Delta bwageze mu Rwanda , bikaba bifite aho bihuriye na ubwiyongere bukabije bwa ubwandu na impfu bya icyo cyorezo biri kuboneka mu gihugu .
Magingo aya Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye ryita ku Buzima , OMS , rivuga ko Delta yagaragaye bwa mbere mu Buhinde ari bwo bwoko " " " " buhanganyikishije " " " " ugereranyije na Alpha yabonetse bwa mbere mu Bwongereza , Beta yagaragaye bwa mbere muri Afurika ya Epfo na Gamma yabonetse muri Brésil .
Abaturarwanda barasabwa gukomeza kubahiriza amabwiriza atangwa na inzego za ubuzima mu gukumira ikwirakwira rya icyorezo , arimo kwambara agapfukamunwa neza , guhana intera , gukaraba intoki kenshi cyangwa gukoresha umuti wica udukoko igihe cyose wakoze aho abandi bakoze .
Barasabwa kwirinda kwikorakora mu maso , ku zuru no ku munwa ndetse bakishyurana bakoresheje ikoranabuhanga aho bishoboka hose .
Ubwiyongere bwa Covid - 19 bugiye gutuma leta ishora miliyari 4 Frw mu byuma bitunganya umwuka .
Kugeza ejo ku itariki 6 Nyakanga hari abarwayi ba Coronavirus bagera ku 15 . 325 ndetse 67 muri bo bararembye mu gihe mu ntangiriro za Kamena abarembye batageraga no ku 10 .
Umuyobozi wa Ikigo cya igihugu kigura imiti na ibikoresho byo kwa muganga , RMS , Harerimana Pie , yavuze ko kuba u Rwanda rugiye gutumiza ibi byuma atari uko umwuka uhari udahagije ahubwo ari ukwirinda ko hazagira abawubura igihe abandura Covid - 19 bakomeje kwiyongera .
Mu kiganiro na The East African yagize ati " " " " Kugeza ubu dufite umwuka uhagije ariko tugiye gutumiza ibindi byuma bikora umwuka [ . . . ] Guverinoma ya u Rwanda yafashe icyemezo cyo kugura ibyo byuma ndetse muri iki cyumweru bizaba byageze mu gihugu . " " " "
" " " " Impamvu twabitumije , niba urugero ibitaro bifite abarwayi ba Coronavirus barembye bikoresha amacupa ya umwuka [ cylindre ] 200 , tugomba kuba dufite nibura andi 300 asaguka yo gukoresha muri ibyo bitaro gusa . " " " "
Mu igenzura ryakozwe na Minisiteri ya Ubuzima na RBC ryashyizwe ahagarara ku itariki 23 Nyakanga 2020 , rigaragaza ko mu Rwanda hari ibyuma bikora umwuka bigera kuri birindwi bitunganya amacupa ya umwuka hafi 7000 ku kwezi rimwe rifite litiro 50 mu gihe ku munsi hakorwa 230 .
Gusa uyu mubare ushobora kurenga aho ku munsi hashobora gukorwa amacupa ya umwuka 335 rimwe rifite litiro 50 .
Naho mu kwezi hakaba hakorwa umwuka ujya mu macupa 10 . 800 .
Sosiyete zitanga iyi serivisi yo gukora umwuka ni Oxymat , Inmatec , Airsep , Craft na Amico .
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda hari ibigo nderabuzima 508 , ibitaro bya Uturere 37 , ibya Intara bine na ibindi bitaro bikuru 8 .
Harerimana Pie yavuze ko bifuza ko muri buri bitaro haba ibyuma bikora umwuka bihoraho kuko hamwe na hamwe bagenda bahazana amacupa arimo umwuka bavomye ahari ibyo byuma biwukora .
Bwa mbere mu Rwanda abantu 16 bishwe na COVID - 19 mu munsi umwe , abayikize ni 816 .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko kuri uyu wa 7 Nyakanga 2021 abishwe na COVID - 19 bakuwe mu duce dutandukanye twa igihugu .
Itangazo rya Minisante rikomeza riti " " " " Twihanganishije imiryango ya abagore barindwi ba imyaka 91 ( Ngororero ) , 73 , 58 ( Rubavu ) , 61 , 36 , 19 ( Kigali ) , 58 ( Musanze ) na abagabo icyenda ba imyaka 73 , 62 , 44 ( Rubavu ) , 71 ( Ngororero ) , 69 , 35 ( Musanze ) , 59 ( Nyagatare ) 52 , 47 ( Kigali ) .
" " " " " " " "
Abahitanywe na COVID - 19 batumye umubare wa abamaze kwicwa na iki cyorezo kuva cyagera mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 bagera kuri 507 .
Ni ku nshuro ya mbere mu Rwanda habonetse umubare munini wa abahitanwe na COVID - 19 [ 16 ] mu munsi umwe kuko abenshi baherukaga kuboneka ari 12 , batangajwe ku wa 6 Nyakanga 2021 .
Kuri uyu munsi , abarwayi 760 ni bo banduye COVID - 19 mu bipimo 7 . 846 byafashwe .
Abarwayi bashya babonetse muri Kigali : 330 , Musanze : 65 , Kamonyi : 52 , Gicumbi : 38 , Rubavu : 37 mu gihe Uturere twa Gisagara , Ruhango , Kirehe na Ngoma nta bwandu bushya bwahabonetse .
Kuri ubu mu gihugu hose abamaze kwandura COVID - 19 ni 45 . 039 mu bipimo 1 . 691 . 850 bimaze gufatwa .
Kuri uyu wa Gatatu hakize abarwayi 816 byatumye abakize bagera ku 29 . 207 mu gihe 15 . 325 bakirwaye , muri bo 67 bakaba barembye .
Kuva ibikorwa byo gukingira COVID - 19 bitangiye mu Rwanda , abaturage 392 . 003 bahawe urukingo .
Abantu 252 . 008 ni bo bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa AstraZeneca barimo 45 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Abagore bitabira serivisi zo kuboneza urubyaro mu Rwanda bageze kuri 64 % .
Muri ubu bushakashatsi bwakozwe mu 2019 / 2020 , NISR , igaragaza ko abagore 34 % bifuza kuzongera kubyara nyuma ya igihe runaka , naho 3 % ari ingumba , mu gihe 10 % bifuzaga kubyara mu gihe cya vuba , 2 % bo nta mwanzuro bafashe .
Abaturage bya umwihariko abagore baganiriye na RBA , bavuze ko zimwe mu mpamvu zatumye bafata icyemezo cyo kurekeraho kubyara ari uko ubuzima bugoye mu bijyanye no kubona ubushobozi cyangwa imibereho .
Uwitwa Uhoranimpuhwe Ruth utuye mu Karere ka Rwamagana , avuga ko we na umugabo we bafite abana babiri aho umwe afite imyaka icyenda , undi umwaka na igice , bombi bavuga ko bafashe icyemezo cyo kuboneza urubyaro .
Ati " " " " Ubu ngubu nafashe agashinge ka amezi atatu , nta kibazo rero njyewe biramfasha . " " " "
Bamwe mu batuye mu Mujyi wa Kigali ubuzima bugoye ari nayo mpamvu bahisemo kuboneza urubyaro abandi bifungisha burundu kubera ko ikiguzi cya umwana kiri hejuru cyane .
Umwe yagize ati " " " " Icyatumye mboneza urubyaro , abana batandatu mu Mujyi wa Kigali , inzu ndayikodesha no kubahahira ibyo kurya [ . . . ] ni abo nta bandi .
Impamvu yatumye mfata icyemezo cyo kuboneza , ba Se twaratandukanye , ubu ninjye ubarera njyenyine ariko ubu no kubatunga bimaze kunanira kubera ko nta mikorere . " " " "
Mugenzi we yagize ati " " " " Njyewe naraboneje !
Mfite agapira ka imyaka itanu mu kuboko kwanjye , ngomba kuboneza kuko ba bana batatu , Imana imbabariye rwose nanarekera abo ngabo . " " " "
Hirya no hino mu gihugu mu bigo nderabuzima hari serivisi zo kuboneza urubyaro zihatangirwa ndetse hakaba na izindi zitangwa na abajyanama ba ubuzima ku buryo ababyeyi baje kwisuzumisha inda ndetse na abaje gukingiza abana bose bakangurirwa kuboneza urubyaro ku bushake .
Umuyobozi wa Ikigo Nderabuzima cya Nyagasambu , Bihibindi Jean Christophe , avuga ko byibuze nka 60 % bya abakanguriwe bahita bafata umwanzuro .
Ati " " " " Abatashye bataboneje , iyo amaze kwemera uburyo yazakoresha amaze kubyara , iyo yabyaye bwa buryo arabutahana . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ariko hari na abavuga bati njyewe nazaza nje gukingiza noneho muri gahunda yo gukingiza , tugira uburyo bwo kwigisha ababyeyi noneho ababishaka bagataha uburyo bwo kuboneza urubyaro . " " " "
Ni ibyo kwishimira ?
Abahanga mu birebana na ubwiyongere bwa abantu na iterambere ryabo , bemeza ko ibi biterwa na izamuka rya imyumvire igihugu gikeneye kubakiraho iterambere rya abagituye , bitewe na uko ubwiyongere bukabije bwa abaturage butakijyanye na ubushobozi bwa igihugu .
Ibi kandi ngo bigira ingaruka mbi ku mibereho ya abaturage muri rusange .
Impuguke mu birebana na Ubwiyongere bwa Abaturage na Iterambere ryabo akaba na Umwarimu muri Kaminuza ya u Rwanda , Dr . Ignace Kabano , avuga ko iki kigero cya abagore baboneza urubyaro ari ikigero igihugu cyakwishimira bitewe na inyungu zirimo .
Yagize ati " " " " Igihugu kibaho kigizwe na abaturage , iterambere ryabo cyangwa ibyo igihugu kinjiza [ umusaruro mbumbe wa igihugu ] bituruka ku bikorwa cyangwa imirimo ya abaturage .
Igihe abaturage batangiye kuringaniza imbyaro bagana mu cyerekezo cya ibikenewe mu muryango , ni inyungu ku gihugu .
Ni ibyo kwishimira muri rusange . " " " "
" " " " Ikindi cya kabiri , bigaragaza ko abaturage , izo serivisi zibafasha kuringaniza urubyaro bazigeraho ni ukuvuga ngo ushatse kwifungisha abona iyo serivisi .
Ushatse gushyira intera hagati ya urubyaro na urundi cyangwa inda na indi arayibona . " " " "
Imibare ya NISR igaragaza ko hakurikijwe uburumbuke mu Rwanda , abagore bo mu mijyi , nibura umwe abarirwa abana 3 . 4 , naho uwo mu cyaro bakaba 4 . 3 .
Ni mu gihe mu 2005 umugore ugejeje igihe cyo kubyara yabarirwaga abana batandatu , mu 2014 / 2015 uwo mubare wari ugeze ku bana 4 . 2 ku mugore naho mu 2019 / 2020 bagera ku bana bane ku mugore .
Iyi mibare yerekana kandi ko abatagerwaho na serivisi zo kuboneza urubyaro bavuye kuri 39 % mu 2005 , bagera kuri 14 % mu 2019 / 2020 .
Abagore bakoresha uburyo bwo kuboneza urubyaro mu 2019 - 2020 bari 64 % .
Huye : Mu bagera ku 127 banduye Covid - 19 , abarenga 60 bari mu Murenge umwe .
Byavuzwe kuri uyu wa Gatatu ubwo urugaga rwa abikorera bo mu Karere ka Huye batangizaga ubukangurambaga bwihariye bwo gukumira Covid - 19 hashyirwaho na abahwituzi muri buri gace .
Umuyobozi wa urwo rugaga , Kayitasire Egide , yavuze ko bashaka ko bo nka abikorera ari bo bafata ingamba mbere na mbere zo kwirinda Covid - 19 no kuyirinda abandi .
Ati " " " " Turashaka ko tutazajya dutegereza abaza kuduhwitura cyangwa abaza kureba ko twubahiriza amabwiriza , ahubwo ni twe twishatsemo ibizubizo kugira ngo tubyikorere ndetse dushyireho na abahwituzi mu bikorera bagenzi bacu bashinzwe kureba uwo begeranye , niba ashyira mu bikorwa ingamba zafashwe zo kwirinda iki cyorezo .
Yavuze ko buri gace gakorerwamo ubucuruzi gafite umuhwituzi wako uzajya ureba niba hari abatubahiriza amabwiriza , yabona hari abayarengaho nkana inshuro nyinshi bagafatirwa ibihano birimo no gufungirwa .
Umuyobozi wa Akarere ka Huye , Sebutege Ange , yavuze ko kugeza ubu imibare ya abanduye Covid - 19 muri Huye yiganje mu mirenge itatu yo mu mujyi ariko umwe muri yo wihariye umubare munini .
Ati " " " " Ubu mu Karere dufite abanduye Covid - 19 bagera ku 127 muri bo 94 bari mu mirenge itatu .
60 bari mu Murenge wa Tumba , 22 bakaba mu Murenge wa Ngoma , hanyuma 12 bakaba mu Murenge wa Mbazi . " " " "
Sebutege yavuze ko nko mu Murenge wa Ngoma mu banduye 12 abagera ku munani ari abo mu Kagari kamwe ka Matyazo .
Ati " " " " Urumva ko bisaba umwihariko wa buri gace na umwihariko wa buri kintu umuntu akora kugira ngo aho uri , ukorera cyangwa ushakira ubuzima wirinde . " " " "
Yakomeje avuga ko mu bantu 127 bose bagaragaraho ubwandu bwa Covid - 19 abarenga 70 bayanduye mu minsi ine ishize , bityo bari gukora ubukangurambaga kugira ngo imibare ya abandura idakomeza kuzamuka .
Yavuze ko isesengura bakoze ryagaragaje ko Umurenge wa Tumba ugaragamo ubwandu bwa Covid - 19 kurusha indi byatewe na uko abawutuye na abawukoreramo biraye bakarenga ku mabwiriza yashyizweho yo kwirinda .
Kugeza ubu mu Karere ka Huye hari ibigo bibiri byafunzwe kuko basanze abakozi babikoramo bose baranduye .
Kimwe gikoramo abantu barindwi naho ikindi ni batandatu .
Sebutege yavuze ko kuri ubu abajyanama ba ubuzima bari gusura ingo zose bareba niba hari umuntu ufite ibimenyetso bya Covid - 19 bakamusaba kujya kwipimisha .
Hafashwe ingamba ko iyo hari urugo rubonetsemo uwanduye , abarurimo bose basabwa kwishyira mu kato kugira ngo babanze basuzumwe .
Bamwe mu bakorera ubucuruzi mu duce twiganjemo Covid - 19 babwiye IGIHE ko na bo bari gukora ibishoboka byose ngo birinde barinda na abakiriya babo kuko iyo imibare izamutse bibagiraho ingaruka mbi .
Hitayezu Pascal ati " " " " Ingamba turi kuzubahiriza kandi twongereye imbaraga kuko iyo imibare ya abanduye izamutse bitugiraho ingaruka nyinshi , kuko iyo bavuze ngo funga urabikora kandi ukwezi kuzashira ukishyura nyira inzu .
Iyo badufungiye hari na ibicuruzwa byangirika birmo nka amata na ibindi . " " " "
Kugeza ubu mu duce icyorezo cya Covid - 19 kigaragaramo cyane mu Karere ka Huye , hafashwe ingamba zihariye zo kugikumira zirimo kuba bafunze insengero zose , abacuruzi bakorera icyarimwe bagabanyijwe ku kigero cya 50 % .
Abantu 12 bishwe na COVID - 19 mu munsi umwe , abayanduye mu Rwanda ni 883 .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko kuri uyu wa 6 Nyakanga 2021 abishwe na COVID - 19 babonetse mu bice bitandukanye bya igihugu ; barimo abagore bane ba imyaka 80 mu Rutsiro , abafite imyaka 77 , 76 ba i Kigali , uwa 69 wa i Ruhango na abagabo umunani ba imyaka 91 muri Gakenke , abafite imyaka 88 , 83 mu Rutsiro , ufite
imyaka 82 wa i Karongi , abafite imyaka 77 , 66 , 51 muri Kigali na uwa 63 wo mu Bugesera .
Kuri uyu munsi , abarwayi 883 ni bo banduye COVID - 19 mu bipimo 6 . 492 byafashwe .
Abarwayi bashya babonetse muri Kigali : 257 , Musanze : 94 , Gicumbi : 46 , mu gihe Uturere twa Gisagara na Ngoma ho nta murwayi wahabonetse .
Kuri ubu mu gihugu hose abamaze kwandura COVID - 19 ni 44 . 279 mu bipimo 1 . 684 . 004 bimaze gufatwa .
Kuri uyu wa Kabiri hakize abarwayi 554 byatumye abakize bagera ku 28 . 391 mu gihe 15 . 397 bakirwaye , muri bo 57 bakaba barembye .
Kuva ibikorwa byo gukingira COVID - 19 bitangiye mu Rwanda , abaturage 392 . 003 bahawe urukingo .
Abantu 251 . 963 ni bo bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa AstraZeneca barimo 244 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Abantu icyenda bahitanywe na Covid - 19 , abarenga 800 barayandura .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko abahitanywe na Covid - 19 mu masaha 24 yashize ari abagore bane barimo uwa imyaka 82 ya amavuko i Kigali , uwa imyaka 76 wa i Rubavu , uwa 62 i Karongi , 57 mu Ruhango na abagabo batanu ba imyaka 79 , 72 , 52 na 51 ba i Kigali na uwa 64 i Rubavu .
Abarwayi bashya 811 babonetse mu bipimo 6 . 766 byafashwe mu masaha 24 yashize bituma umubare wa abamaze kwandura mu Rwanda uba 43 . 396 mu bipimo 1 . 677 . 512 bimaze gufatwa kuva muri Werurwe 2020 .
Muri Kigali ni ho habonetse abanduye benshi bangana na 338 , Musanze 95 , Rusizi 47 , Kamonyi 38 mu gihe mu turere dutandatu nta murwayi mushya wabonetsemo .
Utu ni utwa Bugesera , Gisagara , Rutsiro , Nyagatare , Rwamagana na Nyamasheke .
Mu masaha 24 yashize , hakize abarwayi 231 .
Muri rusange abamaze gusezererwa mu bitaro ni ku 27 . 837 .
Abakirwaye ni 15 . 080 barimo 62 barembye .
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda hamaze gukingirwa abantu 391 . 970 kuva ibi bikorwa byatangira ku wa 5 Werurwe 2021 .
Abantu 251 . 719 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa COVID - 19 rwa AstraZeneca barimo 244 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Batanu bishwe na Coronavirus mu Rwanda , abayanduye ni 889 .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko batanu bishwe na Coronavirus kuri uyu wa 4 Nyakanga 2021 , ari abagore babiri ba imyaka 67 na 36 na abagabo batatu ba imyaka 63 , 58 na 32 bo mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Abarwayi bashya 889 babonetse mu bipimo 6 . 889 byafashwe mu masaha 24 yashize bituma umubare wa abamaze kwandura mu Rwanda uba 42 . 585 mu bipimo 1 . 672 . 746 bimaze gufatwa kuva muri Werurwe 2020 .
Minisante yagaragaje ko ubwandu bwinshi bwiganje muri Kigali ahabonetse abanduye 309 , Musanze [ 99 ] , Gicumbi [ 63 ] , Bugesera [ 56 ] , Rubavu [ 52 ] mu gihe mu Karere ka Kirehe nta murwayi mushya wahabonetse .
Mu masaha 24 yashize , nta murwayi wakize byatumye umubare wa abamaze gusezererwa mu bitaro no gukirira mu ngo zabo uguma ku 27 . 606 .
Kugeza uyu munsi , abarwayi 14 . 509 barimo 61 barembye ni bo bakiri kwitabwaho .
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda hamaze gukingirwa abantu 391 . 954 kuva ibi bikorwa byatangira ku wa 5 Werurwe 2021 .
Abantu 251 . 475 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa AstraZeneca barimo 14 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Ibitaro byitiriwe Umwami Faisal byakeje intambwe yatewe mu myaka 27 ishize .
Dr Kalimba yabigarutseho kuri iki Cyumweru tariki 4 Nyakanga 2021 , ku munsi wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 , mu butumwa yageneye Abanyarwanda na abandi bose bagana ibitaro byitiriwe Umwami Faisal .
Yagize ati " " " " Tuboneyeho gusubiza amaso inyuma tukishimira ibyagezweho mu ishami rya ubuzima na ubuvuzi muri rusange ariko bya umwihariko kuri twebwe hano ku bitaro byitiriwe Umwami Faisal . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Na ubwo urugendo rukiri rurerure , ibyagezweho ni byinshi ari umubare wa abaganga na ubushobozi bwabo ndetse na ibikoresho nkenerwa mu buvuzi dutanga na serivisi zose muri rusange .
Ibi byagezweho kubera ubufatanye na umuhate wa leta yacu . " " " "
Dr Kalimba avuga ko kugira ngo ibi bitaro na urwego rwa ubuzima rukomeza kwiyubaka muri rusange bisaba ko Abanyarwanda batahiriza umugozi umwe mu guhashya icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Ati " " " " Nashishikariza abatugana bose ndetse na Abanyarwanda muri rusange gukomeza kwitwararika kugira ngo duhangane na iki cyorezo kugira ngo dushobore kukinesha ni ukubahiriza amabwiriza twese tuzi atangwa na Minisiteri ya Ubuzima . " " " "
Ibi bitaro bifite abaganga ba inzobere 40 mu basaga 80 bahari .
Ibitaro byitiriwe umwami Faisal , Kigali byashinzwe hagati ya 1987 na 1991 hifashishijwe ikigega cya Arabia Sawudite gishinzwe iterambere ( SFD ) .
Ni ibitaro kuri ubu bya ikitegererezo biri ku rwego rwa Akarere ka Afurika ya Uburasirazuba aho bitanga ubuvuzi bwihariye , harimo gusuzuma indwara no kuvura byihariye .
Covid - 19 : Ko imibare ikomeje kwiyongera , aho ibitanda , Oxygène na ibindi bikoresho ntibiza kuba iyanga ?
Abasobanukiwe gato ntabwo ubwoba bwabo bugarukira kuri Guma mu Rugo , burakomeza bukagera no kwa muganga .
Ese iyi mibare ikomeje kwiyongera , u Rwanda ruraza gushobora guhangana na yo ?
Bya umwihariko rufite ibyangombwa nkenerwa byose ngo abarembye cyane bitabweho cyangwa rurahinduka iciro rya imigani nka aho duherutse kubona abarwayi bahabwaga serum na bya byuma bibongerera umwuka , bakoherezwa mu modoka cyangwa mu rugo kurwarirayo kubera ko ibitanda byabaye bike ?
Mu kwezi kwa Gatandatu gushize konyine , mu Rwanda habonetse abarwayi bashya ba Covid - 19 11267 , barimo 95 yahitanye .
Ni imibare myinshi ugereranyije na amezi yabanje .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima , Dr Daniel Ngamije aherutse gutangaza mu kiganiro na abanyamakuru , ko uko kwiyongera kwa imibare kwajyanye na ukwiyongera kwa abaremba ndetse na abicwa na iyo ndwara .
Mu gihe nta gikozwe ngo ubwiyongere bugabanuke , abaremba cyangwa abapfa bazakomeza .
Muri iyi nkundura ya gatatu ya ubwiyongere bwa Covid - 19 , umuntu yakwibaza niba u Rwanda rufite ibikenewe byose ngo rubashe guhangana na yo .
Minisitiri Ngamije yavuze ko mu barwayi bose ba Covid - 19 u Rwanda rufite , 95 % bari kuvurirwa mu rugo mu gihe 5 % ari bo bari mu bitaro .
Ibyo ntibyavanaho ko ibitaro nka Kanyinya byari byarafunzwe kubera kumanuka kwa abandura , byongeye gufungura imiryango mu gihe ibya Nyarugenge na byo imibare yatumbagiye ikava kuri 20 ubu bakaba basaga 125 .
Niba ibitaro byatangiye kuzura abagera kwa muganga ari 5 % bya abarwayi , hagezeyo 20 % hacura iki ?
Mu bihugu nka Kenya mu minsi yashize mu bitaro bya Kisumu Hospital ahari gukurikiranirwa abarwayi ba Covid - 19 , kubera ubwiyongere bukabije butewe na ubwoko bushya bwa Delta , abarwayi bakeneye kongererwa umwuka barenze ubushobozi bwa igihugu bitabaza ubufasha bwa abasirikare ba Abadage kugira ngo abarwayi barengerwe .
Si ho gusa kuko no mu Buhinde ubwo Delta yagaragaraga bwa mbere abarwayi biyongereye cyane mu buryo buteye impungenge ndetse abakenera umwuka baba benshi cyane bituma bitabaza za bomboni zo mu magaraje ya imodoka mu kuramira ubuzima bwa abaturage bwari mu kaga .
Kugeza ubu imibare ya Ishami rya Umuryango wa Abibumbye igaragaza ko muri Afurika Delta igeze ku kigero cya 25 % nko muri Uganda , mu barwayi bashya abasanganwa ubu bwoko bangana na 97 % naho muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo biri ku kigero cya 79 % bya abandura .
U Rwanda rwiteguye rute ?
Kuva icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyagera mu Rwanda , rwakomeje kugihagurukira ndetse hashyirwaho na ibigo byahariwe gukurikirana abarwayi ba Covid - 19 gusa birimo Kanyinya , Gatenga na ibitaro bya Akarere bya Nyarugenge .
Nubwo ibitaro bya Kanyinya byari byarahagaze kwakira abarwayi , byongeye gutangira gukora nyuma yo kubona ko icyorezo cyongeye gukaza umurego .
Ubushobozi kandi bwarongerewe kuko byibuze kuri buri bitaro bya akarere hari umuntu ushinzwe gufasha abarwayi barembye ndetse na ibitanda bifite ibyangombwa bishobora gufasha abantu barembye .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Ikigo cya Igihugu gishinzwe Ubuzima ( RBC ) , Dr Nsanzimana Sabin aherutse kuvuga ko ibitaro byose byo mu Rwanda bifite ahantu hashobora kuvurirwa abarwayi bari hagati ya bane na batanu barembye cyane .
Bya umwihariko nka Kibungo bafite ahakwakirirwa abarwayi bagera kuri 35 mu gihe Karongi naho bagiye kugira ahashobora kwakirirwa abagera kuri 50 .
Uretse ibi kandi abakurikiranirwa mu rugo bagenzurwa na abajyanama ba Ubuzima mu mudugudu ngo hato badatarabuka bagakongeza imbaga .
Kuri ubu mu Rwanda habarurwa ibitanda 500 byiteguye kwakira abarwayi barembye ba Covid - 19 , muri byo 180 bishobora kwakira abafite ibimenyetso bikomeye cyane , ni ukuvuga abakenera kongererwa umwuka [ ICU ] .
Mu kiganiro na Abanyamakuru kuri uya wa Kabiri tariki ya 29 Kamena 2021 , Minisitiri wa Ubuzima , Dr Daniel Ngamije yijeje ko igihugu gifite ubushobozi bwo kwakira abarwayi bafite ibimenyetso byoroheje ndetse na abafite ibimenyetso bikaze ( abarembye ) ariko ko Leta iri mu rugamba rwo kongera ubushobozi .
Ati " " " " Turacyafite ubushobozi buhagije ndetse na umwuka iyo hari uwukeneye dufite imashini zifite gutuganya umwuka abarwayi bakeneye .
Leta iri gushyira ingufu mu kongera ibitanda , imashini zabasha gukora ku buryo twakuba nka kabiri cyangwa gatatu ubushobozi dufite ubu .
Abarwayi baje kwa muganga nta na umwe utarahawe ubutabazi bukwiriye . " " " "
Nubwo ibihugu bituranye na u Rwanda nka Kenya , Uganda na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo byamaze kugerwamo na ubwoko bushya bwa COVID - 19 buzwi nka Delta , Minisitiri Ngamije yavuze ko hari gukorwa ubushakashatsi bugamije gutahura niba mu Rwanda naho bwaba bwarahageze .
Yagize ati " " " " Ubushakashatsi burakorwa , niba iya Abahinde iri mu bihugu duturanye , nta gitangaza ko yaba iri no mu Rwanda .
Iyi virusi ifite uburyo yihishe kugira ngo ibashe kubaho , birashoboka ariko icya ngombwa ni ugushyira mu bikorwa ariya mabwiriza yatanzwe .
Icya mbere ni ukwirinda , aho gutinda kuri ibi bya virusi nshya . " " " "
Yasabye Abaturarwanda gukomeza kubahiriza ingamba zashyizweho zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Covid - 19 , birinda gukorera ku gitsure cya ubuyobozi ahubwo bakabigira ibyabo kugira ngo icyorezo kibashe gutsindwa .
Batanu bishwe na COVID - 19 , abayanduye biyongeraho 884 .
Abitabye Imana ni abagore batatu ba imyaka 76 bo mu Karere ka Rubavu , ufite 57 wo mu Mujyi wa Kigali na uwa 31 wa i Muhanga ndetse na abagabo babiri barimo uwa imyaka 73 wa i Huye na ufite 49 wa i Kigali .
Itangazo rya Minisante ryo kuri uyu wa Gatanu ryerekanye ko abanduye Coronavirus mu Rwanda ari 884 biganjemo abo muri Kigali ahabonetse 179 .
I Rusizi ni 81 , Kamonyi ni 67 , Bugesera 47 mu gihe mu Turere twa Rwamagana na Nyabihu nta murwayi wahabonetse .
Kuva Coronavirus yaboneka mu Rwanda , hamaze gufatwa ibipimo 1 . 657 . 913 byasanzwemo abanduye 40 . 798 .
Kuri uyu munsi nta murwayi wakize byatumye abakirwaye baguma kuri 27 . 272 .
Abagera kuri 13 . 073 ni bo bakirwaye barimo 43 barembye .
Abantu bamaze kwicwa na Coronavirus mu Rwanda ni 453 .
Abamaze gukingirwa Coronavirus mu Rwanda ni 391 . 888 .
Abantu 251 . 350 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa Coronavirus rwa AstraZeneca barimo 211 bayihawe uyu munsi .
U Bushinwa bwashyizwe ku rutonde rwa ibihugu bitakirangwamo malaria .
Kuva mu myaka ya 1940 , abantu miliyoni 30 barwaraga malaria buri mwaka muri iki gihugu .
Ibintu byatumye gishyira imbaraga mu kuyirwanya cyivuye inyuma , gitera kenshi imiti yica udukoko ahantu hose , gitanga inzitiramibu zirimo umuti ndetse no gutanga imiti ivura malaria .
Amakuru dukesha BBC ni uko u Bushinwa ubu bumaze imyaka ine yikurikiranya nta murwayi wa malaria bubona , ibintu byabuhesheje uburenganzira bwo kwemezwa nka igihugu kitakirangwamo malaria .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa OMS , Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus , yavuze ko kugira ngo u Bushinwa bubashe guhashya burundu iyi ndwara iterwa na umubu wa Anophèle , byabusabye imbaraga zikomeye none nyuma ya imyaka myinshi buyirwanya bwabashije kuyihashya .
Kuri uyu wa 01 Nyakanga 2021 , ishyaka riri ku butegetsi mu Bushinwa , CPC , ryizihije imyaka 100 rimaze rishinzwe ndetse rinagejeje u Bushinwa ku iterambere mu mpande zose harimo na ubuzima .
Umuvugizi wa Minisiteri ya Ububanyi na Amahanga muri iki gihugu , Wang Wenbin , yavuze ko guverinoma ya u Bushinwa na iri shyaka byakoze ibishoboka kugira ngo birinde abaturage .
Ati " " " " CPC na guverinoma ya u Bushinwa , kuva kera byashyize imbere inyungu za abaturage , zirabarinda mu bijyanye na ubuzima , umutekano ndetse na ubukungu .
Guhashya malaria burundu ni umusanzu ukomeye u Bushinwa butanze ku byerekeye ubuzima ndetse na iterambere rya uburenganzira bwa muntu . " " " "
OMS yatangaje ko u Bushinwa bubaye igihugu cya 40 mu bihugu bitakirangwamo malaria ku Isi , mu gihe ahandi ikomeje kuzahaza abantu ndetse iri shami ritangaza ko mu mwaka wa 2019 abagera kuri miliyoni 229 bayirwaye abandi 409 . 000 bagapfa .
94 % bya abayanduye bose ni abo muri Afurika .
Kugira ngo igihugu kijye mu mubare w " " " " ibihugu bitarangwamo malaria , cyandikira OMS kikayereka ko kimaze imyaka ine ikurikirana kitagaragaramo umurwayi na umwe wayo ndetse kikerekana ibimenyetso na uburyo gishobora kwitwara mu gihe yaba igarutse mu gihugu .
Ibihugu biheruka gushyirwa kuri uru rutonde ni Argentine , Algérie ndetse na Uzbekistan .
Malaria ni indwara izahaza uyirwaye , igira ibimenyetso birimo umuriro , kubabara umutwe , kumva ukonje mu mubiri ndetse no gucika intege .
Kugeza ubu iravurwa igakira nubwo hari abo igihitana .
Mu ntangiriro za uyu mwaka hageragejwe urukingo rwayo rwakozwe na itsinda rya abashakashatsi bo muri Kaminuza ya Oxford mu Bwongereza , rugaragaza ko rufite ubushobozi bwo kurinda iyi ndwara ku rugero rwa 77 % mu igeragezwa ryakorewe muri Burkina Faso .
Uru rukingo ntabwo ruremezwa kuko basigaye kurugerageza mu bindi bihugu bine bya Afurika .
Mu mwaka wa 2019 , Nigeria ni cyo gihugu cyari gifite imibare myinshi ya abanduye ndetse bagahitanwa na malaria , igakurikirwa na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Tanzania , Burkina Faso , Mozambique na Niger .
Umubare wa abishwe na malaria mu Rwanda muri 2020 wagabanutseho32 % kuko abahitanywe na yo ari 148 mu gihe muri 2019 bari 218 .
RBC igaragaza ko uturere twa mbere twagaragayemo abarwayi benshi ba malaria muri 2020 ari Nyamasheke , Rusizi , Kayonza , Gisagara , Gasabo , Kamonyi , Rwamagana , Bugesera , Ruhango na Muhanga .
Bwa mbere mu Rwanda abantu 10 bishwe na COVID - 19 mu munsi umwe , abayanduye ni 867 .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko kuri uyu wa 1 Nyakanga 2021 abishwe na COVID - 19 barimo abagore bane ba imyaka 86 , 81 ba i Rubavu , abafite imyaka 72 na 62 ba i Burera na abagabo batandatu ba imyaka 89 , 65 , 56 , 51 , 46 bo muri Kigali na ufite imyaka 25 wo mu Karere ka Rulindo .
Abahitanywe na COVID - 19 batumye umubare wa abamaze kwicwa na iki cyorezo kuva cyagera mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 bagera kuri 448 .
Ni ku nshuro ya mbere mu Rwanda habonetse umubare munini wa abahitanwe na COVID - 19 [ 10 ] mu munsi umwe kuko abenshi baherukaga kuboneka ari icyenda , batangajwe ku 21 Mutarama 2021 .
Kuri uyu munsi , abarwayi 867 ni bo banduye COVID - 19 mu bipimo 9 . 047 byafashwe .
Abarwayi bashya babonetse muri Kigali : 208 , Kamonyi : 74 , Rubavu : 73 , Gicumbi : 66 , Musanze : 46 , Rusizi : 46 , Burera : 46 mu gihe Uturere twa Nyaruguru , Ruhango , Gatsibo na Nyagatare nta bwandu bushya bwahabonetse .
Kuri ubu mu gihugu hose abamaze kwandura COVID - 19 ni 39 . 914 mu bipimo 1 . 650 . 629 bimaze gufatwa .
Kuri uyu wa Kane nta murwayi wakize byatumye abakize baguma ku 27 . 272 mu gihe 12 . 194 bakirwaye , muri bo 37 bakaba barembye .
Mu gihe ubwiyongere bwa abandura na abahitanwa na Coronavirus buzamuka , hakajijwe ingamba zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya iki cyorezo zirimo ko isaha ntarengwa yo kugera mu rugo ari saa Kumi na Ebyiri za umugoroba .
Kuva ibikorwa byo gukingira COVID - 19 bitangiye mu Rwanda , abaturage 391 . 870 bahawe urukingo .
Abantu 251 . 139 ni bo bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa AstraZeneca barimo 875 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Barindwi bishwe na Coronavirus mu Rwanda , 849 barayandura . Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yatangaje ko barindwi bishwe na Coronavirus kuri uyu wa Gatatu , tariki ya 30 Kamena 2021 , ari abagore bane ba imyaka 76 ( Musanze ) , 58 ( Kirehe ) 58 na 51 ( Kigali ) na abagabo batatu ba imyaka 85 ( Kamonyi ) , 82 na 75 ( Karongi ) .
Abarwayi bashya 849 babonetse mu bipimo 10 . 167 byafashwe ituma umubare wa abamaze kwandura mu Rwanda uba 39 . 047 mu bipimo 1 . 641 . 582 bimaze gufatwa kuva muri Werurwe 2020 .
Kuri uyu munsi ubwandu bwinshi bwagaragaye mu Mujyi wa Kigali ahasanzwe abarwayi 199 , Muhanga [ 96 ] , Rubavu [ 95 ] , Gicumbi [ 64 ] , Musanze [ 54 ] , Rulindo [ 40 ] .
Uturere twa Ngoma na Nyabihu ni two tutabonetsemo umurwayi na umwe .
Mu masaha 24 yashize , nta murwayi wakize byatumye umubare wa abamaze gusezererwa mu bitaro no gukirira mu ngo zabo uguma ku 27 . 272 .
Kugeza uyu munsi , abarwayi 11 . 337 barimo 39 barembye ni bo bakiri kwitabwaho .
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda hamaze gukingirwa abantu 391 . 805 kuva ibi bikorwa byatangira ku wa 5 Werurwe 2021 .
Abantu 250 . 264 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya urukingo rwa AstraZeneca barimo 738 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Ibimenyetso bya Coronavirus birimo inkorora , ibicurane , guhumeka bigoranye na umuriro .
Yandura binyuze mu matembabuzi aturuka mu myanya ya ubuhumekero .
Abaturarwanda basabwa gukomeza kubahiriza amabwiriza ya inzego za ubuzima hitabwa cyane cyane ku gukaraba intoki kenshi na amazi na isabune , kwambara udupfukamunwa mu gihe umuntu avuye mu rugo cyangwa ahuye na abantu benshi mu nsisiro cyangwa ahatuye imiryango myinshi .
Gahunda ni Gera mu rugo saa Kumi na ebyiri # Bosebabireba - CP Kabera .
Amabwiriza mashya yatangajwe ku wa Kabiri , tariki ya 29 Kamena 2021 , agena ko ingamba nshya zigomba gushyirwa mu bikorwa guhera tariki ya 1 Nyakanga 2021 mu " " " " Mujyi wa Kigali no mu Turere twa Burera , Gicumbi , Kamonyi , Musanze , Nyagatare , Rubavu , Rutsiro na Rwamagana . " " " "
Aya mabwiriza agena ko ingendo zibujijwe guhera " " " " Saa Kumi na ebyiri za nimugoroba kugeza saa Kumi za mu gitondo . " " " "
Ni mu gihe ibikorwa byose byemerewe gukomeza bizajya bifunga saa Kumi na imwe za nimugoroba .
CP John Bosco Kabera wari mu kiganiro kuri RBA yavuze ko gahunda abantu bose bya umwihariko abo muri ibyo bice bakwiye kubahiriza ari ukugera mu ngo zabo ku isaha yateganyijwe .
Ati " " " " Kuri bose rero , gahunda ni gera mu rugo saa Kumi na ebyiri bose babireba . " " " "
CP Kabera kandi yihanije abantu batangiye kuvuga ko isaha ya saa Kumi na ebyiri [ 18h00 ] , yashyizweho , ari kare cyane bityo bakaba bashobora kuzafatirwa mu duce batuyemo banze kujya mu ngo zabo ngo kuko butari bwira .
Ati " " " " Polisi ntabwo izihanganira abantu batangiye kuvuga ko kugera mu rugo saa Kumi na ebyiri za nimugoroba ari kare cyane bityo bakaba bateganya kuzava mu kazi cyangwa aho bakorera bagorobereza muri Quartier ngo ku bo bategereje ko bwira bakabona kujya mu ngo zabo . " " " "
" " " " Ntabwo Polisi izabyemera !
Abantu barakangurirwa kureka gukora ingendo zitari ngombwa . " " " "
Uretse amabwiriza areba uturere umunani na Umujyi wa Kigali , Guverinoma ya u Rwanda yatangaje ko ibindi bice bisigaye bya igihugu , ingendo zibujijwe guhera saa Kumi na ebyiri za nimugoroba kugeza saa Kumi za mu gitondo .
Ni mu gihe ibikorwa byose byemerewe gukomeza bizajya bifunga saa Kumi na imwe za nimugoroba .
Muri rusange na ubwo hari ingamba zo gukumira ikwirakwira ziba zashyizweho , Abanyarwanda bakangurirwa gukomeza kubahiriza amabwiriza ya inzego za ubuzima asaba gukaraba amazi meza na isabune , kwambara neza agapfukamunwa , kwirinda gukora ingendo zitari ngombwandetse no guhana intera mu gihe habayeho guhura .
Bane bishwe na Coronavirus mu RwandHagiye kwitabazwa Ibitaro bya Intara kubera ubwinshi bwa abandura na abazahazwa na Covid - 19 i Rubavua , naho 36 barembejwe nayo .
Abitabye Imana ni abagore babiri barimo uwa imyaka 104 wa i Kigali na uwa 66 wa i Rubavu , na abagabo babiri barimo uwa imyaka 58 wa i Rubavu na uwa 57 wa i Huye .
Umubare wa abakirwaye wageze ku 10 . 495 barimo 36 barembye ; mu gihe abamaze kwandura icyo cyorezo mu gihugu ubu ari 38 . 198 ubariyemo 814 bashya babonetse mu masaha 24 ashize .
Umujyi wa Kigali ni wo wagaragayemo abarwayi bashya benshi ( 187 ) naho Nyabihu ni ko karere rukumbi katabonetsemo umurwayi mushya .
Raporo ya Minisante igaragaza ko nta murwayi wakize uyu munsi bigatuma umubare wa abakize ukomeza kuba 27 . 272 ; naho ibipimo 10 . 103 byafashwe byatumye ibimaze gufatwa bigera ku 1 . 631 . 415 .
Abagera ku 391 . 785 ni bo bamaze gukingirwa COVID - 19 mu Rwanda .
Muri bo 249 . 526 bahawe dose ya AstraZeneca habariwemo na 400 bayifashe uyu munsi .
Minisante iributsa Abaturarwanda gukomeza kwirinda bubahiriza amabwiriza ya inzego za ubuzima .
Kuva muri Werurwe , abasaga 1700 ni bo bamaze kwandura COVID19 muri Rubavu , aho abasaga 60 % banduye mu kwezi kumwe gusa kwa Kamena 2021 .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na RBA , Guverineri Habitegeko yavuze ko kugeza ubu abarwayi ba Covid - 19 barembye baboneka i Rubavu bagiye kujya boherezwa kuvurirwa ku bitaro bya Kibuye .
Avuga ko kuri ubu i Rubavu hakomeje kugaragara ubwiyongere bukabije bwa abandura Covid - 19 , ndetse ikabazahaza bakaba bari hafi kurenga ubushobozi bwa Ibitaro bya Gisenyi byabakiraga .
Akarere ka Rubavu kari mu twugarijwe bikomeye na ubwandu bwa Covid - 19 bushya aho nko mu Cyumweru gishize hagaragaye abantu bashya banduye iki cyorezo barenga 400 .
Muri rusange imibare ya Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yo ku wa 27 Kamena 2021 , igaragaza ko kuva muri Werurwe 2020 , abantu 36 . 627 ari bo bamaze kwandura Covid - 19 mu bipimo 1 . 614 . 429 bimaze gufatwa hirya no hino mu gihugu .
Inzego zirimo Minisiteri ya Ubuzima zikomeje gusaba Abaturarwanda gukomeza kwirinda icyorezo bubahiriza amabwiriza arimo kwirinda kwihuriza ahantu hafunganye ari benshi kuko byorohereza Coronavirus gukwirakwira .
U Rwanda rurakoza imitwe ya intoki ku ntego yo kubaka ivuriro muri buri kagari .
Muri gahunda ya Guverinoma ya imyaka irindwi ( NST1 ) , harimo umuhigo wa uko buri kagari muri 2 148 turi mu gihugu , kazaba gafite ivuriro rito rizwi nka " " " " Poste de Santé " " " " bitarenze muri 2024 .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima Dr Daniel Ngamije yatangaje ko uwo muhigo uri hafi kweswa , igisigaye akaba ari ukongera serivisi zitangirwa kuri ayo mavuriro ya ibanze .
Yabitangaje kuri iki Cyumweru ubwo hamwe na Umuyobozi Mukuru wa SC Johnson , ikigo cyo muri Amerika kizobereye mu gukora imiti na ibindi bikoresho byifashishwa mu buvuzi , Dr Dr Herbert Fisk Johnson III ndetse na umuyobozi wa Umuryango SFH Rwanda , Manasseh Wandera basuraga ivuriro rya ibanze rya Saruhembe mu Murenge wa Mahama , Akarere ka
Kirehe bakanakurikira igikorwa cyo gukingira Covid - 19 abaturage barengeje imyaka 60 .
Iryo vuriro riherereye mu birometero bike uvuye ku rubibi rwa u Rwanda na Tanzania , ni rimwe mu mavuriro ya ibanze agera kuri 64 yubatswe ku nkunga ya SC Johnson binyuze muri SFH Rwanda .
Minisitiri Ngamije yavuze ko bakeneye abafatanyabikorwa nka abo babafasha gushyira mu bikorwa gahunda Guverinoma yiyemeje , yo kugeza ubuvuzi kuri bose .
Ati " " " " Gukorana na umufatanyabikorwa nka uriya uza tugashyira hamwe twese , tugatanga abakozi , tugatanga ibikoreho , tugatanga imiti , bakadufasha mu bijyanye no kubaka twese tugashyira ingufu hamwe , ni ibintu bishimishije bituma tugenda twongera ubushobozi kugira ngo abantu bacu bavurwe ku gihe kandi neza . " " " "
Dr Ngamije yavuze ko kubera abafatanyabikorwa nka abo , gahunda yo kubaka amavuriro ya ibanze mu tugari twose twa igihugu , iri hafi kugerwaho .
Ati " " " " Mu gihugu hose utugari tudafite postes de santé ntabwo ari twinshi .
Nka aha mu karere ka Kirehe ni tune gusa , utundi twose twarazibonye .
Biraguha ishusho ya uko bihagaze no mu tundi turere .
Imibare isigaye ntabwo ari minini .
Ntabwo ari utugari tugeze kuri 50 mu gihugu hose tutari twabona izi serivisi .
Icyo dushaka gushyiramo ingufu cyane cyane ni ukugira ngo aho batarazibona bazibone ariko na abazibonye dutange serivisi yuzuye . " " " "
Icyakora nubwo amavuriro ya ibanze akomeje kubakawa , Dr Ngamije yavuze ko imbaraga ziri gushyirwa mu kuzongerera ubushobozi kugira ngo zibashe gutanga serivisi nyinshi zikenerwa na abaturage .
Yavuze ko kuri ubu amavuriro mato ari kubakwa guhera umwaka ushize " " " " afite serivisi zose abaturage baba bakeneye kugira ngo tubarinde urugendo rugana ku kigo nderabuzima kuko hari igihe usanga ikigo nderabuzima kiri kure . " " " "
Muri izo serivisi ziri kongerwa mu mavuriro mato harimo nka ububyaza , ubuvuzi bwa amaso , ubwa amenyo na ibindi .
Nibura ivuriro rya ibanze , ribarirwa guha serivisi za ubuvuzi abaturage bari hagati ya ibihumbi bitanu na ibihumbi birindwi .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa SC Johnson , Dr Herbert Fisk Johnson III , yashimiye ubufatanye buri hagati ya ikigo ayoboye na Guverinoma ya u Rwanda mu kugeza ubuvuzi bwa ibanze ku baturage , ashimangira ko bazakomeza gutanga uwo musanzu .
Uretse kubaka amavuriro ya ibanze no gushyiramo ibikoresho , icyo kigo kinafasha Leta ya u Rwanda mu zindi gahunda nko gutanga imiti yo guhashya malaria , kurwanya Covid - 19 aho giherutse gutanga inkingo za Pfizer ibihumbi 60 na ibindi .
Kubaka amavuriro ya ibanze ku rwego rwa utugari no kwegereza serivisi za ubuzima abaturage , ni umwe mu myanzuro 13 yafatiwe mu Mwiherero wa 15 wa abayobozi wabaye mu 2018 .
Ni mu gihe raporo zitandukanye za Minisiteri ya Ubuzima zerekana ko 83 % bya indwara zivurwa , usanga zivurirwa ku rwego rwa utugari na imirenge kuko ari zo nzego zegereye abaturage .
Abantu icyenda bahitanywe na Coronavirus mu Rwanda .
Muri raporo ngarukamunsi ya Minisante hagaragajwe ko mu masaha 24 ashize abamaze kwandura bageze ku 36 . 627 kubera 741 bashya babonetse , naho abakize biyongeraho 113 bagera ku 27 . 090 .
Abarwayi bashya babonetse uyu munsi biganjemo abo muri Kigali ( 217 ) , mu gihe Rulindo ari ko karere rukumbi katabonetsemo umurwayi mushya wa Coronavirus .
Hafashwe kandi ibipimo bishya 7 . 863 bituma umubare wa ibimaze gufatwa uba 1 . 614 . 429 .
Abakirwaye bo ni 9 . 117 barimo 26 barembye .
Ijanisha ku bahitanwa na icyorezo ryagumye kuri 1 , 1 % , irya abandura rirazamuka rigera ku 9 , 4 % naho irya abakira riramanuka rigera ku 73 , 9 % .
Abagera ku 391 . 675 ni bo bamaze gukingirwa mu Rwanda .
Muri bo 248 . 718 bamaze guhabwa doze ya kabiri ya AstraZeneca , barimo 174 bayihawe uyu munsi .
Minisante irasaba Abaturarwanda gukomeza kwirinda icyorezo bubahiriza amabwiriza ya inzego za ubuzima , cyane cyane birinda kwihuriza ahantu hafunganye ari benshi kuko byorohereza Coronavirus gukwirakwira .
Menya ibihugu 11 bimaze kubonekamo Delta Plus , Virus ya rurangiza ya Covid - 19 .
Ubu bwoko bushya bwakangaranyije Isi ubundi bwahawe izina rya B . 1 . 617 . 2 . 1 cyangwa AY . 1 ariko bumenyekana ku rya Delta Plus .
Inzobere mu buzima zikomeje gucukumbura ngo zimenye niba ubu bwoko bwa Delta Plus bwaba bufite umwihariko mu kwandura vuba kurusha ubwabonetse mbere bwa Alpha na ubwa Delta nubwo ngo hakiri kare kumenya nyira izina ingaruka zose zishobora guterwa na iyi virus nshya .
Delta Plus imaze kugaragarara mu bihugu 11 aho abayanduye benshi bamaze kuboneka muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
U Bwongereza ni cyo gihugu cya kabiri gifite abanduye benshi .
Aba mbere bagaragaweho na iyi virus mu Bwongereza bivugwa ko bari baherutse gutemberera mu bihugu bya Nepal na Turikiya .
U Buhinde buza ku mwanya wa gatatu mu kugira umubare munini wa abamaze kwandura Delta Plus aho bagera kuri 40 nka uko leta ya icyo gihugu yabitangaje ku wa Gatatu wa iki cyumweru .
Ibindi bihugu umunani bimaze kugaragaramo ubwo bwoko bushya bwa agakoko ka Coronavirus buzwi nka Delta Plus ni Canada , u Buyapani , Nepal , Pologne , Portugal , u Burusiya , u Busuwisi na Turikiya .
Umubare wa abamaze kwandura Coronavirus mu Rwanda warenze ibihumbi 35 .
Muri raporo ngarukamunsi yo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , Umujyi wa Kigali ni wo wabonetsemo abarwayi benshi ( 343 ) , naho Bugesera , Kirehe , Nyagatare na Rwamagana nta murwayi wahabonetse .
Itangazo ryashyizwe ahagaragara rivuga ko abamaze gukira icyo cyorezo ari 26 . 977 ubariyemo 112 bakize uyu munsi , naho abakirwaye ni 7 . 637 .
Hagaragajwe kandi ko abamaze guhitanwa na icyorezo bageze kuri 404 kubera babiri biyongereho , mu gihe abarembye babaye 26 .
Abaturarwanda 391 . 625 bamaze guhabwa urukingo rwa Coronavirus , ibipimo bimaze gufatwa mu mezi 15 imaze igaragaye mu Rwanda byo ni 1 . 594 . 197 habariwemo na 10 . 585 byafashwe mu masaha 24 ashize .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima iributsa Abaturarwanda gukomeza kubahiriza amabwiriza ya inzego za ubuzima haba abakingiwe na abatarakingiwe , kandi bakirinda guhurira ahantu hafunganye ari benshi kuko byagaragaye ko biha icyuho icyorezo .
Igiciro cyo kwipimisha Covid - 19 kigiye guhinduka .
Ubusanzwe kwipimisha Covid - 19 bikorwa mu buryo bubiri .
Hari ikizamini gifatwa cyihuta cyizwi nka " " " " Antigen Covid - 19 rapid test " " " " cyishyurwa 10 . 000 Frw .
Icyo umuntu apimwa mu mazuru ibisubizo bikaboneka mu minota itarenze 30 cyangwa iri hasi yayo .
Hari ikindi cyitwa " " " " PCR " " " " gifatwa mu kanwa , cyo kiba kigamije gucukumbura ngo kirebe ko umuntu adafite ubwandu bwa Covid - 19 , ibisubizo biboneka nyuma ya amasaha 24 , umuntu akishyura 47 . 200 Frw .
Umuyobozi wa RBC , Dr . Sabin Nsanzimana , ubwo yaganiraga na KT Radio , yavuze ko leta iri hafi kugabanya ikiguzi cyasabwaga mu gihe cyo kwipimisha Coronavirus .
Ati " " " " Twasoje kugirana ibiganiro na sosiyete zitunganya ibikoresho byifashishwa mu gupima Covid - 19 ku buryo byatuma ikiguzi cyo kwipimisha kigabanuka kikagera nibura hagati ya amafaranga ya u Rwanda 5000 na 6000 . " " " "
Dr Nsanzimana yashimangiye ko mu gihe ibi byaba bimaze gushyirwa mu ngiro , u Rwanda rwabasha kongera imibare ya abantu bipimisha icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Nubwo kandi umuyobozi wa RBC atatangaje igihe nyira izina bizashyirirwa mu bikorwa , ariko yavuze ko hari amahirwe menshi ko serivisi yo kwipimisha Covid - 19 yakongerwa mu zitangwa na ubwisungane mu kwivuza bwa Mutuelle de Santé .
Kuva Covid - 19 yagera mu Rwanda , hamaze gufatwa ibipimo 1 . 583 . 612 aho muri byo abantu 34 . 143 basanzwe baranduye .
Icyo abaganga bavuga ku bandura Covid - 19 kandi barahawe urukingo .
Ni ibintu abahanga mu birebana na inkingo bemeza ko nta mpungenge biteye , bitewe na uko nubwo bayirwaye hari ubudahangarwa umubiri wabo uba ufite ku buryo badashobora kuremba nka abatarakingiwe .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima Dr . Ngamije Daniel , aherutse kubwira RBA , ko mu bantu basuzumye harimo abasaga 35 banduye kandi bari barakingiwe , ndetse bamwe baranakingiwe inkingo zombie , ariko ko icya ngombwa ari uko uwakingiwe ataremba .
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ariko ntabwo usanga yazanye ibimenyetso mpuruza ngo usange yagiye kwa muganga . Nta na umwe turajyana mu bitaro yarembye , bivuze ngo urukingo rufite akamaro tugomba kurwitabira ariko tukanamenya ko uwakingiwe agomba kwitwararika kugira ngo atandura ngo yanduze na abandi . " " " "
Ibivugwa na Minisitiri wa Ubuzima kandi bishimangirwa na umuganga unafite inararibonye kuko amaze imyaka irenga 45 muri uyu mwuga , Dr . Muyombano Antoine , uvuga ko urukingo rwongerera umubiri ubudahangarwa ku buryo iyo virusi iwugezemo abasirikare bayirwanya .
Yagize ati " " " " Iyo umuntu yakingiwe ni kimwe no kumuha ka gakoko bashegeshe bamazemo uburozi , ariko basigiye ubushobozi bwo kurinda indwara .
Gukingira rero ni kimwe na urukingo rwa iseru , ni kimwe no gutera umwana agakoko gatera iseru ariko batse bwa bushobozi kugira ngo bagasigire ububasha bwo kurinda ya ndwara umubiri . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Rero iteka iyo uhuye na ako gakoko ukamenya ko ugomba kwirwanaho ugasa na aho wohereza ba basirikare bawurinda , ni kimwe no kuvuga ko umuntu aba ari aho aryamiye amajanja umwanzi yaza noneho ukirwanaho . " " " "
Asobanura uburyo hari abantu batatu bamaze guhitanwa na Covid - 19 kandi bari barakingiwe , Dr Muyombano avuga ko nta gitangaza ko uwakingiwe ashobora guhitanwa na izindi ndwara zidakira zirimo SIDA na izindi .
Ati " " " " Umwana wakingiwe iseru ashobora guhitanwa na indwara ya umutima ibyo si ibintu twahakana ariko ntabwo ashobora guhitanwa na indwara ya iseru , iyo afite umubiri ufite ubushobozi bwo kurwanya na izindi ndwara . " " " "
Yakomeje agira ati " " " " Ni ukuvuga ko niba urukingo rugeze mu mubiri washegeshwe na izindi ndwara ari kanseri , ari SIDA ari indwara ya umutima , ari indwara ya impyiko yapfa azize iyo ndwara , kuko nubwo yaba yarakingiwe ariko ntabwo aba yarakingiwe kuri izo ndwara maze kuvuga . " " " "
Kugeza ubu kuva ibikorwa byo gukingira Coronavirusi mu Rwanda bitangiye ku wa 5 Werurwe 2021 , abagera ku 391 . 058 ni bo bamaze guhabwa inkingo za Covid - 19 zo mu bwoko bwa AstraZeneca na Pfizer .
Leta ya u Rwanda ikomeje gukora ibishoboka byose kugira ngo urukingo rugere ku bantu benshi bashoboka , nibura 60 % .
Mu gihe aba bantu bazaba barakingiwe , inzego zishinzwe ubuzima zivuga ko ari bwo ibintu bishobora kuzasubira mu murongo byahozemo Covid - 19 itaraza .
Ni iki kiri gutera ugutumbagira kwa imibare ya abandura na abahitanwa na Covid - 19 ?
Ni kenshi muri raporo ya buri munsi ya Minisiteri ya Ubuzima igaragaza ishusho ya Covid - 19 , abantu bagiye bakangarana babonye umubare munini wa abanduye bashya ariko uretse ku wa 23 Kamena 2021 , nta wundi munsi abanduye bigeze bagera kuri 900 .
Raporo ya Minisiteri ya Ubuzima igaragaza ko mu Cyumweru kimwe , ni ukuvuga kuva ku wa 17 Kamena - 23 Kamena 2021 , abantu bamaze kwandura Covid - 19 ni 4085 .
Ni muri iki Cyumweru kandi hagiye hagaragara abanduye benshi umunsi umwe kuko nko ku wa 21 Kamena handuye abantu 622 , ku wa 22 Kamena handura abantu 861 mu gihe mu masaha 24 yo ku wa 23 Kamena 2021 , habonetse abarwayi bashya 964 .
Ibi bivuze ko muri iyi minsi itatu ishize ari iya amateka mashya ya Covid - 19 mu Rwanda kuko urebye na umubare wa abamaze kwicwa na iki cyorezo muri iyo minsi itatu ni 15 .
Minisiteri ya Ubuzima yabwiye IGIHE ko kugeza ubu abarwayi bangana na 96 % , bari kwitabwaho bari iwabo mu ngo naho abandi basigaye bari mu bigo byita ku barwayi ba Covid - 19 [ Treatment Centers ] bya Nyarugenge na Kanyinya .
Iyi mibare hari icyo isobanuye
Muri rusange uko imibare ya abandura yiyongera ni ko na abarwayi bakenera kwitabwaho biyongera kuko ubu abarwaye bose ni 6 . 129 barimo 12 barembye .
Ni mu gihe umubare wa abakira uri kugabanyuka kuko bakize mu masaha 24 yashize hakize abantu 22 gusa .
Minisitiri wa Ubuzima , Dr Ngamije Daniel yavuze ko impamvu ziri gutuma imibare ya abandura na abahitanwa na Covid - 19 yiyongera zishingiye cyane ku kudohoka kwa Abanyarwanda ku bijyanye no kubahiriza amabwiriza yashyizweho hagamijwe kwirinda ikwirakwira rya iki cyorezo .
Ati " " " " Muri iyi minsi ishize , imibare ya abandura Covid - 19 ndetse na abajyanwa mu bitaro yongeye kuzamuka , zimwe mu mpamvu zibitera ni uko habayeho kudohoka kwa benshi ndetse no kudakurikiza ingamba zo kwirinda . " " " "
Leta ya u Rwanda ikomeje gukora ibishoboka byose kugira ngo urukingo rugere ku bantu benshi bashoboka , nibura 60 % ya Abanyarwanda bose .
Mu gihe aba bantu bazaba barakingiwe , inzego zishinzwe ubuzima zivuga ko ari bwo ibintu bishobora kuzasubira mu murongo byahozemo Covid - 19 itaraza .
